praṇamya śirasā devau pitāmahamaheśvarau । nāṭyaśāstraṃ pravakṣyāmi brahmaṇā yadudāhṛtam ।। samāptajapyaṃ vratinaṃ svasutaiḥ parivāritam । anadhyāye kadācittu bharataṃ nāṭyakovidam ।।
munayaḥ paryupāsyainamātreyapramukhāḥ purā । papracchuste mahātmāno niyatendriyabuddhayaḥ ।। yo ayaṃ bhagavatā samyaggrathito vedasammitaḥ । nāṭyavedaṃ kathaṃ brahmannutpannaḥ kasya vā kṛte ।।
katyaṅgaḥ kiṃpramāṇaśca prayogaścāsya kīdṛśaḥ । sarvametadyathātattvaṃ bhagavanvaktumarhasi ।। teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ । pratyuvāca tato vākyaṃ nāṭyavedakathāṃ prati ।।
bhavadbhiḥ śucibhirbhūtvā tathā'vahitamānasaiḥ । śrūyatāṃ nāṭyavedasya sambhavo brahmanirmitaḥ ।। pūrvaṃ kṛtayuge viprā vṛtte svāyaṃbhuve antare । tretāyuge atha samprāpte manorvaivasvatasya tu ।।
grāmyadharmapravṛtte tu kāmalobhavaśaṃ gate । īrṣyākrodhādisaṃmūḍhe loke sukhitaduḥkhite ।। devadānavagandharvayakṣarakṣomahoragaiḥ । jambudvīpe samākrānte lokapālapratiṣṭhite ।।
mahendrapramukhairdevairuktaḥ kila pitāmahaḥ । krīḍanīyakamicchāmo dṛṣyaṃ śravyaṃ ca yadbhavet ।। na vedavyavahāro ayaṃ saṃśrāvyaḥ śūdrajātiṣu । tasmātsṛjāparaṃ vedaṃ pañcamaṃ sārvavarṇikam ।।
evamastviti tānuktvā devarājaṃ visṛjya ca । sasmāra caturo vedānyogamāsthāya tattvavit ।। neme vedā yataḥ śrāvyāḥ strīśūdrādyāsu jātiṣu । vedamanyattataḥ srakṣye sarvaśrāvyaṃ tu pañcamam ।।
dharmyamarthyaṃ yaśasyaṃ ca sopadeśyaṃ sasaṅgraham । bhaviṣyataśca lokasya sarvakarmānudarśakam ।। sarvaśātrārthasampannaṃ sarvaśilpapravartakam । nāṭyākhyaṃ pañcamaṃ vedaṃ setihāsaṃ karomyaham ।।
evaṃ saṅkalpya bhagavān sarvavedānanusmaran । nāṭyavedaṃ tataścakre caturvedāṅgasambhavam ।। jagrāha pāṭhyamṛgvedātsāmabhyo gītameva ca । yajurvedādabhinayān rasānātharvaṇādapi ।।
vedopavedaiḥ sambaddho nāṭyavedo mahātmanā । evaṃ bhagavatā sṛṣṭo brahmaṇā sarvavedinā ।। utpādya nāṭyavedaṃ tu brahmovāca sureśvaram । itihāso mayā sṛṣṭaḥ sa sureṣu niyujyatām ।।
kuśalā ye vidagdhāśca pragalbhāśca jitaśramāḥ । teṣvayaṃ nāṭyasaṃjño hi vedaḥ saṃkrāmyatāṃ tvayā ।। tacchṛtvā vacanaṃ śakro brahmaṇā yadudāhṛtam । prāñjaliḥ praṇato bhūtvā pratyuvāca pitāmaham ।।
grahaṇe dhāraṇe jñāne prayoge cāsya sattama । aśaktā bhagavan devā ayogyā nāṭyakarmaṇi ।। ya ime vedaguhyajñā ṛṣayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ । ete asya grahaṇe śaktāḥ prayoge dhāraṇe tathā ।।
śrutvā tu śakravacanaṃ māmāhāmbujasambhavaḥ । tvaṃ putraśatasaṃyuktaḥ prayoktā'sya bhavānagha ।। ājñāpito viditvā'haṃ nāṭyavedaṃ pitāmahāt । putrānadhyāpayāmāsa prayogaṃ cāpi tattvataḥ ।।
śāṇḍilyaṃ caiva vātsyaṃ ca kohalaṃ dattilaṃ tathā । jaṭilambaṣṭakau caiva taṇḍumagniśikhaṃ tathā ।। saindhavaṃ sapulomānaṃ śāḍvaliṃ vipulaṃ tathā । kapiñjaliṃ vādiraṃ ca yamadhūmrāyaṇau tathā ।।
jambudhvajaṃ kākajaṅghaṃ svarṇakaṃ tāpasaṃ tathā । kaidāriṃ śālikarṇaṃ ca dīrghagātraṃ ca śālikam ।। kautsaṃ tāṇḍāyaniṃ caiva piṅgalaṃ citrakaṃ tathā । bandhulaṃ bhallakaṃ caiva muṣṭhikaṃ saindhavāyanam ।।
taitilaṃ bhārgavaṃ caiva śuciṃ bahulameva ca । abudhaṃ budhasenaṃ ca pāṇḍukarṇaṃ sukeralam ।। ṛjukaṃ maṇḍakaṃ caiva śambaraṃ vañjulaṃ tathā । māgadhaṃ saralaṃ caiva kartāraṃ cogrameva ca ।।
tuṣāraṃ pārṣadaṃ caiva gautamaṃ bādarāyaṇam । viśālaṃ śabalaṃ caiva sunāmaṃ meṣameva ca ।। kāliyaṃ bhramaraṃ caiva tathā pīṭhamukhaṃ munim । nakhakuṭṭāśmakuṭṭau ca ṣaṭpadaṃ sottamaṃ tathā ।।
pādukopānahau caiva śrutiṃ cāṣasvaraṃ tathā । agnikuṇḍājyakuṇḍau ca vitaṇḍya tāṇḍyameva ca ।। kartarākṣaṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ kuśalaṃ dussahaṃ tathā । lājaṃ bhayānakaṃ caiva bībhatsaṃ savicakṣaṇam ।।
puṇḍrākṣaṃ puṇḍranāsaṃ cāpyasitaṃ sitameva ca । vidyujjihvaṃ mahājihvaṃ śālaṅkāyanameva ca ।। śyāmāyanaṃ māṭharaṃ ca lohitāṅgaṃ tathaiva ca । saṃvartakaṃ pañcaśikhaṃ triśikhaṃ śikhameva ca ।।
śaṅkhavarṇamukhaṃ śaṇḍaṃ śaṅkukarṇamathāpi ca । śakranemiṃ gabhastiṃ cāpyaṃśumāliṃ śaṭhaṃ tathā ।। vidyutaṃ śātajaṅghaṃ ca raudraṃ vīramathāpi ca । pitāmahājñayā'smābhirlokasya ca guṇepsayā ।।
prayojitaṃ putraśataṃ yathābhūmivibhāgaśaḥ । yo yasminkarmaṇi yathā yogyastasmin sa yojitaḥ ।। bhāratīṃ sātvatīṃ caiva vṛīttimārabhaṭīṃ tathā । samāśritaḥ prayogastu prayukto vai mayā dvijāḥ ।।
parigṛhya praṇamyātha brahmā vijñāpito mayā । athāha māṃ suraguruḥ kaiśikimapi yojaya ।। yacca tasyāḥ kṣamaṃ dravyaṃ tad brūhi dvijasattama । evaṃ tenāsmyabhihitaḥ pratyuktaśca mayā prabhuḥ ।।
dīyatāṃ bhagavandravyaṃ kaiśikyāḥ samprayojakam । nṛttāṅgahārasampannā rasabhāvakriyātmikā ।। dṛṣṭā mayā bhagavato nīlakaṇṭhasya nṛtyataḥ । kaiśikī ṣlakṣṇanaipathyā śṛṅgārarasasambhavā ।।
aśakyā puruṣaiḥ sā tu prayoktuṃ strījanādṛte । tato asṛjanmahātejā manasā'psaraso vibhuḥ ।। nāṭyālaṅkāracaturāḥ prādānmahyaṃ prayogataḥ । mañjukeśīṃ sukeśīṃ ca miśrakeśīṃ sulocanām ।।
saudāminīṃ devadattāṃ devasenāṃ manoramām । sudatīṃ sundarīṃ caiva vidagdhāṃ vipulāṃ tathā ।। sumālāṃ santatiṃ caiva sunandāṃ sumukhīṃ tathā । māgadhīmarjunīṃ caiva saralāṃ keralāṃ dhṛtim ।।
nandāṃ sapuṣkalāṃ caiva kalamāṃ caiva me dadau । svātirbhāṇḍaniyuktastu saha śiṣyaiḥ svayambhuvā ।। nāradādyāśca gandharvā gānayoge niyojitāḥ । evaṃ nāṭyamidaṃ samyagbuddhvā sarvaiḥ sutaiḥ saha ।।
svātināradasaṃyukto vedavedāṅgakāraṇam । upasthito ahaṃ brahmāṇaṃ prayogārthaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। nāṭyasya grahaṇaṃ prāptaṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇyaham । etattu vacanaṃ śrutvā pratyuvāca pitāmahaḥ ।।
mahānayaṃ prayogasya samayaḥ pratyupasthitaḥ । ayaṃ dhvajamahaḥ śrīmān mahendrasya pravartate ।। atredānīmayaṃ vedo nāṭyasaṃjñaḥ prayujyatām । tatastasmindhvajamahe nihatāsuradānave ।।
prahṛṣṭāmarasaṃkīrṇe mahendravijayotsave । pūrvaṃ kṛtā mayā nāndī hyāśīrvacasaṃyutā ।। aṣṭāṅgapadasaṃyuktā vicitrā vedanirmitā । tadante anukṛtirbaddhā yathā daityāḥ surairjitāḥ ।।
sampheṭavidravakṛtā cchedyabhedyāhavālmikā । tato brahmādayo devāḥ prayogaparitoṣitāḥ ।। pradadurmatsutebhyastu sarvopakaraṇāni vai । prītastu prathamaṃ śakro dattavānsvaṃ dhvajaṃ śubham ।।
brahmā kuṭilakaṃ caiva bhṛṅgāraṃ varuṇaḥ śubham । sūryaśchatraṃ śivassiddhiṃ vāyurvyajanameva ca ।। viṣṇuḥ siṃhāsanaṃ caiva kubero mukuṭaṃ tathā । śrāvyatvaṃ prekṣaṇīyasya dadau devī sarasvatī ।।
śeṣā ye devagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ । tasminsadasyabhipretānnānājātiguṇāśrayān ।। aṃśāṃśairbhāṣitaṃ bhāvān rasān rūpaṃ balaṃ tathā । dattavantaḥ prahṛṣṭāste matsutebhyo divaukasaḥ ।।
evaṃ prayoge prārabdhe daityadānavanāśane । abhavankṣubhitāḥ sarve daityā ye tatra saṅgatāḥ ।। virūpākṣa purogāṃśca vighnānprotsāhya te abruvan । na kṣamiṣyāmahe nāṭyametadāgamyatāmiti ।।
tatastairasuraiḥ sārdhaṃ vighnā māyāmupāśritāḥ । vācaśceṣṭāṃ smṛtiṃ caiva stambhayanti sma nṛtyatām ।। tathā vidhvaṃsanaṃ dṛṣṭvā sūtradhārasya devarāṭ । kasmātprayogavaiṣamyamityuktvā dhyānamāviśat ।।
athāpaśyatsado vighnaiḥ samantādparivāritam । sahetaraiḥ sūtradhāraṃ naṣṭasaṃjñaṃ jaḍīkṛtam ।। utthāya tvaritaṃ śakraṃ gṛhītvā dhvajamuttamam । sarvaratnojjvalatanuḥ kiñcidudvṛta locanaḥ ।।
raṅgapīṭhagatānvighnānasurāṃścaiva devarāṭ । jarjarīkṛtadehāṃstānakarojjarjareṇa saḥ ।। nihateṣu ca sarveṣua vighneṣu saha dānavaiḥ । saṃprahṛṣya tato vākyamāhuḥ sarve divaukasaḥ ।।
aho praharaṇaṃ divyamidamāsāditaṃ tvayā । jarjarīkṛtasarvāṅgā yenaite dānavāḥ kṛtāḥ ।। yasmādanena te vighnāḥ sāsurā jarjarīkṛtāḥ । tasmājjarjara eveti nāmato ayaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
śeṣā ye caiva hiṃsārthamupayāsyanti hiṃsakāḥ । dṛṣṭvaiva jarjaraṃ te api gamiṣyantyevameva tu ।। evamevāstviti tataḥ śakraḥ provāca tānsurān । rakṣābhūtaśca sarveṣāṃ bhaviṣyatyeṣa jarjaraḥ ।।
prayoge prastute hyevaṃ sphīte śakramahe punaḥ । trāsaṃ sañjanayanti sma vighnāḥ śeṣāstu nṛtyatām ।। dṛṣṭvā teṣāṃ vyavasitaṃ daityānāṃ viprakārajam । upasthito ahaṃ brahmāṇaṃ sutaiḥ sarvaiḥ samanvitaḥ ।।
niścitā bhagavanvighnā nāṭyasyāsya vināśane । asya rakṣāvidhiṃ samyagājñāpaya sureśvara ।। tataśca viśvakarmāṇaṃ brahmovāca prayatnataḥ । kuru lakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ nāṭyaveśma mahāmate ।।
tato acireṇa kālena viśvakarmā mahacchubham । sarvalakṣaṇasampannaṃ kṛtvā nāṭyagṛhaṃ tu saḥ ।। proktavāndruhiṇaṃ gatvā sabhāyāntu kṛtāñjalīḥ । sajjaṃ nāṭyagṛhaṃ deva tadevekṣitumarhasi ।।
tataḥ saha mahendreṇa suraiḥ sarvaiśca setaraiḥ । āgatastvarito dṛṣṭuṃ druhiṇo nāṭyamaṇḍapam ।। dṛṣṭvā nāṭyagṛhaṃ brahmā prāha sarvānsurāṃstataḥ । aṃśabhāgairbhavadbhistu rakṣyo ayaṃ nāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ ।।
rakṣaṇe maṇḍapasyātha viniyuktastu candramāḥ । lokapālāstathā dikṣu vidikṣvapi ca mārutāḥ ।। nepathyabhūmau mitrastu nikṣipto varuṇo ambare । vedikārakṣaṇe vahnirbhāṇḍe sarvadivaukasaḥ ।।
varṇāścatvāra evātha stambheṣu viniyojitāḥ । ādityāścaiva rudrāśca sthitāḥ stambhāntareśvatha ।। dhāraṇīśvatha bhūtāni śālāsvapsarastathā । sarvaveśmasu yakṣiṇyo mahīpṛṣṭhe mahodadhiḥ ।।
dvāraśālāniyuktau tu krutāntaḥ kāla eva ca । sthāpitau dvārapatreṣu nāgamukhyau mahābalau ।। dehalyāṃ yamadaṇḍastu śūlaṃ tasyopari sthitam । dvārapālau sthitau caubhau niyatirmṛtyureva ca ।।
pārśve ca raṅgapīṭhasya mahendraḥ sthitavānsvayam । sthāpitā mattavāraṇyāṃ vidyuddaityaniṣūdanī ।। stambheṣu mattavāraṇyāḥ sthāpitā paripālane । bhūtayakṣapiśāśca guhyakāśca mahābalāḥ ।।
jarjare tu vinikṣiptaṃ vajraṃ daityanibarhaṇam । tatparvasu vinikṣiptāḥ surendrā hyamitaujasaḥ ।। śiraḥparvasthito brahmā dvitīye śaṅkarastathā । tṛtīye ca sthito viṣṇuścaturthe skanda eva ca ।।
pañcame ca mahānāgāḥ śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ । evaṃ vighnavināśāya sthāpitā jarjare surāḥ ।। raṅgapīṭhasya madhye tu svayaṃ brahmā pratiṣṭhitaḥ । iṣṭyarthaṃ raṅgamadhye tu kriyate puṣpamokṣaṇam ।।
pātālavāsino ye ca yakṣaguhyakapannagāḥ । adhastādraṅgapīṭhasya rakṣaṇe te niyojitāḥ ।। nāyakaṃ rakṣatīndrastu nāyikāṃ ca sarasvatī । vidūṣakamathauṅkāraḥ śeśāstu prakṛtirharaḥ ।।
yānyetāni niyuktāni daivatānīha rakṣaṇe । etānyevādhidaivāni bhaviṣyantītyuvāca saḥ ।। etasminnantare devaiḥ sarvairuktaḥ pitāmahaḥ । sāmnā tāvadime vighnāḥ sthāpyantāṃ vacasā tvayā ।।
pūrvaṃ sāmaṃ prayoktavyaṃ dvitīyaṃ dānameva ca । tayorupari bhedastu tato daṇḍaḥ prayujyate ।। devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā vighnānuvāca ha । kasmādbhavanto nāṭyasya vināśāya samutthitāḥ ।।
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ śrutvā virūpākṣo abravīdvacaḥ । daityairvighnagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ sāmapūrvamidaṃ tataḥ ।। yo ayaṃ bhagavatā sṛṣṭo nāṭyavedaḥ surecchayā । pratyādeśo ayamasmākaṃ surārthaṃ bhavatā kṛtaḥ ।।
tannaitadevaṃ kartavyaṃ tvayā lokapitāmaha । yathā devastathā daityāstvattaḥ sarve vinirgatāḥ ।। vighnānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā brahmā vacanamabravīt । alaṃ vo manyunā daityā viṣādaṃ tyajatānaghāḥ ।।
bhavatāṃ devatānāṃ ca śubhāśubhavikalpakaḥ । karmabhāvānvayāpekṣī nāṭyavedo mayā kṛtaḥ ।। naikāntato atra bhavatāṃ devānāṃ cānubhāvanam । trailokyāsyāsya sarvasya nāṭyaṃ bhāvānukīrtanam ।।
kvaciddharmaḥ kvacitkrīḍā kvacidarthaḥ kvacicchamaḥ । kvaciddhāsyaṃ kvacidyuddhaṃ kvacitkāmaḥ kvacidvadhaḥ ।। dharmo dharmapravṛttānāṃ kāmaḥ kāmopasevinām । nigraho durvinītānāṃ vinītānāṃ damakriyā ।।
klībānāṃ dhārṣṭyajananamutsāhaḥ śūramāninām । abudhānāṃ vibodhaśca vaiduṣyaṃ viduṣāmapi ।। īśvarāṇāṃ vilāsaśca sthairyaṃ duḥkhārditasya ca । arthopajīvināmartho dhṛtirudvegacetasām ।।
nānābhāvopasampannaṃ nānāvasthāntarātmakam । lokavṛttānukaraṇaṃ nāṭyametanmayā kṛtam ।। uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ narāṇāṃ karmasaṃśrayam । hitopadeśajananaṃ dhṛtikrīḍāsukhādikṛt ।।
etadraseṣu bhāveṣu sarvakarmakriyāsvatha । sarvopadeśajananaṃ nāṭyaṃ loke bhaviṣyati ।। duḥkhārtānāṃ śramārtānāṃ śokārtānāṃ tapasvinām । viśrāntijananaṃ kāle nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati ।।
dharmyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ hitaṃ buddhivivardhanam । lokopadeśajananaṃ nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati ।। na tajjñānaṃ na tacchilpaṃ na sā vidyā na sā kalā । nāsau yogo na tatkarma nāṭye asmin yanna dṛśyate ।।
tannātra manyuḥ kartavyo bhavadbhiramarānprati । saptadvīpānukaraṇaṃ nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati ।। yenānukaraṇaṃ nāṭyametattadyanmayā kṛtam ।। devānāmasurāṇāṃ ca rājñāmatha kuṭumbinām ।
brahmarṣīṇāṃ ca vijñeyaṃ nāṭyaṃ vṛttāntadarśakam ।। yo ayaṃ svabhāvo lokasya sukhaduḥkhasamanvitaḥ । so aṅgādyabhinayopeto nāṭyamityabhidhīyate ।। vedavidyetihāsānāmākhyānaparikalpanam ।
vinodakaraṇaṃ loke nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati ।। śrutismṛtisadācārapariśeṣārthakalpanam । vinodajananaṃ loke nāṭyametadbhaviṣyati ।। etasminnantare devān sarvānāha pitāmahaḥ ।
kriyatāmadya vidhivadyajanaṃ nāṭyamaṇḍape ।। balipradānairhomaiśca mantrauṣadhisamanvitaiḥ । bhojyairbhakṣaiśca pānaiśca baliḥ samupakalpatām ।। martyalokagatāḥ sarve śubhāṃ pūjāmavāpsyatha ।
apūjayitvā raṅgaṃ tu naiva prekṣāṃ pravartayet ।। apūjayitvā raṅgaṃ tu yaḥ prekṣāṃ kalpayiṣyati । niṣphalaṃ tasya tat jñānaṃ tiryagyoniṃ ca yāsyati ।। yajñena saṃmitaṃ hyedadraṅgadaivatapūjanam ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena kartavyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ।। nartako arthapatirvāpi yaḥ pūjāṃ na kariṣyati । na kārayiṣyantyanyairvā prāpnotyapacayaṃ tu saḥ ।। yathāvidhiṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yastu pūjāṃ kariṣyati ।
sa lapsyate śubhānarthān svargalokaṃ ca yāsyati ।। evamuktvā tu bhagavāndruhiṇaḥ sahadevataiḥ । raṅgapūjāṃ kuruśveti māmevaṃ samacodayat ।। bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā papracchurmunayastataḥ ।
bhagavan śrotumicchāmo yajanaṃ raṅgasaṃśrayam ।। atha vā yā kriyāstatra lakṣaṇaṃ yacca pūjanam । bhaviṣyadbhirnaraiḥ kāryaṃ kathaṃ tannāṭyaveśmani ।। ihādirnāṭyayogasya nāṭyamaṇḍapa eva hi ।
tasmāttasyaiva tāvattvaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vaktumarhasi ।। teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato abravīt । lakṣaṇaṃ pūjanaṃ caiva śrūyatāṃ nāṭyaveśmanaḥ ।। divyānāṃ mānasī sṛṣṭirgṛheṣūpavaneṣu ca ।
। narāṇāṃ yatnataḥ kāryā lakṣaṇābhihitā kriyā ।। śrūyatāṃ tadyathā yatra kartavyo nāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ । tasya vāstu ca pūjā ca yathā yojyā prayatnataḥ ।।
iha prekṣyāgṛhaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhīmatā viśvakarmaṇā । trividhaḥ sanniveśaśca śāstrataḥ parikalpitaḥ ।। vikṛṣṭaścaturaśraśca tryaśraścaiva tu maṇḍapaḥ । teṣāṃ trīṇi pramāṇāni jyeṣṭhaṃ madhyaṃ tathā'varam ।।
pramāṇameṣāṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ hastadaṇḍasamāśrayam । śataṃ cāṣṭau catuḥṣaṣṭirhastā dvātriṃśadeva ca ।। aṣṭādhikaṃ śataṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭistu madhyamam । kanīyastu tathā veśma hastā dvātriṃśadiṣyate ।।
devānāṃ tu bhavejjyeṣṭhaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ madhyamaṃ bhavet । śeṣāṇāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ tu kanīyaḥ saṃvidhīyate ।। prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ praśastaṃ madhyamaṃ smṛtam । tatra pāṭhyaṃ ca geyaṃ ca sukhaśrāvyataraṃ bhavet ।।
prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ triprakāro vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ । vikṛṣṭaścaturasraśca tryasraścaiva prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। kanīyastu smṛtaṃ tryasraṃ caturasraṃ tu madhyamam । jyeṣṭhaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāṭyavedaprayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
pramāṇaṃ yacca nirdiṣṭaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ viśvakarmaṇā । prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ taccaiva hi nibodhata ।। aṇū rajaśca vālaśca likṣā yūkā yavastathā । aṅgulaṃ ca tathā hasto daṇḍaścaiva prakīrtitaḥ ।।
aṇavo aṣṭau rajaḥ proktaṃ tānyaṣṭau vāla ucyate । vālāstvaṣṭau bhavellikṣā yūkā likṣāṣṭakaṃ bhavet ।। yūkāstvaṣṭau yavo jñeyo yavāstvaṣṭau tathāṅgulam । aṅgulāni tathā hastaścaturviṃśatirucyate ।।
caturhasto bhaveddaṇḍo nirdiṣṭastu pramāṇataḥ । anenaiva pramāṇena vakṣyāmyeṣāṃ vinirṇayam ।। catuḥṣaṣṭikarānkuryāddīrghatvena tu maṇḍapam । dvātriṃśataṃ ca vistāranmartyānāṃ yo bhavediha ।।
ata ūrdhvaṃ na kartavyaḥ kartṛbhirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ । yasmādavyaktabhāvaṃ hi tatra nāṭyaṃ vrajediti ।। maṇḍape viprakṛṣṭe tu pāṭhyamuccāritasvaram । anissaraṇadharmatvādvisvaratvaṃ bhṛśaṃ vrajet ।।
yaścāpyāsyagato bhāvo nānādṛṣṭisamanvitaḥ sa veśmanaḥ prakṛṣṭatvād vrajedavyaktatāṃ parām ।। prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ tasmānmadhyamamiṣyate । yāvatpāṭhyaṃ ca geyaṃ ca tatra śravyataraṃ bhavet ।। prekṣāgṛhāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ triprakāro vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।
vikṛṣṭaścaturasraśca tryasraścaiva prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। kanīyastu smṛtaṃ tryasraṃ caturasraṃ tu madhyamam । jyeṣṭhaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāṭyavedaprayoktṛbhiḥ ।। devānāṃ mānasī sṛṣṭirgṛheṣūpavaneṣu ca ।
yatnabhāvābhiniṣpannāḥ sarve bhāvā hi mānuṣā ।। tasmāddevakṛtairbhāvairna vispardheta mānuṣaḥ । mānuṣasya tu gehasya sampravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। bhūmervibhāgaṃ pūrvaṃ tu parīkṣeta prayojaka ।
tato vāstu pramāṇena prārabheta śubhecchayā ।। samā sthirā tu kaṭhinā kṛṣṇā gaurī ca yā bhavet । bhūmistatraiva kartavyaḥ kartṛbhirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ ।। prathamaṃ śodhanaṃ kṛtvā lāṅgalena samutkṛṣet ।
asthikīlakapālāni tṛṇagulmāṃśca śodhayet ।। śodhayitvā vasumatīṃ pramāṇaṃ nirdiśettataḥ । (trīṇyuttarāṇi saumyaṃ ca viśākhāpi ca revatī । hastitiṣyānurādhāśca praśastā nāṭyakarmaṇi) ।
puṣyanakṣatrayogena śuklaṃ sūtraṃ prasārayet ।। kārpāsaṃ bālbajaṃ vāpi mauñjaṃ vālkalameva ca । sūtraṃ budhaistu kartavyaṃ yasya cchedo na vidyate ।। ardhacchinne bhavetsūtre svāmino maraṇaṃ dhruvam ।
tribhāgacchinnayā rajvā rāṣṭrakopo vidhīyate ।। chinnāyāṃ tu caturbhāge prayokturnāśa ucyate । hastātprabhraṣṭayā vāpi kaścitvapacayo bhavet ।। tasmānnityaṃ prayatnena rajjugrahaṇamiṣyate ।
kāryaṃ caiva prayatnena mānaṃ nāṭyagṛhasya tu ।। muhūrtenānukūlena tithyā sukaraṇena ca । brāhmaṇāṃstarpayitvā tu puṇyāhaṃ vācayettataḥ ।। śāntitoyaṃ tato dattvā tataḥ sūtraṃ prasārayet ।
catuṣṣaṣṭikarānkṛtvā dvidhā kuryātpunaśca tān ।। pṛṣṭhato yo bhavedbhāgo dvidhābhūtasya tasya tu । samamardhavibhāgena raṅgaśīrṣaṃ prakalpayet ।। paścime ca vibhāge atha nepathyagṛhamādiśet ।
vibhajya bhāgānvidhivadyayathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। śubhe nakṣatrayoge ca maṇḍapasya niveśanam । śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣairmṛdaṅgapaṇavādibhiḥ ।। sarvātodyaiḥ praṇuditaiḥ sthāpanaṃ kāryameva tu ।
utsāryāṇi tvaniṣṭāni pāṣaṇḍyāśramiṇastathā ।। kāṣāyavasanāścaiva vikalāścaiava ye narāḥ । niśāyāṃ ca baliḥ kāryā nānābhojanasaṃyutaḥ ।। gandhapuṣpaphalopetā diśo daśa samāśritaḥ ।
pūrveṇa śuklānnayuto nīlānno dakṣiṇena ca ।। paścimena baliḥ pīto raktaścaivottareṇa tu । yādṛśaṃ diśi yasyāṃ tu daivataṃ parikalpitam ।। tādṛśastatra dātavyo balirmantrapuraskṛtaḥ ।
sthāpane brāhmaṇebhyaśca dātavyaṃ ghṛtapāyasam ।। madhuparkastathā rājñe kartṛbhyaśca guḍaudanam । nakṣatreṇa tu kartavyaṃ mūlena sthāpanaṃ budhaiḥ ।। muhūrtenānukūlena tithyā sukaraṇena ca ।
evaṃ tu sthāpanaṃ kṛtvā bhittikarma prayojayet ।। bhittikarmaṇi nirvṛtte stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ tataḥ । tithinakṣatrayogena śubhena karaṇena ca ।। stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ rohiṇyā śravaṇena vā ।
ācāryeṇa suyuktena trirātropoṣitena ca ।। stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ prāpte sūryodaye śubhe । prathame brāhmaṇastambhe sarpissarṣapasaṃskṛtaḥ ।। sarvaśuklo vidhiḥ kāryo dadyātpāyasameva ca ।
tataśca kṣatriyastambhe vastramālyānulepanam ।। sarva raktaṃ pradātavyaṃ dvijebhyaśca guḍaudanam । vaiśyastambhe vidhiḥ kāryo digbhāge paścimottare ।। sarvaṃ prītaṃ pradātavyaṃ dvijebhyaśca ghṛtaudanam ।
śūdrastambhe vidhiḥ kāryaḥ samyakpūrvottarāśraye ।। nīlaprāyaṃ prayatnena kūsaraṃ ca dvijāśanam । pūrvoktabrāhmaṇastambhe śuklamālyānulepane ।। nikṣipetkanakaṃ mūle karṇābharaṇasaṃśrayam ।
tāmraṃ cādhaḥ pradātavyaṃ stambhe kṣatriyasaṃjñake ।। vaiśyastambhasya mūle tu rajataṃ sampradāpayet । śūdrastambhasya mūle tu dadyādāyasameva ca ।। sarveṣveva tu nikṣepyaṃ stambhamūleṣu kāñcanam ।
svastipuṇyāhaghoṣeṇa jayaśabdena caiva hi ।। stambhānāṃ sthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ puṣpamālāpuraskṛtam । ratnadānaiḥ sagodānairvastradānairanalpakaiḥ ।। brāhmaṇāṃstarpayitvā tu stambhānutthāpayettataḥ ।
acalaṃ cāpyakampañca tathaivāvalitaṃ punaḥ ।। stambhasyotthāpane samyagdoṣā hyete prakīrtitāḥ । avṛṣṭiruktā calane valane mṛtyuto bhayam ।। kampane paracakrāttu bhayaṃ bhavati dāruṇam ।
doṣairetairvihīnaṃ tu stambhamutthāpayecchivam ।। pavitre brāhmaṇastambhe dātavyā dakṣiṇā ca gauḥ । śeṣāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ kāryaṃ sthāpane kartṛsaṃśrayam ।। mantrapūtaṃ ca taddeyaṃ nāṭyācāryeṇa dhīmatā ।
purohitaṃ nṛpaṃ caiva bhojayenmadhupāyasaiḥ ।। kartṝnāpi tathā sarvānkṛsarāṃ lavaṇottarām । sarvamevaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā sarvātodyaiḥ pravāditaiḥ ।। abhimantrya yathānyāyaṃ stambhānutthāpayecchuciḥ ।
ayathā'calo girirmerurhimavāṃśca mahābalaḥ ।। jayāvaho narendrasya tathā tvamacalo bhava' । stambhadvāraṃ ca bhittiṃ ca nepathyagṛhameva ca ।। evamutthāpayetajjño vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।
raṅgapīṭhasya pārśve tu kartavyā mattavāraṇī ।। catustambhasamāyuktā raṅgapīṭhapramāṇataḥ । adhyardhahastotsedhena kartavyā mattavāraṇī ।। utsedhena tayostulyaṃ kartavyaṃ raṅgamaṇḍapam ।
tasyāṃ mālyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca gandhaṃ vastraṃ tathaiva ca ।। nānāvarṇāni deyāni tathā bhūtapriyo baliḥ । āyasaṃ tatra dātavyaṃ stambhānāṃ kuśailairadhaḥ ।। bhojane kṛsarāścaiva dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇāśanam ।
evaṃ vidhipuraskāraiḥ kartavyā mattavāraṇī ।। raṅgapīṭhaṃ tataḥ kāryaṃ vidhidṛṣṭeṇa karmaṇā । raṅgaśīrṣastu kartavyaṃ ṣaḍdārukasamanvitam ।। kāryaṃ dvāradvayaṃ cātra nepathyagṛhakasya tu ।
pūraṇe mṛttikā cātra kṛṣṇā deyā prayatnataḥ ।। lāṅgalena samutkṛṣya nirloṣṭatṛṇaśarkaram । lāṅgale śuddhavarṇo tu dhuryo yojyau prayatnataḥ ।। kartāraḥ puruṣaścātra ye aṅgadoṣavivirjitāḥ ।
ahīnāṅgaiśca voḍhavyā mṛttikā piṭakairnavaiḥ ।। evaṃvidhaiḥ prakartavyaṃ raṅgaśīrṣaṃ prayatnataḥ । kūrmapṛṣṭhaṃ na kartavyaṃ matsyapṛṣṭhaṃ tathaiva ca ।। śuddhādarśatalākāraṃ raṅgaśīrṣaṃ praśasyate ।
ratnāni cātra deyāni pūrve vajraṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। vaiḍūryaṃ dakṣiṇe pārśve sphaṭikaṃ paścime tathā । pravālamuttare caiva madhye tu kanakaṃ bhavet ।। evaṃ raṅgaśiraḥ kṛtvā dārukarma prayojayet ।
ūhapratyūhasaṃyuktaḥ nānāśilpaprayojitam ।। nānāsañjavanopetaṃ bahuvyālopaśobhitam । sasālabhañjikābhiśca samantātsamalaṅkṛtam ।। nirvyūhakuharopetaṃ nānāgrathitavedikam ।
nānāvinyāsasaṃyuktaṃ citrajālagavākṣakam ।। supīṭhadhāriṇīyuktaṃ kapotālīsamākulam । nānākuṭṭimavinyastaiḥ stambhaiścāpyupaśobhitam ।। evaṃ kāṣṭhavidhiṃ kṛtvā bhittikarma prayojayet ।
stambhaṃ vā nāgadantaṃ vā vātāyanamathāpi vā ।। koṇaṃ vā sapratidvāraṃ dvāraviddhaṃ na kārayet । kāryaḥ śailaguhākāro dvibhūmirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ ।। mandavātāyanopeto nirvāto dhīraśabdavān ।
tasmānnivātaḥ kartavyaḥ kartṛbhirnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ ।। gambhīrasvaratā yena kutapasya bhaviṣyati । bhittikarmavidhiṃ kṛtvā bhittilepaṃ pradāpayet ।। sudhākarma bahistasya vidhātavyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।
bhittiṣvatha viliptāsu parimṛṣṭāsu sarvataḥ ।। samāsu jātaśobhāsu citrakarma prayojayet । citrakarmaṇi cālekhyāḥ puruṣāḥ srījanāstathā ।। latābandhāśca kartavyāścaritaṃ cātmbhogajam ।
evaṃ vikṛṣṭaṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭyaveśma prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। punareva hi vakṣyāmi caturaśrasya lakṣaṇam । samantataśca kartavyā hastā dvātriṃśadeva tu ।। śubhabhūmivibhāgastho nāṭyajñairnāṭyamaṇḍapaḥ ।
yo vidhiḥ pūrvamuktastu lakṣaṇaṃ maṅgalāni ca ।। vikṛṣṭe tānyaśeṣāṇi caturaśre api kārayet । caturaśraṃ samaṃ kṛtvā sūtreṇa pravibhajya ca ।। bāhyataḥ sarvataḥ kāryā bhittiḥ śliṣṭeṣṭakā dṛḍhā ।
tatrābhyantarataḥ kāryā raṅgapīṭhopari sthitāḥ ।। daśa prayoktṛbhiḥ stambhāḥ śaktā maṇḍapadhāraṇe । stambhānāṃ bāhyataścāpi sopānākṛti pīṭhakam ।। iṣṭakādārubhiḥ kāryaṃ prekṣakāṇāṃ niveśanam ।
hastapramāṇairutsedhairbhūmibhāgasamutthitaiḥ ।। raṅgapīṭhāvalokyaṃ tu kuryādāsanajaṃ vidhim । ṣaḍanyānantare caiva punaḥ stambhānyathādiśam ।। vidhinā sthāpayetajño dṛḍhānmaṇḍapadhāraṇe ।
aṣṭau stambhānpunaścaiva teṣāmupari kalpayet ।। sthāpyaṃ caiva tataḥ pīṭhamaṣṭahastapramāṇataḥ । viddhāsyamaṣṭahastaṃ ca pīṭhaṃ teṣu tato nyaset ।। tatra stambhāḥ pradātavyāstajñairmaṇḍapadhāraṇe ।
dhāraṇīdhāraṇāste ca śālastrībhiralaṅkṛtāḥ ।। nepathyagṛhakaṃ caiva tataḥ kāryaṃ prayatnataḥ । dvāraṃ caikaṃ bhavettatra raṅgapīṭhapraveśanam ।। janapraveśanaṃ cānyadābhimukhyena kārayet ।
raṅgasyābhimukhaṃ kāryaṃ dvitīyaṃ dvārameva tu ।। aṣṭahastaṃ tu kartavyaṃ raṅgapīṭhaṃ pramāṇataḥ । caturaśraṃ samatalaṃ vedikāsamalaṅkṛtam ।। pūrvapramāṇanirdiṣṭā kartavyā mattavāraṇī ।
catuḥstambhasamāyuktā vedikāyāstu pārśvataḥ ।। samunnataṃ samaṃ caiva raṅgaśīrṣaṃ tu kārayet । vikṛṣṭe tūnnataṃ kāryaṃ caturaśre samaṃ tathā ।। evametena vidhinā caturaśraṃ gṛhaṃ bhavet ।
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi tryaśragehasya lakṣaṇam ।। tryaśraṃ trikoṇaṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭyaveśmaprayoktṛbhiḥ । madhye trikoṇamevāsya raṅgapīṭhaṃ tu kārayet ।। dvāraṃ tainaiva koṇena kartavyaṃ tasya veśmanaḥ ।
dvitīyaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ raṅgapīṭhasya pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। vidhiryaścaturaśrasya bhittistambhasamāśrayaḥ । sa tu sarvaḥ prayoktavyastryaśrasyāpi prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। evametena vidhinā kāryā nāṭyagṛhā budhaiḥ ।
punareṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi pūjāmevaṃ yathāvidhiḥ ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpanne kṛte nāṭyagṛhe śubhe । gāvo vaseyuḥ saptāhaṃ saha japyaparairdvijaiḥ ।। tato adhivāsayedveśma raṅgapīṭhaṃ tathaiva ca ।
mantrapūtena toyena prokṣitāṅgo niśāgame ।। yathāsthānāntaragato dīkṣitaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ । trirātropoṣito bhūtvā nāṭyācāryo ahatāmbaraḥ ।। namaskṛtya mahādevaṃ sarvalokodbhavaṃ bhavam ।
jagatpitāmahaṃ caiva viṣṇumindraṃ guhaṃ tathā ।। sarasvatīṃ ca lakṣmīṃ ca siddhiṃ medhāṃ dhṛtiṃ smṛtim । somaṃ sūryaṃ ca maruto lokapālāṃstathāśvinau ।। mitramagniṃ surānvarṇān rudrānkālaṃ kaliṃ tathā ।
mṛtyuṃ ca niyatiṃ caiva kāladaṇḍaṃ tathaiva ca ।। viṣṇupraharaṇaṃ caiva nāgarājaṃ ca vāsukim । vajraṃ vidyutsamudrāṃśca gandharvāpsaraso munīn ।। bhūtān piśācān yakṣāṃśca guhyakāṃśca maheśvarān ।
asurānnāṭyavighnāṃśca tathā'nyāndaityarākṣasān ।। tathā nāṭyakumārīśca mahāgrāmaṇyameva ca । yakṣāṃśca guhyakāṃścaiva bhūtasaṅghāstathaiva ca ।। etāṃścānyāṃśca devarṣīnpraṇamya racitāñjaliḥ ।
yathāsthānāntaragatānsamāvāhya tato vadet ।। bhavadbhirno niśāyāṃ tu kartavyaḥ samparigrahaḥ । sāhāyyaṃ caiva dātavyamasminnāṭye sahānugaiḥ ।। sampūjya sarvānekatra kutapaṃ samprayujya ca ।
jarjarāya prayuñjīta pūjāṃ nāṭyaprasiddhaye ।। tvaṃ mahendrapraharaṇaṃ sarvadānavasūdanam । nirmitassarvadevaiśca sarvavighnanibarhaṇa ।। nṛpasya vijayaṃ śaṃsa ripūṇāṃ ca parājayam ।
gobrāhmaṇaśivaṃ caiva nāṭyasya ca vivardhanam ।। evaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyamupāsyaṃ nāṭyamaṇḍape । niśāyāṃ tu prabhātāyāṃ pūjanaṃ prakramediha ।। ārdrāyāṃ vā maghāyāṃ vā yāmye pūrveṣu vā triṣu ।
āśleṣāmūlayorvāpi kartavyaṃ raṅgapūjanam ।। ācāryeṇa tu yuktena śucinā dīkṣitena ca । raṅgasyodyotanaṃ kāryaṃ devatānāṃ ca pūjanam ।। dinānte dāruṇe ghore muhūrte yamadaivate ।
ācamya tu yathānyāyaṃ devatā vai niveśayat ।। raktāḥ pratisarāḥ sūtraṃ raktagandhāśca pūjitāḥ । raktāḥ sumanasaścaiva yacca raktaṃ phalaṃ bhavet ।। yavaissiddhārthakairlājairakṣataiḥ śālitaṇḍulaiḥ ।
nāgapuṣpasya cūrṇena vituṣābhiḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ ।। etairdravyairyutaṃ kuryāddevatānāṃ niveśanam । ālikhenmaṇḍalaṃ pūrvaṃ yathāsthānaṃ yathāvidhiḥ ।। samantastaśca kartavyaṃ hastā ṣoḍaśa maṇḍalam ।
dvārāṇi cātra kurvīta vidhānena caturdiśam ।। madhye caivātra kartavye dve rekhe tiryagūrdhvage । tayoḥ kakṣyāvibhāgena daivatāni niveśayat ।। padmopaviṣṭaṃ brahmāṇaṃ tasya madhye niveśayet ।
ādau niveśyo bhagavānsārdhaṃ bhūtagaṇaiḥ śivaḥ ।। nārāyaṇo mahendraśca skandaḥ sūryo aśvinau śaśī । sarasvatī ca lakṣmīśca śraddhā medhā ca pūrvataḥ ।। pūrvadakṣiṇato vahnirniveśyaḥ svāhayā saha ।
viśvedevāḥ sagandharvā rudrāḥ sarpagaṇāstathā ।। dakṣiṇena niveśyastu yamo mitraśca sānugaḥ । pitṝnpiśācānuragān guhyakāṃśca niveśayat ।। naiṝtyāṃ rākṣasāṃścaiva bhūtāni ca niveśayat ।
paścimāyāṃ samudrāṃśca varuṇaṃ yādasāṃ patim ।। vāyavyāyāṃ diśi tathā sapta vāyūnniveśayet । tatraiva viniveśyastu garuḍaḥ pakṣibhiḥ saha ।। uttarasyāṃ diśi tathā dhanadaṃ saṃnivieśayet ।
nāṭyasya mātṝśca tathā yakṣānatha saguhyakān ।। tathaivottarapūrvāyāṃ nandyādyāṃśca gaṇeśvarān । brahmarṣibhūtasaṃghāṃśca yathābhāgaṃ niveśayat ।। stambhe sanatkumāraṃ tu dakṣiṇe dakṣameva ca ।
grāmaṇyamuttare stambhe pūjārthaṃ saṃniviśayet ।। anenaiava vidhānena yathāsthānaṃ yathāvidhi । suprasādāni sarvāṇi daivatāni niveśayat ।। sthāne sthāne yathānyāyaṃ viniveśya tu devatāḥ ।
tāsāṃ prakurvīta tataḥ pūjanaṃ tu yathārhataḥ ।। devatābhyastu dātavyaṃ sitamālyānulepanam । gandharvavahnisūryobhyo raktamālyānulepanam ।। gandhaṃ mālyaṃ ca dhūpaṃ ca yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।
datvā tataḥ prakurvīta baliṃ pūjāṃ yathāvidhiḥ ।। brahmāṇaṃ madukarpeṇa pāyasena sarasvatīm । śivaviṣṇumahendrādyāḥ sampūjyā modakairatha ।। ghṛtaudanena hutabhukṣomarkau tu guḍaudanaiḥ ।
viśvedevāḥ sagandharvā munayo madhupāyasaiḥ ।। yamamitrau ca sampūjyāvapūpairmodakaistathā । pitṝnpiśācānuragān sarpiḥkṣīreṇa tarpayet ।। pakvānena tu māṃsena surāsīthuphalāsavaiḥ ।
arcayedbhūtasaṃghāṃśca caṇakaiḥ palalāplutaiḥ ।। anenaiva vidhānena sampūjyā mattavāraṇī । pakvāmena tu māṃsena sampūjyā rakṣasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।। surāmāṃsapradāneana dānavānpratipūjayet ।
śeṣāndevagaṇāṃstajjñaḥ sāpūpotkārikaudanaiḥ ।। matsyaiśca piṣṭabhakṣyaiśca sāgarānsaritastathā । sampūjya varuṇaṃ cāpi dātavyaṃ ghṛtapāyasam ।। nānāphūlaphalaścāpi munīnsampratipūjayet ।
vāyūṃśca pakṣiṇaścaiva vicitrairbhakṣyabhojanaiḥ ।। mātṝrnāṭyasya sarvāstā dhanadaṃ ca sahānugaiḥ । apūpairlājikāmiśrairbhakṣyabhojyaiśca pūjayet ।। evameṣāṃ baliḥ kāryo nānābhojanasaṃśrayaḥ ।
punarmantravidhānena balikarma ca vakṣyate ।। devadeva mahābhāga sarvalokapitāmaha । mantrapūtamimaṃ sarvaṃ pratigṛhṇīṣva me balim ।। devadeva mahābhāga gaṇeśa tripurāntaka ।
pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayodyataḥ ।। nārāyaṇāmitagate padmanābha surottama । pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayārpitaḥ ।। purandarāmarapate vajrapāṇe śatakrato ।
pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva vidhimantrapuraskṛtaḥ ।। devasenāpate skanda bhagavan śaṅkarapriya । baliḥ prītena manasā ṣaṇmukha pratigṛhyatām ।। mahādeva mahāyogindevadeva surottama ।
saṃpragṛhya baliṃ deva rakṣa vighnātsadotthitāt ।। devi devamahābhāge sarasvati haripriye । pragṛhyatāṃ balirmātarmayā bhaktyā samarpitaḥ ।। nānānimittasambhūtāḥ paulastyāḥ sarva eva tu rākṣasendrā mahāsatvāḥ pratigṛhṇīta me balim ।।
lakṣmīḥ siddhirmatirmedhā sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ । mantrapūtamimaṃ devyaḥ pratigṛhṇantu me balim ।। sarvabhūtānubhāvajña lokajīvana māruta । pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayodyataḥ ।।
devavaktra suraśreṣṭha dhūmaketo hutāśana । bhaktyā samudyato deva baliḥ samprati gṛhyatām ।। sarvagrahāṇāṃ pravara tejorāśe divākara । bhaktyā mayodyato deva baliḥ samprati gṛhyatām ।।
sarvagrahapate soma dvijarāja jagatpriya । pragṛhyatāmeṣa balirmantrapūto mayodyataḥ ।। mahāgaṇeśvarāḥ sarve nandīśvarapurogamāḥ । pragṛtāṃ balirbhaktyā mayā samprati coditaḥ ।।
namaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ pratigṛhṇantvimaṃ balim । । kāmapāla namo nityaṃ yasyāyaṃ te vidhiḥ kṛtaḥ ।। nāradastumbaruścaiva viśvāvasupurogamāḥ ।
parigṛhṇantu me sarve gandharvā balimudyatam ।। yamo mitraśca bhagavānīśvarau lokapūjitau । imaṃ me pratigṛhṇītāṃ baliḥ mantrapuraskṛtam ।। rasātalagatebhyaśca pannagebhyo namo namaḥ ।
diśantu siddhiṃ nāṭyasya pūjitāḥ pāpanāśanāḥ ।। sarvāmbhasāṃ patirdevo varuṇo haṃsavāhanaḥ । pūjitaḥ prītamānastu sasamudranadīnadaḥ ।। vainateya mahāsatva sarvapakṣipate vibho ।
pragṛhyatāṃ balirdeva mantrapūto mayodyataḥ ।। dhanādhyakṣo yakṣapatirlokapālo dhaneśvaraḥ । saguhyakassayakṣaśca pratigṛhṇātu me balim ।। namo astu nāṭyamātṛbhyo brāhmyādyābhyo namonamaḥ ।
sumukhībhiḥ prasannābhirbaliradya pragṛhyatām ।। rudrapraharaṇaṃ sarvaṃ pratigṛhṇātu me balim । viṣṇupraharaṇaṃ caiva viṣṇubhaktyā mayodyatam ।। tathā kṛtāntaḥ kālaśca sarvaprāṇivadheśvarau ।
mṛtyuśca niyatiścaiva pratigṛhṇātu me balim ।। yāścāsyāṃ mattavāraṇyāṃ saṃśritā vastudevatāḥ । mantrapūtamimaṃ samyakpratigṛhṇantu me balim ।। anye ye devagandharvā diśo daśa samāśritāḥ ।
divyāntarikṣābhaumāśca tebhyaścāyaṃ baliḥ kṛtaḥ ।। kumbhaṃ salilasampūrṇaṃ puṣpamālāpuraskṛtam । sthāpayedraṅgamadhye tu suvarṇaṃ cātra dāpayet ।। ātodyāni tu sarvāṇi kṛtvā vastrottarāṇi tu ।
gandhairmālyaiśca dhūpaiśca bhakṣyairbhojyaiśca pūjayet ।। pūjayitvā tu sarvāṇi daivatāni yathākramam । jarjarastvabhisampūjyaḥ syāttato vighnajarjaraḥ ।। śvetaṃ śirasi vastraṃ syānnīlaṃ raudre ca parvaṇi ।
viṣṇuparvaṇi vai pītaṃ raktaṃ skandasya parvaṇi ।। mṛḍaparvaṇi citraṃ tu deyaṃ vastraṃ hitārthinā । sadṛśaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ dhūpamālyānulepanam ।। ātodyāni tu sarvāṇi vāsobhiravaguṇṭhayet ।
gandhairmālyaiśca dhūpaiśca bhakṣyabhojaiśca pūjayet ।। sarvamevaṃ vidhiṃ kṛtvā gandhamālyānulepanaiḥ । vighnajarjaraṇārthaṃ tu jarjaraṃ tvabhimantrayet ।। atra vighnavināśārthaṃ pitāmahamukhaissuraiḥ ।
nirmitastvaṃ mahāvīryo vajrasāro mahātanuḥ ।। śiraste rakṣatu bramhā sarvairdevaguṇaiaḥ taha । dvitīyaṃ ca haraḥ parva tṛtīyaṃ ca janārdanaḥ ।। caturthaṃ ca kumāraste pañcamaṃ pannagottamaḥ ।
nityaṃ sarve api pāntu tvāṃ surārthe ca śivo bhava ।। nakṣatre abhijiti tvaṃ hi prasūto ahitasūdana । jayaṃ cābhyudayaṃ caiva pārthivasya samāvaha ।। jarjaraṃ pūjayitvaiavaṃ baliṃ sarvaṃ nividya ca ।
agnau homaṃ tataḥ kuryānmantrāhuitipuraskṛtam ।। hutāśa eva dīptābhirulkābhiḥ parimārjanam । nṛpaternartakīnāṃ ca kuryāddīptyabhivardhanam ।। abhidyotya sahātodyairnṛpatiṃ nartakīstathā ।
mantrapūtena toyena punarabhyukṣya tānvadet ।। mahākule prasūtāḥ stha guṇaughaiścāpyalaṅkṛtāḥ । yadvo janmaguṇopetaṃ tadvo bhavatu nityaśaḥ ।। evamuktvā tato vākyaṃ nṛpatairbhūtaye budhaḥ ।
nāṭyayogaprasiddhyarthamāśiṣassamprayojayet ।। sarasvatī dhṛtirmedhā hrīḥ śrīrlakṣmīssmṛtirmatiḥ । pāntu vo mātaraḥ saumyāssiddhidāśca bhavantu vaḥ ।। homaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ havirmantrapuraskṛtam ।
bhindyātkumbhaṃ tataścaiva nāṭyācāryaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। abhinne tu bhavetkumbhe svāminaḥ śatruto bhayam । bhinne caiva tu vijñeyaḥ svāminaḥ śatrusaṃkṣayaḥ ।। bhinne kumbhe tataścaiva nāṭyacāryaḥ prayatnataḥ ।
pragṛhya dīpikāṃ dīptāṃ sarvaṃ raṅgaṃ pradīpayet ।। kṣveḍitaiḥ sphoṭitaiścaiva valgitaiśca pradhāvitaiḥ । raṅgamadhye tu tāṃ dīptāṃ saśabdāṃ samprayojayet ।। śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣairmṛdaṅgapaṇavaistathā ।
sarvātodyaiḥ praṇaditai raṅge yuddhāni kārayet ।। tatra cchinnaṃ va bhinnaṃ ca dāritaṃ ca saśoṇitam । kṣataṃ pradīptamāyastaṃ nimittaṃ siddhilakṣaṇam ।। samyagiṣṭastu raṅgo vai svāminaḥ śubhamāvahet ।
purasyābālavṛddhasya tathā jānapadasya ca ।। duriṣṭastu tathā raṅgo daivatairduradhiṣṭhitaḥ । nāṭyavidhvasanaṃ kuryānnṛpasya ca tathā'śubham ।। ya evaṃ vidhimutsṛjya yatheṣṭaṃ samprayojayet ।
prāpnotyapacayaṃ śīghraṃ tiryagyoniṃ ca gacchati ।। yajñena sammitaṃ hyetadraṅgadaivatapūjanam । apūjayitvā raṅgaṃ tu naiva prekṣāṃ prayojayet ।। pūjitāḥ pūjayantyete mānitā mānayanti ca ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena kartavyaṃ raṅgapūjanam ।। na tathā pradahatyagniḥ prabhañjanasamīritaḥ । yathā hyapaprayogastu prayukto dahati kṣaṇāt ।। śāstrajñena vinītena śucinā dīkṣitena ca ।
nāṭyācāryeṇa śāntena kartavyaṃ raṅgapūjanam ।। sthānabhraṣṭaṃ tu yo dadyādbalimudvignamānasaḥ । mantrahīno yathā hotā prāyaścittī bhavettu saḥ ।। ityayaṃ yo vidhirdṛṣṭo raṅgadaivatapūjane ।
nave nāṭyagṛhe kāryaḥ prekṣāyāṃ ca prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। evaṃ tu pūjanaṃ kṛtvā mayā proktaḥ pitāmahaḥ । ājñāpaya prabho kṣipraṃ kaḥ prayogaḥ prayujyatām ।। tato asmyukto bhagavatā yojayāmṛtamanthanam ।
etadutsāhajananaṃ suraprītikaraṃ tathā ।। yo ayaṃ samavakārastu dharmakāmārthasādhakaḥ । mayā prāggrathito vidvansa prayogaḥ prayujyatām ।। tasminsamavakāre tu prayukte devadānavāḥ ।
hṛṣṭāḥ samabhavansarve karmabhāvānudarśanāt ।। kasyacitvatha kālasya māmāhāmbujasambhavaḥ nāṭyaṃ sandarśayāmo adya trinetrāya mahātmane ।। tataḥ sārdhaṃ surairgatvā vṛṣabhāṅkaniveśanam । samabhyarcya śivaṃ paścāduvācedaṃ pitāmahaḥ ।।
mayā samavākarastu yo ayaṃ sṛṣṭaḥ surottama । śravaṇe darśane cāsya prasādaṃ kartumarhasi ।। paśyāma iti deveśo druhiṇaṃ vākyamabravīt । tato māmāha bhagavān sajjo bhava mahāmate ।।
tato himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe nānānāgasamākule । bahubhūtagaṇākīrṇe ramyakandaranirzhare ।। pūrvaraṅgaḥ kṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ tatrāyaṃ dvijasattamāḥ । tathā tripuradāhaśca ḍimasaṃjñaḥ prayojitaḥ ।।
tato bhūtagaṇā hṛṣṭāḥ karnabhāvānukīrtanāt । mahādevaśca suprītaḥ pitāmahamathābravīt ।। aho nāṭyamidaṃ samyak tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ mahāmate । yaśasyaṃ ca śubhārthaṃ ca puṇyaṃ buddhivivardhanam ।।
mayāpīdaṃ smṛtaṃ nṛtyaṃ sandhyākāleṣu nṛtyatā । nānākaraṇasaṃyuktairaṅgahārairvibhūṣitam ।। pūrvaraṅgavidhāvasmiṃstvayā samyakprayojyatām । vardhamānakayogeṣu gīteṣvāsāriteṣu ca ।।
mahāgīteṣu caivārthānsamyagevābhineṣyasi । yaścāyaṃ pūrvaraṅgastu tvayā śuddhaḥ prayojitaḥ ।। ebhirvimiśritaścāyaṃ citro nāma bhaviṣyati । śrutvā maheśvaravacaḥ pratyuktastu svayaṃbhuvā ।।
prayogamaṅgahārāṇāmācakṣva surasattama । tatastaṇḍuṃ samāhūya proktavān bhuvaneśvaraḥ ।। prayogamaṅgahārāṇāmācakṣva bharatāya vai । tato ye taṇḍunā proktāstvaṅgahārā mahātmanā ।।
tānvaḥ karaṇasaṃyuktānvyākhyāsyāmi sarecakān । sthirahasto aṅgahārastu tathā paryastakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sūcividdhastathā caiva hyapaviddhastathaiva ca । ākṣiptako atha vijñeyastathā coddhaṭṭitaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
viṣkambhaścaiva samproktastathā caivāparājitaḥ । viṣkambhāpasṛtaścaiava mattākrīḍastathaiva ca ।। svastiko recitaścaiva pārśvasvastika eva ca । vṛścikāpasṛtaḥ prokto bhramaraśca tathāparaḥ ।।
mattaskhalitakaścaiva madādvilasitastathā । gatimaṇḍalako jñeyaḥ paricchinnastathaiva ca ।। parivṛttacito atha syāttathā vaiśākharecitaḥ । parāvṛtto atha vijñeyastathā caivāpyalātakaḥ ।।
pārśvacchedo atha samprokto vidyudbhrāntastathaiva ca । ūrūdvṛttastathā caiva syādālīḍhastathaiva ca ।। recitaścāpi vijñeyastathaivācchuritaḥ smṛtaḥ । ākṣiptarecitaścaiva sambhrāntaśca tathāparaḥ ।।
apasarpastu vijñeyastathā cārdhanikuṭṭakaḥ । dvātriṃśadete samproktā aṅgahārāstu nāmataḥ ।। eteṣāṃ tu pravakṣyāmi prayogaṃ karaṇāśrayam । hastapādapracāraśca yathā yojyaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
aṅgahāreṣu vakṣyāmi karaṇeṣu ca vai dvijāḥ । sarveṣāmaṅgahārāṇāṃ niṣpattiḥ karaṇairyataḥ ।। tānyataḥ sampravakṣyāmi nāmataḥ karmatastathā । hastapādasamāyogo nṛtyasya karaṇaṃ bhavet ।।
dve nṛttakaraṇe caiva bhavato nṛttamātṛkā । dvābhyāṃ tribhiścaturbhirvāpyaṅgahārastu mātṛbhiḥ ।। tribhiḥ kalāpakaṃ caiva caturbhiḥ ṣaṇḍakaṃ bhavet । pañcaiva karaṇāni syuḥ saṅghātaka iti smṛtaḥ ।।
ṣaḍbhirvā saptabhirvāpi aṣṭabhirnavabhistathā । karaṇairiha saṃyuktā aṅgahārāḥ prakīrtāḥ ।। eteṣāmeva vakṣyāmi hastapādavikalpanam । talapuṣpapuṭaṃ pūrvaṃ vartitaṃ valitoru ca ।।
apaviddhaṃ samanakhaṃ līnaṃ svastikarecitam । maṇḍalasvastikaṃ caiva nikuṭṭakamathāpi ca ।। tathaivārdhanikuṭṭaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca । ardharecitakaṃ caiva vakṣaḥsvastikameva ca ।।
unmattaṃ svastikaṃ caiva pṛṣṭhasvastikameva ca । dikṣvastikamalātaṃ ca tathaiva ca kaṭīsamam ।। ākṣiptarecitaṃ caiva vikṣiptākṣiptakaṃ tathā । ardhasvastikamuddiṣṭamañcitaṃ ca tathāparam ।।
bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ proktamūrdhvajānu tathaiva ca । nikuñcitaṃ ca mattalli tvardhamattalli caiva hi ।। syādrecakanikkuṭṭaṃ ca tathā pādāpaviddhakam । valitaṃ ghūrṇitaṃ caiva lalitaṃ ca tathāparam ।।
daṇḍapakṣaṃ tathā caiva bhujaṅgatrastarecitam । nūpuraṃ caiva samproktaṃ tathā vaiśākharecitam ।। bhramaraṃ caturaṃ caiva bhujaṅgāñcitameva ca । daṇḍarecitakaṃ caiva tathā vṛścikakuṭṭitam ।।
kaṭibhrāntaṃ tathā caiva latāvṛścikameva ca । chinnaṃ ca karaṇaṃ proktaṃ tathā vṛścikarecitam ।। vṛścikaṃ vyaṃsitaṃ caiva tathā pārśvanikuṭṭakam । lalāṭatilakaṃ krāntaṃ kuñcitaṃ cakramaṇḍalam ।।
uromaṇḍalamākṣiptaṃ tathā talavilāsitam । argalaṃ cātha vikṣiptamāvṛttaṃ dolapādakam ।। vivṛttaṃ vinivṛttaṃ ca pārśvakrāntaṃ niśumbhitam । vidyutbhrāntamatikrāntaṃ vivartitakameva ca ।।
gajakrīḍitakaṃ caiva talasaṃsphoṭitaṃ tathā । garuḍaplutakaṃ caiva gaṇḍasūci tathāparam ।। parivṛttaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ pārśvajānu tathaiva ca । gṛdhrāvalīnakaṃ caiva sannataṃ sūcyathāpi ca ।।
ardhasūcīti karaṇaṃ sūcividdhaṃ tathaiva ca । apakrāntaṃ ca samproktaṃ mayūralalitaṃ tathā ।। sarpitaṃ daṇḍapādaṃ ca hariṇaplutameva ca । preṅkholitaṃ nitambaṃ ca skhalitaṃ karihastakam ।।
prasarpitakamuddiṣṭaṃ siṃhavikrīḍataṃ tathā । siṃhākarṣitamudvṛttaṃ tathopasṛtameva ca ।। talasaṃghaṭṭitaṃ caiva janitaṃ cāvahitthakam । niveśamelakākrīḍamūrūdvṛttaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
madaskhalitakaṃ caiva viṣṇukrāntamathāpi ca । sambhrāntamatha viṣkambhamudghaṭṭitamathāpi ca ।। vṛṣabhakrīḍitaṃ caiva lolitaṃ ca tathāparam । nāgāpasarpitaṃ caiva śakaṭāsyaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
gaṅgāvataraṇaṃ caivetyuktamaṣṭādhikaṃ śatam । aṣṭottaraśataṃ hyetatkaraṇānāṃ mayoditam ।। nṛtye yuddhe niyuddhe ca tatha gatiparikrame । gatipracāre vakṣyāmi yuddhacārīvikalpanam ।।
yatra tatrāpi saṃyojyamācāryairnāṭyaśaktinaḥ । prāyeṇa karaṇe kāryo vāmo vakṣaḥsthitaḥ karaḥ ।। caraṇasyānugaścāpi dakṣiṇastu bhavetkaraḥ । hastapādapracārantu kaṭipārśvorusaṃyutam ।।
uraḥpṛṣṭhodaropetaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ nibodhata । yāni sthānāni yāścāryo nṛtyahastāstathaiva ca ।। sā mātṛketi vijñeyā tadyogātkaraṇaṃ bhavet । kaṭī karṇasamā yatra korparāṃsaśirastathā ।।
samunnatamuraścaiva sauṣṭhavaṃ nāma tadbhavet । vāme puṣpapuṭaḥ pārśve pādo agratalasañcaraḥ ।। tathā ca sannataṃ pārśvaṃ talapuṣpapuṭaṃ bhavet । kuñcitau maṇibandhe tu vyāvṛttaparivartitau ।।
hastau nipatitau corvorvartitaṃ karaṇaṃ tu tat । śukatuṇḍau yadā hastau vyāvṛttaparivartitau ।। urū ca valitau yasminvalitorukamucyate । āvartya śukatuṇḍākhyamūrupṛṣṭhe nipātayet ।।
vāmahataśca vakṣaḥstho apyapaviddhaṃ tu tadbhavet । śliṣṭau samanakhau padau karau cāpi pralimbitau ।। dehaḥ svābhāviko yatra bhavetsamanakhaṃ tu tat । patākāñjali vakṣaḥsthaṃ prasāritaśirodharam ।।
nihañcitāṃsakūṭaṃ ca tallinaṃ karaṇaṃ smṛtam । svastikau recitāviddhau viśliṣṭau kaṭisaṃśritau ।। yatra tatkaraṇaṃ jñeyaṃ budhaiḥ svastikarecitam । svastikau tu karau kṛtvā prāṅgamukhordhvatalau samau ।।
tathā ca maṇḍalaṃ sthānaṃ maṇḍalasvastikaṃ tu tat । nikuṭṭitau yadā hastau svabāhuśiraso antare ।। pādau nikuṭṭitau caiva jñeyaṃ tattu nikuṭṭakam । añcitau bāhuśirasi hastastvabhimukhāṅguliḥ ।।
nikuñcitārdhayogena bhavedarthanikuṭṭakam । paryāyaśaḥ kaṭiśchinnā bāhvoḥ śirasi pallavau ।। punaḥpunaśca karaṇaṃ kaṭicchinaṃ tu tadbhavet । apaviddhakaraḥ sūcyā pādaścaiva nikuṭṭitaḥ ।।
saṃnnataṃ yatra pārśvaṃ ca tadbhaveardharecitam । svastikau caraṇau yatra karau vakṣasi recitau ।। nikuñcitaṃ tathā vakṣo vakṣassvastikameva tat । āñcitena tu pādena recitau tu karau yadā ।।
unmataṃ karaṇaṃ tattu vijñeyaṃ nṛtyakovidaiḥ । hastābhyāmatha pādābhyāṃ bhavataḥ svastikau yadā ।। tatsvastikamiti proktaṃ karaṇaṃ karaṇārthibhiḥ । vikṣiptākṣiptabāhubhyāṃ svastikau caraṇau yadā ।।
apakrāntārdhasūcibhyāṃ tatpṛṣṭhasvastikaṃ bhavet । pārśvayoragrataścaiva yatra śliṣṭaḥ karo bhavet ।। svastikau hastapādābhyāṃ taddikṣvastikamucyate । alātaṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā vyaṃsayeddakṣiṇaṃ karam ।।
ūrdhvajānukramaṃ kuryādalātakamiti smṛtam । svastikāpasṛtaḥ pādaḥ karau nābhikaṭisthitau ।। pārśvamudvāhitaṃ caiva karaṇaṃ tatkaṭīsamam । hastau hṛdi bhavedvāmaḥ savyaścākṣiptarecitaḥ ।।
recitaścāpaviddhaśca tatsyādākṣiptarecitam । vikṣiptaṃ hastapādaṃ ca tasaivākṣepaṇaṃ punaḥ ।। yatra tatkaraṇaṃ jñeyaṃ vikṣiptākṣiptaptakaṃ dvijāḥ । svastikau caraṇau kṛtvā karihastaṃ ca dakṣiṇam ।।
vakṣasthāne tathā vāmamardhasvastikamādiśet । vyāvṛttaparivṛttastu sa eva tu karo yadā ।। añcito nāsikāgre tu tadañcitamudāhṛtam । kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya tryaśramūruṃ vivartayet ।।
kaṭijānuvivartācca bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ bhavet । kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya janustanasamaṃ nyaset ।। prayogavaśagau hastāvūrdhvajānu prakīrtitam । vṛścikaṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā karaṃ pārśve nikuñcayet ।।
nāsāgre dakṣiṇaṃ caiva jñeyaṃ tattu nikuñcitam । vāmadakṣiṇapādābhyāṃ ghūrṇamānopasarpaṇaiḥ ।। udveṣṭitāpaviddhaiśca hastairmattallyudāhṛtam । sskhalitāpasṛtau pādau vāmahastaśca recitaḥ ।।
savyahastaḥ kaṭisthaḥ syādardhamattalli tatsmṛtam । recito dakṣiṇo hastaḥ pādaḥ savyo nikuṭṭitaḥ ।। dolā caiva bhavedvāmastadrecitanikuṭṭitam । kāryau nābhitaṭe hastau prāṅmukhau khaṭakāmukhau ।।
sūcīviddhāvapakrāntau pādau pādāpaviddhake । apaviddho bhaveddhastaḥ sūcīpādastathaiava ca ।। tathā trikaṃ vivṛttaṃ ca valitaṃ nāma tadbhavet । vartitāghūrṇitaḥ savyo hasto vāmaśca dolitaḥ ।।
svastikāpasṛtaḥ pādaḥ karaṇaṃ ghūrṇitaṃ tu tat । karihasto bhavedvāmo dakṣiṇaśca vivartitaḥ ।। bahuśaḥ kuṭṭitaḥ pado jñeyaṃ tallalitaṃ budhaiḥ । ūrdhvajānuṃ vidhāyātha tasyopari latāṃ nyaset ।।
daṇḍpakṣaṃ tatproktaṃ karṇaṃ nṛtyavedibhiḥ । bhujañgatrāsitaṃ kṛtvā yatrobhāvapi recitau ।। vāmapārśvasthtau hastau bhujaṅgatrastarecitam । trikaṃ suvalitaṃ kṛtvā latārecitakau karau ।।
nūpurśca tathā pādaḥ karaṇe nūpure nyaset । recitau hastapādau ca kaṭī grīvā ca recitā ।। vaiśākhasthānakenaitadbhavevaiśākharecitam । ākṣiptaḥ svastikaḥ pādaḥ karau codveṣṭitau tathā ।।
trikasya valanāccaiva jñeyaṃ bhramarakaṃ tu tat । añcitaḥ syātkaro vāmaḥ savyaścatura eva tu ।। dakṣiṇaḥ kuṭṭitaḥ pādaścaturaṃ tatprakīrtitam । bhujaṅgatrāsitaḥ pādo dakṣiṇo recitaḥ karaḥ ।।
latākhyaśca karo vāmo bhujaṅgāñcitakaṃ bhavet । vikṣiptaṃ hastapādaṃ tu samantādyatra daṇḍavat ।। recyate taddhi karaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ daṇḍakarecitam । vṛścikaṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā dvāvapyatha nikuṭṭitau ।।
vidhātavyau karau tattu jñeyaṃ vṛścikakuṭṭitam । sūciṃ kṛtvāpaviddhaṃ ca dakṣiṇaṃ caraṇaṃ nyaset ।। recitā ca kaṭiryatra kaṭibhrāntaṃ taducyate । añcitaḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ pādaḥ kuñcitordhvatalāṅguliḥ ।।
latākhyaśca karo vāmastallatāvṛścikaṃ bhavet । alapadmaḥ kaṭīdeśe chinnā paryāyaśaḥ kaṭī ।। vaiśākhasthānakeneha tacchinnaṃ karaṇaṃ bhavet । vṛścikaṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā svastikau ca karavubhau ।।
recitau viprakīrṇau ca karau vṛścikarecitam । bāhuśīrṣāñcitau hastau pādaḥ pṛṣṭhāñcitastathā ।। dūrasannatapṛṣṭhaṃ ca vṛścikaṃ tatprakīrtitam । ālīḍhaṃ sthānakaṃ yatra karau vakṣasi recitau ।।
ūrdhvādho viprakīrṇau ca vyaṃsitaṃ karaṇaṃ tu tat । hastau tu svastikau pārśve tathā pādo nikuṭṭitaḥ ।। yatra tatkaraṇaṃ jñeyaṃ budhaiḥ pārśvanikuṭṭitam । vṛścikaṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā pādasyāṅguṣṭhakena tu ।।
lalāṭe tilakaṃ kuryāllalāṭatilakaṃ tu tat । pṛṣṭhataḥ kuñcitaṃ kṛtvā vyatikrāntakramaṃ tataḥ ।। ākṣiptau ca karau kāryau krāntake karaṇe dvijāḥ । ādyaḥ pādo nataḥ kāryaḥ savyahastaśca kuñcitaḥ ।।
uttāno vāmapārśvasthastatkuñcitamudāhṛtam । pralambitābhyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ yadgātreṇānatena ca ।। abhyantarāpaviddhaḥ syāttajjñeyaṃ cakramaṇḍalam । svastikāpasṛtau pādāvapaviddhakramau yadā ।।
uromaṇḍalakau hastāvuromaṇḍalikastu tat । ākṣiptaṃ hastapādaṃ ca kriyate yatra vegataḥ ।। ākṣiotaṃ nāma karaṇaṃ vijñeyaṃ tatdvijottamāḥ । ūrdhvāṅgulitalaḥ pādaḥ pārśvenordhvaṃ prasāritaḥ ।।
prakuryādañcitatalau hastau talavilāsite । pṛṣṭhataḥ prasṛtaḥ pādau dvau tālāvardhameva ca ।। tasyeva cānugo hastaḥ puratastvargalaṃ tu tat । vikṣiptaṃ hastapādaṃ ca pṛṣṭhataḥ pārśvato api vā ।।
ekamārgagataṃ yatra tadvikṣiptamudāhṛtam । prasārya kuñcitaṃ pādaṃ punarāvartayet drutam ।। prayogavaśagau hastau tadāvartamudāhṛtam । kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya pārśvātpārśvaṃ tu ḍolayet ।।
prayogavaśagau hastau ḍolāpādaṃ taducyate । ākṣiptaṃ hastapādaṃ ca trikaṃ caiva vivartayet ।। recitau ca tathā hastau vivṛtte karaṇe dvijāḥ । sūcīviddhaṃ vidhāyātha trikaṃ tu vinivartayet ।।
karau ca recitau kāryau vinivṛtte dvijottamaḥ । pārśvakrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā purastādatha pātayet ।। prayogavaśagau hastau pārśvakrāntaṃ taducyate । pṛṣṭhataḥ kuñcitaḥ pādau vakṣaścaiva samunnatam ।।
tilake ca karaḥ sthāpyastannistambhitamucyate । pṛṣṭhato valitaṃ pādaṃ śiroghṛṣṭaṃ prasārayet ।। sarvato maṇḍalāviddhaṃ vidyudbhrāntaṃ taducyate । atikrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā purastātsaṃprasārayet ।।
prayogavaśagau hastāvatikrānte prakīrtitau । ākṣiptaṃ hastapādaṃ ca trikaṃ caiva vivartitam ।। dvitīyo recito hasto vivartitakameva tat । karṇe añcitaḥ karo vāmo latāhastaśca dakṣiṇaḥ ।।
dolāpādastathā caiva gajakrīḍitakaṃ bhavet । drutamutkṣipya caraṇaṃ purastādatha pātayet ।। talasaṃsphoṭitau hastau talasaṃsphoṭite matau । pṛṣṭhaprasāritaḥ pādaḥ latārecitakau karau ।।
samunnataṃ śiraścaiva garuḍaplutakaṃ bhavet । sūcipādo nataṃ pārśvameko vakṣaḥsthitaḥ karaḥ ।। dvitīyaścāñcito gaṇḍe gaṇḍasūcī taducyate । ūrdhvāpaveṣṭitau hastau sūcīpādo vivartitaḥ ।।
parivṛttatrikaṃ caiva parivṛttaṃ taducyate । ekaḥ samasthitaḥ pāda ūrupṛṣṭhe sthito aparaḥ ।। muṣṭihastaśca vakṣaḥsthaḥ pārśvajānu taducyate । pṛṣṭhaprasāritaḥ pādaḥ kiñcitañcita jānukaḥ ।।
yatra prasārito bāhū tatsyāt gṛdhrāvalīnakam । utplutya caraṇau kāryāvagrataḥ svastikasthitau ।। sannatau ca tathā hastau sannataṃ tadudāhṛtam । kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya kuryādagrasthitaṃ bhuvi ।।
prayogavaśagau hastau sā sūcī parikīrtitā । alapadmaḥ śirohastaḥ sūcīpādaśca dakṣiṇaḥ ।। yatra tatkaraṇaṃ jñeayamardhasūcīti nāmataḥ । pādasūcyā yadā pādo dvitīyastu pravidhyate ।।
kaṭivakṣaḥsthitau hastau sūcīvidhaṃ taducyate । kṛtvoruvalitaṃ pādamapakrāntakramaṃ nyaset ।। prayogavaśagau hastavapakrāntaṃ taducyate । vṛścikaṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā recitau ca tathā karau ।।
tathā trikaṃ vivṛttaṃ ca mayūralalitaṃ bhavet । añcitāpasṛtau pādau śiraśca parivāhitam ।। recitau ca tathā hastau tatsarpitamudāhṛtam । nūpuraṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā daṇḍapādaṃ prasārayet ।।
kṣiprāviddhakaraṃ caiva daṇḍapādaṃ taducyate । atikrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā samutplutya nipātayet ।। jaṅghāñcitopari kṣiptā tadvidyāddhariṇaplutam । ḍolāpādakramaṃ kṛtvā samutplutya nipātayet ।।
parivṛttatrikaṃ caiva tatpreṅkholitamucyate । bhujāvūrdhvaviniṣkrāntau hastau cābhimukhāṅgulī ।। baddhā cārī tatha caiva nitambe karaṇe bhavet । dolāpādakramaṃ kṛtvā hastau tadanugāvubhaua ।।
recitau ghūrṇitau vāpi skhalitaṃ karaṇaṃ bhavet । eko vakṣaḥsthito hastaḥ prodveṣṭitatalo aparaḥ ।। añcitaścaraṇaścaiva prayojyaḥ karihastake । ekastu recito hasto latākhyastu tathā paraḥ ।।
prasarpitatalau pādau prasarpitakameva tat । alātaṃ ca puraḥkṛtvā dvitīyaṃ ca drutakramam ।। hastau pādānugau cāpi siṃhavikrīḍite smṛtau । pṛṣṭhaprasarpitaḥ pādastathā hastau nikuñcitau ।।
punastathaiva kartavyau siṃhākarṣtake dvijāḥ । ākṣiptahastamākṣiptadehamākṣiptapādakam ।। advṛttagātramityetadudvṛtāṃ karaṇaṃ smṛtam । ākṣiptacaraṇaścaiko hastau tasyaiva cānugau ।।
ānataṃ ca tatha gātraṃ tayopasṛtakaṃ bhavet dolāpādakramaṃ kṛtvā talasaṅghaṭṭitau karau ।। recayecca karaṃ vāmaṃ talasaṅghaṭṭite sadā । eko vakṣaḥsthito hasto dvtīyaśca pralambitaḥ ।। talāgrasaṃsthitaḥ pādo janite karaṇe bhavet ।
janitaṃ karaṇaṃ kṛtvā hastau cābhimukhāṅgulī ।। śanairnipatito caiva jñeyaṃ tadavahitthakam । karau vakṣaḥsthitau kāryāvurau nirbhugnameva ca ।। maṇḍalasthānakaṃ caiva niveśaṃ karaṇaṃ tu tat ।
talasañcarapādābhyāmutplutya patanaṃ bhavet ।। saṃnataṃ valitaṃ gātramelakākrīḍitaṃ tu tat । karamāvṛttakaraṇamūrupṛṣṭhe añcitaṃ nyaset ।। jaṅghāñcitā tathodvṛttā hyūrūdvṛttaṃ tu tadbhavet ।
karau pralambitau kāryo śiraśca parivāhitam ।। pādau ca valitāvidhdaua madaskhalitake dvijāḥ । puraḥ prasāritaḥ pādaḥ kuñcito gaganonmukhaḥ ।। karau ca recitau yatra viṣṇukrāntaṃ taducyate ।
karamāvartitaṃ kṛtvā hyūrupṛṣṭhe nikuñcayet ।। ūruścaiva tathāviddhaḥ sambhrāntaṃ karaṇaṃ tu tat । apaviddhaḥ karaḥ sūcyā pādaścaiva nikuṭṭitaḥ ।। vakṣaḥsthaśca karo vāmo viṣkambhe karaṇe bhavet ।
pādāvuddhaṭṭitau kāryau talasaṅghaṭṭitau karau ।। nataśca pārśvaṃ kartavyaṃ budhairuddhaṭṭite sadā । prayujyālātakaṃ pūrvaṃ hastau cāpi hi recayet ।। kuñcitāvañcitau caiva vṛṣabhakrīḍite sadā ।
recitāvañcitau hastau lolitaṃ vartitaṃ śiraḥ ।। ubhayoḥpārśvayoryatra tallolitamudāhṛtam । svastikāpasṛtau pādau śiraśca parivāhitam ।। recitau ca tathā hastau syātāṃ nāgāpasarpite ।
niṣaṇṇāṅgastu caraṇaṃ prasārya talasañcaram ।। udvāhitamuraḥ kṛtvā śakaṭāsyaṃ prayojayet । ūrdhvāṅgulitalau pādau tripatākāvadhomukhau ।। hastau śirassannataṃ ca gaṅgāvataraṇaṃ tviti ।
yāni sthānāni yāścāryo vyāyāme kathitāni tu ।। pādapracārastveṣāṃ tu karaṇānāmayaṃ bhavet । ye cāpi nṛttahastāstu gaditā nṛttakarmaṇi ।। teṣāṃ samāsato yogaḥ karaṇeṣu vibhāvyate ।
prāyeṇa karaṇe kāryo vāmo vakṣaḥsthitaḥ karaḥ ।। caraṇaścānugaścāpi dakṣiṇastu bhavetkaraḥ । cāryaścaiva tu yāḥ proktā nṛttahastāstathaiva ca ।। sā mātṛketi vijñeyā tadbhedātkaraṇāni tu ।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hyetatkaraṇānāṃ mayoditam ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi hyaṅgahāravikalpanam । prasāryotkṣipya ca karau samapādaṃ prayojayet ।। vyaṃsitāpasṛtaṃ savyaṃ hastamūrdhvaṃ prasārayet ।
pratyālīḍhaṃ tataḥ kuryāt tathaiva ca nikuṭṭakam ।। ūrūdvṛttaṃ tataḥ kuryādakṣiptaṃ svastikaṃ tataḥ । nitambaṃ kari hastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ ca yogataḥ ।। sthirahasto bhavedeṣa tvaṅgahāro harapriyaḥ ।
talapuṣpāpaviddhe dve vartitaṃ saṃnikuṭṭikam ।। ūrūdvṛttaṃ tathākṣiptamuromaṇḍalameva ca । nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ।। eṣa paryastako nāma hyaṅgahāro harodbhavaḥ ।
alapallavasūcīṃ ca kṛtvā vikṣiptameva ca ।। āvartitaṃ tataḥ kuryāttathaiava ca nikuṭṭakam । ūrūdvṛttaṃ tathākṣiptamuromaṇḍalameva ca ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ sūcīviddho bhavedayam ।
apaviddhaṃ tu karaṇaṃ sūcīviddhaṃ tathaiva ca ।। udveṣṭitena hastena trikaṃ tu parivartayet । uromaṇḍalakau hastau kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ।। apaviddho aṅgahārāśca vijñeyo ayaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।
karaṇaṃ nūpuraṃ kṛtvā vikṣiptālātake punaḥ ।। punarākṣiptakaṃ kuryāduromaṇḍalakaṃ tathā । nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ।। ākṣiptakaḥ sa vijñeyo hyaṅgahāraḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।
udveṣṭitāpaviddhastu karaḥ pādo nikuṭṭitaḥ ।। punastainaiva yogena vāmapārśve bhavedatha । uromaṇḍalakau hastau nitambaṃ karihastakam ।। kartavyaṃ sakaṭicchinnaṃ nṛtye tūddhaṭṭite sadā ।
paryāyodveṣṭitau hastau pādau caiva nikuṭṭitau ।। kuñcitāvañcitaua caiva hyūrūdvṛttaṃ tathaiva ca । caturaśraṃ karaṃ kṛtvā pādena ca nikuṭṭakam ।। bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ caiva karaṃ codviṣṭitaṃ punaḥ ।
paricchinnaṃ ca kartavyaṃ trikaṃ bhramarakeṇa tu ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ viṣkambhe parikīrtitam । daṇḍapādaṃ karaṃ caiva vikṣipyākṣipya caiva hi ।। vyaṃsitaṃ vāmahastaṃ ca saha pādena sarpayet ।
nikuṭṭakadvayaṃ kāryamākṣiptaṃ maṇḍalorasi ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kartavyamaparājite । kuṭṭitaṃ karaṇaṃ kṛtvā bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā ।। recitena tu hastena patākaṃ hastamādiśet ।
ākṣiptakaṃ prayuñjīta hyuromaṇḍalakaṃ tathā ।। latākhyaṃ sakaṭakacchinnaṃ viṣkambhāpasṛte bhavet । trikaṃ suvalitaṃ kṛtvā nūpuraṃ karaṇaṃ tathā ।। bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ savyaṃ tathā vaiśākharecitam ।
ākṣiptakaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā paricchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ।। bāhyabhramarakaṃ kuryāduromaṇḍalameva ca । nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ।। mattākrīḍo bhavedeṣa hyaṅgahāro harapriyaḥ ।
recitaṃ hastapādaṃ ca kṛtvā vṛścikameva ca ।। punastenaiva yogena vṛścikaṃ samprayojayet । nikuṭṭakaṃ tathā caiva savyāsavyakṛtaṃ kramāt ।। latākhyaḥ sakaṭicchedo bhavetsvastikarecite ।
pārśve tu svastikaṃ baddhvā kāryaṃ tvatha nikuṭṭakam ।। dvitīyasya ca pārśvasya vidhiḥ syādyameva hi । tataśca karamāvartya hyūrūpṛṣṭhe nipātayet ।। ūrūdvṛttaṃ tataḥ kuryādākṣiptaṃ punareva hi ।
nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ।। pārśvasvastika ityeṣa hyaṅgahāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ । vṛścikaṃ karaṇaṃ kṛtvā latākhyaṃ hastameva ca ।। tameva ca karaṃ bhūyo nāsāgre sannikuñcayet ।
tamevodveṣṭitaṃ kṛtvā nitambaṃ parivartayet ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ vṛścikāpasṛte bhavet । kṛtvā nūpurapādaṃ tu tathākṣiptakameva ca ।। paricchinnaṃ ca kartavyaṃ sūcīpādaṃ tathaiva ca ।
nitambaṃ karihastaṃ cāpyuromaṇḍalakaṃ tathā ।। kaṭīcchinnaṃ tataścaiva bhramaraḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ । matallikaraṇaṃ kṛtvā karamāvartya dakṣiṇam ।। kapolasya pradeśe tu kāryaṃ samyaṅnikuñcitam apaviddhaṃ drutaṃ caiva talasaṃsphoṭasaṃyutam ।।
karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ mattaskhalitake bhavet । dolaiḥ karaiḥ pracalitaiḥ svastikāpasṛtaiḥ padaiḥ ।। añcitairvalitairhastaistalasaṅghaṭṭitaistathā । nikuṭṭitaṃ ca kartavyamūrūdvṛtaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ madādvilasite bhavet । maṇḍalaṃ sthānakaṃ kṛtvā tathā hastau ca recitau ।। udghaṭṭitena pādena mattallikaraṇaṃ bhavet । ākṣiptaṃ karaṇaṃ caiva hyuromaṇḍalameva ca ।।
kaṭicchinnaṃ tathā caiva bhavettu gatimaṇḍale । samapādaṃ prayujyātha paricchinnaṃ tvanantaram ।। āviddhena tu pādena bāhyabhramarakaṃ tathā । vāmasūcyā tvatikrāntaṃ bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā ।।
karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ paricchinne vidhīyate । śirasastūpari sthāpyau svastiakau vicyutau karau ।। tataḥ savyaṃ karaṃ cāpi gātramānamya recayet । punarutthāpayettatra gātramunnamya recitam ।।
latākhyau ca karau kṛtvā vṛścikaṃ samprayojayet । recitaṃ karihastaṃ ca bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā ।। ākṣiptakaṃ prayuñjīta svastikaṃ pādameva ca । parāṅgmukhavidhirbhūya evameva bhavediha ।।
karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ parivṛttakarecitee । recitau saha gātreṇa hyapaviddhau karau yadā ।। punastenaiva deśena gātramunnamya recayet । kuryānnūpurapādaṃ ca bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ tathā ।।
recitaṃ maṇḍalaṃ caiva bāhuśīrṣe nikuñcayet । ūrūdvṛttaṃ tathākṣiptamuromaṇḍalameva ca ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kuryādvaiśākharecite । ādyaṃ tu janitaṃ kṛtvā pādamekaṃ prasārayet ।।
tathaivālātakaṃ kuryāt trikaṃ tu parivartayet । añcitaṃ vāmahastaṃ ca gaṇḍadeśe nikuṭṭayet ।। kaṭicchinnaṃ tathā caiva parāvṛtte prayojayet । svastikaṃ karaṇaṃ kṛtvā vyaṃsitau ca karau punaḥ ।।
alātakaṃ prayuñjīta hyūrdhvajānu nikuñcitam । ardhasūcī ca vikṣiptamudvṛttākṣiptake tathā ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnamaṅgahāre hyalātake । nikuṭya vakṣasi karāvūrdhvajānu prayojayet ।।
ākṣiptasvastikaṃ kṛtvā trikaṃ tu parivartayet । uromaṇḍalakau hastau nitambaṃ karihastakam ।। kaṭicchinnaṃ tathā caiva pārśvacchede vidhīyate । sūcīvāmapadaṃ dadhyādvidyudbhrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam ।।
dakṣiṇena punaḥ sūcī vidyudbhrāntaṃ ca vāmataḥ । paricchinnaṃ tathā caiva hyatikrāntaṃ ca vāmakam ।। latākhyaṃ sakaṭicchinnaṃ vidyudbhrāntaśca sa smṛtaḥ । kṛtvā nūpurapādaṃ tu savyavāmau pralambitau ।।
karau pārśve tatastābhyāṃ vikṣiptaṃ samprayojayet । tābhyāṃ sūcī tathā caiva trikaṃ tu parivartayet ।। latākhyaṃ sakaṭicchinnaṃ kurtādudvṛttake sadā । ālīḍhavyaṃsitau hastau bāhuśīrṣe nikuṭṭayet ।।
nūpuraścaraṇo vāmastathālātaśca dakṣiṇaḥ । tenaivākṣiptakaṃ kuryāduromaṇḍalakau karau ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnamālīḍhe samprayojayet । hastaṃ tu recitaṃ kṛtvā pārśvamānasya recayet ।।
punastenaiva yogena gātramānasya recayet । recitaṃ karaṇaṃ kāryamuromaṇḍalameva ca ।। kaṭicchinnaṃ tu kartavyamaṅgahāre tu recite । nūpuraṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā trikaṃ tu parivartayet ।।
vyaṃsitena tu hastena trikameva vivartayet । vāmaṃ cālātakaṃ kṛtvā sūcīmatraiva yojayet ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kuryādācchurite sadā । recitau svastikau pādau recitau svastikau karau ।।
kṛtvā viśleṣamevaṃ tu tenaiva vidhinā punaḥ । punarutkṣepaṇaṃ caiva recitaireva kārayet ।। udvṛttākṣiptake caiva hyuromaṇḍalameva ca । nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca kaṭicchinnaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
ākṣiptarecito hyeṣa karaṇānāṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ । vikṣipta karaṇaṃ kṛtvā hastapādaṃ mukhāgamam ।। vāmasūcisahakṛtaṃ vikṣipedvāmakaṃ karam । vakṣaḥsthāne bhavetsavyo valitaṃ trikameva ca ।।
nūpurākṣiptake caiva hyardhasvastikameva ca । nitambaṃ karihastaṃ ca hyuromaṇḍalakaṃ tathā ।। kaṭicchinnaṃ ca kartavyaṃ sambhrānte nṛttayoktṛbhiḥ । apakrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā vyaṃsitaṃ hastameva ca ।।
kuryādudveṣṭitaṃ caiva hyardhasūcīṃ tathaiva ca । vikṣiptaṃ sakaṭicchinnamudvṛttākṣiptake tathā ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kartavyamapasarpite । kṛtvā nūpurapādaṃ ca drutamākṣipya ca kramam ।।
pādasya cānugau hastau trikaṃ ca parivartayet । nikuṭya karapādaṃ cāpyuromaṇḍalakaṃ punaḥ ।। karihastaṃ kaṭicchinnaṃ kāryamardhanikuṭṭake । dvātriṃśadete samproktā hyaṅgahārā dvijottamāḥ ।।
caturo recakāṃścāpi gadato me nibodhata । pādarecaka ekaḥ syāt dvitīyaḥ kaṭirecakaḥ ।। kararecakastṛtīyastu caturthaḥ kaṇṭharecakaḥ । [recitākhyaḥ pṛthagbhāve valane cābhidhīyate ।
udvāhanātpṛthagbhāvāccalanāccāpi recakaḥ ।। pārśvātpārśve tu gamanaṃ skhalitaiścalitaiḥ padaiḥ । vividhaiścaiva pādasya pādarecaka ucyate ।। trikasyodvartanaṃ caiva chaṭīvalanameva ca ।
tathā'pasarpaṇaṃ caiva kaṭirecaka ucyate ।। udvartanaṃ parikṣepo vikṣepaḥ parivartanam । visarpaṇaṃ ca hastasya hastarecaka ucyate ।। udvāhanaṃ sannamanaṃ tathā pārśvasya sannatiḥ ।
bhramaṇaṃ cāpi vijñeyo grīvāyā recako budhaiḥ] ।। recakairaṅgahāraiśca nṛtyantaṃ vīkṣya śaṅkaram ।। sukumāraprayogeṇa nṛtyantīṃ caiva pārvatīm । mṛdañgabherīpaṭahairbhāṇḍaḍiṇḍimagomukhaiḥ ।।
paṇavairdaduraiścaiva sarvātodyaiḥ pravāditaiḥ । dakṣayajñe vinihate sandhyākāle maheśvaraḥ ।। nānāṅgahāraiḥ prānṛtyallayatālavaśānugaiaḥ । piṇḍibandhāṃstato dṛṣṭvā nandibhadramukhā gaṇāḥ ।।
cakruste nāma piṇḍīnāṃ bandhamāsāṃ salakṣaṇam । īśvarasyeśvarī pinḍī nandinaścāpi paṭṭasī ।। caṇḍikāyā bhavetpiṇḍī tathā vai siṃhavāhinī । tārkṣyapiṇḍī bhavedviṣṇoḥ padmapiṇḍī svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।।
śakrasyairāvatī piṇḍī jhaṣapiṇḍī tu mānmathī । śikhipiṇḍī kumārasya rūpapiṇḍī bhavecchriyaḥ ।। dhārāpiṇḍī ca jāhnavyāḥ pāśapiṇḍī yamasya ca । vāruṇī ca nadīpiṇḍī yākṣī syāddhanadasya tu ।।
halapiṇḍī balasyāpi sarpapiṇḍī tu bhoginām । gāṇeśvarī mahāpiṇḍī dakṣayajñavimardinī ।। triśūlākṛtisaṃsthānā raudrī syādandhakadviṣaḥ । evamanyāsvapi tathā devatāsu yathākramam ।।
dhvajabhūtāḥ prayoktavyāḥ piṇḍībandhāḥ sucihnitāḥ । recakā aṅgahārāśca piṇḍībandhātasthaiva ca ।। sṛṣṭvā bhagavatā dattāstaṇḍave munaye tadā । tenāpi hi tataḥ samyaggānabhāṇḍasamanvitaḥ ।।
nṛttaprayogaḥ sṛṣṭo yaḥ sa tāṇḍava iti smṛtaḥ । yadā prāptyarthamarthānāṃ tajjñairabhinayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। kasmānṛttaṃ kṛtaṃ hyetatkaṃ svabhāvamapekṣate । na gītakārthasambaddhaṃ na cāpyarthasya bhāvakam ।।
kasmānnṛttaṃ kṛtaṃ hyetadgīteṣvāsāriteṣu ca । atrocyate na khalvarthaṃ kañcinnṛttamapekṣate ।। kiṃ tu śobhāṃ prajanayediti nṛttaṃ pravartitam । prāyeṇa sarvalokasya nṛttamiṣṭaṃ svabhāvataḥ ।।
maṅgalamiti kṛtvā ca nṛttametatprakīrtitam । vivāhaprasavāvāhapramodābhyuadayādiṣu ।। vinodakāraṇaṃ ceti nṛttametatpravartitam । ataścaiva pratikṣepādbhūtasaṅghaiḥ pravartitāḥ ।।
ye gītakādau yujyante samyaṅnṛttavibhāgakāḥ । devena cāpi samproktastaṇḍustāṇḍavapūrvakam ।। gītaprayogamāśritya nṛttametatpravartyatām । prāyeṇa tāṇḍavavidhirdevastutyāśrayo bhavet ।।
sukumāraprayogaśca śṛṅgārarasasambhavaḥ । tasya taṇḍuprayuktasya tāṇḍavasya vidhikriyām ।। vardhamānakamāsādya sampravakṣyami lakṣaṇam । kalānāṃ vṛddhimāsādya hyakṣarāṇāṃ ca vardhanāt ।।
layasya vardhanāccāpi vardhamānakamucyate । kṛttvā kutapavinyāsaṃ yathāvaddvijasattamāḥ ।। āsāritaprayogastu tataḥ kāryaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ । tatra tūpohanaṃ kṛttvā tantrīgānasamanvitam ।।
kāryaḥ praveśo nartakyā bhāṇḍavādyasamanvitaḥ । viśuddhakaraṇāyāṃ tu jātyāṃ vādyaṃ prayojayet ।। gatyā vādyānusāriṇyā tasyāścārīṃ prayojayet । vaiśākhasthānakeneha sarvarecakacāriṇī ।।
puṣpāñjalidharā bhūtvā praviśedraṅgamaṇḍapam । puṣpāñjaliṃ visṛjyātha raṅgapīṭhaṃ parītya ca ।। praṇamya devatābhyaśca tato abhinayamācaret । yatrābhineyaṃ gītaṃ syāttatra vādyaṃ na yojayet ।।
aṅgahāraprayoge tu bhāṇḍavādyaṃ vidhīyate । samaṃ raktaṃ vibhaktaṃ ca sphuṭaṃ śuddhaprahārajam ।। nṛttāṅgagrāhi vādyajñairvādyaṃ yojyaṃ tu tāṇḍave । prayujya gītavādye tu niṣkrāmennartakī tataḥ ।।
anenaiva vidhānena praviśantyaparāḥ pṛthak । anyāścānukrameṇātha piṇḍīṃ badhnanti yāḥ striyaḥ ।। tāvatparyastakaḥ kāryo yāvatpiṇḍī na badhyate । piṇḍīṃ baddhvā tataḥ sarvā niṣkrāmeyuḥ striyastu tāḥ ।।
piṇḍībandheṣu vādyaṃ tu kartavyamiha vādakaiaḥ । paryastakapramāṇena citraughakaraṇānvitam ।। tatropavāhanaṃ bhūyaḥ kāryaṃ pūrvavadeva hi । tataścāsāritaṃ bhūyo gāyanaṃ tu prayojayet ।।
pūrveṇaiva vidhānena praviśeccāpi nartakī । gītakārthaṃ tvabhinayed dvitīyāsāritasya tu ।। tadeva ca punarvastu nṛttenāpi pradarśayet । āsārite samāpte tu niṣkrāmennartakī tataḥ ।।
pūrvavatpraviśantyanyāḥ prayogaḥ syātsa eva hi । evaṃ pade pade kāryo vidhirāsāritasya tu ।। bhāṇḍavādyakṛte caiva tathā gānakṛte api ca । ekā tu prathamaṃ yojyā dve dvitīyaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
tisro vastu tṛtīyaṃ tu catasrastu caturthakam । piṇḍīnāṃ vidhayaścaiva catvāraḥ samprakīrtitāḥ ।। piṇḍī śṛṅkhalikā caiva latābandho atha bhedyakaḥ । piṇḍībandhastu piṇḍatvādgulmaḥ śṛṅkhalikā bhavet ।।
jālopanaddhā ca latā sanṛtto bhedyakaḥ smṛtaḥ । piṇḍībandhaḥ kaniṣṭhe tu śṛṅkhalā tu layāntare ।। madhyame ca latābandho jyeṣṭhe caivātha bhedyakaḥ । piṇḍīnāṃ vividhā yoniryantraṃ bhadrāsanaṃ tathā ।।
śikṣāyogastathā caiva prayoktavyaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ । evaṃ prayogaḥ kartavyo vardhamāne tapodhanāḥ ।। gītānāṃ chandakānāṃ ca bhūyo vakṣyāmyahaṃ vidhim । yāni vastunibaddhāni yāni cāṅgikṛtāni tu ।।
gītāni teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi prayogaṃ nṛttavādyayoḥ । tatrāvataraṇaṃ kāryaṃ nartakyāḥ sārvabhāṇḍikam ।। kṣepapratikṣepakṛtaṃ bhāṇḍopohanasaṃskṛtam । prathamaṃ tvabhineyaṃ syadgītake sarvavastukam ।।
tadeva ca punarvastu nṛtteenāpi pradarśeyat । yo vidhiḥ pūrvamuktastu nṛttābhinayavādite ।। āsāritavidhau sa syādgītānāṃ vastukeṣvapi । evaṃ vastunibandhānāṃ gītakānāṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
śṛṇutāṅganibaddhānāṃ gītānāmapi lakṣaṇam । ya eva vastukavidhirnṛttābhinayavādite ।। tamevāṅganibaddheṣu cchandakeṣvapi yojayet । vādyaṃ gurvakṣarakṛtaṃ tathālpākṣarameva ca ।।
mukhe sopohane kuryādvarṇānāṃ viprakarṣataḥ । yadā gītivaśādaṅgaṃ bhūyo bhūyo nivartate ।। tatrādyamabhineyaṃ syāccheṣaṃ nṛttena yojayet । yadā gītivaśādaṅgaṃ bhūyo bhūyo nivartate ।।
tripāṇilayasaṃyuktaṃ tatra vādyaṃ prayojayet । yathā layastathā vādyaṃ kartavyamiha vādakaiḥ ।। [tataṃ cānugataṃ cāpi oghaṃ ca karaṇānvitam । sthire tattvaṃ prayoktavyaṃ madhye cānugataṃ bhavet ।।
bhūyaścaughaḥ prayoktavyastveṣa vādyagato vidhiḥ । chandogītakamāsādya tvaṅgāni parivartayet ।। eṣa kāryo vidhirnityaṃ nṛttābhinayavādite । yāni vastunibaddhāni teṣāmante graho bhavet ।
aṅgānāṃ tu parāvṛttāvādāveva graho mataḥ] ।। evameṣa vidhiḥ kāryo gīteṣvāsāriteṣvapi । devastutyāśrayaṃ hyetatsukumāraṃ nibodhata ।। strīpuṃsayostu saṃlāpo yastu kāmasamudbhavaḥ ।
tajjñeyaṃ sukumāraṃ hi śṛṅgārarasasambhavam ।। yasyāṃ yasyāmavasthāyāṃ nṛttaṃ yojyaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । tatsarvaṃṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tacca me śṛṇuta dvijāḥ ।। aṅgavastunivṛttau tu tathā varṇanivṛttiṣu ।
tathā cābhudayasthāne nṛttaṃ tajjñaḥ prayojayet ।। yattu saṃdṛśyate kiñciddampatyormadanāśrayam । nṛttaṃ tatra prayoktavyaṃ praharṣārthaguṇodbhavam ।। yatra sannihite kānte ṛtukālādidarśanam ।
gītakārthābhisaṃbaddhaṃ nṛttaṃ tatrāpi ceṣyate ।। khaṇḍiatā vipralabdhā vā kalahāntaritāpi vā । yasminnaṅge tu yuvatirna nṛttaṃ tatra na yojayet ।। sakhīpravṛtte saṃlāpe tathā'sannihite priye ।
na hi nṛttaṃ prayoktavyaṃ yasyā na proṣitaḥ priyaḥ ।। [dūtyāśrayaṃ yadā tu syādṛtukālādi darśanam । autsukyacintāsaṃbaddhaṃ na nṛttaṃ tatra yojayet] ।। yasminnaṅge prasādaṃ tu gṛhnīyānnāyikā kramāt ।
tataḥprabhṛti nṛttaṃ tu śeṣeṣvaṅgeṣu yojayet ।। devastutyāśrayakṛtaṃ yadaṅgaṃ tu bhavedatha । māheśvarairaṅgahārairuddhataistatprayojayet ।। yattu śṛṅgārasaṃbaddhaṃ gānaṃ strīpuruṣāśrayam ।
devīkṛtairaṅgahārairlalitaistatprayojayet ।। catuṣpadā narkuṭake khañjake parigītake । vidhānaṃ sampravakṣyāmi bhāṇḍavādyavidhiṃ prati ।। khañjanarkuṭasaṃyuktā bhasvedyā tu catuṣpadā ।
pādānte sannipāte tu tasyā bhāṇḍagraho bhavet ।। yā dhruvā chandasā yaktā samapādā samākṣarā । tasyāḥ pādāvasāne tu pradeśinyā graho bhavet ।। kṛtvaikaṃ parivartaṃ tu gānasyābhinayasya ca ।
punaḥ pādanivṛttiṃ tu bhāṇḍavādyena yojayet ।। a~ṅgavastunivṛtau tu varṇāntaranivṛttiṣu । tathopasthāpane caiva bhāṇḍavādyaṃ prayojayet ।। ye api cāntaramārgāssyuḥ tantrivākkaraṇaiḥ kṛtāḥ ।
teṣu sūcī prayoktavyā bhāṇḍena saha tāṇḍave ।। maheśvarasya caritaṃ ya idaṃ samprayojayet sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā śivalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। evameṣa vidhiḥ sṛ ṣṭastāṇḍavasya prayogataḥ । bhūyaḥ kiṃ kathyatāmanyannāṭyavedavidhiṃ prati ।।
bharatasya vacaḥ śrutvā nāṭyasantānakāraṇam । punarevābruvanvākyamṛṣayo hṛṣṭamānasāḥ ।। yathā nāṭyasya janmedaṃ jarjarasya ca sambhavaḥ । vighnānāṃ śamanaṃ caiva daivatānāṃ ca pūjanam ।।
tadasmābhiḥ śrutaṃ sarvaṃ gṛhītvā cāvadhāritam । nikhilena yathātattvamicchāmo vedituṃ punaḥ ।। pūrvaraṅgaṃ mahātejaḥ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam । yathā buddhyāmahe brahmaṃstathā vyākhyātumarhasi ।।
teṣāṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ । pratyuvāca punarvākyaṃ pūrvaraṅgavidhiṃ prati ।। pūrvaraṅgaṃ mahābhāgā gadato me nibodhata । pādabhāgāḥ kalāścaiva parivartāstathaiva ca ।।
yasmādraṅge prayogo ayaṃ pūrvameva prayujyate । tasmādayaṃ pūrvaraṅgo vijñeyo dvijasattamāḥ ।। asyāṅgāni tu kāryāṇi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ । tantrībhāṇḍasamāyoagaiḥ pāṭhyayogakṛtaistathā ।।
pratyāhāro avataraṇaṃ tathā hyārambha eva ca । āśrāvaṇā vaktrapāṇistathā ca parighaṭṭanā ।। saṅghoṭanā tataḥ kāryā mārgāsāritameva ca । jyeṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni tathaivāsāratāni ca ।।
etāni tu bahirgītānyantaryavanikāgataiḥ । prayoktṛbhiḥ prayojyāni tantrībhāṇḍakṛtāni ca ।। tataḥ sarvaistu kutapaiḥ saṃyuktānīha kārayet । vighaṭya vai yavanikāṃ nṛttapāṭhyakṛtāni tu ।।
gītānāṃ madrakādīnāṃ yojyamekaṃ tu gītakam । vardhamānamathāpīha tāṇḍavaṃ yatra yujyate ।। tataścotthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ parivartanameva ca । nāndī śuṣkāvakṛṣṭā ca raṅgadvāraṃ tathaiva ca ।।
cāri caiva tataḥ kāryā mahācārī tathaiva ca । trikaṃ prarocanāṃ cāpi pūrvaraṅge bhavanti hi ।। etānyaṅgāni kāryāṇi pūrvaraṅgavidhau dvijāḥ । eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇamahaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।।
kutapasya tu vinyāsaḥ pratyāhāra iti smṛtaḥ । tathāvataraṇaṃ proktaṃ gāyikānāṃ niveśanam ।। parigītakriyārambha ārambha iti kīrtitaḥ । ātodyarañjanārthaṃ tu bhavedāśrāvaṇāvidhiḥ ।।
vādyavṛttivibhāgārthaṃ vaktrapāṇirvidhīyate । tantryojaḥkaraṇārthaṃ tu bhavecca parighaṭṭanā ।। tathā pāṇivibhāgārthaṃ bhavetsaṃghoṭanāvidhiḥ । tantrībhāṇḍasamāyogānmārgāsāritamiṣyate ।।
kalāpātavibhāgārthaṃ bhavedāsāritakriyā । kīrtanāddevatānāṃ ca jñeyo gītavidhistathā ।। [ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyami hyutthāpanavidhikriyām] ।। yasmādutthāpayantyatra prayogaṃ nāndipāṭhakāḥ ।
pūrvameva tu raṅge asmiṃstasmādutthāpanaṃ smṛtam ।। yasmācca lokapālānāṃ parivṛtya caturdiśam । vandanāni prakurvanti tasmācca parivartanam ।। āśīrvacanasaṃyuktā nityaṃ yasmātprayujyate ।
devadvijanṛpādīnāṃ tasmānnāndīti saṃjñitā ।। atra śuṣkākṣaraireva hyavakṛṣṭā dhruvā yataḥ । tasmācchuṣkāvakṛṣṭeyaṃ jarjaraślokadarśitā ।। yasmādabhinayastvatra prathamaṃ hyavatāryate ।
raṅgadvāramato jñeyaṃ vāgaṅgābhinayātmakam ।। śṛṅgārasya pracaraṇāccārī samparikīrtitā । raudrapracaraṇāccāpi mahācārīti kīrtitā ।। vidūṣakaḥ sūtradhārastathā vai pāripārśvakaḥ ।
yatra kurvanti sañjalpaṃ taccāpi trigataṃ matam ।। upakṣepeṇa kāvyasya hetuyuktisamāśrayā । siddhenāmantraṇā yā tu vijñeyā sa prarocanā ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi hyāśrāvaṇavidhikriyām ।
bahirgītavidhau samyagutpattiṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā ।। citradakṣiṇavṛtau tu saptarūpe pravartite । sopohane sanirgīte devastutyabhinandite ।। nāradādyaistu gandharvaiḥ sabhāyāṃ devadānavāḥ ।
nirgītaṃ śrāvitāḥ samyaglayatālasamanvitam ।। tacchrutvā tu sukhaṃ gānaṃ devastutyabhinanditam abhavankṣubhitāḥ sarve mātsaryāddaityarākṣasāḥ ।। sampradhārya ca te anyonyamityavocannavasthitāḥ । nirgītaṃ tu savāditramidaṃ gṛhṇīmahe vayam ।।
saptarūpeṇa santuṣṭā devāḥ karmānukīrtanāt । vayaṃ gṛhṇīma nirgītaṃ tuṣyāmo atraiva sarvadā ।। te tatra tuṣṭā daityāstu sādhayanti punaḥ punaḥ । ruṣṭāścāpi tato devāḥ pratyabhāṣanta nāradam ।।
ete tuṣyanti nirgīte dānavā saha rākṣasaiḥ । praṇaśyatu prayogo ayaṃ kathaṃ vā manyate bhavān ।। devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā nārado vākyamabravīt । dhātuvādyāśrayakṛtaṃ nirgītaṃ mā praṇaśyatu ।।
kintūpohanasaṃyuktaṃ dhātuvādyavibhūṣitam । bhaviṣyatīdaṃ nirgītaṃ saptarūpavidhānataḥ ।। nirgītenāvabaddhāśca daityadānavarākṣasāḥ । na kṣobhaṃ na vighātaṃ ca kariṣyantīha toṣitāḥ ।।
evaṃ nirgītametattu daityānāṃ spardhayā dvijāḥ । devānāṃ bahumānena bahirgītamiti smṛtam ।। dhātubhiścitravīṇāyāṃ gurulaghvakṣarānvitam । varṇālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ prayoktavyaṃ budhairatha ।।
nirgītaṃ geyate yasmādapadaṃ varṇayojanāt । asūyayā ca devānāṃ bahirgītamidaṃ smṛtam ।। nirgītaṃ yanmayā proktaṃ saptarūpasamanvitam । utthāpanādikaṃ yacca tasya kāraṇamucyate ।।
āśrāvaṇāyāṃ yuktāyāṃ daityāstuṣyanti nityaśaḥ । vaktrapāṇau kṛte caiva nityaṃ tuṣyanti dānavāḥ ।। parighaṭṭanayā tuṣṭā yuktāyāṃ rākṣasāṃ gaṇāḥ । saṅghoṭanakriyāyāṃ ca tuṣyantyapi ca guhyakāḥ ।।
mārgāsāritamāsādya tuṣṭā yakṣā bhavanti hi । gītakeṣu prayukteṣu devāstuṣyanti nityaśaḥ ।। vardhamāne prayukte tu rudrastuṣyati sānugaḥ । tathā cotthāpane yukte brahmā tuṣṭo bhavediha ।।
tuṣyanti lokapālāśca prayukte parivartane । nāndīprayoge atha kṛte prīto bhavati candramāḥ ।। yuktāyāmavakṛṣṭāyāṃ prītā nāgā bhavanti hi । tathā śuṣkāvakṛṣṭāyāṃ prītaḥ pitṛgaṇo bhavet ।।
raṅgadvāre prayukte tu viṣṇuḥ prīto bhavediha । jarjarasya prayoge tu tuṣṭā vighnavināyakāḥ ।। tathā cāryā prayuktāyāmumā tuṣṭā bhavediha । mahācāryā prayuktāyāṃ tuṣṭo bhūtagaṇo bhavet ।।
āśrāvaṇādicāryantametaddaivatapūjanam । pūrvaraṅge mayā khyātaṃ tathā cāṅgavikalpanam ।। devastuṣyanti yo yena yasya yanmanasaḥ priyam । tattathā pūrvaraṅge tu mayā prokaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
sarvadaivatapūjārhaṃ sarvadaivatapūjanam । dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ pūrvaraṅgapravartanam ।। daityadānavatuṣṭyarthaṃ sarveṣāṃ ca divaukasām । nirgītāni sagītāni pūrvaraṅgakṛtāni tu ।।
[yā vidyā yāni śilpāni yā gatiryaśca ceṣṭitam । lokālokasya jagatastadasminnāṭakāśraye] ।। nirgītānāṃ sagītānāṃ vardhamānasya caiva hi । dhruvāvidhāne vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ karma caiva hi ।।
prayujya gītakavidhiṃ vardhamānamathāpi ca । gītakānte tataścāpi kāryā hyutthāpanī dhruvā ।। adau dve ca caturthaṃ cāpyaṣṭamaikādaśe tathā । gurvakṣarāṇi jānīyatpāde hyekādaśe tathā ।।
catuṣpadā bhavetsā tu caturaśrā tathaiva ca । caturbhissannipātaiśca trilayā triyatistathā ।। parivartāśca catvāraḥ pāṇayastraya eva ca । jātyā caiva hi viślokā tāṃ ca tālena yojayet ।।
śamyā tu dvikalā kāryā talo dvikala eva ca । punaścaikakalā śamyā sannipātaḥ kalātrayam ।। evamaṣṭakalaḥ kāryaḥ sannipāto viacakṣaṇaiḥ । catvāraḥ sannipātāśca parivartaḥ sa ucyate ।।
pūrvaṃ sthitalayaḥ kāryaḥ parivarto vicakṣaṇaiḥ । tṛtīye sannipāte tu tasyā bhāṇḍagraho bhavet ।। ekasminparivarte tu gate prāpte dvitīyake । kāryaṃ madhyalaye tajjñaiḥ sūtradhārapraveśanam ।।
puṣpāñjaliṃ samādāya rakṣāmaṅgalasaṃskṛtāḥ । śuddhavastrāḥ sumanasastathā cādbhutadṛṣṭayaḥ ।। sthānantu vaiṣṇavaṃ kṛtvā sauṣṭhavāṅgapuraskṛtam । dīkṣitāḥ śucayaścaiva praviśeyuḥ samaṃ trayaḥ ।।
bhṛṅgārajarjaradharau bhavetāṃ pāripārśvikau । madhye tu sūtrabhṛttābhyāṃ vṛttaḥ pañcapadīṃ vrajet ।। padāni pañca gaccheyurbrahmaṇo yajanecchayā । padānāñcāpi vikṣepaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।।
tritālāntaraviṣkambhamutkṣipeccaraṇaṃ śanaiḥ pārśvotthānotthitaṃ caiva tanmadhye pātayetpunaḥ ।। evaṃ pañcapadīṃ gatvā sūtradhāraḥ sahetaraḥ । sūcīṃ vāmapade dadyādvikṣepaṃ dakṣiṇena ca ।। puṣpāñjalyapavargaśca kāryo brāhme atha maṇḍale ।
raṅgapīṭhasya madhye tu svayaṃ brahmā pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। tataḥ salalitairhastairabhivandya pitāmaham । abhivādāni kāryāṇi trīṇi hastena bhūtale ।। kālaprakarṣahetośca pādānāṃ pravibhāgataḥ ।
sūtradhārapraveśādyo vandanābhinayāntakaḥ ।। dvitīyaḥ parivartastu kāryo madhyalayāśritaḥ । tataḥ paraṃ tṛtīye tu maṇḍalasya pradakṣiṇam ।। bhavedācamanaṃ caiva jarjaragrahaṇaṃ tathā ।
utthāya maṇḍalāttūrṇaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pādamuddharet ।। vedhaṃ tenaiva kurvīta vikṣepaṃ vāmakena ca । punaśca dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ pārśvasaṃsthaṃ samuddharet ।। tataśca vāmavedhastu vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca ।
ityanena vidhānena samyakkṛtvā pradikṣaṇam ।। bhṛṅgārabhṛtamāhūya śaucaṃ cāpi samācaret । yathānyāyaṃ tu kartavyā tena hyācamanakriyā ।। ātmaprokṣaṇamevādbhiḥ kartavyaṃ tu yathākramam ।
prayatnakṛtaśaucena sūtradhāreṇa yatnataḥ ।। sannipātasamaṃ grāhyo jarjaro vighnajarjaraḥ । pradakṣiṇādyo vijñeyo jarjaragrahaṇāntakaḥ ।। tṛtīyaḥ parivartastu vijñeyo vai drute laye ।
gṛhītvā jarjaraṃ tvaṣṭau kalā japyaṃ prayojayet ।। vāmavedhaṃ tataḥ kuryādvikṣepaṃ dakṣiṇasya ca । tataḥ pañcapadīṃ caiva gacchettu kutaponmukhaḥ ।। vāmavedhastu tatrāpi vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya tu ।
jarjaragrahaṇādyo ayaṃ kutapābhimukhāntakaḥ ।। caturthaḥ parivartastu kāryo drutalaye punaḥ । karapādanipātāstu bhavntyatra tu ṣoḍaśa ।। tryaśre dvādaśa pātāstu bhavanti karapādayoḥ ।
vandanānyatha kāryāṇi trīṇi hastena bhūtale ।। ātmaprokṣaṇamadbhiśca tryaśre naiva vidhīyate । evamutthāpanaṃ kāryaṃ tatastu parivartanam ।। caturaśraṃ laye madhye sannipātairathāṣṭabhiḥ ।
yasyā laghūni sarvāṇi kevalaṃ naidhanaṃ guru ।। bhavedatijagatyāntu sā dhruvā parivartanī । vārtikena tu mārgeṇa vādyenānugatena ca ।। lalitaiḥ pādavinyāsairvandyā devā yathādiśam ।
dvikalaṃ pādapatanaṃ pādacāryā gataṃ bhavet ।। vāmapādena vedhastu kartavyo nṛttayoktṛbhiḥ । dvitālāntaraviṣkambho vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca ।। tataḥ pañcapadīṃ gacchedatikrāntaiḥ padaratha ।
tato abhivādanaṃ kuryāddevatānāṃ yathādiśam ।। vandeta prathamaṃ pūrvāṃ diśaṃ śakrādhidaivatām । dvitīyāṃ dakṣiṇāmāśāṃ vandeta yamadevatām ।। vandeta paścimāmāśāṃ tato varuṇadaivatām ।
caturthīmuttarāmāśāṃ vandeta dhanadāśrayām ।। diśāṃ tu vandanaṃ kṛtvā vāmavedhaṃ prayojayet । dakṣiṇena ca kartavyaṃ vikṣepaparivartanam ।। prāṅgmukhastu tataḥ kuryātpuruṣastrīnapuṃsakaiḥ ।
tripadyā sūtrabhṛdrudrabrahmopendrābhivādanam ।। dakṣiṇaṃ tu padaṃ puṃso vāmaṃ strīṇāṃ prakīrtitam । punardakṣiṇameva syānnātyutkṣiptaṃ napuṃsakam ।। vandeta pauruṣeṇeśaṃ strīpadena janārdanam ।
napuṃsakpadenāpi tathaivāmbujasambhavam ।। parivartanamevaṃ syāttasyānte praviśettataḥ । caturthakāraḥ puṣpāṇi pragṛhya vidhipūrvakam ।। yathāvattena kartavyaṃ pūjanaṃ jarjarasya tu ।
kutapasya ca sarvasya sūtradhārasya caiva hi ।। tasya bhāṇḍasamaḥ kāryastajjñairgatiparikramaḥ । na tatra gānaṃ kartavyaṃ tatra stobhakriyā bhavet ।। caturthakāraḥ pūjāṃ tu sa kṛtvāntarhito bhavet ।
tato geyāvakṛṣṭā tu caturaśrā sthitā dhruvā ।। guruprāyā tu sā kāryā tathā caivāvapāṇikā । sthāyivarṇāśrayopetā kalāṣṭakavinirmitā ।। [caturthaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva saptamaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ tathā ।
laghūni pāde paṅktyāntu sāvakṛṣṭā dhruvā smṛtā] ।। sūtradhāraḥ paṭhettatra madhyamaṃ svaramāśritaḥ । nāndīṃ padairdvādaśabhiraṣṭabhirvā'pyalaṅkṛtām ।। namo astu sarvadevebhyo dvijātibhyaḥ śubhaṃ tathā ।
jitaṃ somena vai rājñā śivaṃ gobrāhmaṇāya ca ।। brahmottaraṃ tathaivāstu hatā brahmadviṣastathā । praśāstvimāṃ mahārājaḥ pṛthivīṃ ca sasāgarām ।। rāṣṭraṃ pravardhatāṃ caiva raṅgasyāśā samṛddhyatu ।
prekṣākarturmahāndharmo bhavatu brahmabhāṣitaḥ ।। kāvyakarturyaśaścāstu dharmaścāpi pravardhatām । ijyayā cānayā nityaṃ prīyantāṃ devatā iti ।। nāndīpadāntareṣveṣu hyevamāryeti nityaśaḥ ।
vadetāṃ samyaguktābhirvāgbhistau pāripārśvikau ।। evaṃ nāndī vidhātavyā yathāvallakṣaṇānvitā । tataśśuṣkāvakṛṣṭā syājjarjaraślokadarśikā ।। navaṃ gurvākṣarāṇyādau ṣaḍlaghūni gurutrayam ।
śuṣkāvakṛṣṭā tu bhavetkalā hyaṣṭau pramāṇataḥ ।। digle digle digle digle jambukapalitakate tecām । kṛtvā śuṣkāvakṛṣṭāṃ tu yathāvaddvijasattamāḥ ।। tataḥ ślokaṃ paṭhedekaṃ gambhīrasvarasaṃyutam ।
devastotraṃ puraskṛtya yasya pūjā pravartate ।। rājño vā yatra bhaktiḥ syādatha vā brahmaṇasstavam । gaditvā jarjaraślokaṃ raṅgadvāre ca yatsmṛtam ।। paṭhedanyaṃ punaḥ ślokaṃ jarjarasya vināśanam ।
jarjaraṃ namayitvā tu tataścārīṃ prayojayet ।। pāripārśvikayośca syātpaścimenāpasarpaṇam । aṅkitā cātra kartavyā dhruvā madhyalayānvitā ।। caturbhiḥ sannipātaiśca caturaśrā pramāṇataḥ ।
ādyamantyaṃ caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ca tathā guru ।। yasyāṃ hrasvāni śeṣāṇi sā jñeyā tvaṅkitā budhaiḥ । asyāḥ prayogaṃ vakṣyāmi yathā pūrvaṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। sahomayā krīḍitavānnānābhāvaviceṣṭataiḥ ।
kṛtvā'vahitthaṃ sthānaṃ tu vāmaṃ cādhomukhaṃ bhujam ।। caturaśramuraḥ kāryamañcitaścāpi mastakaḥ । nābhipradeśe vinyasya jarjaraṃ ca tulādhṛtam ।। vāmapallavahastena pādaistālāntarotthitaiḥ ।
gacchetpañcapadīṃ caiva savilāsāṅgaceṣṭitaiḥ ।। vāmavedhastu kartavyo vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca । śṛṅgārarasasaṃyuktāṃ paṭhedāryāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। cārīślokaṃ gaditvā tu kṛtvā ca parivartanam ।
taireva ca padaḥ kāryaṃ paścimenāpasarpaṇam ।। pāripārśvikahaste tu nyasya jarjaramuttamam । mahācārīṃ tataścaiva prayuñjīta yathāvidhi ।। caturaśrā dhruvā tatra tathā drutalayānvitā ।
caturbhissannipātaiśca kalā hyaṣṭau pramāṇataḥ ।। ādyaṃ caturthamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ daśamaṃ guru । laghu śeṣaṃ dhruvāpāde caturviṃśatike bhavet ।। pādatalāhatipātitaśailaṃ kṣobhitabhūtasamagrasamudram ।
tāṇḍavanṛtyamidaṃ pralayānte pātu jagatsukhadāyi harasya ।। bhāṇḍonmukhena kartavyaṃ pādavikṣepaṇaṃ tataḥ । sūcīṃ kṛtvā punaḥ kuryādvikṣepaparivartanam ।। atikrāntaiḥ salalitaiḥ pādairdrutalayānvitaiḥ ।
tritālāntaramutkṣepairgacchetpañcapadīṃ tataḥ ।। tatrāpi vāmavedhastu vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca । taireva ca padaiḥ kāryaṃ prāṅmukhenāpasarpaṇam ।। punaḥ padāni trīṇyeva gacchetprāṅmukha eva tu ।
tataśca vāmavedhaḥ syādvikṣepo dakṣiṇasya ca ।। tato raudrarasaṃ ślokaṃ pādasaṃharaṇaṃ paṭhet । tasyānte tu tripadyātha vyāharetpāripārśvikau ।। tayorāgamane kāryaṃ gānaṃ narkuṭakaṃ budhaiḥ ।
tathā ca bhāratībhede trigataṃ samprayojayet ।। vidūṣakastvekapadāṃ sutradhārasmitāvahām । asambaddhakathāprāyāṃ kuryātkathanikā tataḥ ।। (vitaṇḍāṃ gaṇḍasaṃyuktāṃ tālikāñca prayojayet ।
kastiṣṭhati jitaṃ kenetyādikāvyaprarūpiṇīm ।। pāripārśvakasañjalpo vidūṣakavirūpitaḥ । sthāpitaḥ sūtradhāreṇa trigataṃ samprayujyate) ।। prarocanā ca kartavyā siddhenopanimatraṇam ।
raṅgasiddhau punaḥ kāryaṃ kāvyavastunirūpaṇam ।। sarvameva vidhiṃ kṛtvā sūcīvedhakṛtairatha । pādairanāviddhagatairniṣkrāmeyuḥ samaṃ trayaḥ ।। evameṣa prayoktavyaḥ pūrvaraṅgo yathāvidhi ।
caturaśro dvijaśreṣṭhāstryaśraṃ cāpi nibodhata ।। ayameva prayogaḥ syādaṅgānyetāni caiva hi । tālapramāṇaṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ kevalaṃ tu viśeṣakṛt ।। śamyā tu dvikalā kāryā tālo hyekakalastathā ।
punaścaikakalā śamyā sannipātaḥ kalādvayam ।। anena hi pramāṇena kalātālalayānvitaḥ । kartavyaḥ pūrvaraṅgastu tryaśro apyutthāpanādikaḥ ।। ādyaṃ caturthaṃ daśamamaṣṭamaṃ naidhanaṃ guru ।
yasyāstu jāgate pāde sā tryaśrotthāpinī dhruvā ।। vādyaṃ gatipracāraśca dhruvā tālastathaiva ca । saṃkṣiptānyeva kāryāṇi tryaśre nṛttapravedibhiḥ ।। vādyagītapramāṇena kuryādaṅgaviceṣṭitam ।
vistīrṇamatha saṃkṣiptaṃ dvipramāṇavinirmitam ।। hastapādapracārastu dvikalaḥ parikīrtitaḥ । caturaśre parikrānte pātāḥ syuḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu ।। tryaśre dvādaśa pātāstu bhavanti karapādayoḥ ।
etatpramāṇaṃ vijñeyamubhayoḥ pūrvaraṅgayoḥ ।। kevalaṃ parivarte tu gamane tripadī bhavet । digvandane pañcapadī caturaśre vidhīyate ।। ācāryabuddhyā kartavyastryaśrastālapramāṇataḥ ।
tasmānna lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ punaruktaṃ bhavedyataḥ ।। evameṣa prayoktavyaḥ pūrvaraṅgo dvijottamāḥ । tryaśraśca caturaśraśca śuddho bhāratyupāśrayaḥ ।। evaṃ tāvadayaṃ śuddhaḥ pūrvaraṅgo mayoditaḥ ।
citratvamasya vakṣyāmi yathākāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। vṛtte hyutthāpane viprāḥ kṛte ca parivartane । caturthakāradattābhiḥ sumanobhiralaṅkṛte ।। udāttairgānairgandharvaiḥ parigīte pramāṇataḥ ।
devadundubhayaścaiva ninadaiyurbhṛśaṃ yataḥ ।। siddhāḥ kusumamālābhirvikireyuḥ samantataḥ । aṅgahāraiśca devyastā upanṛtyeyuragrataḥ ।। yastāṇḍavavidhiḥ prokto nṛte piṇḍīsamanvitaḥ ।
recakairaṅgahāraiśca nyāsopanyāsasaṃyutaḥ ।। nāndīpadānāṃ madhye tu ekaikasminpṛthakpṛthak । prayoktavyo budhaiḥ samyakcitrabhāvamabhīpsubhiḥ ।। evaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ śuddhaṃ citraṃ prayatnataḥ ।
tataḥparaṃ prayuñjīta nāṭakaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam ।। tatastvantarhitāḥ sarvā bhaveyurdivyayoṣitaḥ । niṣkrāntāsu ca sarvāsu nartakīṣu tataḥ param ।। pūrvaraṅge prayoktavyamaṅgajātamataḥparam ।
evaṃ śuddho bhaveccitraḥ pūrvaraṅgo vidhānataḥ ।। kāryo nātiprasaṅgo atra nṛtāgītavidhiṃ prati । gīte vādye ca nṛtte ca pravṛtte atiprasaṅgataḥ ।। khedo bhavetprayoktṝṇāṃ prekṣakāṇāṃ tathaiva ca ।
khinnānāṃ rasabhāveṣu spaṣṭatā nopajāyate ।। tataḥ śeṣaprayogastu na rāgajanako bhavet । (lakṣanena vinā bāhyalakṣaṇādvistṛtaṃ bhavet । lokaśāstrānusāreṇa tasmānnāṭyaṃ pravartate) ।।
