caturasro bhavedvāmaḥ savyahastaśca recitaḥ । vijñeyau nṛttatattvajñairdharecitasaṃjñakau ।। añcitau kūrparāṃsau tu tripatākau karau kṛtau । kiñcittiryaggatāvetau smṛtāvuttanavañcitau ।।
maṇibandhamuktau tu patākau pallavau smṛtau । bāhuśīrṣādviniṣkrāntau nitambāviti kīrtitau ।। keśadeśādviniṣkrāntau paripārśvotthitau yadā । vijñeyo keśabandhau tu karavācāryasammatau ।।
tiryakprasāritau caiva pārśvasaṃsthau tathaiva ca । latākhyau ca karau jñeyau nṛttābhinayanaṃ prati ।। samunnato latāhastaḥ pārśvātpārśva vilolitaḥ । tripatāko aparaḥ karṇe karihastaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
kaṭiśīrṣaniviṣṭāgrau tripatākau yadā karau । pakṣavañcitakau hastau tadā jñeyau prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। tāveva tu parāvṛttau pakṣapradyotakau smṛtau । adhomukhatalāviddhau jñeyau garuḍapakṣakau ।।
haṃsapakṣakṛtau hastau vyāvṛttaparivartitau । tathā prasāritabhujau daṇḍapakṣāviti smṛtau ।। ūrdhvamaṇḍalinau hastāvūrdhvadeśavivartanāt । tāveva pārśvavinyastau pārśvamaṇḍalinau smṛtau ।।
udveṣṭitau bhavedekau dvitīyaścāpaveṣṭitaḥ । bhramitāvurasaḥ sthāne hyuromaṇḍalinau smṛtau ।। alapallavakārālāvurodvabhramaṇakramāt । pārśvāvartaśca vijñeyāvuraḥ pārśvārdhamaṇḍalau ।।
hastau tu maṇībandhānte kuñcitāvañcitau yadā । khaṭakākhyau tu tau syātāṃ muṣṭikasvastikau tadā ।। padmakośau yadā hastau vyāvṛttaparivartitau । nalinīpadmakośau tu tadā jñeyau prayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
karāvudveṣṭitāgrau tu pravidhāyālapallavau । ūrdhvaprasaritāviddhau kartavyāvulbaṇāviti ।। pallavau ca śirodeśe saṃprāptau lalitau smṛtau । karpūrasvastikagatau latākhyau valitāviti ।।
karaṇe tu prayoktavyo nṛttahasto viśeṣataḥ । tathārthābhinaye caiva patākāyāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। saṃkaro api bhavetteṣāṃ prayogo arthavaśātpunaḥ । prādhānyena punaḥ saṃjñā nāṭye nṛtte kareṣviha ।।
viyutāḥ saṃyutāścaiva nṛttahastāḥ prakīrtitāḥ । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi karān karaṇasaṃśrayān ।। sarveṣāmeva hastānāṃ nāṭyahastanideśibhiḥ । vidhātavyā prayatnena karaṇaṃ tu caturvidham ।।
apaveṣṭitamekaṃ syāt udveṣṭitamathāparam । vyāvartitaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu caturthaṃ parivartitam ।। āveṣṭyante yadaṅgulyastarjanādyā yathākramam । abhyantareṇa karaṇaṃ tadāveṣṭitamucyate ।।
udveṣṭyante yadaṅgulyaḥ tarjanyādyā bahirmukham । kramaśaḥ karaṇaṃ viprāstadudveṣṭitamucyate ।। āvartyante kaniṣṭhādyā hyaṅgulyo abhyantareṇa tu । yathā krameṇa karaṇaṃ tad vyāvartitamucyate ।।
udvartyante kaniṣṭhādyā bāhyataḥ kramaśo yadā । aṅgulyaḥ karaṇaṃ viprāstaduktaṃ parivartitam ।। nṛtte abhinayayoge vā pāṇibhirvartanāśraye । mukhabhrunetrayuktāni karaṇāni prayojayet ।।
tiryaktathordhvasaṃstho hyadhomukhaścāñcito apaviddhastu । maṇḍalagatistathā svastikaśca pṛṣṭhānusāri ca ।। udveṣṭitaḥ prasārita ityete vai smṛtāḥ prakārāstu । bāhvoriti karaṇagatā vijñeyā nityaṃ nṛttaprayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
hastānāṃ karaṇavidhirmayā samāsena nigadito viprāḥ । ata ūrdhvaṃ vyākhyāsye hṛdayodarapārśvakarmāṇi ।। ābhugnamatha nirbhugnaṃ tathā caiva prakampitam । udvāhitaṃ samaṃ caiva uraḥ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam ।।
nimnamunnatapṛṣṭhaṃ ca vyābhugnāṃsaṃ ślathaṃ kvacit ābhugnaṃ taduro jñeyaṃ karma cāsya nibodhata ।। saṃbhramaviṣādamūrcchāśokabhayavyādhihṛdayaśalyeṣu । kāryaṃ śītasparśe varṣe lājānvite arthavaśāt ।। stabdhaṃ ca nimnapṛṣṭhaṃ ca nirbhugnāṃsaṃ samunnatam ।
uro nirbhugnametaddhi karma cāsya nibodhata ।। stambhe mānagrahaṇe vismayadṛṣṭe ca satyavacane ca । ahamiti ca darpavacane garvotseke tu kartavyam ।। [dīrghaniśvasite caiva jṛmbhaṇe moṭane tathā ।
bibboke ca punaḥ strīṇāṃ tadvijñeyaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ] ।। ūrdhvotkṣepairuro yatra nirantarakṛtaiḥ kṛtam । prakampitaṃ tu vijñeyamuro nāṭyaprayoktṛbhiḥ ।। hasitaruditādisaṃbhramabhayaśramavyādhipīḍitārtheṣu ।
nānābhāvopagataṃ kāryamuro nāṭyayogeṣu ।। hasitaruditeṣu kārye śrame bhaye śvasakāśayoścaiva । hikkāduḥkhe ca tathā nāṭyajñairarthayogena ।। udvāhitamūrdhvagatamuro jñeyaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।
dīrghocchvasanatā loke jṛmbhanādiṣu cekṣyate ।। sarvaiḥ sasauṣṭhavairañgaiścaturasrakṛtaiḥ kṛtam । uraḥ saman tu vijñeyaṃ svasthaṃ sauṣṭhavasaṃyutam ।। etaduktaṃ maya samyagarasastu vikalpanam ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi pārśvayoriha lakṣaṇam ।। nataṃ samunnataṃ caiva prasāritavivartito । tathāpasṛtamevaṃ tu pārśvayoḥ karma pañcadhā ।। kaṭirbhavettu vyābhugnā pārśvamābhugnameva ca ।
tathaivāpasṛtāṃsaṃ ca kiñcitpārśvanataṃ smṛtam ।। tasyaiva cāparaṃ pārśvaṃ viparītaṃ tu yuktitaḥ । kaṭīpārśvabhujāṃsaiścābhyunnatairutaṃ bhavet ।। āyāmanādubhayataḥ pāśvayoḥ syāt prasāritam ।
parivartātrikasyāpi vivartitamiheṣyate ।। vivartitāpanayanād bhavedapasṛtaṃ punaḥ । pārśvalakṣaṇamityuktaṃ viniyogaṃ nibodhata ।। upasarpe nataṃ kāryamunnataṃ cāpasarpaṇe ।
prasāritaṃ praharṣādau parivṛtte vivartitam ।। vinivṛtte tvapasṛtaṃ pārśvamarthavaśādbhavet । etāni pārśvakarmāṇi jaṭharasya nibodhata ।। kṣāmaṃ khalvaṃ ca pūrṇaṃ ca samproktamudaraṃ tridhā ।
tanu kṣāmaṃ nataṃ khalvaṃ pūrṇamādhmātamucyate ।। kṣāmaṃ hāsye atha rudite niḥśvāse jṛmbhane bhavet । vyādhite tapasi śrānte kṣudhārte khalvamiṣyate ।। pūrṇamucchvasite sthūle vyādhitātyaśanādiṣu ।
ityetadudaraṃ proktaṃ kaṭyāḥ karma nibodhata ।। kṣāmaṃ khalvaṃ samaṃ pūrṇamudaraṃ syāccaturvidham । chinā caiva nivṛttā ca recitā kampitā tathā । udvāhitā caiva kaṭī nāṭye nṛtte ca pañcadhā ।।
kaṭī madhyasya valanātcchinā saṃparikīrtitā । parāṅgmukhasyābhimukhī nivṛttā syānnivartitā ।। sarvato bhramaṇāccāpi vijñeyā recitā kaṭī । tiryaggatāgatā kṣiptā kaṭī jñeyā prakampitā ।।
nitambapārśvodvahanāt śaneirudvāhitā kaṭī । kaṭīkarma mayā proktaṃ viniyogaṃ nibodhata ।। chinnā vyāyāmasambhrāntavyāvṛttaprekṣaṇādiṣu । nivṛttā vartane caiva recitā bhramaṇādiṣu ।।
kubjavāmananīcānāṃ gatau kāryā prakampitā । sthūleṣūdvāhiotā yojyā strīṇāṃ līlāgateṣu ca ।। kampanaṃ valanaṃ caiva stambhanodvartane tathā । nivartanaṃ ca pañcaitānyūrukarmāṇi kārayet ।।
namanonnamanātpārṣṇermuhuḥ syādūrukampanam । gacchedabhyantaraṃ jānu yatra tadvalanaṃ smṛtam ।। stambhanaṃ cāpi vijñeyamapaviddhakriyātmakam । valitāviddhakaraṇādūrvorudvartanaṃ smṛtam ।।
pārṣṇirabhyantaraṃ gacchedyatra tattu nivartanam । gatiṣvadhamapātraṇāṃ bhaye cāpi hi kampanam ।। valanaṃ caiva hi kartavyaṃ strīṇāṃ svairaparikrame । sādhvase ca viṣāde ca stambhanaṃ tu prayojayet ।।
vyāyāme tāṇḍave caiva kāryamudvartanaṃ budhaiḥ । nivartanaṃ tu kartavyaṃ sambhrādiparibhrame ।। yathādarśanamanyacca lokād grāhyaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । ityūrvrorlakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ jaṅghāyāstu nibodhata ।।
āvartitaṃ nataṃ kṣiptamudvāhitamathāpi ca । parivṛttaṃ tathā caiva jaṅghākarmāṇi pañcadhā ।। vāmo dakṣiṇapārśvena dakṣiṇaścāpi vāmataḥ । pādo yatra vrajedviprāḥ tadāvartitamucyate ।।
jaṅghāsvastikayogena kramādāvartitaṃ nayet । jānunaḥ kuñcanāccaiva nataṃ jñeyaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । vikṣepāccaiva jaṅghāyāḥ kṣiptamityabhidhīyate ।। [nataṃ syājjānunamanāt kṣiptaṃ vikṣepaṇād bahi] ।
udvāhitaṃ ca vijñeyamūrdhvamūdvāhanādapi । pratīpanayanaṃ yattu parivṛttaṃ taducyate ।। āvartitaṃ prayoktavyaṃ vidūṣakaparikrame । nataṃ cāpi hi kartavyaṃ sthānāsanagatādiṣu ।।
kṣiptaṃ vyāyāmayogeṣu tāṇḍave ca prayujyate । tathā codvāhitaṃ kuryādāviddhagamanādiṣu ।। tāṇḍaveṣu prayoktavyaṃ parivṛttaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । ityetajjaṅghayoḥ karma pādayostu nibodhata ।।
udghaṭṭitaḥ samaścaiva tathāgratalasañcaraḥ । añcitaḥ kuñcitaścaiva pādaḥ pañcavidha smṛtaḥ ।। sthitvā pādatalāgreṇa pārṣṇirbhūmau nipātyate । yasya pādasya karaṇe bhavedudghaṭṭitastu saḥ ।।
ayamudveṣṭitakaraṇe tvanukaraṇārthaṃ prayogamāsādya । drutamadhyamapracāraḥ sakṛdasakṛdā prayoktavyaḥ ।। svabhāvaracite bhūmau samasthāne ca yo bhavet । samaḥ pādaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ svabhāvābhinayāśrayaḥ ।।
sthirasvabhāvābhinaye nānākaraṇasaṃśraye । calitaśca punaḥ kāryo vidhijñaiḥ pādarecite ।। samasyaiva yadā pārṣṇiḥ pādasyābhyantare bhavet । bahiḥ pārśvasthito aṅguṣṭhastryaśrapādastu sa smṛtaḥ ।।
tyaktvā samapadaṃ sthānamaśvakrānte tathaiva ca । syādviklavādiṣvartheṣu tryaśraḥ pādo yathāvidhiḥ ।। asyaiva samapādasya pārṣṇirabhyantare bhavet । tryaśrapādaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sthānakādiṣu saṃśrayaḥ ।।
utkṣiptā tu bhavetpārṣṇiḥ prasṛtoṅguṣṭhakastathā । aṅgulyaścāñcitāḥ sarvā pāde agratalasañcaraḥ ।। todananikuṭṭane sthitaniśumbhane bhūmitāḍane bhramaṇe । vikṣepavividharecakapārṣṇikṛtāgamanametena ।।
pārṣṇiryasyāñcitā bhūmau pādamagratalaṃ tathā । aṅgulyaścāñcitāḥ sarvāḥ sa pādastvañcitaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pādāgratalasañcāre vartitodvartite tathā । eva pādāhate kāryo nānābhramarakeṣu ca ।।
utkṣiptā yasya pārṣṇī syādaṅgulyaḥ kuṅcitāstathā । tathā kuñcitamadhyaśca sa pādaṃ kuñcitaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। udattagamane caiva vartitodvartite tathā । utkṣiptā tu bhavetpārṣṇiraṅguṣṭhāgreṇa saṃsthitaḥ ।।
vāmaścaiva svabhāvasthaḥ sūcīpādaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । nṛtte nūpurakaraṇe prayogastasya kīrtyate ।। atikrāntakrame caiva pādametaṃ prayojayet । pādajaṅghorukaraṇaṃ karma kārya prayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
pādasya karaṇaṃ sarva jaṅghorukṛtamiṣyate । yathā pādaḥ pravarteta tathaivoruḥ pravartate ।। anayoḥ samānakaraṇāt pādacārī prayojayet । ityetadaṅgajaṃ proktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ karma caiva hi ।।
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi cārīvyāyāmalakṣaṇam ।। evaṃ pādasya jaṅghāyā ūrvoḥ kaṭyāstathaiva ca । samānakaraṇe ceṣṭā sā cārītyabhidhīyate ।। vidhānopagatāścāryo vyāyacchante parasparam ।
yasmādaṅgasamāyuktāstasmādvyāyāma ucyate ।। ekapādapracāro yaḥ sā cārītyabhisaṃjñitā । dvipādakramaṇaṃ yattu karaṇaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।। karaṇānāṃ samāyogaḥ khaṇḍamityabhidhīyate ।
khaṇḍaistribhiścaturbhirvā saṃyuktaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhavet ।। cārībhiḥ prasṛtaṃ nṛttaṃ cārībhiśceṣṭitaṃ tathā । cārībhiḥ śastramokṣaśca cāryo yuddhe ca kīrtitāḥ ।। yadetatprastutaṃ nāṭyaṃ taccārīṣveva saṃjñitam ।
nahi cāryā vinā kiñcinnāṭye aṅgaṃ saṃpravartate ।। tasmāccārīvidhānasya sampravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam । yā yasmiṃstu yathā yojyā nṛtte yuddhe gatau tathā ।। samapādā sthitāvartā śakaṭāsyā tathaiva ca ।
adhyardhikā cāṣagatirvicyavā ca tathāparā ।। eḍakākrīḍitā baddhā urudvṛttā tathāḍḍitā । utspanditā ca janitā syanditā cāpasyanditā ।। samotsaritamattallī mattallī ceti ṣoḍaśa ।
etā bhaumyaḥ smṛtāścāryaḥ śṛṇutākāśikīḥ punaḥ ।। atikrāntā hyapakrāntā pārśvakrāntā tathaiva ca । ūrdhvajānuśca sūcī ca tathā nūpurapādikā ।। ḍolapādā tathākṣiptā āviddhodvṛttasaṃjñite ।
vidyudbhrāntā hyalātā ca bhujaṅgatrāsitā tathā ।। mṛgaplutā ca daṇḍā ca bhramarī ceti ṣoḍaśa । ākāśikyaḥ smṛtā hyetā lakṣaṇaṃ ca nibodhata ।। pādairnirantarakṛtaistathā samanakhairapi ।
samapādā smṛtā cārī vijñeyā sthānasaṃśrayā ।। bhūmighṛṣṭena pādena kṛtvābhyantaramaṇḍalam । punarutsādayedanyaṃ sthitāvarttā tu sā smṛtā ।। niṣaṇṇāṅgastu caraṇaṃ prasārya talasañcaram ।
udvāhitamuraḥ kṛtvā śakaṭāsyāṃ prayojayet ।। savyasya pṛṣṭhato vāmaścaraṇastu yadā bhavet । tasyāpasarpaṇaṃ caiva jñeyā sādhyardhikā budhaiḥ ।। pādaḥ prasāritaḥ savyaḥ punaścaivopasarpitaḥ ।
vāmaḥ savyāpasarpī ca cāṣagatyāṃ vidhīyate ।। vicyavāt samapādāyā vicyavāṃ samprayojayet । nikuṭṭayaṃstalāgreṇa pādasya dharaṇītalam ।। talasañcarapādābhyāmutplutya patanaṃ tu yat ।
paryāyataśca kriyate eḍakākrīḍitā tu sā ।। anyonyajaṅghāsaṃvegāt kṛtvā tu svastikaṃ tataḥ । ūrubhyām valanaṃ yasmāt sā baddhā cāryudāhṛtā ।। talasañcarapādasya pārṣṇirbāhyonmukhī yadā ।
jaṅghāñcitā tathodvṛttā ūrudvṛtteti sā smṛtā ।। agrataḥ pṛṣṭhato vāpi pādastu talasañcaraḥ । dvitīyapādo nirghṛṣṭaḥ yasyāṃ syādaḍḍitā tu sā ।। śanaiḥ pādo nivarteta bāhyenābhyantareṇa ca ।
yadrecakānusāreṇa sā cāryutsyanditā smṛtā ।। muṣṭihastaśca vakṣaḥsthaḥ karo anyaśca pravartitaḥ । talasañcarapādaśca janitā cāryudāhṛtā ।। pañcatālāntaraṃ pādaṃ prasārya syanditāṃ nyaset ।
dvitīyena tu pādena tathāpasyanditāmapi ।। talasañcarapādābhyām ghūrṇamānopasarpaṇaiḥ । samotsaritamattallī vyāyāme samudāhṛtā ।। ubhābhyāmapi pādābhyāṃ ghūrṇamānopasarpaṇaiḥ ।
udveṣṭitāpaviddhaiśca hastairmattallyudāhṛtā ।। etā bhaumyaḥ smṛtāścāryo niyuddhakaraṇāśrayāḥ । ākāśakīnāṃ cārīṇāṃ sampravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya purataḥ samprasārayet ।
utkṣipya pātayeccainamatikrāntā tu sā smṛtā ।। ūrubhyāṃ valanaṃ kṛtvā kuñcitaṃ pādamuddharet । pārśve vinikṣipeccainamapakrāntā tu sā smṛtā ।। kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya pārśvenotpatanaṃ nyaset ।
udghaṭṭitena pādena pārśvakrāntā vidhīyate ।। kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya jānustanasamaṃ nyaset । dvitīyaṃ ca kramāt stabdhamūrdhvajānuḥ prakīrtitā ।। kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya jānūrdhvaṃ samprasārayet ।
pātayeccāgrayogena sā sūcī parikīrtitā ।। pṛṣṭhato hyañcitaṃ kṛtvā pādamagratalena tu । drutaṃ niryātayedbhūmau cārī nūpurapādikā ।। kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya pārśvātpārśvaṃ tu dolayet ।
pātayedañcitaṃ caivaṃ dolapādā tu sā smṛtā ।। kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya ākṣipya tvañcitaṃ nyaset । jaṅghāsvastikasaṃyuktā cākṣiptā nāma sā smṛtā ।। svastikasyāgrataḥ pādaḥ kuñcitastu prasāritaḥ ।
nipatedañcitāviddha āviddhā nāma sā smṛtā ।। pādamāviddhamāveṣṭya samutkṣipya nipātayet । parivṛttya dvitīyaṃ ca sodvṛttā cāryudāhṛtā ।। pṛṣṭhato valitaṃ pādaṃ śiroghṛṣṭaṃ prasārayet ।
sarvato maṇḍalāviddhaṃ vidyudbhrāntā tu sā smṛtā ।। pṛṣṭhaḥ prasāritaḥ pādo valito abhyantarīkṛtaḥ । pārṣṇiprapatitaścaiva hyalātā samprakīrtitā ।। kuñcitaṃ pādamutkṣipya tryaśramūruṃ vivartayet ।
kaṭijānuvivartācca bhujaṅgatrāsitā bhavet ।। atikrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā samutplutya nipātayet । jaṅghāñcitoparikṣiptā sā jñeyā hariṇaplutā ।। nūpuraṃ caraṇaṃ kṛtvā purataḥ samprasārayet ।
kṣipramāviddhakaraṇaṃ daṇḍapādā tu sā smṛtā ।। atikrāntakramaṃ kṛtvā trikaṃ tu parivartayet । dvitīyapādabhramaṇāttalena bhramarī smṛtā ।। ākāśikyaḥ smṛtā hyetā lalitāṅgakriyātmakāḥ ।
dhanurvajrāsiśastrāṇāṃ prayoktavyā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। agragau pṛṣṭhagau vāpi hyanugau cāpi yogataḥ । pādayostu dvijā hastau kartavyau nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ।। yataḥ pādastato hasto yato hastastatastrikam ।
pādasya nirgamaṃ jñātvā tathopāṅgāni yojayet ।। pādacāryāṃ yathā pādo dharaṇīmeva gacchati । evaṃ hastaścaritvā tu kaṭideśaṃ samāśrayet ।। etāścāryo mayā proktā lalitāṅgakriyātmakāḥ ।
sthānānyāsāṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvaśastravimokṣaṇe ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ samapādaṃ ca vaiśākhaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tathā । pratyālīḍhaṃ tathālīḍhaṃ sthānānyetāni ṣaṇ nṛṇāṃ ।। dvau tālāvardhatālaśca pādayorantaraṃ bhavet ।
tayoḥ samasthitastvekaḥ tryaśraḥ pakṣasthito aparaḥ ।। kiñcidañcitajaṅghaṃ ca sauṣṭhavāṅgapuraskṛtam । vaiṣṇavaṃ sthānametaddhi viṣṇuratrādhidaivatam ।। sthānenānena kartavyaḥ saṃllāpastu svabhāvajaḥ ।
nānākāryāntarāpetairnṛbhiruttamamadhyamaiḥ ।। cakrasya mokṣaṇe caiva dhāraṇe dhanuṣastathā । dhairyadānāṅgalīlāsu tathā krodhe prayojayet ।। idameva viparyastaṃ praṇayakrodha iṣyate ।
upālambhakṛte caiva praṇayodvegayostathā ।। śaṅkāsūyogratācintāmatismṛtiṣu caiva hi । dainye capalatāyoge garvābhīṣṭeṣu śaktiṣu ।। śṛṅgārādbhutabībhatsavīraprādhānyayojitam ।
samapāde samau pādau tālamātrāntarasthitau ।। svabhāvasauṣṭhavopetau brahmā cātrādhidaivatam । anena kāryaṃ sthānena vipramaṅgaladhāraṇam ।। rūpaṇe pakṣiṇāṃ caiva varaṃ kautukameva ca ।
svasthānaṃ syandanasthānāṃ vimānasthāyināmapi ।। liṅgasthānāṃ vratasthānāṃ sthānametattu kārayet । tālāstrayo ardhatālaśca pādayorantaraṃ bhavet ।। tālāṃstrīnardhatālāṃśca niṣaṇṇoruṃ prakalpayet ।
tryaśrau vakṣaḥsthitau caiva tatra pādo prayojayet ।। vaiśākhasthānametaddhi skandaścātrādhidaivatam । sthānenānena kartavyamaśvānāṃ vāhanaṃ budhaiḥ ।। vyāyāmanirgamaścaiva sthūlapakṣinirūpaṇam ।
śarāṇāṃ ca samutkṣepo vyāyāmakaraṇe tathā ।। recakeṣu ca kartavyamidameva prayoktṛbhiḥ । aindre tu maṇḍale pādau catustālāntarasthitau ।। tryaśrau pakṣaḥsthitau caiva kaṭijānū samau tathā ।
dhanurvajrāsiśastrāṇi maṇḍalena prayojayet ।। vāhanaṃ kuñjarāṇāṃ tu sthūlapakṣinirūpaṇam । asyaiva dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ pañca tālān prasārya tu ।। ālīḍhaṃ sthānakaṃ kuryād rudraścātrādhidaivatam ।
anena kāryaṃ sthānena vīraraudrakṛtaṃ tu yat ।। uttarottarasañjalpo roṣāmarṣakṛtastu yaḥ । mallānāñcaiva saṃpheṭaḥ śatrūṇāṃ ca nirūpaṇam ।। tathābhidravaṇaṃ caiva śastrāṇāṃ caiva mokṣaṇam ।
kuñcitaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā vāmaṃ pādaṃ prasārya ca ।। ālīḍhaparivartastu pratyālīḍhamiti smṛtam । ālīḍhasaṃhitaṃ śastraṃ pratyālīḍhena mokṣayet ।। nānāśastravimokṣo hi kāryo anena prayoktṛbhiḥ ।
nyāyāccaiva hi vijñeyāścatvāraḥ śastramokṣaṇe ।। bhārataḥ sātvataścaiva vārṣagaṇyo atha kaiśikaḥ । bhārate tu kaṭīcchedyaṃ pādacchedyaṃ tu sātvate ।। vakṣaso vārṣagaṇye tu śiraśchedyantu kaiśike ।
ebhiḥ prayoktṛbhirnyāyairnānācārīsamutthitaiḥ ।। pravicārya prayoktavyaṃ nānāśastravimokṣaṇe । nyāyāśritairaṅgahārairnyāyāccaiva samutthitaiḥ ।। yasmād yuddhāni vartante tasmānnyāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
vāmahaste vinikṣipya kheṭakaṃ śastrapheṭakam ।। śastramādāya hastena pravicāramathācaret । prasārya ca karau samyak punarākṣipya caiva hi ।। kheṭakaṃ bhrāmayet paścāt pārśvāt pārśvamathāpi ca ।
śiraḥparigamaścāpi kāryaḥ śastreṇa yoktṛbhiḥ ।। kapolasyāntare vāpi śastrasyodveṣṭanaṃ tathā । punaśca khaḍgahastena lalitodveṣṭitena ca ।। kheṭakena ca kartavyaḥ śiraḥparigamo budhaiḥ ।
evaṃ pracāraḥ kartavyo bhārate śastramokṣaṇe ।। sātvate ca pravakṣyāmi pravicāraṃ yathāvidhiḥ । sa eva pravicārastu khaḍgakheṭakayoḥ smṛtaḥ ।। kevalaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ śastraṃ kartavyaṃ khalu sātvate ।
gatiśca vārṣagaṇye api sātvatena krameṇa tu ।। śastrakheṭakayoścāpi bhramaṇaṃ saṃvidhīyate । śiraḥ parigamastadvacchastrasyeha bhavettathā ।। urasyudveṣṭanaṃ kāryaṃ śastrasyāṃśe athavā punaḥ ।
bhārate pravicāro ayaṃ kartavyaḥ sa tu kaiśike ।। vibhramayya tathā śastraṃ kevalaṃ mūrdhni pātayet । pravicārā prayoktavyā hyevamete aṅgalīlayā ।। dhanurvajrāsiśastrāṇāṃ prayoktavyā vimokṣaṇe ।
na bhedyaṃ nāpi tu cchedyaṃ na cāpi rudhirasrutiḥ ।। raṅge praharaṇe kāryo na cāpi vyaktaghātanam । saṃjñāmātreṇa kartavyaṃ śastrāṇāṃ mokṣaṇaṃ budhaiḥ ।। athavābhinayopetaṃ kuryācchedyaṃ vidhānataḥ ।
aṅgasauṣṭhavasaṃyuktairaṅgahārairvibhūṣitam ।। vyāyāmaṃ kārayet samyak layatālasamanvitam । sauṣṭhave hi prayatnastu kāryo vyāyāmasevibhiḥ ।। sauṣṭhave lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ vartanākramayojitam ।
śobhā sarvaiva nityaṃ hi sauṣṭhavaṃ samupāśritā ।। acañcalamakubjaṃ cāsannagātramathāpi ca । nātyuccaṃ calapādañca sauṣṭhavāṅgaṃ prayojayet ।। kaṭī karṇasamā yatra kūrparāṃsaśirastathā ।
samunnatamuraścaiva sauṣṭhavaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।। nahi sauṣṭhavahīnāṅgaḥ śobhate nāṭyanṛttayoḥ । atra nityaṃ prayatno hi vidheyo madhyamottamaiḥ ।। nāṭyaṃ nṛttaṃ ca sarvaṃ hi sauṣṭhave saṃpratiṣṭhitam ।
kaṭīnāmabhicarau hastau vakṣaścaiva samunnatam ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ sthānamityaṅgaṃ caturaśramudāhṛtam । parimārjanamādānaṃ sandhānaṃ mokṣaṇam tathā ।। dhanuṣastu prayoktavyaṃ karaṇaṃ tu caturvidham ।
saṃmārjanaṃ parāmarṣamādānaṃ grahaṇaṃ kriyā ।। sandhānaṃ śaravinyāso vikṣepo mokṣaṇaṃ bhavet । tailābhyaktena gātreṇa yavāgūmṛditena ca ।। vyāyāmaṃ kārayet śrīmān bhittāvākālike tathā ।
yogyāyāṃ mātṛkā bhittistasmādbhittiṃ samāśrayet ।। bhittau prasāritāṅgantu vyāyāmaṃ kārayennaram । balārthaṃ ca niṣeveta nasyaṃ bastividhiṃ tathā ।। snigdhānyanyāni ca tathā rasakaṃ pānakaṃ tathā ।
āhāre adhiṣṭhitāḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇe yogyāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। tasmādyogyāprasidhyarthamāhāre yatnavān bhavet । aśuddhakāyaṃ praklāntamatīvakṣutpipāsitam ।। atipītaṃ tathā bhuktaṃ vyāyāmaṃ naiva kārayet ।
acalairmadhuraigātraiścaturaśreṇa vakṣasā ।। vyāyāmaṃ kārayeddhīmān naramaṅgakriyātmakam । evaṃ vyāyāmasaṃyoge kāryaścārīkṛto vidhiḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi maṇḍalānāṃ vikalpanam ।
iti bharatīye nāṭyaśāstre cārīvidhāno nāma daśamo adhyāyaḥ । atha ekādaśo adhyāyaḥ । etāścāryo mayā proktā yathāvacchastramokṣaṇe । cārīsaṃyogajānīha maṇḍalāni nibodhata ।।
atikrāntaṃ vicitraṃ ca tathā lalitasañcaram । sūcīviddhaṃ daṇḍapādaṃ vihṛtālātake tathā ।। vāmabandhaṃ salalitaṃ krāntañcākāśagāmi ca । maṇḍalāni dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ ! bhūmigāni nibodhata ।।
bhramarāskandite syātāmāvartaṃ ca tataḥ param । samākranditamapyāhureḍakākrīḍitaṃ tathā ।। aḍḍitaṃ śakaṭāsyaṃ ca tathā'dhyardhakameva ca । piṣṭakuṭṭaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ tathā cāṣagataṃ punaḥ ।।
etānyapi daśoktāni bhūmigānīha nāmataḥ । ādyaṃ pādaṃ ca janitaṃ kṛtvodvāhitamācaret ।। alātaṃ vāmakaṃ caiva pārśvakrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam । sūcīvāmaṃ punaścaiva pārśvakrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam ।।
sūcīṃ vāmakramaṃ dadyādapakrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam । sūcīvāmaṃ punaścaiva trikaṃ ca parivartayet ।। tathā dakṣiṇamudvṛttamalātañcaiva vāmakam । paricchinnaṃ tu kartavyaṃ bāhyabhramarakeṇa hi ।।
atikrāntaṃ punarvāmaṃ daṇḍapādañca dakṣiṇam । vijñeyametad vyāyāme tvatikrāntaṃ tu maṇḍalam ।। ādyaṃ tu janitaṃ kṛtvā tenaiva ca nikuṭṭakam । āspanditaṃ tu vāmena pārśvakrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam ।।
vāmaṃ sūcīpadaṃ dadyādapakrāntañca dakṣiṇam । bhujaṅgatrāsitaṃ vāmamatikrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam ।। udvṛttaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ caivā'lātaṃ caivātra vāmakam । pārśvakrāntaṃ punaḥ savyaṃ sūcīvāmakramaṃ tathā ।।
vikṣepo dakṣiṇasya syādapakrāntaṃ ca vāmakam । bāhyabhramarakaṃ caiva vikṣepaṃ caiva yojayet ।। vijñeyametadvyāyāme vicitraṃ nāma maṇḍalam । kṛtvordhvajānucaraṇamādyaṃ sūcīṃ prayojayet ।।
apakrāntaḥ punarvāma ādyaḥ pārśvagato bhavet । vāmasūcīṃ punardadyāt trikañca parivartayet ।। pārśvakrāntaṃ punaścādyamatikrāntañca vāmakam । sūcīvāmakramaṃ kṛtvā hyapakrāntaśca vāmakam ।।
pārśvakrāntaṃ punaścādyamatikrāntaṃ ca vāmakam । paricchinnaṃ ca kartavyaṃ bāhyabhramaṇakena hi ।। eṣa cārīprayogastu kāryo lalitasañcaraiḥ । sūcīvāmapadaṃ dadyāt trikañca parivartayet ।।
pārśvakrāntaḥ punaścādyo vāmo atikrānta eva ca । sūcīmādyaṃ punardadyādatikrāntañca vāmakam ।। pārśvakrāntaṃ punaścādyaṃ sūcīviddhe tu maṇḍale । ādyastu janito bhūtvā sa ca daṇḍakramo bhavet ।।
vāmasūcīṃ punardadyāt trikañca parivartayet । udvṛtto dakṣiṇaśca syādalātaścaiva vāmakaḥ ।। pārśvakrāntaḥ punaścādyo bhujaṅgatrāsitastathā । atikrāntaḥ punarvāmo daṇḍapādaśca dakṣiṇaḥ ।।
vāmasūcītrikāvarto daṇḍapāde tu maṇḍale । ādyaṃ tu janitaṃ kṛtvā tenaiva ca nikuṭṭakam ।। āspanditaṃ ca vāmena hyudvṛttaṃ dakṣiṇena ca । alātaṃ vāmakaṃ pādaṃ sūcīṃ dadyāttu dakṣiṇam ।।
pārśvakrāntaḥ punarvāma ākṣipto dakṣiṇastathā । samāvartya trikaṃ caiva daṇḍapādaṃ prasārayet ।। sūcīvāmapadaṃ dadyāt trikaṃ tu parivartayet । bhujaṅgatrāsitaścādyo vāmo atikrānta eva ca ।।
eṣa cārīprayogastu vihṛte maṇḍale bhavet । sūcīmādyakramaṃ kṛtvā cā'pakrāntaṃ ca vāmakam ।। pārśvakrāntastataścādyo apyalātaścaiva vāmakaḥ । bhrāntvā cārībhiretābhiḥ paryāyeṇātha maṇḍalam ।।
ṣaṭsaṃkhyaṃ saptasaṃkhyaṃ ca lalitaiḥ pādavikramaiḥ । adhikuryādapakrāntamatikrāntaṃ ca vāmakam ।। apakrantaḥ punaścādyo vāmo atikrānta eva ca । pādabhramarakaśca syādalāte khalu maṇḍale ।।
sūcīmādyakramaṃ kṛtvā hyapakrāntaṃ ca vāmakam । ādyo daṇḍakramaścaiva sūcīpādastu vāmakaḥ ।। kāryastrikavivartaśca pārśvakrāntaśca dakṣiṇaḥ । ākṣiptaṃ vāmakaṃ kuryāt daṇḍapārśvaṃ ca dakṣiṇam ।।
urudvṛttaṃ ca tenaiva kartavyaṃ dakṣiṇena tu । sūcīvāmakramaṃ kṛtvā trikaṃ ca parivartayet ।। alātaśca bhavedvāmaḥ pārśvakrāntaśca dakṣiṇaḥ । atikrāntaḥ punarvāmo vāmabandhe tu maṇḍale ।।
sūcīmādyakramaṃ kṛtvā hyapakrāntaṃ ca vāmakam । pārśvakrāntaḥ punaścādyo bhujaṅgatrāsitaḥ sa ca ।। atikrāntaḥ punarvāma ākṣipto dakṣiṇastathā । atikrāntaḥ punarvāma urudvṛttastathaiva ca ।।
alātaśca punarvāmaḥ pārśvakrāntaśca dakṣiṇaḥ । sūcīvāmaṃ punardadyādapakrāntastu dakṣiṇaḥ ।। atikrāntaḥ punarvāmaḥ kāryo lalitasaṃjñakaḥ । eṣa pādaprasārastu lalite maṇḍale bhavet ।।
sūcīvāmakramaṃ kṛtvā hyapakrāntaśca vāmakam । pārśvakrāntaṃ punaścādyaṃ vāmapārśvakramaṃ tathā ।। bhrāntvā cārībhiretābhiḥ paryāyeṇātha maṇḍalam । vāmasūcīṃ tato dadyādapakrāntaṃ ca dakṣiṇam ।।
svabhāvagamane hyetanmaṇḍalaṃ saṃvidhīyate । krāntametattu vijñeyaṃ nāmato nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ।। etānyākāśagāmīni jñeyānyevaṃ daśaiva tu । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bhaumānāmiha lakṣaṇam ।।
ādyastu janitaḥ kāryo vāmaścāspandito bhavet । śakaṭāsyaḥ punaścādyo vāmaścāpi prasāritaḥ ।। ādyo bhramarakaḥ kāryastrikaṃ ca parivartayet । āskanditaḥ punarvāmaḥ śakaṭāsyaśca dakṣiṇaḥ ।।
vāmaḥ pṛṣṭhāpasarpī ca dadyād bhramarakaṃ tathā । sa evāspanditaḥ kāryastvetad bhramaramaṇḍalam ।। ādyo bhramarakaḥ kāryo vāmaścaivāḍḍito bhavet । kāryastrikavivarttaśca śakaṭāsyaśca dakṣiṇaḥ ।।
urudvṛttaḥ sa eva syādvāmaścaivāpasarpitaḥ । kāryastrikavivarttaśca dakṣiṇaḥ spandito bhavet ।। śakaṭāsyo bhavedvāmastadevāsphoṭanaṃ bhavet । etadāspanditaṃ nāma vyāyāme yuddhamaṇḍalam ।।
ādyastu janitaṃ kṛtvā vāmaścaiva nikuṭṭakam । śakaṭāsyaḥ punaścādya urudvṛttaḥ sa eva tu ।। pṛṣṭhāpasarpī vāmaśca sa ca cāṣagatirbhavet । āspanditaḥ punardakṣaḥ śakaṭāsyaśca vāmakaḥ ।।
ādyo bhramarakaścaiva trikaṃ ca parivartayet । pṛṣṭhāpasarpī vāmaścetyāvartaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhavet ।। samapādaṃ budhaḥ kṛtvā sthānaṃ hastau prasārayet । nirantarāvūrdhvatalāvāveṣṭyodveṣṭya caiva hi ।।
kaṭītaṭe vinikṣipya cādyamāvarttayet kramāt । yathākramaṃ punarvāmamāvartena prasārayet ।। cārayā cānayā bhrāntvā paryāyeṇātha maṇḍalam । samotsaritametattu kāryaṃ vyāyāmamaṇḍalam ।।
pādaistu bhūmisaṃyuktaiḥ sūcīviddhaistathaiva ca । eḍakākrīḍitaiścaiva tūrṇaistrikavivartitaiḥ ।। sūcīviddhāpaviddhaiśca krameṇāvṛttya maṇḍalam । eḍakākrīḍitaṃ vidyāt khaṇḍamaṇḍalasaṃjñitam ।।
savyamudghaṭṭitaṃ kṛtvā tenaivāvartamācaret । tenaivāskanditaḥ kāryaḥ śakaṭāsyaśca vāmakaḥ ।। ādyaḥ pṛṣṭhāpasarpī ca sa ca cāṣagatirbhavet । aḍḍitaśca punarvāma ādyaścaivāpasarpitaḥ ।।
vāmo bhramarakaḥ kārya ādya āskandito bhavet । tenaivāsphoṭanaṃ kuryādetadaḍḍitamaṇḍalam ।। ādyaṃ tu janitaṃ kṛtvā tenaiva ca nikuṭṭakam । sa eva śakaṭāsyaśca vāmaścāskandito bhavet ।।
vijñeyaṃ śakaṭāsyaṃ tu vyāyāme yuddhamaṇḍalam । pādaiśca śakaṭāsyasthaiḥ paryāyeṇātha maṇḍalam ।। ādyastu janito bhūtvā sa evāskandito bhavet । apasarpī punarvāmaḥ śakaṭāsyaśca dakṣiṇaḥ ।।
bhrāntvā cārībhiretābhiḥ paryāyeṇātha maṇḍalam । adhyardhametadvijñeyaṃ niyuddhe cāpi maṇḍalam ।। sūcīmādyakramaṃ kṛtvā hyapakrāntaṃ ca vāmakam । bhujaṅgatrāsitaścādya evameva tu vāmakaḥ ।।
bhujaṅgatrāsitairbhrāntvā pādairapi ca maṇḍalam । piṣṭakuṭṭaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ cārībhirmaṇḍalaṃ budhaiḥ ।। sarvaiścāṣagataiḥ pādaiḥ paribhrāmya tu maṇḍalam । etaccāṣagataṃ vidyānniyuddhe cāpi maṇḍalam ।।
nānācārīsamutthāni maṇḍalāni samāsataḥ । uktānyataḥ paraṃ caiva samacārīṇi yojayet ।। samacārīprayogo yastatsamaṃ nāma maṇḍalam । ācāryabuddhyā tānīha kartavyāni prayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
etāni khaṇḍāni samaṇḍalāni yuddhe niyuddhe ca parikrame ca । līlāṅgamādhuryapuraskṛtāni kāryāṇi vādyānugatāni tajjñaiḥ ।। evaṃ vyāyāmasaṃyoge kāryaṃ maṇḍalakalpanam । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi gatīstu prakṛtisthitāḥ ।।
tatropavahanaṃ kṛtvā bhāṇḍavādyapuraskṛtam । yathāmārgarasopetaṃ prakṛtīnāṃ praveśane ।। dhruvāyāṃ saṃprayuktāyāṃ paṭe caivāpakarṣite । kāryaḥ praveśaḥ pātrāṇāṃ nānārtharasasambhavaḥ ।।
sthānaṃ tu vaiṣṇavaṃ kṛtvā hyuttame madhyame tathā । samunnataṃ samaṃ caiva caturasramurastathā ।। bāhuśīrṣe prasanne ca nātyutkṣipte ca kārayet । grīvāpradeśaḥ kartavyo mayūrāñcitamastakaḥ ।।
karṇādaṣṭāṅgulasthe ca bāhuśīrṣe prayojayet । urasaścāpi cibukaṃ caturaṅgulasaṃsthitam ।। hastau tathaiva kartavyau kaṭīnābhitaṭasthitau । dakṣiṇo nābhisaṃsthastu vāmaḥ kaṭitaṭasthitaḥ ।।
pādayorantaraṃ kāryaṃ dvau tālāvardhameva ca । pādotkṣepastu kartavyaḥ svapramāṇavinirmitaḥ ।। catustālo dvitālaścāpyekatālastathaiva ca । catustālastu devānāṃ pārthivānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।
dvitālaścaiva madhyānāṃ tālaḥ strīnīcaliṅginām । catuṣkalo atha dvikalastathā hyekakalaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। catuṣkalo hyuttamānāṃ madhyānāṃ dvikalo bhavet । tathā caikakalaḥ pādo nīcānāṃ saṃprakīrtitaḥ ।।
sthitaṃ madhyaṃ drutaṃ caiva samavekṣya layatrayam । yathāprakṛtināṭyajño gatimevaṃ prayojayet ।। dhairyopapannā gatiruttamānāṃ madhyā gatirmadhyamasammatānām । drutā gatiśca pracurādhamānāṃ layatrayaṃ sattvavaśena yojyam ।।
eṣa eva tu vijñeyaḥ kalātālalaye vidhiḥ । punargatipracārasya prayogaṃ śruṇutānaghāḥ ।। svabhāvāttūttamagatau kāryaṃ jānukaṭīsamam । yuddhacārīprayogeṣu jānustanasamaṃ nyaset ।।
pārśvakrāntaiḥ salalitaiḥ pādairvādyānvitairatha । raṅgakoṇonmukhaṃ gacchet samyak pañcapadāni ca ।। vāmavedhaṃ tataḥ kuryādvikṣepaṃ dakṣiṇena tu । parivṛtya dvitīyaṃ tu gacchet koṇaṃ tataḥ param ।।
tatrāpi vāmavedhastu vikṣepo dakṣiṇena ca । tato bhāṇḍonmukho gacchet tānyeva tu padāni ca ।। evaṃ gatāgataiḥ kṛtvā padānāmiha viṃśatim । vāmavedhaṃ tataḥ kuryāt vikṣepaṃ dakṣiṇasya ca ।।
raṅge vikṛṣṭe bharatena kāryo gatāgataiḥ pādagatipracāraḥ । tryaśrastrikoṇe caturasraraṅge gatipracāraścaturasra eva ।। yaḥ samaiḥ saṃhito gacchettatra kāryo layāśrayaḥ । catuṣkalo atha dvikalastathaivaikakalaḥ punaḥ ।।
atha madhyamanīcaistu gacchedyaḥ parivāritaḥ । catuṣkalamathārdhaṃ ca tathā caikakalaṃ punaḥ ।। daityadānavayakṣāṇāṃ nṛpapannagarakṣasām । catustālapramāṇena kartavyātha gatirbudhaiḥ ।।
divaukasāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ madhyamā gatiriṣyate । tatrāpi coddhatā ye tu teṣāṃ devaiḥ samā gatiḥ ।। yadā manuṣyā rājānasteṣāṃ devagatiḥ katham । atrocyate kathaṃ naiṣā gatī rājñāṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
iha prakṛtayo divyā divyamānuṣya eva ca । mānuṣya iti vijñeyā nāṭyanṛttakriyāṃ prati ।। devānāṃ prakṛtirdivyā rājñāṃ vai divyamānuṣī । yā tvanyā lokaviditā mānuṣī sā prakīrtitā ।।
devāṃśajāstu rājāno vedādhyātmasu kīrtitāḥ । evaṃ devānukaraṇe doṣo hyatra na vidyate ।। ayaṃ vidhistu kartavyaḥ svacchandagamanaṃ prati । saṃbhramotpātaroṣeṣu pramāṇaṃ na vidhīyate ।।
sarvāsāṃ prakṛtīnāṃ tu avasthāntarasaṃśrayā । uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ gatiḥ kāryā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। caturardhakalaṃ vā syāt tadardhakalameva ca । avasthāntaramāsādya kuryād gativiceṣṭitam ।।
jyeṣṭhe catuṣkalaṃ hyatra madhyame dvikalaṃ bhavet । dvikalā cottame yatra madhye tvekakalā bhavet ।। kalikaṃ madhyame yatra nīceṣvardhakalaṃ bhavet । evamardhārdhahīnaṃ tu jaḍānāṃ saṃprayojayet ।।
jvarārte ca kṣudhārte ca tapaḥśrānte bhayānvite । vismite cāvahitthe ca tathautsukyasamanvite ।। śṛṅgāre caiva śoke ca svacchandagamane tathā । gatiḥ sthitalayā kāryādhikalāntarapātitā ।।
punaścintānvite caiva gatiḥ kāryā catuṣkalā । asvasthakāmite caiva bhaye vitrāsite tathā ।। āvege caiva harṣe ca kārye yacca tvarānvitam । aniṣṭaśravaṇe caiva kṣepe cādbhutadarśane ।।
api cātyāyike kārye duḥkhite śatrumārgaṇe । aparāddhānusaraṇe śvāpadānugatau tathā ।। eteṣvevaṃ gatiṃ prājño vikalāṃ saṃprayojayet । uttamānāṃ gatiryā tu na tāṃ madhyeṣu yojayet ।।
yā gatirmadhyamānāṃ tu na tāṃ nīceṣu yojayet । gatiḥ śṛṅgāriṇī kāryā svasthakāmitasambhavā ।। dūtīdarśitamārgastu praviśedraṅgamaṇḍalam । sūcayā cāpyabhinayaṃ kuryādarthasamāśrayam ।।
hṛdyairgandhaistathā vastrairalaṅkāraiśca bhūṣitaḥ । nānāpuṣpasugandhābhirmālābhiḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ ।। gacchet salalitaiḥ pādairatikrāntasthitaistathā । tathā sauṣṭhavasaṃyuktairlayatālavaśānugaiḥ ।।
pādayoranugau hastau nityaṃ kāryau prayoktṛbhiḥ । utkṣipya hastaṃ pātena pādayośca viparyayāt ।। pracchannakāmite caiva gatiṃ bhūyo nibodhata । visarjitajanaḥ srastastathā dūtīsahāyavān ।।
nirvāṇadīpo nātyarthaṃ bhūṣaṇaiśca vibhūṣitaḥ । velāsadṛśavastraśca saha dūtyā śanaistathā ।। vrajet pracchannakāmastu pādairniśśabdamandagaiḥ । śabdaśaṃkyutsukaśca syādavalokanatatparaḥ ।।
vepamānaśarīraśca śaṃkitaḥ praskhalan muhuḥ । rase raudre tu vakṣyāmi daityarakṣogaṇān prati ।। eka eva rasasteṣāṃ sthāyī raudro dvijottamāḥ । nepathyaraudro vijñeyastvaṅgaraudrastathaiva ca ।।
tathā svabhāvajaścaiva tridhā raudraḥ prakalpitaḥ । rudhiraklinnadeho yo rudhirārdramukhastathā ।। । tathā piśitahastaśca raudro nepathyajastu saḥ । bahubāhurbahumukho nānāpraharaṇākulaḥ ।।
sthūlakāyastathā prāṃśuraṅgaraudraḥ prakīrtitaḥ । raktākṣaḥ piṅgakeśaśca asito vikṛtasvaraḥ ।। rūkṣo nirbhartsanaparo raudraḥ so ayaṃ svabhāvajaḥ । catustālāntarotkṣiptaiḥ pādaistvantarapātitaiḥ ।।
gatirevaṃ prakartavyā teṣāṃ ye cāpi tadvidhāḥ । ahṛdyā tu mahī yatra śmaśānaraṇakaśmalā ।। gatiṃ tatra prayuñjīta bībhatsābhinayaṃ prati । kvacidāsannapatitaiḥ vikṛṣṭapatitaiḥ kvacit ।।
elakākrīḍitaiḥ pādairuparyupari pātitaiḥ । teṣāmevānugairhastairbībhatse gatiriṣyate ।। atha vīre ca karttavyā pādavikṣepasaṃyutā । drutapracārādhiṣṭhānā nānācārīsamākulā ।।
pārśvakrāntaidrutāviddhaiḥ sūcīviddhaistathaiva ca । kalākālagataiḥ pādairāvege yojayet gatim ।। uttamānāmayaṃ prāyaḥ prokto gatiparikramaḥ । madhyānāmadhamānāṃ ca gatiṃ vakṣyāmyahaṃ punaḥ ।।
vismaye caiva harṣe ca vikṣiptapadavikramān । āsādya tu rasaṃ hāsyametaccānyaṃ ca yojayet ।। punaśca karuṇe kāryā gatiḥ sthirapadairatha । bāṣpāmburuddhanayanaḥ sannagātrastathaiva ca ।।
utkṣiptapātitakarastathā sasvanarodanaḥ । gacchettathādhyadhikayā pratyagrāpriyasaṃśraye ।। eṣā strīṇāṃ prayoktavyā nīcasattve tathaiva ca । uttamānāṃ tu kartavyā sadhairyā bāṣpasaṅgatā ।।
niḥśvāsairāyatotsṛṣṭaistathaivordhvanirīkṣitaiḥ । na tatra sauṣṭhavaṃ kāryaṃ na pramāṇaṃ tathāvidham ।। madhyānāmapi sattvajñā gatiryojyā vidhānataḥ । uraḥpātahatotsāhaḥ śokavyākulacetanaḥ ।।
nātyutkṣiptaiḥ padairgacchet iṣṭabandhunipātane । gāḍhaprahāre kāryā ca śithilāṅgabhujāśrayā ।। vighūṇitaśarīrā ca gatiścūrṇapadairatha । śītena cābhibhūtasya varṣeṇābhidrutasya ca ।।
gatiḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ kāryā strīnīcaprakṛtāvatha । piṇḍīkṛtya tu gātrāṇi teṣāṃ caiva prakampanam ।। karau vakṣasi nikṣipya kubjībhūtastathaiva ca । dantoṣṭhasphuraṇaṃ caiva cibukasya prakampanam ।।
kāryaṃ śanaiśca kartavyaṃ śītābhinayane gatau । tathā bhayānake caiva gatiḥ kāryā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। strīṇāṃ kāpuruṣāṇāṃ ca ye cānye sattvavarjitāḥ । visphārite cale netre vidhutaṃ ca śirastathā ।।
bhayasaṃyuktayā dṛṣṭyā pārśvayośca vilokanaiḥ । drutaiścūrṇapadaiścaiva baddhvā hastaṃ kapotakam ।। pravepitaśarīraśca śuṣkoṣṭhasskhalitaṃ vrajet । eṣānukaraṇe kāryā tarjane trāsane tathā ।।
sattvaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca vikṛtaṃ svaram । eṣā strīṇāṃ prakarttavyā nṛṇāṃ cākṣiptavikramā ।। kvacidāsannapatitairvikṛṣṭapatitaiḥ kvacit । elakākrīḍitaiḥ pādairuparyupari pātitaiḥ ।।
eṣāmevānugairhastairgatiṃ bhīteṣu yojayet । vaṇijāṃ sacivānāṃ ca gatiḥ kāryā svabhāvajā ।। kṛtvā nābhitaṭe hastamuttānakhaṭakāmukham । ādyaṃ cārālamuttānaṃ kuryātpārśvaṃ stanāntare ।।
na niṣaṇṇaṃ na ca stabdhaṃ na cāpi parivāhitam । kṛtvā gātraṃ tathā gacchettena caiva krameṇa tu ।। atikrāntairpadairviprā dvitālāntaragāmibhiḥ । yatīnāṃ śramaṇānāṃ ca ye cānye tapasi sthitāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ kāryā gatirye tu naiṣṭhikaṃ vratamāśritāḥ । ālolacakṣuśca bhavedyugamātranirīkṣaṇaḥ ।। upasthitasmṛtiścaiva gātraṃ sarvaṃ vidhāya ca । acañcalamanāścaiva yathāvalliṅgamāśritaḥ ।।
vinītaveṣaśca bhavet kaṣāyavasanastathā । prathamaṃ samapādena sthitvā sthānena vai budhaḥ ।। hastaṃ ca caturaṃ kṛtvā tathā caikaṃ prasārayet । prasannaṃ vadanaṃ kṛtvā prayogasya vaśānugaḥ ।।
aniṣaṇṇena gātreṇa gatiṃ gacched vyatikramāt । uttamānāṃ bhavedeṣā liṅgināṃ ye mahāvratāḥ ।। ebhireva viparyastairguṇairanyeṣu yojayet । tathā vratānugāvasthā hyanyeṣāṃ liṅgināṃ gatiḥ ।।
vibhrāntā vāpyudāttā vā vibhrāntanibhṛtāpi vā । śakaṭāsyasthitaiḥ pādairatikrāntaistathaiva ca ।। kāryā pāśupatānāṃ ca gatiruddhatagāminī । andhakāre atha yāne ca gatiḥ kāryā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
bhūmau visarpitaiḥ pādairhastairmārgapradarśibhiḥ । rathasthasyāpi kartavyā gatiścūrṇapadairatha ।। samapādaṃ tathā sthānaṃ kṛtvā rathagatiṃ vrajet । dhanurgṛhītvā caikena tathā caikena kūbaram ।।
sūtaścāsya bhavedevaṃ pratodapragrahākulaḥ । vāhanāni vicitrāṇi kartavyāni vibhāgaśaḥ ।। drutaiścūrṇapadaiścaiva gantavyaṃ raṅgamaṇḍale । vimānasthasya kartavyā hyeṣaiva syandinī gatiḥ ।।
āroḍhumudvahed gātraṃ kiñcit syādunmukhasthitam । asyaiva vaiparītyena kuryāccāpyavarohaṇam ।। adho avalokanaiścaiva maṇḍalāvartanena ca । ākāśagamane caiva kartavyā nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
sthānena samapādena tathā cūrṇapadairapi । vyomnaścāvataredyastu tasyaitāṃ kārayet gatim ।। ṛjvāyatonnatanataiḥ kuṭilāvartitairatha । bhraśyataśca tathākāśādapaviddhabhujā gatiḥ ।।
vikīrṇavasanā caiva tathā bhūgatalocanā । prāsādadrumaśaileṣu nadīnimnonnateṣu ca ।। ārohaṇāvataraṇaṃ ca kāryamarthavaśādbudhaiḥ । prāsādārohaṇaṃ kāryaṃ atikrāntaiḥ padairatha ।।
udvāhya gātraṃ pādaṃ ca sopāne nikṣipennaraḥ । tathāvataraṇaṃ caiva gātramānamya recayet ।। prāsāde yanmayā proktaḥ pratāraḥ kevalo bhavet । kiñcinnatāgrakāyā tu pratāre gatiriṣyate ।।
jalapramāṇāpekṣā tu jalamadhye gatirbhavet । toye alpe vasanotkarṣaḥ prājye pāṇivikarṣaṇaiḥ ।। prasārya bāhumekaikaṃ muhurbārivikarṣaṇaiḥ । tiryak prasāritā caiva hiyamāṇā ca vāriṇā ।।
aśeṣāṅgākulādhūtavadanā gatiriṣyate । nausthasyāpi prayoktavyā drutaiścūrṇapadairgatiḥ ।। atikrāntena pādena dvitīyenāñcitena ca । prāsādārohaṇe yattu tadevādriṣu kārayet ।।
kevalamūrdhvanikṣepamadriṣvaṅgaṃ bhavedatha । drume cārohaṇaṃ kāryamatikrāntaiḥ sthitaiḥ padaiḥ ।। sūcīviddhairapakrāntaiḥ pārśvakrāntaistathaiva ca । etadevāvataraṇaṃ saritsvapi niyojayet ।।
anenaiva vidhānena kartavyaṃ gaticeṣṭitam । saṃjñāmātreṇa kartavyānyetāni vidhipūrvakam ।। kasmānmṛta iti prokte kiṃ kartavyaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । aṅkuśagrahaṇānnāgaṃ khalīnagrahaṇāddhayam ।।
pragrahagrahaṇādyānamevamevāpareṣvapi । aśvayāne gatiḥ kāryā vaiśākhasthānakena tu ।। yathā cūrṇapadaiścitrairuparyupari pātitaiḥ । pannagānāṃ gatiḥ kāryā pādaiḥ svastikasaṃjñitaiḥ ।।
pārśvakrāntaṃ padaṃ kuryāt svastikaṃ recayediha । viṭasyāpi tu kartavyā gatirlalitavikramā ।। pādairākuñcitaiḥ kiñcit tālābhyantarapātitaiḥ । svasauṣṭhavasamāyuktau tathā hastau padānugau ।।
khaṭakāvardhamānau tu kṛtvā viṭagatiṃ vrajet । kañcukīyasya kartavyā vayovasthāviśeṣataḥ ।। avṛddhasya prayogajño gatimevaṃ prayojayet । ardhatālotthitaiḥ pādairviṣkambhaiḥ ṛjubhistathā ।।
samudvahannivāṅgāni paṅkalagna iva vrajet । atha vṛddhasya kartavyā gatiḥ kampitadehikā ।। viṣkambhanakṛtaprāṇā mandotkṣiptapadakramā । kṛśasyāpyabhineyā vai gatirmandaparikramā ।।
vyādhigraste jvarārte ca tapaḥśrānte kṣudhānvite । viṣkambhanakṛtaprāṇaḥ kṛśaḥ kṣāmodarastathā ।। kṣāmasvarakapolaśca dīnanetrastathaiva ca । śanairutkṣepaṇaṃ caiva kartavyaṃ hastapādayoḥ ।।
kampanaṃ caiva gātrāṇāṃ kleśanaṃ ca tathaiva ca । dūrādhvānaṃ gatasyāpi gatirmandapadakramā ।। vikūṇanaṃ ca gātrasya jānunośca vimardanam । sthūlasyāpi tu kartavyā gatirdehānukarṣiṇī ।।
samudvahanabhūyiṣṭhā mandotkṣiptapadakramā । viṣkambhagāmī ca bhavenniḥśvāsabahulastathā ।। śramasvedābhibhūtaśca vrajeccūrṇapadaistathā । mattānāṃ tu gatiḥ kāryā made taruṇamadhyame ।।
vāmadakṣiṇapādābhyāṃ ghūrṇamānāpasarpaṇaiḥ । avakṛṣṭe pade caiva hyanavasthitapādikā ।। vighūrṇitaśarīrā ca karaiḥ praskhalitaistathā । unmattasyāpi kartavyā gatistvaniyatakramā ।।
bahucārīsamāyuktā lokānukaraṇāśrayā । rūkṣasphuṭitakeśaśca rajodhvastatanustathā ।। animittaprakathano bahubhāṣī vikāravān । gāyatyakasmāddhasati saṅge cāpi na sajjate ।।
nṛtyatyapi ca saṃhṛṣṭo vādayatyapi vā punaḥ । kadāciddhāvati javāt kadācidavatiṣṭhate ।। kadācidupaviṣṭastu śayānaḥ syāt kadācana । nānācīradharaścaiva rathyāsvaniyatālayaḥ ।।
unmatto bhavati hyevaṃ tasyaitāṃ kārayed gatim । sthitvā nūpurapādena daṇḍapādaṃ prasārayet ।। baddhāṃ cārīṃ tathā caiva kṛtvā svastikameva ca । anena cārīyogena paribhrāmya tu maṇḍalam ।।
bāhyabhramarakaṃ caiva raṅgakoṇe prasārayet । trikaṃ sulalitaṃ kṛtvā latākhyaṃ hastameva ca ।। viparyayagatairhastaiḥ padbhyāṃ saha gatirbhavet । trividhā tu gatiḥ kāryā khañjapaṅgukavāmanaiḥ ।।
vikalāṅgaprayogeṇa kuhakābhinayaṃ prati । ekaḥ khañjagatau nityaṃ stabdho vai caraṇo bhavet ।। tathā dvitīyaḥ kāryastu pādo agratalasañcaraḥ । stabdhenotthāpanaṃ kāryamaṅgasya caraṇena tu ।।
gamanena niṣaṇṇaḥ syādanyena caraṇena tu । itareṇa niṣīdecca krameṇānena vai vrajet ।। eṣā khañjagatiḥ kāryā talaśalyakṣateṣu ca । pādenāgratalasthena hyañcitena vrajettathā ।।
niṣaṇṇadehā paṅgostu natajaṅghā tathaiva ca । sarvasaṅkucitāṅgā ca vāmane gatiriṣyate ।। na tasya vikramaḥ kāryo vikṣepaścaraṇasya ca । sodvāhitā cūrṇapadā sā kāryā kuhanātmikā ।।
vidūṣakasyāpi gatirhāsyatrayasamanvitā । aṅgavākyakṛtaṃ hāsyaṃ hāsyaṃ nepathyajaṃ smṛtam ।। danturaḥ khalatiḥ kubjaḥ khañjaśca vikṛtānanaḥ । ya īdṛśaḥ praveśaḥ syādaṅgahāsyaṃ tu tadbhavet ।।
yadā tu bakavadgacchedullokitavilokitaiḥ । anyāyatapadatvācca aṅgahāsyo bhavetsa tu ।। kāryahāsyaṃ tu vijñeyamasaṃbaddhaprabhāṣaṇāt । anarthakairvikāraiśca tathā cāślīlabhāṣitaiḥ ।।
cīracarmamaśībhasmagairikādyaistu maṇḍitaḥ । yastādṛśo bhavedviprā hāsyo nepathyajastu saḥ ।। tasmāttu prakṛtiṃ jñātvā bhāvaḥ kāryastu tattvataḥ । gatipracāraṃ vibhajet nānāvasthāntarātmakam ।।
svabhāvajāyāṃ vinyasya kuṭilaṃ vāmake kare । tadā dakṣiṇahaste ca kuryāccaturakaṃ punaḥ ।। pārśvamekaṃ śiraścaiva hasto atha caraṇastathā । paryāyaśaḥ sannamayellayatālavaśānugaḥ ।।
svabhāvajā tu tasyaiṣā gatiranyā vikārajā । alābhalābhāt muktasya stabdhā tasya gatirbhavet ।। kāryā caiva hi nīcānāṃ ceṭādīnāṃ parikramāt । adhamā iti ye khyātā nānāśīlāśca te punaḥ ।।
pārśvasekaṃ śiraścaiva karaḥ sacaraṇastathā । śakārasyāpi kartavyā gatiścañcaladehikā । gatau nameta ceṭānāṃ dṛṣṭiścārdhavicāriṇī ।। vastrābharaṇasaṃsparśairmuhurmuhuravekṣitaiḥ ।
gātrairvikāravikṣiptaiḥ lambavastrasrajā tathā ।। sagarvitā cūrṇapadā śakārasya gatirbhavet । jātyā nīceṣu yoktavyā vilokanaparā gatiḥ ।। asaṃsparśācca lokasya svāṅgāni vinigūhya ca ।
mlecchānāṃ jātayo yāstu pulindaśabarādayaḥ ।। teṣāṃ deśānusāreṇa kāryaṃ gativiceṣṭitam । pakṣiṇāṃ śvāpadānāṃ ca paśūnāṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।। svasvajātisamutthena svabhāvena gatirbhavet ।
siṃharkṣavānarāṇāṃ ca gatiḥ kāryā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। yā kṛtā narasiṃhena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā । ālīḍhasthānakaṃ kṛtvā gātraṃ tasyaiva cānugam ।। jānūpari karaṃ hyekamaparaṃ vakṣasi sthitam ।
avalokya diśaḥ kṛtvā cibukaṃ bāhumastake ।। gantavyaṃ vikramairviprāḥ pañcatālāntarotthitaiḥ । niyuddhasamaye caiva raṅgāvataraṇe tathā ।। siṃhādīnāṃ prayoktavyā gatireṣā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।
śeṣāṇāmarthayogena gatiṃ sthānaṃ ca yojayet ।। vāhanārthaprayogeṣu raṅgāvataraṇeṣu ca । evametāḥ prayoktavyā narāṇāṃ gatayo budhaiḥ ।। noktā yā yā mayā hyatra grāhyāstāstāśca lokataḥ ।
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi strīṇāṃ gativiceṣṭitam ।। strīṇāṃ sthānāni kāryāṇi gatiṣvābharaṇeṣu ca । āyataṃ cāvahitthaṃ ca aśvakrāntamathāpi ca ।। sthānānyetāni nārīṇāmatha lakṣaṇamucyate ।
vāmaḥ svabhāvato yatra pādo viracitaḥ samaḥ ।। tālamātrāntare nyastastryaśraḥ pakṣasthito aparaḥ । prasannamānanamuraḥ samaṃ yatra samunnatam ।। latānitambagau hastau sthānaṃ jñeyaṃ tadāyatam ।
dakṣiṇastu samaḥ pādaḥ tryaśraḥ pakṣasthito aparaḥ ।। vāmaḥ samunnatakaṭiścāyate sthānake bhavet । āvāhane visarge ca tathā nirvarṇaneṣu ca ।। cintāyāṃ cāvahitthe ca sthānametat prayojayet ।
raṅgāvataraṇārambhaḥ puṣpāñjalivisarjanam ।। manmatherṣyodbhavaṃ kopaṃ tarjanyaṅgulimoṭanam । niṣedhagarvagāmbhīryamaunaṃ mānāvalambanam ।। sthāne asmin saṃvidhātavyaṃ digantaranirūpaṇam ।
samo yatra sthito vāmastryaśraḥ pakṣasthito aparaḥ ।। samunnatakaṭirvāmastvavahitthaṃ tu tadbhavet । puro vicalitastryaśrastadanyopasṛtaḥ samaḥ ।। pādastālāntaranyastastrikamīṣatsamunnatam ।
pāṇirlatākhyo yatraikastadanyastu nitambagaḥ ।। avahitthaṃ samākhyātaṃ sthānamāgamabhūṣaṇaiḥ । strīṇāmetat smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ saṃlāpe tu svabhāvaje ।। niścaye paritoṣe ca vitarke cintane tathā ।
vilāsalīlāvibvokaśṛṃgārātmanirūpaṇe ।। sthānametatprayoktavyaṃ bharturmārgavilokane । pādaḥ samasthitaścaika ekaścāgratalāñcitaḥ ।। sūcīviddhamaviddhaṃ vā tadaśvakrāntamucyate ।
skhalitaṃ ghūrṇitaṃ caiva galitāmbaradhāraṇam ।। kusumastabakādānaṃ parirakṣaṇameva ca । vitrāsanaṃ salalitaṃ taruśākhāvalambanam ।। sthāne asmin saṃvidhānīyaṃ strīṇāmetatprayoktṛbhiḥ ।
śākhāvalambane kāryaṃ stabakagrahaṇe tathā ।। viśrāmeṣvatha devānāṃ narāṇāṃ cārthayogataḥ । sthānakaṃ tāvadeva syādyāvacceṣṭā pravartate ।। bhagnaṃ ca sthānakaṃ nṛtte cārī cetsamupasthitā ।
evaṃ sthānavidhiḥ kāryaḥ strīṇāṃ nṛṇāmathāpi ca ।। punaścāsāṃ pravakṣyāmi gatiṃ prakṛtisaṃsthitām । kṛtvāvahitthaṃ sthānaṃ tu vāmaṃ cādhomukhaṃ karam ।। nābhipradeśe vinyasya savyaṃ ca khaṭakāmukham ।
tataḥ salalitaṃ pādaṃ tālamātrasamutthitam ।। dakṣiṇaṃ vāmapādasya bāhyapārśve vinikṣipet । tenaiva samakālaṃ ca latākhyaṃ vāmakaṃ bhujam ।। dakṣiṇaṃ vinametpārśvaṃ nyasennābhitaṭe tataḥ ।
nitambe dakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā hastaṃ codveṣṭya vāmakam ।। tato vāmapadaṃ dadyāt latāhastaṃ ca dakṣiṇam । līlayodvāhitenātha śirasānugatena ca ।। kiñcinnatena gātreṇa gacchetpañcapadīṃ tataḥ ।
yo vidhiḥ puruṣāṇāṃ tu raṅgapīṭhaparikrame ।। sa eva pramadānāṃ vai kartavyo nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ । ṣaṭkalaṃ tu na kartavyaṃ tathāṣṭakalameva ca ।। pādasya patanaṃ tajjñaiḥ khedanaṃ tadbhavetstriyāḥ ।
sayauvanānāṃ nārīṇāmevaṃ kāryā gatirbudhaiḥ ।। sthavīyasīnāmetāsāṃ sampravakṣyāmyahaṃ gatim । kṛtvāpaviddhaṃ sthānantu vāmaṃ nyasya kaṭītaṭe ।। ādyaṃ cārālamuttānaṃ kuryānnābhistanāntare ।
na niṣaṇṇaṃ na ca stabdhaṃ na cāpi parivāhitam ।। kṛtvā gātraṃ tato gacchettenaiveha krameṇa tu । preṣyāṇāmapi kartavyā gatirudbhrāntagāminī ।। kvacidunnamitairgātraiḥ āviddhabhujavikramā ।
sthānaṃ kṛtvāvahitthaṃ ca vāmaṃ cādhomukhaṃ bhujam ।। nābhipradeśe vinyasya savyaṃ ca khaṭakāmukham । ardhanārīgatiḥ kāryā strīpuṃsābhyāṃ vimiśritā ।। udāttalalitairgātraiḥ pādairlīlāsamanvitaiḥ ।
yā pūrvamevābhihitā hyuttamānāṃ gatirmayā ।। strīṇāṃ kāpuruṣāṇāṃ ca tato ardhārdhaṃ tu yojayet । madhyamottamanīcānāṃ nṛṇāṃ yad gaticeṣṭitam ।। strīṇāṃ tadeva kartavyā lalitaiḥ padavikramaiḥ ।
bālānāmapi kartavyā svacchandapadavikramā ।। na tasyāḥ sauṣṭhavaṃ kāryaṃ na pramāṇaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । tṛtīyā prakṛtiḥ kāryā nāmnā caiva napuṃsakā ।। narasvabhāvamutsṛjya strīgatiṃ tatra yojayet ।
viparyayaḥ prayoktavyaḥ puruṣastrīnapuṃsake ।। svabhāvamātmanastyaktvā tadbhāvagamanādiha । vyājena krīḍayā vāpi tathā bhūyaṃ ca vañcanāt ।। strī puṃsaḥ prakṛtiṃ kuryāt strībhāvaṃ puruṣo api ca ।
dhairyodāryeṇa sattvena buddhyā tadvacca karmaṇā ।। strī pumāṃsaṃ tvabhinayet veṣavākyaviceṣṭitaiḥ । strīveṣabhāṣitairyuktaṃ preṣitāpreṣitaistathā ।। mṛdusannagatiścaiva pumān strībhāvamācaret ।
jātihīnāśca yā nāryaḥ pulindaśabarāṅganāḥ ।। yāścāpi tāsāṃ kartavyā tajjātisadṛśī gatiḥ । vratasthānāṃ tapaḥsthānāṃ liṅgasthānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। khasthānāṃ caiva nārīṇāṃ samapādaṃ prayojayet ।
uddhatā ye aṅgahārāḥ syuḥ yāścāryo maṇḍalāni ca ।। tāni nāṭyaprayogajñairna kartavyāni yoṣitām । tathāsanavidhiḥ kāryo nṛṇāṃ strīṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। nānābhāvasamāyuktastathā ca śayanāśrayaḥ ।
viṣkambhitāñcitau pādau trikaṃ kiñcitsamunnatam ।। hastau kaṭyūruvinyastau svasthe syādupaveśane । pādaḥ prasāritaḥ kiñcidekaścaivāsanāśrayaḥ ।। śiraḥ pārśvanataṃ caiva sacinta upaveśane ।
cibukopāśritau hastau bāhuśīrṣāśritaṃ śiraḥ ।। sampraṇaṣṭendriyamanāḥ śokautsukyopaveśane । prasārya bāhū śithilau tathā śropāśrayāśritaḥ ।। mohamūrcchāmadaglāniviṣādeṣūpaveśayet ।
sarvapiṇḍīkṛtāṅgastu saṃyuktaiḥ pādajānubhiḥ ।। vyādhivrīḍitanidrāsu dhyāne copaviśennaraḥ । tathā cotkaṭikaṃ sthānaṃ sphikpārṣṇīnāṃ samāgamaḥ ।। pitrye nivāpe japye ca sandhyāsvācamane api ca ।
viṣkambhitaṃ punaścaivaṃ jānuṃ bhūmau nipātayet ।। priyāprasādane kāryaṃ homādikaraṇeṣu ca । mahīgatābhyāṃ jānubhyāmadhomukhamavasthitam ।। devābhigamane caiva ruṣitānāṃ prasādane ।
śoke cākrandane tīvre mṛtānāṃ caiva darśane ।। trāsane ca kusattvānāṃ nīcānāṃ caiva yācane । homayajñakriyāyāṃ ca preṣyāṇāṃ caiva kārayet ।। munīnāṃ niyameṣveṣa bhavedāsanajo vidhiḥ ।
tathāsanavidhiḥ kāryo vividho nāṭakāśrayaḥ ।। strīṇāṃ ca puruṣāṇāṃ ca bāhyaścābhyantarastathā । ābhyantarastu nṛpaterbāhyo bāhyagatasya ca ।। devānāṃ nṛpatīnāṃ ca dadyāt siṃhāsanaṃ dvijaḥ ।
purodhasāmamātyānāṃ bhavedvetrāsanaṃ tathā ।। muṇḍāsanaṃ ca dātavyaṃ senānīyuvarājayoḥ । kāṣṭhāsanaṃ dvijātīnāṃ kumārāṇāṃ kuthāsanam ।। evaṃ rājasabhāṃ prāpya kāryastvāsanajo vidhiḥ ।
strīṇāṃ cāpyāsanavidhiṃ sampravakṣyāmyahaṃ punaḥ ।। siṃhāsanaṃ tu rājñīnāṃ devīnāṃ muṇḍamāsanam । purodho amātyapatnīnāṃ dadyādvetrāsanaṃ tathā ।। bhoginīnāṃ tathā caiva vastraṃ carma kutho api vā ।
brāhmaṇītāpasīnāṃ ca paṭṭāsanamathāpi ca ।। veśyānāṃ ca pradātavyamāsanaṃ ca mayūrakam । śeṣāṇāṃ pramadānāṃ tu bhaved bhūmyāsanaṃ dvijāḥ ।। evamābhyantaro jñeyo bāhyaścāsanajo vidhiḥ ।
tathā svagṛhavārtāsu cchandenāsanamiṣyate ।। niyamasthamunīnāṃ ca bhavedāsanajo vidhiḥ । liṅgināmāsanavidhiḥ kāryo vratasamāśrayaḥ ।। bruṣīmuṇḍāsanaprāyaṃ vetrāsanamathāpi ca ।
home yajñakriyāyāṃ ca pitrye arthe ca prayojayet ।। sthānīyā ye ca puruṣāḥ kulavidyāsamanvitāḥ । teṣāmāsanasatkāraḥ karttavya iha pārthivaiḥ ।। same samāsanaṃ dadyāt madhye madhyamamāsanam ।
atirikte atiriktaṃ ca hīne bhūmyāsanaṃ bhavet ।। upādhyāyasya nṛpatergurūṇāmagrato budhaiḥ । bhūmyāsanaṃ tathā kāryamathavā kāṣṭhamāsanam ।। naunāgarathayāneṣu bhūmikāṣṭhāsaneṣu ca ।
sahāsanaṃ na duṣyeta gurūpādhyāyapārthivaiḥ ।। ākuñcitaṃ samaṃ caiva prasāritavivartane । udvāhitaṃ nataṃ caiva śayane karma kīrtyate ।। sarvairākuñcitairaṅgaiḥ śayyāviddhe tu jānunī ।
sthānamākuñcitaṃ nāma śītārtānāṃ prayojayet ।। uttānitamukhaṃ caiva srastamuktakaraṃ tathā । samaṃ nāma prasuptasya sthānakaṃ saṃvidhīyate ।। ekaṃ bhujamupādhāya samprasāritajānukam ।
sthānaṃ prasāritaṃ nāma sukhasuptasya kārayet ।। adhomukhasthitaṃ caiva vivartitamiti smṛtam । śastrakṣatamṛtotkṣiptamattonmatteṣu kārayet ।। aṃsopari śiraḥ kṛtvā karpūrakṣobhameva ca ।
udvāhitaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ līlayā veśane prabhoḥ ।। īṣatprasārite jaṅghe yatra srastau karāvubhau । ālasyaśramakhedeṣu nataṃ sthānaṃ vidhīyate ।। gatiprācārastu mayodito ayaṃ noktaśca yaḥ so arthavaśena sādhyaḥ ।
ataḥ paraṃ raṅgaparikramasya vakṣyāmi kakṣyāṃ pravibhāgayuktām ।। ye tu pūrvaṃ mayā proktāstrayo vai nāṭyamaṇḍapāḥ । teṣāṃ vibhāgaṃ vijñāya tataḥ kakṣyāṃ prayojayet ।। ye nepathyagṛhadvāre mayā pūrvaṃ prakīrtite ।
tayorbhāṇḍasya vinyāso madhye kāryaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। kakṣyāvibhāgo nirdeśyo raṅgapīṭhaparikramāt । parikrameṇa raṅgasya kakṣyā hyanyā vidhīyate ।। kakṣyāvibhāge jñeyāni gṛhāṇi nagarāṇi ca ।
udyānārāmasaritastvāśramā aṭavī tathā ।। pṛthivī sāgarāścaiva trailokyaṃ sacarācaram । varṣāṇi saptadvīpāśca parvatā vividhāstathā ।। alokaścaiva lokaśca rasātalamathāpi ca ।
daityanāgālayāścaiva gṛhāṇi bhavanāni ca ।। nagare vā vane vāpi varṣe vā parvate api vā । yatra vārtā pravarteta tatra kakṣyāṃ pravartayet ।। bāhyaṃ vā madhyamaṃ vāpi tathaivābhyantaraṃ punaḥ ।
dūraṃ vā sannikṛṣṭaṃ vā deśaṃ tu parikalpayet ।। pūrvapraviṣṭā ye raṅgaṃ jñeyāste abhyantarā budhaiḥ । paścātpraviṣṭā vijñeyāḥ kakṣyābhāge tu bāhyataḥ ।। teṣāṃ tu darśanecchuryaḥ praviśedraṅgamaṇḍapam ।
dakṣiṇābhimukhaḥ so atha kuryādātmanivedanam ।। yato mukhaṃ bhavedbhāṇḍaṃ dvāraṃ nepathyakasya ca । sā mantavyā tu dik pūrvā nāṭyayoge na nityaśaḥ ।। niṣkrāmedyaśca tasmādvai sa tenaiva tathā vrajet ।
yatastasya kṛtaṃ tena puruṣeṇa nivedanam ।। niṣkrānto arthavaśāccāpi praviśedyadi tadgṛham । yataḥ prāptaḥ sa puruṣastena mārgeṇa niṣkramet ।। athavārthavaśāccāpi tenaiva saha gacchati ।
tathaiva praviśet gehamekākī sahito api vā ।। tayoścāpi praviśatoḥ kakṣyāmanyāṃ vinirdiśet । parikrameṇa raṅgasya tvanyā kakṣyā vidhīyate ।। samaiśca sahito gacchennīcaiśca parivāhitaḥ ।
atha prekṣaṇikāścāpi vijñeyā hyagrato gatau ।। saiva bhūmistu bahubhirvikṛṣṭā syātparikramaiḥ । madhyā vā sannikṛṣṭā vā teṣāmevaṃ vikalpayet ।। nagare vā vane vāpi sāgare parvate api vā ।
divyānāṃ gamanaṃ kāryaṃ dvīpe varṣeṣu vā punaḥ ।। ākāśena vimānena māyayāpyatha vā punaḥ । vividhābhiḥ kriyābhirvā nānārthābhiḥ prayogataḥ ।। nāṭake cchannaveṣāṇāṃ divyānāṃ bhūmisañcaraḥ ।
mānuṣe kāraṇādeṣāṃ yathā bhavati darśanam ।। bhārate tvatha haime vā harivarṣa ilāvṛte । ramye kiṃpuruṣe vāpi kuruṣūttarakeṣu vā ।। divyānāṃ chandagamanaṃ sarvavarṣeṣu kīrtitam ।
bhārate mānuṣāṇāñca gamanaṃ saṃvidhīyate ।। gacchedyadi vikṛṣṭastu deśakālavaśānnaraḥ । aṅkacchede tamanyasmin nirdiśeddhi praveśake ।। ahnaḥ pramāṇaṃ gatvā tu kāryalābhaṃ vinirdiśed ।
tathālābhe tu kāryasya aṅkacchedo vidhīyate ।। kṣaṇo muhūrto yāno vā divaso vāpi nāṭake । ekāṅke sa vidhātavyo bījasyārthavaśānugaḥ ।। aṅkacchede tu nirvṛttaṃ māsaṃ vā varṣameva vā ।
nordhvaṃ varṣātprakartavyaṃ kāryamaṅkasamāśrayam ।। evaṃ tu bhārate varṣe kakṣyā kāryā prayogataḥ । mānuṣāṇāṃ gatiryā tu divyānāntu nibodhata ।। himavatpṛṣṭhasaṃsthe tu kailāse parvatottame ।
yakṣāśca guhyakāścaiva dhanadānucarāśca ye ।। rakṣaḥpiśācabhūtāśca sarve haimavatāḥ smṛtāḥ । hemakūṭe ca gandharvā vijñeyāḥ sāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। sarve nāgāśca niṣadhe śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ ।
mahāmerau trayastriṃśad jñeyā devagaṇā budhaiḥ ।। nīle tu vaiḍūryamaye siddhā brahmarṣayastathā । daityānāṃ dānavānāñca śvetaparvata iṣyate ।। pitaraścāpi vijñeyā śṛṅgavantaṃ samāśritāḥ ।
ityete parvatāḥ śreṣṭhā divyāvāsāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। teṣāṃ kakṣyāvibhāgaśca jambūdvīpe bhavedayam । teṣāṃ na ceṣṭitaṃ kāryaṃ svaiḥ svaiḥ karmaparākramaiḥ ।। pariccha daviśeṣastu teṣāṃ mānuṣalokavat ।
sarve bhāvāśca divyānāṃ kāryā mānuṣasaṃśrayāḥ ।। teṣāntvanimiṣatvaṃ yattanna kāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । iha bhāvā rasāścaiva dṛṣṭāveva pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।। dṛṣṭyā hi sūcito bhāvaḥ punaraṅgairvibhāvyate ।
evaṃ kakṣyāvibhāgastu mayā prokto dvijottamāḥ ।। punaścaiva pravakṣyāmi pravṛttīnāntu lakṣaṇam । caturvidhā pravṛttiśca proktā nāṭyaprayogataḥ । āvantī dākṣiṇātyā ca pāñcālī coḍhramāgadhī ।।
atrāha pravṛttiriti kasmāt? ucyate pṛthivyāṃ nānādeśaveṣabhāṣācāravārtāḥ prakhyāpayatīti vṛttiḥ । pravṛttiśca nivedane । atrāha - yathā pṛthivyāṃ bahavo deśāḥ santi, kathamāsāṃ caturvidhatvam upapannaṃ, samānalakṣaṇaścāsāṃ prayoga ucyate, satyametat । samānalakṣaṇa āsāṃ prayogaḥ । kintu nānādeśaveṣabhāṣācāro loka iti kṛtvā lokānumatena vṛttisaṃśritasya nāṭyasya vṛttīnāṃ mayā caturvidhatvamabhihitaṃ bhāratī sāttvatī kaiśikyārabhaṭī ceti । vṛttisaṃśritaiśca prayogairabhihitā deśāḥ । yataḥ pravṛtticatuṣṭayamabhinirvṛttaṃ prayogaścotpāditaḥ । tatra dākṣiṇātyāstāvat bahunṛttagītavādyā kaiśikīprāyāḥ caturamadhuralalitāṅgābhinayāśca । tadyathā - mahendro malayaḥ sahyo mekalaḥ pālamañjaraḥ । eteṣu ye śritā deśāḥ sa jñeyo dakṣiṇāpathaḥ ।। kosalāggstośalāścaiva kaliṅgā yavanā khasāḥ ।
draviḍāndhramahārāṣṭrā vaiṣṇā vai vānavāsajāḥ ।। dakṣiṇasya samudrasya tathā vindhyasya cāntare । ye deśāsteṣu yuñjīta dākṣiṇātyāṃ tu nityaśaḥ ।। āvantikā vaidiśikāḥ saurāṣṭrā mālavāstathā ।
saindhavāstvatha sauvīrā āvartāḥ sārbudeyakāḥ ।। dāśārṇāstraipurāścaiva tathā vai mārtikāvatāḥ । kurvantyāvantikīmete pravṛttiṃ nityameva tu ।। sāttvatīṃ kaiśikīṃ caiva vṛttimeṣāṃ samāśritā ।
bhavet pryogo nāṭye atra sa tu kāryaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। aṅgā vaṅgāḥ kaliṅgāśca vatsāścaivoḍhramāgadhāḥ । pauṇḍrā nepālakāścaiva antargiribahirgirāḥ ।। tathā plavaṅgamā jñeyā maladā mallavartakāḥ ।
brahmottaraprabhṛtayo bhārgavā mārgavāstathā ।। prājyotiṣāḥ pulindāśca vaidehāstāmraliptakāḥ । prāṅgāḥ prāvṛtayaścaiva yuñjantīhoḍhramāgadhīm ।। anye api deśāḥ prācyāṃ ye purāṇe samprakīrtitāḥ ।
teṣu prayujyate hyeṣā pravṛttiścoḍhramāgadhī ।। pāñcālā saurasenāśca kāśmīrā hastināpurāḥ । bāhlīkā śalyakāścaiva madrakauśīnarāstathā ।। himavatsaṃśritā ye tu gaṅgāyāścottarāṃ diśam ।
ye śritā vai janapadāsteṣu pāñcālamadhyamāḥ ।। pāñcālamadhyamāyāṃ tu sāttvatyārabhaṭī smṛtā । prayogastvalpagītārtha āviddhagativikramaḥ ।। dvidhā kriyā bhavatyāsāṃ raṅgapīṭhaparikrame ।
pradakṣiṇapradeśā ca tathā cāpyapradakṣiṇā ।। āvantī dākṣiṇātyā ca pradakṣiṇaparikrame । apasavyapradeśāstu pāñcālī coḍhramāgadhī ।। āvantyāṃ dākṣiṇātyāyāṃ pārśvadvāramathottaram ।
pāñcālyāmoḍhramāgadhyāṃ yojyaṃ dvāraṃ tu dakṣiṇam ।। ekībhūtāḥ punaścaitāḥ prayoktavyāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ । pārṣadaṃ deśakālau vāpyarthayuktimavekṣya ca ।। yeṣu deśeṣu yā kāryā pravṛttiḥ parikīrtitā ।
tadvṛttikāni rūpāṇi teṣu tajjñaḥ prayojayet ।। ekībhūtāḥ punastvetā nāṭakādau bhavanti hi । avekṣya vṛttibāhulyaṃ tattatkarma samācaret ।। sārthe bāhulyamekasya śeṣāṇāmatha buddhimān ।
yeṣāmanyasya bāhulyaṃ pravṛttiṃ pūrayettadā ।। prayogo dvividhaścaiva vijñeyo nāṭakāśrayaḥ । sukumārastathāviddho nāṭyayuktisamāśrayaḥ ।। yattvāviddhāṅgahārantu cchedyabhedyāhavātmakam ।
māyendrajālabahulaṃ pustanepathyasaṃyutam ।। puruṣairbahubhiryuktamalpastrīkaṃ tathaiva ca । sāttvatyārabhaṭīyuktaṃ nāṭyamāviddhasaṃjñitam ।। ḍimaḥ samavakāraśca vyāyogehāmṛgau tathā ।
etānyāviddhasaṃjñāni vijñeyāni prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। eṣāṃ prayogaḥ kartavyo daityadānavarākṣasaiḥ । uddhatā ye ca puruṣāḥ śauryavīryabalānvitāḥ ।। nāṭakaṃ saprakaraṇaṃ bhāṇo vīthyaṅkanāṭike ।
sukumāraprayogāṇi mānuṣeṣvāśritāstu ye ।। atha bāhyaprayogeṣu prekṣāgṛhavivarjite । vidikṣvapi bhavedraṅgaḥ kadācid bharturājñayā ।। pṛṣṭha kutapaṃ nāṭye yuktā yato mukhaṃ bharatāḥ ।
sā pūrvā mantavyā prayogakāle tu nāṭyajñaiḥ ।। raṅgasya digbhāgaviniścitāni । prācyāṃ pratīcyāṃ ca diśi praveśaḥ ।। vinā pramāṇādvidiśaḥ prayoge ।
prācīṃ diśaṃ tāṃ manasā'dhyavasyet ।। vayo anurūpaḥ prathamantu veśo veśo anurūpaśca gatipracāraḥ । pāṭhyānurūpābhinayaśca kāryaḥ ।। dharmī yā dvividhā proktā mayā pūrvaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।
laukikī nāṭyadharmī ca tayorvakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। svabhāvabhāvopagataṃ śuddhaṃ tvavikṛtaṃ tathā । lokavārtākriyopetamaṅgalīlāvivarjitam ।। svabhāvābhinayopetaṃ nānāstrīpuruṣāśrayam ।
yadīdṛśaṃ bhavennāṭyaṃ lokadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। ativākyakriyopetamatisattvātibhāvakam । līlāṅgahārābhinayaṃ nāṭyalakṣaṇalakṣitam ।। svarālaṅkārasaṃyuktamasvasthapuruṣāśrayam ।
yadīdṛśaṃ bhavennāṭyaṃ nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। lokaprasiddhaṃ dravyantu yadā nāṭye prayujyate । mūrtimat sābhilāṣañca nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। āsannoktantu yadvākyaṃ na śṛṇvanti parasparam ।
anuktaṃ śrūyate vākyaṃ nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। śailayānavimānāni carmavarmāyudhadhvajāḥ । mūrtimantaḥ prayujyante nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। ya ekāṃ bhūmikāṃ kṛtvā kurvītaikāntare aparām ।
kauśalyādekakatvādvā nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। yā gamyā pramadā bhūtvā gamyā bhūmiṣu yujyate । gamyā bhūmiṣvagamyā ca nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। lalitairaṅgavinyāsaistathotkṣiptapadakramaiḥ ।
nṛtyate gamyate yacca nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। yo ayaṃ svabhāvo lokasya sukhaduḥkhakriyātmakaḥ । so aṅgābhinayasaṃyukto nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। yaścetihāsavedārtho brahmaṇā samudāhṛtaḥ ।
divyamānuṣaratyarthaṃ nāṭyadharmī tu sā smṛtā ।। yaśca kakṣyāvibhāgo ayaṃ nānāvidhisamāśritaḥ । raṅgapīṭhagataḥ prokto nāṭyadharmī tu sā bhavet ।। nāṭyadharmīpravṛttaṃ hi sadā nāṭyaṃ prayojayet ।
na hyaṅgābhinayātkiñcidṛte rāga pravartate ।। sarvasya sahajo bhāvaḥ sarvo hyabhinayo arthataḥ । aṅgālaṅkāraceṣṭābhirnāṭyadharmī prakīrtitā ।। evaṃ kakṣyāvibhāgastu dharmī yuktaya eva ca ।
vijñeyā nāṭyatattvajñaiḥ prayoktavyāśca tattvataḥ ।। ukto mayehābhinayo yathāvat śākhākṛto yaśca kṛto aṅgahāraiḥ । punaśca vākyābhinayaṃ yathāvadvakṣye svaravyañjanavarṇayuktam ।। yo vāgabhinayaḥ prokto mayā pūrvaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।
lakṣaṇaṃ tasya vakṣyāmi svaravyañjanasambhavam ।। vāci yatnastu kartavyo nāṭyasyeyaṃ tanuḥ smṛtā । aṅganepathyasattvāni vākyārthaṃ vyañjayanti hi ।। vāṅmayānīha śāstrāṇi vāṅniṣṭhāni tathaiva ca ।
tasmādvācaḥ paraṃ nāsti vāg hi sarvasya kāraṇam ।। āgamanāmākhyātanipātopasargasamāsataddhitairyuktaḥ । sandhivacanavibhaktyupagrahaniyukto vācikābhinayaḥ ।। dvividhaṃ hi smṛtaṃ pāṭhyaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ prākṛtaṃ tathā ।
tayorvibhāgaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। vyañjanāni svarāścaiva sandhayo atha vibhaktayaḥ । nāmākhyātopasargāśca nipātāstaddhitāstathā ।। etairaṅgaiḥ samāsaiśca nānādhātusamāśrayam ।
vijñeyaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ pāṭhyaṃ prayogañca nibodhata ।। akārādyāḥ svarā jñeyā aukārāntāścaturdaśa । hakārāntāni kādīni vyañjanāni vidurbudhāḥ ।। tatra svarāścaturdaśa - a ā i ī u ū ṛ ṝ ḷ ḹ e ai o au iti svarā jñeyāḥ ।।
śa ṣa sa ha iti vyañjanavargaḥ । varge varge samākhyātau dvau varṇau prāgavasthitau । aghoṣā iti ye tvanye saghoṣāḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ ।। aṣṭau sthānāni varṇānāmuraḥ kaṇṭhaḥ śirastathā ।
jihvāmūlaśca dantāśca nāsikoṣṭhau ca tālu ca ।। a ku ha visarjanīyāḥ kaṇṭhyāḥ । i cu ya śāstālavyāḥ । ṛ ṭu ra ṣā mūrdhanyāḥ । ḷ tu la sā dantyāḥ । u pūpadhmānīyā oṣṭhyāḥ । -pa -pha iti paphābhyāṃ prāk ardhavisargasadṛśaḥ upadhmānīyaḥ । -ka -kha iti kakhābhyāṃ prāk ardhavisargasadṛśo jihvamūlīyaḥ । e ai kaṇṭhyatālavyau । o au kaṇṭhyoṣṭhyau । vakāro dantyoṣṭhyaḥ । ṅa ña ṇa na mā anunāsikāḥ । visarjanīyaḥ aurasyaḥ ityeke । sarvavarṇānāṃ mukhaṃ sthānamityapare । dvau dvau varṇau tu vargādyau śaṣasāśca trayo apare ।
aghoṣā ghoṣavantastu tato anye parikīrtitāḥ ।। ete ghoṣāghoṣāḥ kaṇṭhyoṣṭhyā dantyajihvānunāsikyāḥ । ūṣmāṇastālavyāḥ visarjanīyāśca boddhavyāḥ ।। gaghaṅa jajhaña ḍaḍhaṇa dadhana babhama tathaiva yaralavā matā ghoṣāḥ ।
kakha cacha ṭaṭha tatha papha iti vargeṣvaghoṣāḥ syuḥ ।। kakhagaghaṅāḥ kaṇṭhasthāstālusthānāstu cachajajhañāḥ । ṭaṭhaḍaḍhaṇā mūrdhanyāstathadadhanāścaiva dantasthāḥ ।। paphababhamāstvoṣṭhyāḥ syuḥ dantyā ḷlasā ahau ca kaṇṭhasthau ।
tālavyā icuyaśā syurṛṭuraṣā mūrdhasthitā jñeyāḥ ।। ḷḹ dantyau oau kaṇṭhoṣṭhyau eaikārau ca kaṇṭhatālavyau । kaṇṭhyo visarjanīyo jihvāmūlamudbhavaḥ kakhayoḥ ।। paphayoroṣṭhasthānaṃ bhavedukāraḥ svaro vivṛtaḥ ।
spṛṣṭāḥ kādyā māntāḥ śaṣasahakārāstathā vivṛtāḥ ।। antasthāḥ saṃvṛtajāḥ ṅañaṇanamā nāsikodbhavā jñeyāḥ । ūṣmāṇaśca śaṣasahāḥ yaralavavarṇāstathaiva cāntaḥsthāḥ ।। jihvāmūlīyaḥ -kaḥ -pa upadhmānīyasaṃjñayā jñeyaḥ ।
kacaṭatapā svaritāḥ syuḥ khachaṭhathaphā syuḥ sadā kramyāḥ ।। kaṇṭhyorasyān vidyāt ghajhaḍhadhabhān pāṭhyasaṃprayoge tu । vedyo visarjanīyo jihvāsthāne sthito varṇaḥ ।। ete vyañjanavarṇāḥ samāsataḥ saṃjñayā mayā kathitāḥ ।
śabdaviṣayaprayoge svarāṇstu bhūyaḥ pravakṣyāmi ।। yasmin sthāne sa samo vijñeyo yaḥ savarṇasaṃjño asau । ya ime svarāścaturdaśa nirdiṣṭāstatra vai daśa samānāḥ । pūrvo hrasvaḥ teṣāṃ paraśca dīrgho avagantavyaḥ ।।
itthaṃ vyañjanayogaiḥ svaraiśca sākhyātanāmapadavihitaiḥ । kāvyanibandhāśca syurdhātunipātopasargāstu ।। ebhirvyañjanavargairnāmākhyātopasarganipātaiḥ । taddhitasandhivibhaktibhiradhiṣṭhitaḥ śabda ityuktaḥ ।।
pūrvācāryairuktaṃ śabdānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ samāsayogena । vistaraśaḥ punareva prakaraṇavaśāt saṃpravakṣyāmi ।। arthapradhānaṃ nāma syādākhyātaṃ tu kriyākṛtam । dyotayantyupasargāstu viśeṣaṃ bhāvasaṃśrayam ।।
tatprāhuḥ saptavidhaṃ ṣaṭkārakasaṃyutaṃ prathitasādhyam । nirdeśasaṃpradānāpadānaprabhṛtisaṃjñābhiḥ ।। nāmākhyātārthaviṣayaṃ viśeṣaṃ dyotayanti te । pṛthaktatropasargebhyo nipātā niyame acyute ।।
saṃpratyatītakālakriyādisaṃyojitaṃ prathitasādhyam । vacanaṃ nāgatayuktaṃ susadṛśasaṃyojanavibhaktam ।। pañcaśatadhātuyuktaṃ pañcaguṇaṃ pañcavidhamidaṃ vāpi । svādyadhikāraguṇairarthaviśeṣairvibhūṣitanyāsam ।
prātipadikārthaliṅgairyuktaṃ pañcavidhamidaṃ jñeyam ।। ākhyātaṃ pāṭhyakṛtaṃ jñeyaṃ nānārthāśrayaviśeṣam । vacanaṃ nāmasametaṃ puruṣavibhaktaṃ tadākhyātam ।। prātipadikārthayuktāndhātvarthānupasṛjanti ye svārthaiḥ ।
upasargā hyupadiṣṭāstasmāt saṃskāraśāstre asmin ।। prātipadikārthayogāddhātucchandoniruktayuktyā ca । yasmānnipatanti pade tasmātproktā nipātāstu ।। pratyayavibhāgajanitāḥ prakarṣasaṃyogasatvavacanaiśca ।
yasmātpūrayate arthān pratyaya uktastatastasmāt ।। loke prakṛtipratyayavibhāgasaṃyogasatvavacanaiśca । tāṃstān pūrayate arthāṃsteṣu yastaddhitastasmāt ।। ekasya bahūnāṃ vā dhātorliṅgasya vā padānāṃ vā ।
vibhajantyarthaṃ yasmāt vibhaktayastena tāḥ proktāḥ ।। viśiṣṭāstu svarā yatra vyañjanaṃ vāpi yogataḥ । sandhīyate pade yasmāttasmāt sandhiḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। varṇapadakramasiddhaḥ padaikayogācca varṇayogācca ।
sandhīyate ca yasmāttasmāt sandhiḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ ।। luptavibhaktirnāmnāmekārthaṃ saṃharatsamāso api । tatpuruṣādikasaṃjñairnirdiṣṭaḥ ṣaḍvidho viprāḥ ।। ebhiḥ śabdavidhānairvistāravyañjanārthasaṃyuktaiḥ ।
padabandhāḥ kartavyā nibaddhabandhāstu cūrṇā vā ।। vibhaktyantaṃ padaṃ jñeyaṃ nibaddhaṃ cūrṇameva ca । tatra cūrṇapadasyeha sannibodhata lakṣaṇam ।। anibaddhapadaṃ chandovidhānāniyatākṣaram ।
arthāpekṣyakṣarasyūtaṃ jñeyaṃ cūrṇapadaṃ budhaiḥ ।। nibaddhākṣarasaṃyuktaṃ yaticchedasamanvitam । nibaddhaṃ tu padaṃ jñeyaṃ pramāṇaniyatātmakam ।। evaṃ nānārthasaṃyuktaiḥ pādairvarṇavibhūṣitaiḥ ।
caturbhistu bhavedyuktaṃ chando vṛttābhidhānavat ।। ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ smṛtānyebhiḥ pādaiśchandasi saṃkhyayā । samañcārdhasamañcaiva tathā viṣamameva ca ।। chandoyuktaṃ samāsena trividhaṃ vṛttamiṣyate ।
nānāvṛttiviniṣpannā śabdasyaiṣā tanūssmṛtā ।। chandohīno na śabdo asti na cchandaśśabdavarjitam । tasmāttūbhyasaṃyogo nāṭyasyodyotakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ekākṣaraṃ bhaveduktamatyuktaṃ dvyakṣaraṃ bhavet ।
madhyaṃ tryakṣaramityāhuḥ pratiṣṭhā caturakṣarā ।। supratiṣṭhā bhavet pañca gāyatrī ṣaḍ bhavediha । saptākṣarā bhaveduṣṇigaṣṭākṣarānuṣṭubucyate ।। navākṣarā tu bṛhatī paṅktiścaiva daśākṣarā ।
ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub jagatī dvādaśākṣarā ।। trayodaśā'tijagatī śakvarī tu caturdaśā । atiśakvarī pañcadaśā ṣoḍaśāṣṭiḥ prakīrtitā ।। atyaṣṭiḥ syātsaptadaśā dhṛtiraṣṭādaśākṣarā ।
ekonaviṃśatirdhṛtiḥ kṛtirviṃśatireva ca ।। prakṛtiścaikaviṃśatyā dvāviṃśatyākṛtistathā । vikṛtiḥ syāt trayoviṃśā caturviṃśā ca saṃkṛtiḥ ।। pañcaviṃśatyatikṛtiḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyutkṛtirbhavet ।
ato adhikākṣaraṃ chando mālāvṛttaṃ tadiṣyate ।। chandasāṃ tu tathā hyete bhedāḥ prastārayogataḥ । asaṃkhyeyapramāṇāni vṛttānyāhurato budhāḥ ।। gāyatrīprabhṛtittveṣāṃ pramāṇaṃ saṃvidhīyate ।
prayogajāni sarvāṇi prāyaśo na bhavanti hi ।। vṛttāni ca catuṣṣaṣṭirgāyatryāṃ kīrtitāni tu । śataṃ viṃśatiraṣṭau ca vṛttānyuṣṇihyathocyate ।। ṣaṭpañcāśacchate dve ca vṛttānāmapyanuṣṭubhi ।
śatāni pañca vṛtānāṃ bṛhatyāṃ dvādaśaiva ca ।। paṅktyāṃ sahasraṃ vṛttānāṃ caturviṃśatireva ca । traiṣṭubhe dve sahasre ca catvāriṃśattathāṣṭa ca ।। sahasrāṇyapi catvāri navatiśca ṣaḍuttarā ।
jagatyāṃ samavarṇānāṃ vṛttānāmiha sarvaśaḥ ।। aṣṭau sahasrāṇi śataṃ dvyadhikā navatiḥ punaḥ । jagatyāmatipūrvāyāṃ vṛttānāṃ parimāṇataḥ ।। śatāni trīṇyaśītiśca sahasrāṇyapi ṣoḍaśa ।
vṛttāni caiva catvāri śakvaryāḥ parisaṃkhyayā ।। dvātriṃśacca sahasrāṇi sapta caiva śatāni ca । aṣṭau ṣaṣṭiśca vṛttāni hyāśrayantyatiśakvarīm ।। pañcaṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi sahasrārdhañca saṃkhyayā ।
ṣaṭtriṃśaccaiva vṛttāni hyaṣṭyāṃ nigaditāni ca ।। ekatriṃśatsahasrāṇi vṛttānāñca dvisaptatiḥ । tathā śatasahasrañca chandāṃsyatyaṣṭisaṃjñite ।। dhṛtyāmapi hi piṇḍena vṛttānyākalpitāni tu ।
tajjñaiḥ śatasahasre dve śatamekaṃ tathaiva ca ।। dviṣaṣṭiśca sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśacca yogataḥ । catvāri caiva vṛttāni samasaṃkhyāśrayāṇi tu ।। atidhṛtyāṃ sahasrāṇi caturviṃśatireva ca ।
tathā śatasahasrāṇi pañca vṛttaśatadvayam ।। aṣṭāśītiśca vṛttāni vṛttajñaiḥ kathitāni ca । kṛtau śatasahasrāṇi daśa proktāni saṃkhyayā ।। catvāriṃśattathā cāṣṭau sahasrāṇi śatāni ca ।
pañcaṣaṭsaptatiścaiva vṛttānāṃ parimāṇataḥ ।। tathā śatasahasrāṇāṃ prakṛtau viṃśatirbhavet । sapta vai gaditāstvatra navatiścaiva saṃkhyayā ।। sahasrāṇi śataṃ caikaṃ dvipañcāśattathaiva ca ।
vṛttāni parimāṇena vṛttajñairgaditāni tu ।। catvāriṃśattathaikañca lakṣāṇāmatha saṃkhyayā । tathā ceha sahasrāṇi navatiścaturuttarā ।। śatatrayaṃ samākhyātaṃ hyākṛtyāṃ caturuttaram ।
jñeyā śatasahasrāṇāmaśītistryadhikā budhaiḥ ।। aṣṭāśīti sahasrāṇi vṛttānāṃ ṣaṭ śatāni ca । aṣṭau caiva tu vṛttāni vikṛtyāṃ gaditāni tu ।। tathā śatasahasrāṇi saptaṣaṣṭiśca saptatiḥ ।
sapta caiva sahasrāṇi ṣoḍaśe dve śate tathā ।। koṭiścaiveha vṛttāni saṃkṛtau kathitāni vai । koṭitrayañcābhikṛtyāṃ pañcatriṃśadbhiranvitam ।। pañcāśadbhiḥ sahasraiśca caturbhiradhikaistathā ।
catuṣṭayaṃ śatānām ca dvātriṃśadbhiḥ samanvitam ।। ṣaṭ koṭayastathotkṛtyāṃ lakṣāṇāmekasaptatiḥ । catuṣṣaṣṭiśatānyaṣṭau sahasrāṇyaṣṭa caiva hi ।। uktādutkṛtiparyantavṛttasaṃkhyāṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
etena ca vikalpena vṛtteṣveteṣu nirdiśet ।। sarveṣāṃ chandasāmevaṃ vṛttāni kathitāni vai । tisraḥ koṭayo daśa tathā sahasrāṇāṃ śatāni tu ।। catvāriṃśattathā dve ca sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu ।
saptabhiḥ sahitānyeva sapta caiva śatāni ca ।। ṣaḍviṃśatirihānyāni vyākhyātāni samāsataḥ । samāni gaṇanāyuktimāśritya kathitāni vai ।। sarveṣāṃ chandasāmevaṃ trikairvṛttaṃ prayojayet ।
jñeyāścāṣṭau trikāstatra saṃjñābhiḥ sthānamaccharam ।। trīṇyakṣarāṇi vijñeyastriko aṃśaḥ parikalpitaḥ । gurulaghvakṣarakṛtaḥ sarvavṛtteṣu nityaśaḥ ।। gurupūrvo bhakāraḥ syānmakāre tu gurutrayam ।
jakāro gurumadhyasthaḥ sakāro antyagurustathā ।। laghumadhyasthito rephastakāro antyalaghuḥ paraḥ । laghupūrvo yakārastu nakāre tu laghutrayam ।। ete hyaṣṭau trikāḥ prājñairvijñeyā brahmasambhavāḥ ।
lāghavārthaṃ punaramī chandojñānamavekṣya ca ।। ebhirvinirgatāścānyā jātayo atha samādayaḥ । asvarāḥ sasvarāścaiva procyante vṛttalakṣaṇaiḥ ।। gurvekaṃ giti vijñeyaṃ tathā laghu liti smṛtam ।
niyataḥ padavicchedo yatirityabhidhīyate ।। guru dīrghaṃ plutañcaiva saṃyogaparameva ca । sānusvāravisargaṃ ca tathāntyañca laghu kvacit ।। gāyatryāṃ dvau trikau jñeyau uṣṇik caikādhikākṣarā ।
anuṣṭup dvyadhikā caiva bṛhatyāṃ ca trikāstrayaḥ ।। ekākṣarādhikā paṅktistriṣṭup ca dvyadhikākṣarā । catustrikā tu jagatī saikātijagatī punaḥ ।। śakvarī dvyadhikā pañcatrikā jñeyātiśakvarī ।
ekādhikākṣarāṣṭiśca dvyadhikātyaṣṭirucyate ।। ṣaṭtrikāstu dhṛtiḥ proktā saikā cātidhṛtistathā । kṛtiśca dvyadhikā proktā prakṛtyāṃ sapta vai trikāḥ ।। ākṛtistvadhikaikena dvyadhikā vikṛtistathā ।
aṣṭatrikāḥ saṃkṛtau syāt saikā cābhikṛtiḥ punaḥ ।। utkṛtirdvyadhikā caiva vijñeyā gaṇamānataḥ । gurvekaṃ ga iti proktaṃ guruṇī gāviti smṛtau । laghvekaṃ la iti jñeyaṃ laghunī lāviti smṛtau ।।
saṃpadvirāmapādāśca daivatasthānamakṣaram । varṇaḥ svaro vidhirvṛttamiti chandogato vidhiḥ ।। naivātiriktaṃ hīnaṃ vā yatra saṃpadyate kramaḥ । vidhāne cchandasāmeṣa saṃpadityabhisaṃjñitaḥ ।।
yatrārthasya samāptiḥ syāt sa virāma iti smṛtaḥ । pādaśca padyaterdhātoścaturbhāga iti smṛtaḥ ।। agnyādidaivataṃ proktaṃ sthānaṃ dvividhamucyate । śarīrāśrayasaṃbhūtaṃ digāśrayamathāpi ca ।।
śārīraṃ mantrasaṃbhūtaṃ chando gāyatrasaṃjñitam । kruṣṭe madhyaṃ dinaṃ proktaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ parikīrtyate ।। tṛtīyasavanañcāpi śīrṣaṇyaṃ jāgataṃ hi yat । hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutañcaiva trividhañcākṣaraṃ smṛtam ।।
śvetādayastathā varṇā vijñeyāśchandasāmiha । tāraścaiva hi mandraśca madhyamastrividhaḥ svaraḥ ।। dhruvāvidhāne caivāsya saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam । vidhirgaṇakṛtaścaiva tathaivārthakṛto bhavet ।।
chandato yasya pāde syāddhīnaṃ vā'dhikameva vā । akṣaraṃ nicṛditi proktaṃ bhūrik ceti dvijottamāḥ ।। akṣarābhyāṃ sadā dvābhyāmadhikaṃ hīnameva vā । tacchando nāmato jñeyaṃ svarāḍiti virāḍapi ।।
sarveṣāmeva vṛttānāṃ tajjñairjñeyā gaṇāstrayaḥ । divyo divyetaraścaiva divyamānuṣa eva ca ।। gāyatryuṣṇiganuṣṭup ca bṛhatī paṅktireva ca । triṣṭup ca jagatī caiva divyo ayaṃ prathamo gaṇaḥ ।।
tathātijagatī caiva śakvarī cātiśakvarī । aṣṭiratyaṣṭirapi ca dhṛtiścātidhṛtirgaṇaḥ ।। kṛtiśca prakṛtiścaiva hyākṛtirvikṛtistathā । saṃkṛtyabhikṛtī caiva utkṛtirdivyamānuṣā ।।
eteṣāṃ chandasāṃ bhūyaḥ prastāravidhisaṃśrayam । lakṣaṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi naṣṭamuddiṣṭameva ca ।। prastāro akṣaranirdiṣṭo mātroktaśca tathaiva hi । dvikau glāviti varṇoktau miśrau cetyapi mātrikau ।।
guroradhastādādyasya prastāre laghu vinyaset । agratastu samādeyā guravaḥ pṛṣṭhatastathā ।। prathamaṃ gurubhirvarṇairlaghubhistvavasānajam । vṛttantu sarvachandassu prastāravidhireva tu ।।
gurvadhastāllaghuṃ nyasya tathā dvidvi yathoditam । nyasyet prastāramārgo ayamakṣaroktastu nityaśaḥ ।। mātrāsaṃkhyāvinirdiṣṭo gaṇo mātrāvikalpitaḥ । miśrau glāviti vijñeyau pṛthak lakṣyavibhāgataḥ ।।
mātrāgaṇo guruścaiva laghunī caiva lakṣite । āryāṇāṃ tu caturmātrāprastāraḥ parikalpitaḥ ।। gītakaprabhṛtīnāntu pañcamātro gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ । vaitālīyaṃ puraskṛtya ṣaṇmātrādyāstathaiva ca ।।
tryakṣarāstu trikā jñeyā laghugurvakṣarānvitāḥ । mātrāgaṇavibhāgastu gurulaghvakṣarāśrayaḥ ।। antyād dviguṇitādrūpād dvidvirekaṃ gurorbhavet । dviguṇāñca laghoḥ kṛtvā saṃkhyāṃ piṇḍena yojayet ।।
ādyaṃ sarvaguru jñeyaṃ vṛttantu samasaṃjñitam । kośaṃ tu sarvalaghvantyaṃ miśrarūpāṇi sarvataḥ ।। vṛttānāṃ tu samānānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ saṃyojya tāvatīm । rāśyūnāmardhaviṣamāṃ samāsādabhinirdiśet ।।
ekādikāṃ tathā saṃkhyāṃ chandaso viniveśya tu । yāvat pūrṇantu pūrveṇa pūrayeduttaraṃ gaṇam ।। samānāṃ viṣamāṇāṃ ca saṃguṇayya tathā sphuṭam । rāśyūnāmabhijānīyādviṣamāṇāṃ samāsataḥ ।।
evaṃ kṛtvā tu sarveṣāṃ pareṣāṃ pūrvapūraṇam । kramānnaidhanamekaikaṃ pratilomaṃ visarjayet ।। sarveṣāṃ chandasāmevaṃ laghvakṣaraviniścayam । jānīta samavṛttānāṃ saṃkhyāṃ saṃkṣepatastathā ।।
vṛttasya parimāṇantu chitvārdhena yathākramam । nyasellaghu yathā saikamakṣaraṃ guru cāpyatha ।। evaṃ vinyasya vṛttānāṃ naṣṭoddiṣṭavibhāgataḥ । gurulaghvakṣarāṇīha sarvachandassu darśayet ।।
iti chandāṃsi yānīha mayoktāni dvijottamāḥ । vṛttānyeteṣu nāṭye asmin prayojyāni nibodhata ।। chandāṃsyevaṃ hi yānīha mayoktāni dvijottamāḥ । vṛttāni teṣu nāṭye asmin prayojyāni nibodhata ।।
ādye punarantye dve dve guruṇī cet । sā syāttanumadhyā gāyatrasamutthā ।। saṃtyaktavibhūṣā bhraṣṭāñjananetrā । hastārpitagaṇḍā kiṃ tvaṃ tanumadhyā ।।
laghugaṇa ādau bhavati catuṣkaḥ । guruyugamantye makarakaśīrṣā ।। svayamupayāntaṃ bhajasi na kāntam । bhayakari kiṃ tvaṃ makarakaśīrṣā ।।
ekamātraṃ ṣaṭke syād dvitīyaṃ pāde । khyātarūpā vṛtte sā mālinī nāmnā ।। ṣaḍakṣarakṛte pāde laghu yatra dvitīyakam । śeṣāṇi tu gurūṇi syurmālinī sā matā yathā ।।
snānagandhādhikyairvastrabhūṣāyogaiḥ । vyaktamevāsau tvaṃ mālinī prakhyātā ।। dvitīyaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva laghu yatra pratiṣṭhitam । śeṣāṇi ca gurūṇi syurmālatī nāma sā yathā ।।
śobhate baddhayā ṣaṭpadāviddhayā । mālatīmālayā māninī līlayā ।। dvitīyaṃ ca caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ca yadā laghu । yasyāḥ saptākṣare pāde jñeyā sā tūddhatā yathā ।।
sau trikau yadi pāde hyantimaśca gakāraḥ । uṣṇigutthitapādā uddhatā khalu nāmnā ।। dantakṛntakṛtāstraṃ vyākulālakaśobham । śaṃsatīva tavāsyaṃ nirdayaṃ ratayuddham ।।
ādau dve nidhane caiva guruṇī yatra vai sadā । pāde saptākṣare jñeyā nāmnā bhramaramālikā ।। pāde pāde niviṣṭau samyagviracitau tsau । antye yadi gakāraḥ sā tu bhramaramālā ।।
nānākusumacitre prāpte surabhimāse । eṣā bhramati mattā kānte bhramaramālā ।। ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca pañcamaṃ saptamaṃ tathā । gurūṇyaṣṭākṣare pāde siṃhalekheti sā yathā ।।
jātu yasya gau na, pāde saṃsthitaḥ samasvarūpe । tāmanuṣṭubāśrayasthāṃ vāvadanti siṃhalekhām ।। yattvayā hyanekabhāvaiśceṣṭitaṃ rahaḥ sugātri । tanmano mama praviṣṭaṃ vṛttamadya siṃhalekham ।।
caturthaṃ ca dvitīyaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhamaṣṭamameva ca । gurūṇyaṣṭākṣare pāde yatra tanmattaceṣṭitam ।। yadā tu jātparau ralau gakāra eva ca sthitaḥ । anuṣṭubudbhavaṃ tadā vadanti mattaceṣṭitam ।।
carāvaghūrṇitekṣaṇaṃ vilambitākulālakam । asaṃsthitaiḥ padaiḥ priyā karoti mattaceṣṭitam ।। aṣṭākṣarakṛte pāde sarvāṇyeva bhavanti hi । gurūṇi yasminsā nāmnā vidyunmāleti kīrtitā ।।
mau gau cāntyau yasyāḥ pāde pādasyānte vicchedaśca । sā cānuṣṭupchandasyuktā nityaṃ sadbhirvidyunmālā ।। sāmbhobhārairānānadbhiḥ śyāmāmbhodairvyāpte vyomni । ādityāṃśuspardhinyeṣā dikṣu bhrāntā vidyunmālā ।।
pañcamaṃ saptamaṃ cāntyaṃ guru pāde aṣṭake tathā । chandojñairjñeyametattu vṛttaṃ cittavilāsitam ।। smitavaśaviprakāśairdaśanapadairamībhiḥ । varatanu pūrṇacandraṃ tava mukhamāvṛṇoti ।।
navākṣarakṛte pāde trīṇi syurnaidhanāni ca । gurūṇi yasyāḥ sā nāmnā jñeyā madhukarī yathā ।। ṣaḍiha yadi laghūni syurnidhanagatamakāraścet । budhajanabṛhatīsaṃsthā bhavati madhukarī nāmnā ।।
kusumitamabhipaśyantī vividhatarugaṇaiśchannam । vanamatiśayagandhāḍhyaṃ bhramati madhukarī hṛṣṭā ।। daśākṣarakṛte pāde trīṇyādau trīṇi naidhane । yasyā gurūṇi sā jñeyā paṅktirutpalamālikā ।।
trīṇyādau yadi hi gurūṇi syuścatvāro yadi laghavo madhye । paṅktāvantagatamakāraḥ syādvijñeyā kuvalayamālākhyā ।। asmiṃste śirasi tadā kānte vaiḍūryasphaṭikasuvarṇāḍhye । śobhāṃ svāṃ na vahati tāṃ baddhā suśliṣṭā kuvalayamāleyam ।।
dvitīyaṃ ca caturthaṃ ca ṣaṣṭamaṣṭamameva ca । hrasvaṃ daśākṣare pāde yatra sā śikhisāriṇī ।। jau trikau hi pādagau tu yasya gau ca saṃśritau tathā samau stau । paṅktiyogasupratiṣṭhitāṅgī sā mayūrasāriṇīti nāmnā ।।
naiva te asti saṃgamo manuṣyairnāpi kāmabhogacihnamanyat । garbhiṇīva dṛśyase hyanārye kiṃ mayūrasāriṇī tvamevam ।। ādyaṃ caturthamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ daśamaṃ tathā । gurūṇi traiṣṭubhe pāde yatra syurdodhakaṃ tu tat ।।
bhau tu bhagāviti yasya gaṇāḥ syuḥ syācca yatistricaturbhirathā'smin । traiṣṭubhameva hi tatkhalu nāmnā dodhakavṛttamiti pravadanti ।। praskhalitāprapadapravicāyaṃ mattavighūrṇitagātravilāsam । paśya vilāsini kuñjarametaṃ dodhakavṛttamayaṃ prakaroti ।।
ādau dvau pañcamaṃ caivāpyaṣṭamaṃ naidhanaṃ tathā । guruṇyekādaśe pāde yatra tanmoṭakaṃ yathā ।। eṣo ambudatulyanisvanaravaḥ kṣīvaḥ skhalamānavilambagatiḥ । śrutvā ghanagarjitamadritaṭe vṛkṣān pratimoṭayati dviradaḥ ।।
navamaṃ saptamaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ tṛtīyaṃ ca bhavellaghu । sarvāsvavasthāsu ca kāmatantre yogyāsi kiṃ vā bahunendravajrā ।। ebhireva tu saṃyuktā laghubhistraiṣṭubhī yadā । upendravajrā vijñeyā laghvādāviha kevalam ।।
priye śriyā varṇaviśeṣaṇena smitena kāntyā sukumārabhāvaiḥ । amī guṇā rūpaguṇānurūpā bhavanti te kiṃ tvamupendravajrā ।। ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ navamaṃ tathā । gurūṇyekādaśe pāde yatra sā tu rathoddhatā ।।
kiṃ tvayā subhaṭa dūravarjitaṃ nātmano na suhṛdāṃ priyaṃ kṛtam । yatpalāyanaparāyaṇasya te yāti dhūliradhunā rathoddhatā ।। kiṃ tvayā kumatisaṅgayā sadā nājñayeva suhṛdāṃ priyaṃ kṛtam । yad gṛhādvacanaroṣakampitā yāti tūrṇamabalā rathoddhatā ।।
ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca saptamaṃ daśamaṃ guru । yasyāstu traiṣṭubhe pāde vijñeyā svāgatā hi sā ।। adya me saphalamāyatanetre jīvitaṃ madanasaṃśrayabhāvam । āgatāsi bhavanaṃ mama yasmātsvāgataṃ tava varoru niṣīda ।।
ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca navamaṃ caiva laghunī traiṣṭubhe yadi । gurūṇyanyāni pāde tu sā jñeyā śālinī yathā ।। duḥśīlaṃ vā nirguṇaṃ vāparaṃ vā loke dhairyādapriyaṃ na bravīṣi । tasmācchīlaṃ sādhuhetoḥ suvṛttaṃ mādhuryātsyātsarvathā śālinī tvam ।।
tṛtīyaṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca navamaṃ dvādaśaṃ tathā । gurūṇi jāgate pāde yatra tattoṭakaṃ bhavet ।। yadi so atra bhavettu samudrasamastriṣu cāpi tathā niyamena yatiḥ । satataṃ jagatīvihitaṃ hi tataṃ gaditaṃ khalu toṭakavṛttamidam ।।
kimidaṃ kapaṭāśrayadurviṣahaṃ bahuśāṭhyamatholbaṇarūkṣakatham । svajanapriyasajjanabhedakaraṃ nanu toṭakavṛttamidaṃ kuruṣe ।। ādyaṃ tṛtīyamantyaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭhameva ca । tathopāntyaṃ jagatyāṃ ca guru cetkumudaprabhā ।।
yau trikau tathā nyau yadi khalu pāde ṣaḍbhireva varṇairyadi ca yatiḥ syāt । nityasaṃniviṣṭā jagatividhāne nāmataḥ prasiddhā kumudanibhā sā ।। manmathena viddhā salalitabhāvā nṛttagītayogā pravikasitākṣī । nindyamadya kiṃ tvaṃ vigalitaśobhā candrapādayuktā kumudavatī ca ।।
yadi khalu pāde nyau trikau yathā yau yatirapi varṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhireva cetsyāt । jagatividhāne nityasaṃniviṣṭā kumudanibhā sā nāmataḥ prasiddhā ।। kumudanibhā tvaṃ kāmabāṇaviddhā kimasi natabhrūḥ śītavātadagdhā । mṛdunalinīvāpāṇḍuvaktraśobhā kathamapi jātā hyagrataḥ sakhīnām ।।
dvādaśākṣarake pāde saptamaṃ daśamaṃ laghu । ādau pañcākṣaracchedaścandralekhā tu sā yathā ।। vaktraṃ saumyaṃ te padmapatrāyatākṣaṃ kāmasyāvāsaṃ sunāsoccaprahāsam । kāmasyāpīdaṃ kāmamāhartukāmaṃ kānte kāntyā tvaṃ candralekheva bhāsi ।।
tṛtīyamantyaṃ navamaṃ pañcamaṃ ca yadā guru । dvādaśākṣarake pāde yatra sā pramitākṣarā ।। smitabhāṣiṇī hyacapalāparuṣā nibhṛtāpavādavimukhī satatam । api kasyacidyuvatirasti sukhā pramitākṣarā sa hi pumāñjayati ।।
dvitīyamantyaṃ daśamaṃ caturthaṃ pañcamāṣṭame । gurūṇi dvādaśe pāde vaṃśasthā jagatī tu sā ।। yadi trikau jtau bhavatastu pādatastathaiva ca jrāvavasānasaṃsthitau । tadā hi vṛttaṃ jagatīpratiṣṭhitaṃ vadanti vaṃśasthamitīha nāmataḥ ।।
na me priyā tvaṃ bahumānavarjitāṃ priyaṃ priyā te paruṣābhibhāṣiṇī । tathā ca paśyāmyahamadya vigrahaṃ dhruvaṃ hi vaṃśasthagatiṃ kariṣyati ।। caturthamantyaṃ daśamaṃ saptamaṃ ca yadā guru । bhaveddhi jāgate pāde tadā syāddhariṇaplutā ।।
paruṣavākyakaśābhihitā tvayā bhayavilokanapārśvanirīkṣaṇā । varatanuḥ pratataplutasarpaṇairanukaroti gatairhariṇaplutam ।। saptamaṃ navamaṃ cāntyamupāntyaṃ ca yadā guru । dvādaśākṣarake pāde kāmadatteti sā yathā ।।
karajapadavibhūṣitā yathā tvaṃ sudati daśanavikṣatādharā ca । gatirapi caraṇāvalagnamandā tvamasi mṛganibhākṣi kāmadattā ।। ādyaṃ caturthaṃ daśamaṃ saptamaṃ ca yadā laghu । pāde tu jāgate yasyā aprameyā tu sā yathā ।।
na te kācidanyā samā dṛśyate strī nṛloke viśiṣṭā guṇairadvitīyaiḥ । trilokyāṃ guṇajjñān samāhṛtya sarvān jagatyaprameyāsi sṛṣṭā vidhātrā ।। dvitīyaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva hyaṣṭamekādaśe yathā । pāde yatra laghūni syuḥ padminī nāma sā yathā ।।
rāstrikāḥ sāgarākhyā niviṣṭā yadā syāt trike ca trike yuktarūpā yatiḥ । sanniviṣṭā jagatyāstatassā budhair nāmataścāpi saṃkīrtyate padminī ।। dehatoyāśayā vaktrapadmojjvalā netrabhṛṅgākulā dantahaṃsasmitā । keśapāśacchadā cakravākastanī padminīva priye bhāsi me sarvadā ।।
phullapadmānanā tvaṃ dvirephekṣaṇā keśapatracchadā cakravākastanī । pītatoyāvalī baddhakāñcīguṇā padminīva priye bhāsi nīre sthitā ।। ādau ṣaṭ daśamaṃ caiva pāde yatra laghūnyatha । śeṣāṇi tu gurūṇi syurjāgate puṭasaṃjñitā ।।
yadi caraṇaniviṣṭau nau tathā myau yatividhirapi yuktyāṣṭābhiriṣṭaḥ । bhavati ca jagatīsthaḥ sarvadāsau ya iha hi puṭavṛttaṃ nāmatastu ।। upavanasalilānāṃ bālapadmairbhramaraparabhṛtānāṃ kaṇṭhanādaiḥ । madanamadavilāsaiḥ kāminīnāṃ kathayati puṭavṛttaṃ puṣpamāsaḥ ।।
dvitīyāntye caturthaṃ ca navamaikādaśe guru । vicchedo atijagatyāṃ tu caturbhiḥ sā prabhāvatī ।। kathaṃ nvidaṃ kamalaviśālalocane gṛhaṃ dhanaiḥ pihitakare divākare । acintayantyabhinavavarṣavidyutastvamāgatā sutanu yathā prabhāvatī ।।
trīṇyādāvaṣṭamaṃ caiva daśamaṃ naidhanadvayam । gurūṇyatijagatyāṃ tu tribhiśchedaiḥ praharṣiṇī ।। bhāvasthairmadhurakathaiḥ subhāṣitaistvaṃ sāṭopaskhalitavilambitairgataiśca । śobhāḍhyairharasi manāṃsi kāmukānāṃ suvyaktaṃ hyatijagatī praharṣiṇī ca ।।
ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ caiva daśamaikādaśe laghu । trayodaśākṣare pāde jñeyaṃ mattamayūrakam ।। vidyunnaddhāḥ sendradhanurañjitadehā vātoddhūtāḥ śvetavalākākṛtaśobhāḥ । ete meghā garjitanādojjvalacihnāḥ prāvṛṭkālaṃ mattamayūrāḥ kathayanti ।।
ādau dve caturthaṃ caiva cāṣṭamaikādaśe guru । antyopāntye ca śakvaryā vasantatilakā yathā ।। citrairvasantakusumaiḥ kṛtakeśahastā sragdāmamālyaracanā suvibhūṣitāṅgī । nānāvasantakavibhūṣitakarṇapāśā sākṣādvasantatilakeva vibhāti nārī ।।
pañcādau śakvarī pāde gurūṇi trīṇi naidhane । pañcākṣarādau ca yatirasaṃbādhā tu sā yathā ।। mānālokajñaḥ sutabalakulaśīlāḍhyo yasminsammānaṃ na sadṛśamanu paśyeddhi । gacchettaṃ tyaktvā drutagatiraparaṃ deśaṃ kīrṇā nānārthairavaniriyamasaṃbādhā ।।
catvāryādau gurūṇi syurdaśamaikādaśe tathā । antyopāntye ca śakvaryāḥ pāde tu śarabhā yathā ।। eṣā kāntā vrajati lalitā vepamānā gulmaiścchannaṃ vanamabhinavaiḥ saṃpraviddham । hā hā kaṣṭaṃ kimidamiti no vedmi mūḍho vyaktaṃ kānte śarabhalalitāntvaṃ karoṣi ।।
adau ṣaṭ daśamaṃ caiva laghu caiva trayodaśam । yatrātiśakvare pāde jñeyā nāndīmukhī tu sā ।। na khalu tava kadācitkrodhatāmrāyatākṣaṃ bhrukuṭivalitabhaṅgaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ mayāsyam । kimiha bahubhiruktairyā mamecchā hṛdisthā tvamasi madhuravākyā devi nāndīmukhīva ।।
