ādyaṃ caturthaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca naidhanaṃ ca yadā guru । ṣoḍaśākṣarake pāde yatrebhalalitaṃ tu tat ।। bhrau yadi nāśca nityamiha viracitacaraṇaḥ gaśca tathā vai bhavati nidhanamupagataḥ । syādapi cāṣṭimeva yadi satatamanugataṃ tatkhalu vṛttamagravṛṣabhagajavilasitam ।।
kālatoyadharaiḥ sudhīradhanapaṭupaṭaharavaiḥ sarjakadambanīpakuṭajakusumasurabhiḥ । kandalasendragopakaracitamavanitalaṃ vīkṣya karotyasau vṛṣabhagajavilasitam ।। ādyātparāṇi vai pañca dvādaśaṃ satrayodaśaḥ । antyopāntye ca dīrghāṇi lalitapravaraṃ hi tat ।।
yadā ymau pādasthau bhavata iha cetstau tathā gau tathā ṣaḍbhiścānyairyatirapi ca varṇairyathā syāt । tadapyaṣṭau nityaṃ samanugatamevoktamanyaiḥ prayogajñairvṛttaṃ pravaralalitaṃ nāmatastu ।। nakhālīḍhaṃ gātraṃ daśanakhacitaṃ coṣṭhagaṇḍaṃ śiraḥ puṣponmiśraṃ pravilulitakeśālakāntam । gatiḥ khinnā ceyaṃ vadanamapi saṃbhrāntanetram aho ślāghyaṃ vṛttaṃ pravaralalitaṃ kāmaceṣṭam ।।
ādyātparāṇi pañcātha dvādaśaṃ satrayodaśam । antyaṃ saptadaśe pāde śikhariṇyāṃ gurūṇi ca ।। caturbhistasyaiva pravaralalitasya trikagaṇair yadā lau gaścānte bhavati caraṇe atyaṣṭigadite । yadā ṣaḍbhiścchedo bhavati yadi mārgeṇa vihitas tadā vṛtteṣveṣā khalu śikhariṇī nāma gaditā ।।
mahānadyā bhogaṃ pulinamiva bhāti te jaghanaṃ tathāsyaṃ netrāḍhyaṃ bhramarasahitaṃ paṅkajamiva । gatirmandā ceyaṃ sutanu tava ceṣṭā sulalitā stanābhyāṃ tābhyāṃ tvaṃ śikhariṇi supīnāsi vanite ।। yatra pañca laghūnyādau trayodaśacaturdaśe । ṣoḍaśaikādaśe caiva tatsyādvṛṣabhaceṣṭitam ।।
yadi hi caraṇe nsau slau gaḥ kramādviniveśitār yadi khalu yatiḥ ṣaḍbhirvarṇairstathā daśabhiḥ punaḥ । yadi vihitaṃ syādatyaṣṭiḥ prayogasukhāśrayaṃ vṛṣabhalalitaṃ vṛttaṃ jñeyaṃ tathā hariṇīti vā ।। jaladhararavaṃ śrutvā śrutvā madocchrayadarpito vilikhitamahīśṛṅgākṣepairvṛṣaiḥ pratinardya ca । svayuvativṛto goṣṭhādgoṣṭhaṃ prayāti ca nirbhayo vṛṣabhalalitaṃ citraṃ vṛttaṃ karoti ca śādvale ।।
catvāryādau ca daśamaṃ guru yatra trayodaśaṃ caturdaśaṃ tathāntye dve caikādaśamathāpi ca ।। yadā saptadaśe pāde śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha । bhavanti yasminsā jñeyā śrīdharī nāmato yathā ।। mo bhnau ca syuścaraṇaracitāstau gurū ca praviṣṭāśchedaḥ śiṣṭo yadi ca daśabhiḥ syāttathānyaiścaturbhiḥ ।
atyaṣṭau ca pratiniyamitā varṇataḥ spaṣṭarūpā sā vijñeyā dvijamunigaṇaiḥ śrīdharī nāmatastu ।। snānaiścūrṇaiḥ sukhasurabhibhirgandhavāsaiśca dhūpaiḥ puṣpaiścānyaiḥ śirasi racitairvastrayogaiśca taistaiḥ । nānāratnaiḥ kanakakhacitairaṅgasaṃbhogasaṃsthairvyaktaṃ kānte kamalanilayā śrīdharīvātibhāsi ।। ādyaṃ caturthaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca daśamaṃ naidhanaṃ guru ।
tadvaṃśapatrapatitaṃ daśabhiḥ saptabhiryatiḥ ।। yathā eṣa gajo adrimastakataṭe kalabhaparivṛtaḥ krīḍati vṛkṣagulmagahane kusumabhiranate । megharavaṃ niśamya muditaḥ pavanajavasamaḥ sundari vaṃśapatrapatitaṃ punarapi kurute ।। dvitīyamantyaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāpyaṣṭamaṃ dvādaśaṃ tathā ।
caturdaśaṃ pañcadaśaṃ pāde saptadaśākṣare ।। bhavanti yatra dīrghāṇi śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha । vilambitagatiḥ sā tu vijñeyā nāmato yathā ।। yadā dviruditau hi pādamabhisaṃśritau jsau trikau tathaiva ca punastayornidhanamāśritau yau lagau ।
tadaṣṭiratipūrvikā yatirapi svabhāvādyathā vilambitagatistadā nigaditā dvijairnāmataḥ ।। vighūrṇitavilocanā pṛthuvikīrṇahārā punaḥ pralambaraśanā calatskhalitapādamandaklamā । na me priyamidaṃ janasya bahumānarāgeṇa yanmadena vivaśā vilambitagatiḥ kṛtā tvaṃ priye ।। pañcādau pañcadaśakaṃ dvādaśaikādaśe guru ।
caturdaśaṃ tathāntye dve citralekhā dhṛtau smṛtā ।। yathā nānāratnāḍhyairbahubhiradhikaṃ bhūṣaṇairaṅgasaṃsthairnānā gandhāḍhyairmadanajanakairaṅgarāgairvicitraiḥ । keśaiḥ snānāḍhyaiḥ kusumabharitairvastrarāgaiśca taistaiḥ kānte saṃkṣepāt kimiha bahunā citralekheva bhāsi ।। antyaṃ saptadaśaṃ caiva ṣoḍaśaṃ sacaturdaśam ।
trayodaśaṃ dvādaśaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhamaṣṭamameva ca ।। trīṇyādau ca gurūṇi syuryasmiṃstvekonaviṃśake । pāde laghūni śeṣāṇi śārdūlakrīḍitaṃ tu tat ।। msau jsau tau guru ca prayoganiyatā yasminniviṣṭāstrikā ādyā cāntyayatiścatustrikayutā jñeyā parā saptabhiḥ ।
nityaṃ yatpadamāśritā hyatidhṛtirnityaṃ kavīnāṃ priyaṃ tajjñeyaṃ khalu vṛttajātinipuṇaiḥ śārdūlavikrīḍitam ।। nānāśastraśataghnitomarahatāḥ prabhraṣṭasarvāyudhāḥ nirbhinnodarapādabāhuvadanā nirṇāśitāḥ śatravaḥ । dhairyotsāhaparākramaprabhṛtibhistaistairvicitrairguṇair vṛttaṃ te ripughāti bhāti samare śārdūlavikrīḍitam ।। tāvattvaṃ vijitendriyaḥ śubhamate sarvātmanā pratyahaṃ dāne śīlavidhau ca yojaya manaḥ svargāpavargāpaham ।
yāvad vyādhijarāpracaṇḍanakharo vyāyatsaṭābhirbhṛśaṃ mṛtyuste na karoti jīvitamṛgaiḥ śārdūlavikrīḍitam ।। catvāryādau ca ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ sacaturdaśam । tathā pañcadaśaṃ caiva ṣiḍaśaṃ naidhanaṃ tathā ।। etāni ca gurūṇi syuḥ śeṣāṇi tu laghūnyatha ।
pāde yatra kṛtau jñeyā nāmnā suvadanā tu sā ।। mrau mnau ybhau lgau ca samyagyadi ca viracitāḥ pāde kramavaśād vicchedaḥ saptabhiḥ syātpunarapi ca yatiḥ saptākṣarakṛtā । yadyeṣā saṃśritā syātkṛtimapi ca punaḥ śliṣṭākṣarapadā vidvadbhirvṛttajātau tata iha gaditā nāmnā suvadanā ।। netre līlālasānte kamaladalanibhe bhrūcāpavinate raktoṣṭhaṃ pīnamadhyaṃ samasahitaghanāḥ snigdhāśca daśanāḥ ।
karṇāvaṃsapralambau cibukamapi nataṃ ghoṇā surucirā vyaktaṃ tvaṃ martyaloke varatanu vihitāsyekā suvadanā ।। catvāryādau tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ saptamaṃ ca caturdaśam । aṣṭādaśaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā pañcadaśaṃ punaḥ ।। antyopāntye gurūṇyatra laghūnyanyāni sarvadā ।
ekaviṃśatike pāde sragdharā nāma sā yathā ।। mrau mnau yau yaśca samyagyadi hi viracitāḥ syustrikāḥ pādayoge varṇaiḥ pūrvopadiṣṭairyatirapi ca punaḥ saptabhiḥ saptabhiḥ syāt । vṛttaṃ samyagyadi syātprakṛtimanugataṃ tatvavidbhiḥ pradiṣṭaṃ vijñeyaṃ vṛttajātau kavijanadayitā sragdharā nāmatastu ।। cūtāśokāravindaiḥ kuravakatilakaiḥ karṇikāraiḥ śirīṣaiḥ punnāgaiḥ pārijātairvakulakuvalayaiḥ kiṃśukaiḥ sātimuktaiḥ ।
etairnānāprakāraiḥ bahulasurabhibhirviprakīrṇaiśca taistair vāsantaiḥ puṣpavṛndairnaravara vasudhā sragdharevādya bhāti ।। caturthamādyaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca daśamaṃ dvādaśaṃ tathā । ṣoḍaśāṣṭādaśe caiva naidhanaṃ ca gurūṇyatha ।। dvāviṃśatyakṣare pāde śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha ।
bhavanti yatra tajjñeyaṃ bhadrakaṃ nāmato yathā ।। bhrau caraṇe yadā viniyatau trikau kramavaśādathātikṛtividhau nrau ca tataḥ paraṃ ca rucirāvanantarakṛtau nagāvapi punaḥ । tacca daśāṣṭavarṇaracitā caturṣvapi tathā yatiśca satataṃ bhadrakavṛttameva khalu nāṭyayogakuśalairbudhairnigaditam ।। utplutamekahastacaraṇaṃ dvitīyakararecitaṃ vaṃśamṛdaṅgavādyamadhuraṃ vicitrakaraṇānugaṃ bahuvidham ।
bhadrakametadadya subhage vidagdhagaticeṣṭitaiḥ sulalitair nṛtyasi vibhramākulapadaṃ viviktarasabhāvitaṃ śaśimukhi ।। antyamekonaviṃśaṃ ca saptamaṃ satrayodaśam । ekādaśaṃ saptadaśaṃ pañcamaṃ ca gurūṇyatha ।। śeṣāṇi ca laghūni syurvikṛtyāścaraṇe budhaiḥ ।
vṛttaṃ tadaśvalalitaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāmato yathā ।। yadi ca nakāra ādiracitaḥ pade viracito anta eva lagau yadi ca nabhau tridhā ca nihitau krameṇa khalu madhyāvapi tathā । yadi ca samāśritaṃ hi vikṛtiṃ yatiśca daśabhistathaikasahitais tata iha kīrtitaṃ munigaṇairviśuddhacaritaistadaśvalalitam ।। vividhaturaṅganāgarathayodhasaṅkulamalaṃ balaṃ samuditaṃ śaraśataśaktikuntaparidhāsiyaṣṭivitataṃ bahupraharaṇam ।
ripuśatamuktaśastraravabhītaśaṅkitabhaṭaṃ bhayākuladiśaṃ kṛtamabhivīkṣya saṃyugamukhe samarpitaguṇaṃ tvayāśvalalitam ।। ṣaḍādāvaṣṭamaṃ caiva hyekādaśacaturdaśe । viṃśaṃ saptadaśaṃ caiva trayoviṃśaṃ tathaiva ca ।। etāni ca laghūni syuḥ śeṣāṇyatha gurūṇi ca ।
caturviṃśatike pāde meghamāleti sā yathā ।। yadi khalu caraṇasthitau nau trikau kṛtikāravyāstathā rāḥ syuḥ kramāt । bhavati yadi yatistathā saptabhiḥ saptabhistriṣvato anyā yatiḥ pañca vidyāttathā ।। pavanabalasamāhṛtā tīvragambhīranādā balākāvalīmekhalā kṣitidharasadṛśoccarūpā mahānīladhūmāñjanābhāmbugarbhodbhavā ।
surapatidhanurujjvalābaddhakakṣyā taḍiddyotasannāhapaṭṭījvalā gaganatalavisāriṇī prāvṛṣaṇyā dṛḍhaṃ meghamālādhikaṃ śobhate ।। ādyaṃ caiva caturthaṃ ca pañcamaṃ ṣaṣṭhameva ca । navamaṃ daśamaṃ caiva naidhanaṃ ca bhavedguru ।। laghūnyanyāni śeṣāṇi pāde syuḥ pañcaviṃśake ।
vṛttajjñaiḥ sā tu vijñeyā krauñcapādīti nāmataḥ ।। bhmau yadi pāde sbhāvapi ceṣṭāvabhikṛtirapi ca hi yadi khalu vihitā nāśca samudrāḥ syurviniviṣṭā yadi ca khalu guru bhavati nidhanagatam । pañcabhirādau chedamupetā punarapi yatiriha yadi khalu daśabhiḥ krauñcapadeyaṃ vṛttavidhāne suragaṇapitṛgaṇamunigaṇavihitā ।। yaḥ kila dākṣaṃ vidrutasomaṃ kratuvaramacamasamapagatakalaśaṃ pātitayūpaṃ kṣiptacaṣālaṃ vicayanamasamidhamapaśukacarukam ।
kārmukamuktenāśu cakāra vyapagatasuragaṇapitṛgaṇamiṣuṇā nityamasau te daityagaṇāriḥ pradahatu makhamiva ripugaṇamakhilam ।। yā kapilākṣī piṅgalakeśī kaliruciranudinamanunayakaṭhinā dīrghatarābhiḥ sthūlasirābhiḥ parivṛtavapuratiśayakuṭilagatiḥ । āyatajaṅghā nimnakapolā laghutarakucayugaparigatahṛdayā sā parihāryā krauñcapadā strī dhruvamiha niravadhisukhamabhilaṣatā ।। aṣṭāvādau gurūṇi syustathā caikonaviṃśakam ।
ekaviṃśaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ caturviṃśaṃ sanaidhanam ।। etāni guru saṃkhyāni śeṣāṇi ca laghūnyatha । ṣaḍviṃśatyakṣare pāde tadbhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam ।। yasyāṃ mau to nāḥ strau nityaṃ praticaraṇamatha gaditakāstrikā hyanupūrvaśaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyāmekonāyāṃ ca yadi hi khalu yatirabhidhā caturbhirathāṣṭābhiḥ । paścādantyau lgau saṃyojyau yadi bhavati
vikasanaparaṃ bhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam ।। yathā rūpopetāṃ devaiḥ sṛṣṭāṃ samadagaja vilasitagatiṃ nirīkṣya tilottamāṃ prādakṣiṇyātprāptāṃ draṣṭuṃ bahuvadana macalanayanaṃ śiraḥ kṛtavān hariḥ । dīrghaṃ niśvasyāntargūḍhaṃ stanavadana kanakavalayaṃ bhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam ।। daṇḍakaṃ nāma vijñeyamutkṛteradhikataram ।
meghamālādikaṃ tatsyānnau cādau kāguhā trikāḥ ।। dviradakaraviluptahintālatālīvanāstvāṃ namasyanti vindhyādayaḥ parvatāḥ । muditajalacarākulāḥ saṃprakīrṇamalāḥ kīrtayantīva kīrtiṃ mahānimnagāḥ ।। etāni samavṛttāni mayoktāni dvijottamāḥ ।
viṣamārdhasamānāṃ tu punarvakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। yatra pādāstu viṣamā nānāvṛttasamudbhavāḥ । grathitāḥ pādayogena tad vṛttaṃ viṣamaṃ smṛtam ।। dvau samaṃ dvau ca viṣamau vṛtte ardhaviṣame tathā ।
sarvapādaiśca viṣamairvṛttaṃ viṣamamucyate ।। hrasvādyamatha dīrghādyaṃ dīrghaṃ hrasvamathāpi vā । yugmojaviṣamaiḥ pādaiḥ vṛttamardhasamaṃ bhavet ।। pāde siddhe samaṃ siddhaṃ viṣamaṃ sārvapādikam ।
dvayorardhasamaṃ vidyādeṣa chedastu pādataḥ ।। chedāstu ye mayā proktā samavṛttavikalpitaḥ । trikairviṣamavṛttānāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। naidhane anyatarasyāṃ vai prathame pāda iṣyate ।
dvitīye caraṇe ca syādityanuṣṭup samāsataḥ ।। sau gau tu prathame pāde srau lgau cāpi dvitīyake । yugme ardhaviṣame pāde jñeyā pathyā tu sā trikaiḥ ।। priyadaivatamitrāsi priyasaṃbandhibāndhavā ।
priyadānaratā pathyā dayite tvaṃ priyāsi me ।। mrau gau tu prathame pāde ysau lgau ca dvitīyake । pāde bhau lgau tṛtīye ca caturthe tu tasau lagau ।। naivācāro na te mitraṃ na saṃbandhiguṇapriyā ।
sarvathā sarvaviṣamā pathyā na bhavasi priye ।। ayujorlakṣaṇaṃ hyetadviparītaṃ tu yatra ca । pathyā hi viparītā sā vijñeyā nāmato yathā ।। kṛtena ramaṇasya kiṃ sakhi roṣeṇa te apyartham ।
viparītā na pathyāsi tvaṃ jaḍe kena mohitā ।। caturthādakṣarādyatra trilaghu syādayuktataḥ । anuṣṭupcapalā sā tu vijñeyā nāmato yathā ।। na khalvasyāḥ priyatamaḥ śrotavyaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ sakhyā ।
nāradasya pratikṛtiḥ kathyate capalā hīyam ।। vipulā tu yuji jñeyā laghutvātsaptamasya tu । sarvatra saptamasyaiva keṣāṃcidvipulā yathā ।। saṃkṣiptā vajramadhye hi hemakumbhanibhastanī ।
vipulāsi priye śroṇyāṃ pūrṇacandranibhānane ।। gaṅgeva meghopagame āplāvitavasundharā । kūlavṛkṣānārujantī sravantī vipulā balāt ।। āgatā meghasamaye bhīru bhīrukulodgate ।
ekarātrau paragṛhaṃ corī bandhanamarhasi ।। evaṃ vividhayogāstu pathyāpādā bhavanti hi । yugmojaviṣamaiḥ pādaiḥ śeṣairanyaistrikairyathā ।। gurvantakaḥ sarvalaghustriko nityaṃ hi neṣyate ।
prathamādakṣarādyatra caturthātprāglaghuḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pathyāpādaṃ samāsthāpya trīṇyante tu gurūṇyatha । bhavanti pāde satataṃ budhaistadvakramiṣyate ।। dantakṣatādharaṃ subhru jāgaraglānanetraṃ ca ।
ratisaṃbhogakhinnaṃ te darśanīyataraṃ vaktram ।। ityeṣā sarvaviṣamā nāmato anuṣṭubucyate । tadvidāṃ matavaiṣamyaṃ trikādakṣaratastathā ।। pāde ṣoḍaśamātrāstu gāthāṃśakavikalpitāḥ ।
caturbhiraṃśakairjñeyā vṛttajñairvānavāsikā ।। asaṃsthitapadā suvihvalāṅgī madaskhalitaceṣṭitairmanojñā । kva yāsyasi varoru suratakāle viṣamā kiṃ vānavāsikā tvam ।। sjau sgau ca prathame pāde tathā caiva tṛtīyake ।
ketumatyāṃ gaṇāḥ proktāḥ bhrau ngau gaśca sadā budhaiḥ ।। sphuritādharaṃ cakitanetraṃ raktakapolamambujadalākṣam । kimidaṃ ruṣāpahṛtaśobhaṃ ketumatīsamaṃ vada mukhaṃ te ।। vaktrasyāparapūrvasya cādau nau ro lagau trikāḥ ।
najau rajau dvitīye ca śeṣāgraṃ punareva tu ।। prathame ca tṛtīye nau ralau gaśca prakīrtitaḥ । gaṇāścāparavaktre tu najau jrau dvicaturthayoḥ ।। sutanu jalaparītalocanaṃ jaladaniruddhamivendumaṇḍalam ।
kimidamaparavaktrameva te śaśivadane adya mukhaṃ parāṅmukham ।। nau yau tu prathame pāde njau jrau gaśca tathāpare । yatra tatpuṣpitāgrā syādyadi śeṣaṃ tu pūrvavat ।। pavanabalavidhūtacāruśākhaṃ pramuditakokilakaṇṭhanādaramyam ।
madhukaraparigīyamānaśabdaṃ varatanu paśya vanaṃ supuṣpitāgram ।। sjau slau cādau yathā nsau jgau bhnau jlau gaśca tathā punaḥ । sjau sjau gaśca trikā hyete udgatāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। tava romarājiratibhāti sutanu madanasya mañjarī ।
nābhikamalavivarotpatitā bhramarāvalīva kusumātsamudgatā ।। sjau slau ca tato nsau jgau nau sau ceti tṛtīyake । sjau sjau gaśca caturthe tu lalitāyā gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। lalitākulabhramitacāru vasanakaracārupallavā ।
pravikasitakamalakāntimukhī pravibhāsi devī surataśramāturā ।। evametāni vṛttāni samāni viṣamāṇi ca । nāṭakādyeṣu kāvyeṣu prayoktavyāni sūribhiḥ ।। santyanyānyapi vṛttāni yānyuktānīha piṇḍaśaḥ ।
na ca tāni prayojyāni na śobhāṃ janayanti hi ।। yānyataḥ pratiṣiddhāni gītake tāni yojayet । dhruvāyoge tu vakṣyāmi teṣāṃ caiva vikalpanam ।। vṛttalakṣaṇamevaṃ tu samāsena mayoditam ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi hyāryāṇāmapi lakṣaṇam ।। pathyā ca vipulā caiva caṣalā mukhato aparā । jaghane capalā caiva āryāḥ pañca prakīrtitāḥ ।। āsāṃ tu saṃpravakṣyāmi yatimātrāvikalpanam ।
lakṣaṇaṃ niyamaṃ caiva vikalpaguṇasaṃśrayam ।। yatiśchedastu vijñeyaścaturmātro gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ । dvitīyāntyau yujau pādāvayujau tvaparau smṛtau ।। gurumadhyavihīnastu caturgaṇasamanvitaḥ ।
ayuggaṇo vidhātavyo yuggaṇastu yathepsitaḥ ।। ṣaṣṭho vai dvivikalpastu naidhano hyekasaṃsthitaḥ । paścādardhe tu ṣaṣṭhaḥ syādekamātrastu kevalaḥ ।। dvivikalpastu ṣaṣṭho yo gurumadhyo bhavettu saḥ ।
tathā sarvalaghuścaiva yatisaṃjñāsamāśritā ।। dvitīyādilaghurjñeyaḥ saptame pañcame yatiḥ । prathamādirathāntye ca pañcame vā vidhīyate ।। gaṇeṣu triṣu pādasya yasyāḥ pathyā tu sā bhavet ।
ataśca vipulānyā tu vijñeyā yatilakṣaṇā ।। ayujaḥ sarvaguravo gurumadhyā gaṇā yujaḥ । yasyāḥ syuḥ pādayoge tu vijñeyā capalā hi sā ।। triṃśadādye tu vijñeyāḥ saptaviṃśatiścāpare ।
ubhayorardhayorjñeyo mātrāpiṇḍo vibhāgaśaḥ ।। triṃśattasyāśca yadi syuretāni dviguṇāni tu । trīṇyakṣarāṇi cānyāni nyasya saṃkhyāvibhāgaśaḥ ।। etāni laghusaṃjñāni nirdiṣṭāni samāsataḥ ।
sarveṣāṃ caivamāryāṇāmakṣarāṇāṃ yathākramam ।। ardhāṣṭamagaṇārdhā ca savavāryā prakīrtitā । ṣaṣṭhaśca dvivikalpastu naidhane hyekasaṃsthitaḥ ।। paścādvā yo gaṇaḥ ṣaṣṭha ekamātraḥ sa ucyate ।
dvivikalpastu yaḥ ṣaṣṭho gurumadhyo bhavettu saḥ ।। yathā sarvalaghuścaiva yatiḥ saṃkhyāsamāśritā । sā dvitīyā dvilaghukā saptame prathame yatiḥ ।। gurumadhyavihīnastu caturgaṇasamanvitaḥ ।
ayuggaṇo vidhātavyaḥ yuggaṇastu sa eva ca ।। prathamatṛtīyau pādau dvādaśamātrau bhavettu sā pathyā । vipulānyā khalu gaditā pūrvoditalakṣaṇopetā ।। raktamṛdupadmanetrā sitadīrghabahulamṛdukeśī ।
kasya tu pṛthumṛdujaghanā tanubāhvaṃ sodarī pathyā ।। vipulajaghanavadanastananayanaistāmrādharoṣṭhakaracaraṇaiḥ । āyatanāsāgaṇḍairlalāṭakarṇaiḥ śubhā kanyā ।। dvitīyaśca caturthaśca gurumadhyagato bhavet ।
ubhayorardhayoryatra vijñeyā capalā yathā ।। udbhaṭagāminī paruṣabhāṣiṇī kāmacihnakṛtaveṣā । jānāti māṃsayuktā surāpriyā sarvataścapalā ।। pūrvārdhe lakṣaṇaṃ hyetadasyāḥ sa ca mukhena tu ।
paścimārdhe tu capalā yasyāḥ sā jaghanena tu ।। āryāmukhe tu capalā tathāpi cāryā na me yataḥ sā kim । dakṣā gṛhakṛtyeṣu tathā duḥkhe bhavati duḥkhārtā ।। varamṛganayane capalāsi varoru śaśāṅkadarpaṇanibhāsye ।
kāmasya sārabhūte na pūrvamadacārujaghanena ।। ubhayorardhayoretallakṣaṇaṃ dṛśyate yadi । vṛttajñaiḥ sā tu vijñeyā sarvataścapalā sakhi ।। kāryau dvādaśamātrau ca pādāvādyau tṛtīyakau ।
aṣṭādaśa dvitīyaṃ ca tathā pañcadaśottamā ।। catuḥpañcaprakārāṇāṃ catuṣkāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ । prastārayogamāsādya bāhulyaṃ saṃpradarśayet ।। pañcapañcāśadādyā tu triṃśadādyā tathaiva ca ।
āryā tvakṣarapiṇḍena vijñeyātra prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। triṃśatastvatha varṇebhyo laghuvarṇatrayaṃ bhavet । śeṣāṇi gurusaṃkhyāni hyevaṃ sarvatra nirdiśet ।। sarveṣāmeva cāryāṇāmakṣarāṇāṃ yathākramam ।
sarveṣāṃ jātivṛttānāṃ pūrvamuttarasaṃkhyayā ।। vikalpagaṇanāṃ kṛtvā saṃkhyāpiṇḍena nirdiśet । āryāgītirathāryaiva kevalaṃ tvaṣṭabhirgaṇaiḥ ।। itarārthe jaḥ ṣaṣṭhastu nalaghugaṇa iṣyate ।
vṛttairevaṃ tu vividhairnānāchandassamudbhavaiḥ । kāvyabandhāstu kartavyāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇānvitāḥ ।। vibhūṣaṇaṃ cākṣarasaṃhatiśca śobhābhimānau guṇakīrtanaṃ ca । protsāhanodāharaṇe niruktaṃ guṇānuvādo atiśayaśca hetuḥ ।।
sārūpyamithyādhyavasāyasiddhi padoccayākrandamanorathāśca । ākhyānayāñcāpratiṣedhapṛcchā dṛṣṭāntanirbhāsanasaṃśayāśca ।। āśīḥ priyoktiḥ kapaṭaḥ kṣamā ca prāptiśca paścāttapanaṃ tathaiva । arthānuvṛttirhyupapattiyuktī kāryo anunītiḥ paridevanaṃ ca ।।
ṣaṭtriṃśadetāni hi lakṣaṇāni proktāni vai bhūṣaṇasaṃmitāni । kāvyeṣu bhāvārthagatāni tajjñaiḥ samyag prayojyāni yathārasaṃ tu ।। alaṅkārairguṇaiścaiva bahubhiḥ samalaṅkṛtam । bhūṣaṇairiva vinyastaistad bhūṣaṇamiti smṛtam ।।
yatrālpairakṣaraiḥ śliṣṭairvicitramupavarṇyate । tamapyakṣarasaṅghātaṃ vidyāllakṣaṇasaṃjñitam ।। siddhairarthaissamaṃ kṛtvā hyasiddho arthaḥ prasādhyate । yatra ślakṣṇavicitrārthā sā śobhetyabhidhīyate ।।
dhāryamāṇastu bahubhirvacanaiḥ kāryayuktibhiḥ । na yaḥ paryavatiṣṭheta so abhimānastu saṃjñitaḥ ।। kīrtyamānairguṇairyatra vividhārthasamudbhavaiḥ । doṣā na parikathyante tajjñeyaṃ guṇakīrtanam ।।
loke guṇātiriktānāṃ bahūnāṃ yatra nāmabhiḥ । eko abhiśabdyate yastu vijñeyaṃ guṇakīrtanam ।। utsāhajananaiḥ spaṣṭairarthairopamyasaṃśrayaiḥ । prasiddhairupagūḍhaṃ ca jñeyaṃ protsāhanaṃ budhaiḥ ।।
yatraikasyāpi śabdasya darśanātsubahūnyapi । yānti siddhimanuktāni tadudāharaṇaṃ smṛtam ।। niruktaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ tathyaṃ cātathyameva vā । siddhiprasādhitaṃ tathyamatathyaṃ cāprasādhitam ।।
guṇānuvādo hīnānāmuttamairupamākṛtaḥ । uttamārthaviśeṣo yaḥ sa cāpyatiśayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। bahūnāṃ bhāṣamāṇānāmekasyārthavinirṇayāt । siddhopamānavacanaṃ heturityabhisaṃjñitaḥ ।।
apadeśastu parokṣo yasmādutpadyate anukaraṇena । lakṣaṇasamānakaraṇāt sārūpyaṃ tattu nirdeśyam ।। abhūtapūrvairyatrārthaistulyasyārthasya nirṇayaḥ । sa mithyādhyavasāyastu procyate kāvyalakṣaṇe ।।
bahūnāṃ tu pradhānānāṃ madhye yannāma kīrtyate । ekārthasādhanakṛtaṃ sā siddhiriti kīrtyate ।। guṇairbahubhirekārthaiḥ padairyaḥ saṃpraśasyate । padoccayaṃ tu tadvidyānnānārthagrathanātmakam ।।
ātmabhāvamupanyasya parasādṛśyayuktibhiḥ । tīvrārthabhāṣaṇaṃ yatsyādākrandaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ ।। hṛdayasthasya bhāvasya suspaṣṭārthapradarśanam । anyāpadeśakathanairmanoratha iti smṛtaḥ ।।
apṛṣṭairathavā pṛṣṭairnirṇayaḥ kriyate tu yaḥ । ākhyānamiti tajjñeyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam ।। ādau yatkrodhajananamante harṣapravardhanam । yattu priyaṃ punarvākyaṃ sā yāñcā parikīrtitā ।।
kāryeṣu viparīteṣu yadi kiñcit pravartate । nivāryate ca kāryajjñaiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। yatrākārodbhavairvākyairātmānamathavā param । pṛcchannivābhidhatte arthaṃ sā pṛcchetyabhisaṃjñitā ।।
vidvān pūrvopalabdhau yatsamatvamupapādayet । nidarśanakṛtastajjñaiḥ sa dṛṣṭānta iti smṛtaḥ ।। anekayuktimadvākyamanekārthaprasādhakam । anekavākyasaṃyuktaṃ tannirbhāsanamucyate ।।
aparijñātatattvārthaṃ yatra vākyaṃ samāpyate । so anekatvādvicārāṇāṃ saṃśayaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। yatra śāstrārthasampannāṃ manorathasamudbhavām । aprārthanīyāmanyāṃ vā vidustāmāśiṣaṃ budhāḥ ।।
ādau yat krodhajananamante harṣapravardhanam । tat priyaṃ vacanaṃ jñeyamāśīrvādasamanvitam ।। chalayuktyā tvanyeṣāmabhisandhānābhibhāvakaṃkapaṭam । dvitriprayogayukto vijñeyaḥ kapaṭasaṅghātaḥ ।।
durjanodāhṛtai rūkṣaiḥ sabhāmadhye atitāḍitaḥ । akrodhaḥ krodhajananairvākyairyaḥ sā kṣamā bhavet ।। dṛṣṭvaivāvayavaṃ kañcidbhāvo yatrānumīyate । prāptiṃ tāmabhijānīyāllakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam ।।
akāryaṃ sahasā kṛtvā'kṛtvā kāryamathāpi vā । santāpo manaso yastu paścāttāpaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। praśrayeṇārthasaṃyuktaṃ yatparasyānuvartanam । snehāddākṣiṇyayogādvā sānuvṛttistu saṃjñitā ।।
prāptānāṃ yatra doṣāṇāṃ kriyate śamanaṃ punaḥ । sā jñeyā hyupapattistu lakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam ।। sādhyate yo arthasambandho mahadbhiḥ samavāyataḥ । parasparānukūlyena sā yuktiḥ parikīrtitā ।।
yatrāpasārayan doṣaṃ guṇamarthena yojayet । guṇābhivādaṃ doṣān vā kāryaṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ viduḥ ।। apūrvakrodhajanitamaparādhaṃ pramṛjya yat । sevārthaṃ madhuraṃ vākyamanunītiḥ prakīrtitā ।।
doṣairyadanyanāmoktaiḥ prasiddhārthaiḥ prayojayet । anyatrārthena sambaddhaṃ jñeyaṃ tat paridevanam ।। upamā rūpakaṃ caiva dīpakaṃ yamakaṃ tathā । alaṅkārāstu vijñeyā catvāro nāṭakāśrayāḥ ।।
yatkiñcit kāvyabandheṣu sādṛśyenopamīyate । upamā nāma sā jñeyā guṇākṛtisamāśrayā ।। ekasyaikena sā kāryā hyanekenāthavā punaḥ । anekasya tathaikena bahūnāṃ bahubhistathā ।।
tulyaṃ te śaśinā vaktramityekenaikasaṃśrayā । śaśāṅkavat prakāśante jyotīṃṣīti bhavettu yā ।। ekasyānekaviṣayā sopamā parikīrtitā । śyenabarhiṇabhāsānāṃ tulyārthamiti yā bhavet ।।
ekasya bahubhiḥ sāmyādupamā nāṭakāśrayā । bahūnāṃ bahubhirjñeyā ghanā iva gajā iti ।। praśaṃsā caiva nindā ca kalpitā sadṛśī tathā । yā kiñcitsadṛśī jñeyā sopamā pañcadhā budhaiḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā tu tāṃ viśālākṣīṃ tutoṣa manujādhipaḥ । munibhiḥ sādhitāṃ kṛcchrāt siddhiṃ mūrtimatīmiva ।। sā taṃ sarvaguṇairhīnaṃ sasvaje karkaśacchavim । vane kaṇṭakinaṃ vallī dāvadagdhamiva drumam ।।
kṣaranto dānasalilaṃ lālāmantharagāminaḥ । mataṅgajā virājante jaṅgamā iva parvatāḥ ।। yattvayādya kṛtaṃ karma paricittānurodhinā । sadṛśaṃ tattavaiva syādatimānuṣakarmaṇaḥ ।।
sampūrṇacandravadanā nīlotpaladalekṣaṇā । mattamātaṅgagamanā samprāpteyaṃ sakhī mama ।। upamāyā budhairete bhedā jñeyāḥ samāsataḥ । śeṣā ye lakṣaṇairnoktāste grāhyāḥ kāvyalokataḥ ।।
nānādhikaraṇārthānāṃ śabdānāṃ saṃpradīpakam । ekavākyena saṃyuktaṃ taddīpakamucyate ।। prasṛtaṃ madhuraṃ cāpi guṇaiḥ sarvairalaṅkṛtam । kāvye yannāṭake viprāstaddīpakamiti smṛtam ।।
sarāṃsi haṃsaiḥ kusumaiśca vṛkṣā mattairdvirephaiśca saroruhāṇi । goṣṭhībhirudyānavanāni caiva tasminnaśūnyāni sadā kriyante ।। svavikalpena racitaṃ tulyāvayavalakṣaṇam । kiñcitsādṛśyasampannaṃ yadrūpaṃ rūpakaṃ tu tat ।।
nānādravyānurāgādyairyadaupamyaguṇāśrayam । rūpanirvarṇanāyuktaṃ tadrūpakamiti smṛtam ।। padmānanāstāḥ kumudaprahāsā vikāsinīlotpalacārunetrāḥ । vāpīstriyo haṃsakulairnaḥ svanadbhirvirejuranyonyamivāhvayantyaḥ ।।
śabdābhyāsastu yamakaṃ padādiṣu vikalpitam । viśeṣadarśanañcāsya gadato me nibodhata ।। pādāntayamakaṃ caiva kāñcīyamakameva ca । samudgayamakaṃ caiva vikrāntayamakaṃ tathā ।।
yamakaṃ cakravālaṃ ca sandaṣṭayamakaṃ tathā । padādiyamakañcaiva hyāmreḍitamathāpi ca ।। caturvyavasitañcaiva mālāyamakameva ca । etādṛśavidhaṃ jñeyaṃ yamakaṃ nāṭakāśrayam ।।
caturṇāṃ yatra pādānāmante syātsamamakṣaram । tadvai pādāntayamakaṃ vijñeyaṃ nāmato yathā ।। divīva lagnaṃ tapanīyamaṇḍalam । yathā taruṇyāḥ stanabhāramaṇḍalam ।।
lokānāṃ prabhaviṣṇurdaityendragadānipātanasahiṣṇuḥ । jayati suradaityajiṣṇurbhagavānasuravaramathanakārī viṣṇuḥ ।। pādasyānte tathā cādau syātāṃ yatra same pade । tatkāñcīyamakaṃ caiva vijñeyaṃ sūribhiryathā ।।
vyaktāvyaktā sārajanīnāṃ rajanīnām । rāmā rāmā vismayate ca smayate ca ।। ardhenaikena yadvṛttaṃ sarvameva samāpyate । samudgayamakaṃ nāma tajjñeyaṃ paṇḍitairyathā ।।
śobhate pravarakānanahastī । śobhate pravarakānanahastī ।। ekaikaṃ pādamutkramya dvau pādau sadṛśau yadi । vikrāntayamakaṃ nāma tadvijñeyamidaṃ yathā ।।
sa pūrvaṃ vāraṇo bhūtvā dviśṛṅga iva parvataḥ । abhavaddantavaikalyādviśṛṅga iva parvataḥ ।। pūrvasyāntena pādasya parasyādiryadā samaḥ । cakravaccakravālaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ nāmato yathā ।।
tulyātpādadvayādantyādekenādiryadā samaḥ । sarvatra cakravālantu tadvijñeyaṃ budhairyathā ।। śailā yathā śatrubhirāhatā hatā hatāśca bhūyastvanupuṅkhapuṅkhagaiḥ । khagaiśca sarvairyudhi sañcitāścitāścitādhirūḍhā nihitāstalaistalaiḥ ।।
ādau dvau yatra pādau tu bhavetāmakṣare samau । sandaṣṭayamakaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ tadbudhairyathā ।। paśya paśya ramaṇasya me guṇān yena yena vaśagāṃ karoti mām । yena yena hi sameti darśanaṃ tena tena vaśagāṃ karoti mām ।।
ādau pādasya tu yatra syāt samāveśaḥ samākṣaraḥ । pādādiyamakaṃ nāma tadvijñeyaṃ budhairyathā ।। viṣṇuḥ sṛjati bhūtāni viṣṇuḥ saṃharate prajāḥ । viṣṇuḥ prasūte trailokyaṃ viṣṇurlokādhidaivatam ।।
pādasyāntaṃ padaṃ yatra dvirdvirekamihocyate । jñeyamāmreḍitaṃ nāma yamakaṃ tatra sūribhiḥ ।। vijṛmbhitaṃ niḥśvasitaṃ muhurmuhuḥ kathaṃ vidheyaṃ smaraṇaṃ pade pade । yathā ca te dhyānamidaṃ punaḥ punardhuvaṃgatā te rajanī vinā vinā ।।
sarve pādāḥ samā yatra bhavanti niyatākṣarāḥ । caturvyavasitaṃ nāma tadvijñeyaṃ budhairyathā ।। vāraṇānāmayameva kālo vāraṇānāmayameva kālaḥ । vāraṇānāmayameva kālo vāraṇānāmayameva kālaḥ ।।
nānārūpaiḥ svarairyuktaṃ yatraikaṃ vyañjanaṃ bhavet । tanmālāyamakaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ paṇḍitairyathā ।। lalī balī halī mālī khelī mālī salī jalī । khalo balo abalo mālī musalī tvābhirakṣatu ।।
asau hi rāmā rativigrahapriyā rahaḥpragalbhā ramaṇaṃ manogatam । ratena rātriṃ ramayet pareṇa vā na cedudeṣyattaruṇaḥ paro ripuḥ ।। na puṣkarākṣaḥ kṣatajokṣitākṣaḥ kṣaratkṣatevyaḥ kṣatajaṃdurīkṣaḥ । kṣatairgavākṣairiva saṃvṛtājñaḥ sākṣāt sahasrākṣa ivāvabhāti ।।
ebhirarthakriyāpekṣaiḥ kāryaṃ kāvyaṃ tu lakṣaṇaiḥ । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi kāvye doṣān guṇāṃstathā ।। gūḍhārthamarthāntaramarthahīnaṃ bhinnārthamekārthamabhiplutārtham । nyāyāvapetaṃ viṣamaṃ visandhi śabdacyutaṃ vai daśa kāvyadoṣāḥ ।।
paryāyaśabdābhihataṃ gūḍhārthamabhisaṃjñitam । avarṇyaṃ varṇyate yatra tadarthāntaramiṣyate ।। arthahīnaṃ tvasambaddhaṃ sāvaśeṣārthameva ca । bhinnārthamabhivijñeyamasabhyaṃ grāmyameva ca ।।
vivakṣito anya evārtho yatrānyārthena bhidyate । bhinnārthaṃ tadapi prāhuḥ kāvyaṃ kāvyavicakṣaṇāḥ ।। aviśeṣābhidhānaṃ yat tadekārthamiti smṛtam । abhiplutārthaṃ vijñeyaṃ yat padena samasyate ।।
nyāyādapetaṃ vijñeyaṃ pramāṇaparivarjitam । vṛttabhedo bhavedyatra viṣamaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।। anupaśiṣṭaśabdaṃ yat tadvisandhīti kīrtitam । śabdacyutañca vijñeyamaśabdasvarayojanāt ।।
ete doṣāstu vijñeyāḥ sūribhirnāṭakāśrayāḥ । guṇā viparyayādeṣāṃ mādhuryaudāryalakṣaṇāḥ ।। śleṣaḥ prasādaḥ samatāsamādhirmādhuryamojaḥ padasaukumāryam । arthasya ca vyaktirudāratā ca kāntiśca kāvyasya guṇā daśaite ।।
īpsitenārthajātena sambaddhānāṃ parasparam । śliṣṭatā yā padānāṃ hi śleṣa ityabhidhīyate ।। vicāragahanaṃ yatsyāt sphuṭañcaiva svabhāvataḥ । svataḥ supratibaddhañca śliṣṭaṃ tat parikīrtyate ।।
apyanukto budhairyatra śabdo artho vā pratīyate । sukhaśabdārthasaṃyogāt prasādaḥ parikīrtyate ।। nāticūrṇapadairyuktā na ca vyarthābhidāyibhiḥ । durbodhanaiśca na kṛtā samatvāt samatā matā ।।
anyonyasadṛśā yatra tathā hyanyonyabhūṣaṇāḥ । alaṅkārā guṇāścaiva samāḥ syuḥ samatāṃ matāḥ ।। abhiyuktairviśeṣastu yo arthasyehopalakṣyate । tena cārthena sampannaḥ samādhiḥ parikīrtyate ।।
upamāsviha dṛṣṭānāmarthānāṃ yatnatastathā । prāptānāṃ cātisaṃkṣepāt samādhirnirṇayo yataḥ ।। bahuśo yacchrutaṃ vākyamuktaṃ vāpi punaḥ punaḥ । nodvejayati yasmāddhi tanmādhuryamiti smṛtam ।।
samāsavadbhirvividhairvicitraiśca padairyutam । sānusvārairudāraiśca tadojaḥ parikīrtyate ।। avagīto api hīno api syādudāttāvabhāsakaḥ । yatra śabdārthasampattistadojaḥ parikīrtitam ।।
sukhaprayojyairyacchabdairyuktaṃ suśliṣṭasandhibhiḥ । sukumārārthasaṃyuktaṃ saukumāryaṃ taducyate ।। suprasiddhābhidhānā tu lokakarmavyavasthitā । yā kriyā kriyate kāvye sārthavyaktiḥ pratīyate ।।
yasyārthānupraveśena manasā parikalpyate । anantaraṃ prayogastu sā'rthavyaktirudāhṛtā ।। divyabhāvaparītaṃ yacchṛṅgārādbhutayojitam । anekabhāvasaṃyuktamudāratvaṃ prakīrtitam ।।
anekārthaviśeṣairyat sūktaiḥ sauṣṭhavasaṃyutaiḥ । upetamaticitrārthaiḥ udāttaṃ tacca kīrtyate ।। yanmanaśśrotraviṣayamāhlādayati hīnduvat । līlādyarthopapannāṃ vā tāṃ kāntiṃ kavayo viduḥ ।।
yo manaśśrotraviṣayaḥ prasādajanako bhavet । śabdabandhaḥ prayogeṇa sa kānta iti bhaṇyate ।। evamete hyalaṅkārā guṇā doṣāśca kīrtitāḥ । prayogameṣāṃ ca punarvakṣyāmi rasasaṃśrayam ।।
laghvakṣaraprāyakṛtamupamārūpakāśrayam । kāvyaṃ kāryaṃ tu nāṭyajñaiḥ vīraraudrādbhutāśrayam ।। gurvakṣaraprāyakṛtaṃ bībhatse karuṇe tathā । kadācidraudravīrābhyāṃ yadāgharṣaṇajaṃ bhavet ।।
rūpadīpakasaṃyuktamāryāvṛttasamāśrayam । śṛṅgāre ca rase vīre kāvyaṃ syānnāṭakāśrayam ।। uttarottarasaṃyuktaṃ vīre kāvyaṃ tu yadbhavet । jagatyatijagatyāṃ vā saṃkṛtyāṃ vāpi tadbhavet ।।
tathaiva yuddhasampheṭā utkṛtyāṃ saṃprakīrtitau । karuṇe śakvarī jñeyā tathaivātidhṛtirbhavet ।। yadvīre kīrtitaṃ cchandaḥ tadraudre api prayojayet । śeṣāṇāmarthayogena cchandaḥ kāryaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
yacchandaḥ pūrvamuddiṣṭaṃ viṣamārdhasame samam । udāramadhuraiḥ śabdaistatkāryaṃ tu rasānugam ।। śabdānudāramadhurān pramadābhidheyān nāṭyāśrayeṣu kṛtiṣu prayayeta kartum । tairbhūṣitā bahu vibhānti hi kāvyabandhāḥ padmākarā vikasitā iva rājahaṃsaiḥ ।।
trividhaṃ hyakṣaraṃ kāryaṃ kavibhirnāṭakāśrayam । hrasvaṃ dīrghaṃ plutañcaiva rasabhāvavibhāvakam ।। ekamātraṃ bhaved hrasvaṃ dvimātraṃ dīrghamiṣyate । plutaṃ caiva trimātraṃ syādakṣaraṃ svarayojanāt ।।
smṛte cāsūyite caiva tathā ca paridevite । paṭhatāṃ brāhmaṇānāñca plutamakṣaramiṣyate ।। akārastu smṛte kāryaṃ ūkāraścāpyasūyite । paridevite tu hākāra oṃkāro adhyayane tathā ।।
hrasvadīrghaplutānīha yathābhāvaṃ yathārasam । kāvyayogeṣu sarveṣu hyakṣarāṇi prayojayet ।। cekrīḍitaprabhṛtibhirvikṛtaistu śabdaiḥ yuktā na bhānti lalitā bharataprayogāḥ । yajñakriyeva rurucarmadhuraiḥ kṛtāktaiḥ veśyā dvijairiva kamaṇḍaludaṇḍahastaiḥ ।।
mṛdulalitapadārthaṃ gūḍhaśabdārthahīnaṃ budhajanasukhabhogyaṃ yuktimannṛttayogyam । bahurasakṛtamārgaṃ sandhisandhānayuktaṃ bhavati jagati yogyaṃ nāṭakaṃ prekṣakāṇām ।। bhūṣaṇākṣarasaṅghātau śobhodāharaṇe tathā । hetusaṃśayadṛṣṭāntāḥ prāptābhiprāya eva ca ।।
nidarśanaṃ niruktaṃ ca siddhiścātha viśeṣaṇam । guṇātipātātiśayau tulyatarkaḥ padoccayaḥ ।। dṛṣṭaṃ caivopadiṣṭaṃ ca vicārastadviparyayaḥ । bhraṃśaścānunayo mālā dākṣiṇyaṃ garhaṇaṃ tathā ।।
arthāpattiḥ prasiddhiśca pṛcchā sārūpyameva ca । manorathaśca leśaśca kṣobho atha guṇakīrtanam ।। jñeyānyanuktasiddhiśca priyaṃ vacanameva ca । ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇānyeva kāvyabandheṣu nirdiśet ।।
alaṅkārairguṇaiścaiva bahubhiḥ samalaṃkṛtam । bhūṣaṇairiva citrārthaistad bhūṣaṇamiti smṛtam ।। yatrālpairakṣaraiḥ śliṣṭairvicitramupavarṇyate । tamapyakṣarasaṅghātaṃ vidyāllakṣaṇasaṃjñitam ।।
siddhairarthaiḥ samaṃ kṛtvā hyasiddho arthaḥ prayujyate । yatra śliṣṭā vicitrārthā sā śobhetyabhidhīyate ।। yatra tulyārthayuktena vākyenābhipradarśanāt । sādhyante nipuṇairarthāstadudāharaṇaṃ smṛtam ।।
yat prayojanasāmarthyāt vākyamiṣṭārthasādhakam । samāsoktaṃ manogrāhi sa heturiti saṃjñitaḥ ।। aparijñātatattvārthaṃ vākyaṃ yatra samāpyate । anekatvādvicārāṇāṃ sa saṃśaya iti smṛtaḥ ।।
sarvalokamanogrāhi yastu pakṣārthasādhakaḥ । hetornidarśanakṛtaḥ sa dṛṣṭānta iti smṛtaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvaivāvayavān kāṃścid bhāvo yatrānumīyate । prāptiṃ tāmapi jānīyāllakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam ।।
abhūtapūrvo yo apyarthaḥ sādṛśyātparikalpitaḥ । lokasya hṛdayagrāhī so abhiprāya iti smṛtaḥ ।। yatrārthānāṃ prasiddhānāṃ kriyate parikīrtanam । parāpekṣādyudāsārthaṃ tannidarśanamucyate ।।
niravadyasya vākyasya pūrvoktārthaprasiddhaye । yaducyate tu vacanaṃ niruktaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।। bahūnāṃ ca pradhānānāṃ nāma yatrābhikīrtyate । abhipretārthasiddhyarthaṃ sā siddhirabhidhīyate ।।
siddhān bahūn pradhānārthān uktvā yatra prayujyate । viśeṣayuktaṃ vacanaṃ vijñeyaṃ tadviśeṣaṇam ।। guṇābhidhānairvividhairviparītārthayojitaiḥ । guṇātipāto madhurairniṣṭhurārthairbhavedatha ।।
bahūn guṇān kīrtayitvā sāmānyajanasambhavān । viśeṣaḥ kīrtyate yastu jñeyaḥ so atiśayo budhaiḥ ।। rūpakairupasābhirvā tulyārthaiḥ suprayojitaiḥ । apratyakṣārthasaṃsparśastulyatarkaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।
bahūnāṃ ca prayuktānāṃ padānāṃ bahubhiḥ padaiḥ । uccayaḥ sadṛśārtho yaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ padoccayaḥ ।। yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ yathārūpaṃ ca varṇyate । yatpratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā dṛṣṭaṃ tadvarṇato api vā ।।
parigṛhya tu śāstrārthaṃ yadvākyamabhidhīyate । vidvanmanoharaṃ svantamupadiṣṭaṃ taducyate ।। pūrvāśayasamānārthairapratyakṣārthasādhanaiḥ । anekopādhisaṃyukto vicāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
vicārasyānyathābhāvastathā dṛṣṭopadiṣṭayoḥ । sandehātkalpyate yastu sa vijñeyo viparyayaḥ ।। vācyamarthaṃ parityajya dṛṣṭādibhiranekadhā । anyasminneva patanādiha bhraṃśaḥ sa iṣyate ।।
ubhayoḥ prītijanano viruddhābhiniviṣṭayoḥ । arthasya sādhakaścaiva vijñeyo anunayo budhaiḥ ।। īpsitārthaprasiddhyarthaṃ kīrtyate yatra sūribhiḥ । prayojanānyanekāni sā māletyabhisaṃjñitā ।।
hṛṣṭaiḥ prasannavadanairyatparasyānuvartanam । kriyate vākyaceṣṭābhistaddākṣiṇyamiti smṛtam ।। yatra saṃkīrtayan doṣaṃ guṇamarthena darśayet । guṇātipātād doṣādvā garhaṇaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।।
arthāntarasya kathane yatrānyo arthaḥ pratīyate । vākyamādhuryasampannā sārthāpattirudāhṛtā ।। vākyaiḥ sātiśayairuktā vākyārthasya prasādhakaiḥ । lokaprasiddhairbahubhiḥ prasiddhiriti kīrtitā ।।
yatrākārodbhavairvākyairātmānamathavā param । pṛcchyate cābhidhatte arthaṃ sā pṛcchetyabhisaṃjñitā ।। dṛṣṭaśrutānubhūtārthakathanādisamudbhavam । sādṛśyaṃ kṣobhajananaṃ sārūpyamiti saṃjñitam ।।
hṛdayasthasya vākyasya gūḍhārthasya vibhāvakam । anyāpadeśaiḥ kathanaṃ manoratha iti smṛtaḥ ।। yadvākyaṃ vākyakuśalairupāyenābhidhīyate । sadṛśārthābhiniṣpattyāḥ sa leśa iti kīrtitaḥ ।।
paradoṣairvicitrārthairyatrātmā parikīrtyate । adṛṣṭo apyanyo api vā kaścit sa tu kṣobha iti smṛtaḥ ।। loke guṇātiriktānāṃ guṇānāṃ yatra nāmabhiḥ । eko api śabdyate tattu vijñeyaṃ guṇakīrtanam ।।
prastāvenaiva śeṣo arthaḥ kṛtsno yatra pratīyate । vacanena vinānuktasiddhiḥ sā parikīrtitā ।। yatprasannena manasā pūjyaṃ pūjayituṃ vacaḥ । hṛṣṭaprakāśanārthaṃ tu sā priyoktirudāhṛtā ।।
etāni kāvyasya ca lakṣaṇāni ṣaṭtriṃśaduddeśanidarśanāni । prabandhaśobhākaraṇāni tajjñaiḥ samyak prayojyāni rasāyanāni ।। varttayiṣyāmyahaṃ viprā daśarūpavikalpanam । nāmataḥ karmataścaiva tathā caiva prayogataḥ ।।
nāṭakaṃ saprakaraṇamaṅko vyāyoga eva ca । bhāṇaḥ samavakāraśca vīthī prahasanaṃ ḍimaḥ ।। īhāmṛgaśca vijñeyā daśeme nāṭyalakṣaṇe । eteṣāṃ lakṣaṇamahaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।।
sarveṣāmeva kāvyānāṃ mātṛkā vṛttayaḥ smṛtāḥ । ābhyo vinisṛtaṃ hyetaddaśarūpaṃ prayogataḥ ।। jātibhiḥ śrutibhiścaiva svarā grāmatvamāgatāḥ । yathā tathā vṛttibhedaiḥ kāvyabandhā bhavanti hi ।।
grāmau pūrṇasvarau dvau tu yathā vai ṣaḍjamadhyamau । sarvavṛttiviniṣpannau kāvyabandhau tathā tvimau ।। jñeyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ caiva tathā nāṭakameva ca । sarvavṛttiviniṣpannaṃ nānābandhasamāśrayam ।।
vīthī samavakāraśca tathehāmṛga eva ca । utsṛṣṭikāṅko vyāyogo bhāṇaḥ prahasanaṃ ḍimaḥ ।। kaiśikīvṛttihīnāni rūpāṇyetāni kārayet । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi kāvyabandhavikalpanam ।।
prakhyātavastuviṣayaṃ prakhyātodāttanāyakaṃ caiva । rājarṣivaṃśyacaritaṃ tathaiva divyāśrayopetam ।। nānāvibhūtibhiryutamṛddhivilāsādibhirguṇaiścaiva । aṅkapraveśakāḍhyaṃ bhavati hi tannāṭakaṃ nāma ।।
nṛpatīnāṃ yaccaritaṃ nānārasabhāvaceṣṭitaṃ bahudhā । sukhaduḥkhotpattikṛtaṃ bhavati hi tannāṭakaṃ nāma ।। asyāvasthopetaṃ kāryaṃ prasamīkṣya binduvistārāt । kartavyo aṅkaḥ so api tu guṇānvitaṃ nāṭyatattvajñaiḥ ।।
aṅka iti rūḍhiśabdo bhāvaiśca rasaiśca rohayatyarthān । nānāvidhānayukto yasmāttasmādbhavedaṅkaḥ ।। aṅkasamāptiḥ kāryā kāvyacchedena bījasaṃhāraḥ । vastuvyāpī binduḥ kāvyasamuttho atra nityaṃ syāt ।।
yatrārthasya samāptiryatra ca bījasya bhavati saṃhāraḥ । kiñcidavalagnabinduḥ so aṅka iti sadāvagantavyaḥ ।। ye nāyakā nigaditāsteṣāṃ pratyakṣacaritasaṃyogaḥ । nānāvasthopetaḥ kāryastvaṅko aviprakṛṣṭastu ।।
nāyakadevīgurujanapurohitāmātyasārthavāhānām । naikarasāntaravihito hyaṅka iti sa veditavyastu ।। pañcākṣarā daśaparā hyaṅkāḥ syurnāṭake prakaraṇe ca । niṣkrāmaḥ sarveṣāṃ yasminnaṅkaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ ।।
krodhaprasādaśokāḥ śāpotsargo atha vidravodvāhau । adbhutasambhavadarśanamaṅke pratyakṣajāni syuḥ ।। ekadivasapravṛttaḥ kāryastvaṅko arthabījamadhikṛtya । āvaśyakakāryāṇāmavirodhena prayogeṣu ।।
ekāṅkena kadācidbahūni kāryāṇi yojayeddhīmān । āvaśyakāvirodhena tatra kāvyāni kāryāṇi ।। raṅgaṃ tu ye praviṣṭāḥ sarveṣāṃ bhavati tatra niṣkrāmaḥ । bījārthayuktiyuktaṃ kṛtvā kāvyaṃ yathārtharasam ।।
na bahūnīha kāryāṇi tvekāṅke viniyojayet । āvaśyakānāṃ kāryāṇāṃ virodho hi tathā bhavet ।। jñātvā divasāvasthāṃ kṣaṇayāmamuhūrtalakṣaṇopetām । vibhajetsarvamaśeṣaṃ pṛthakpṛthakkāvyamaṅkeṣu ।।
divasāvasānakāryaṃ yadyaṅke nopapadyate sarvam । aṅkacchedaṃ kṛtvā praveśakaistadvidhātavyam ।। viprakṛṣṭaṃ tu yo deśaṃ gacchetkāryavaśānugaḥ । aṅkacchede atha saṃkṣepānnirdiśettaṃ praveśakaiḥ ।।
sannihitanāyako aṅkaḥ kartavyo nāṭake prakaraṇe vā । parijanakathānubandhaḥ praveśako nāma vijñeyaḥ ।। prakaraṇanāṭakaviṣaye pañcādyā daśaparā bhavantyaṅkāḥ । aṅkāntarasandhiṣu ca praveśakāsteṣu tāvantaḥ ।।
anayorantaravihitaḥ praveśako arthakriyāṃ samabhivīkṣya । saṃkṣepārthaḥ sandhiṣvarthānāṃ saṃvidhātavyaḥ ।। aṅkacchedaṃ kṛtvā māsakṛtaṃ varṣasañcitaṃ vāpi । tatsarvaṃ kartavyaṃ varṣādūrdhvaṃ na tu kadācit ।।
yaḥ kaścitkāryavaśādgacchati puruṣaḥ prakṛṣṭamadhvānam । tatrāpyaṅkacchedaḥ kartavyaḥ pūrvavattajñaiḥ ।। aṅkāntarānusārī saṃkṣepārthamadhikṛtya bindūnām । prakaraṇanāṭakaviṣaye praveśakaḥ saṃvidhātavyaḥ ।।
nottamamadhyamapuruṣairācarito nāpyudāttavacanakṛtaḥ । prākṛtabhāṣācāraḥ prayogamāśritya kartavyaḥ ।। kālotthānagatirasau vyākhyāsaṃrambhakāryaviṣayāṇām । arthābhidhānayuktaḥ praveśakaḥ syādanekārthaḥ ।।
bahvāśrayamapi kāryaṃ praveśakaiḥ saṃkṣipecca sandhiṣu vā । bahucūrṇapadairyuktaṃ janayati khedaṃ prayogasya ।। yatrārthasya samāptirna bhavatyaṅke prayogabāhulyāt । vṛttāntasvalpakathaiḥ praveśakaiḥ so abhidhātavyaḥ ।।
yuddhaṃ rājyabhraṃśo maraṇaṃ nagaroparodhanaṃ caiva । pratyakṣāṇi tu nāṅke praveśakaiḥ saṃvidheyāni ।। aṅke praveśake ca prakaraṇamāśritya nāṭake vāpi । na vadhaḥ kartavyaḥ syādyo abhyudayī nāyakaḥ khyātaḥ ।।
apasaraṇameva kāryaṃ grahaṇaṃ vā sandhireva vā yojyaḥ । kāvyaśleṣairbahubhiryathārasaṃ nāṭyatattvajñaiḥ ।। na mahājanaparivāraṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭakaṃ prakaraṇaṃ vā । ye tatra kāryapuruṣāścatvāraḥ pañca vā te syuḥ ।।
kāryaṃ gopucchāgraṃ kartavyaṃ kāvyabandhamāsādya । ye codāttā bhāvāste sarve pṛṣṭhataḥ kāryāḥ ।। sarveṣāṃ kāvyānāṃ nānārasabhāvayuktiyuktānām । nirvahaṇe kartavyo nityaṃ hi raso adbhutastajjñaiḥ ।।
nāṭakalakṣaṇametanmayā samāsena kīrtitaṃ vidhivat । prakaraṇamataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇayuktyā pravakṣyāmi ।। yatra kavirātmaśaktyā vastu śarīraṃ ca nāyakaṃ caiva । autpattikaṃ prakurute prakaraṇamiti tadbudhairjñeyam ।।
yadanārṣamathāhāryaṃ kāvyaṃ prakarotyabhūtaguṇayuktam । utpannabījavastu prakaraṇamiti tadapi vijñeyam ।। yannāṭake mayoktaṃ vastu śarīraṃ ca vṛttibhedāśca । tatprakaraṇe api yojyaṃ salakṣaṇaṃ sarvasandhiṣu tu ।।
vipravaṇikṣacivānāṃ purohitāmātyasārthavāhānām । caritaṃ yannaikavidhaṃ jñeyaṃ tatprakaraṇaṃ nāma ।। nodāttanāyakakṛtaṃ na divyacaritaṃ na rājasambhogam । bāhyajanasaṃprayuktaṃ tajjñeyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ tajjñaiḥ ।।
dāsaviṭaśreṣṭhiyutaṃ veśastryupacārakāraṇopetam । mandakulastrīcaritaṃ kāvyaṃ kāryaṃ prakaraṇe tu ।। sacivaśreṣṭhibrāhmaṇapurohitāmātyasārthavāhānām । gṛhavārtā yatra bhavenna tatra veśyāṅganā kāryā ।।
yadi veśayuvatiyuktaṃ na kulastrī saṅgamo api syāt । atha kulajanaprayuktaṃ na veśayuvatirbhavettatra ।। yadi vā kāraṇayuktyā veśakulastrīkṛtopacāraḥ syāt । avikṛtabhāṣācāraṃ tatra tu pāṭhyaṃ prayoktavyam ।।
madhyamapuruṣairnityaṃ yojyo viṣkambhako atra tattvajjñaiḥ । saṃskṛtavacanānugataḥ saṃkṣepārthaḥ praveśakavat ।। śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo vā dvividho viṣkambhako api kartavyaḥ । madhyamapātraḥ śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo nīcamadhyakṛtaḥ ।।
aṅkāntarālavihitaḥ praveśako arthakriyāṃ samabhivīkṣya । saṃkṣepātsandhīnāmarthānāṃ caiva kartavyaḥ ।। anayośca bandhayogādanyo bhedaḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ kāryaḥ । prakhyātastvitaro vā nāṭakayoge prakaraṇe vā ।।
prakaraṇanāṭakabhedādutpādyaṃ vastu nāyakaṃ nṛpatim । antaḥpurasaṅgītakakanyāmadhikṛtya kartavyā ।। strīprāyā caturaṅkā lalitābhinayātmikā suvihitāṅgī । bahunṛttagītapāṭhyā ratisambhogātmikā caiva ।।
rājopacārayuktā prasādanakrodhadambhasaṃyuktā । nāyakadevīdūtī saparijanā nāṭikā jñeyā ।। antarbhāvagatā hyeṣā bhāvayorubhayoryataḥ । ata eva daśaitāni rūpāṇītyuditāni vai ।।
prakaraṇanāṭakalakṣaṇamuktaṃ viprā mayā samāsena । vakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ yuktyā samavakāram ।। devāsurabījakṛtaḥ prakhyātodāttanāyakaścaiva । tryaṅkastathā trikapaṭastrividravaḥ syāttriśṛṅgāraḥ ।।
dvādaśanāyakabahulo hyaṣṭādaśanāḍikāpramāṇaśca । vakṣyāmyasyāṅkavidhiṃ yāvatyo nāḍikā yatra ।। aṅkastu saprahasanaḥ savidravaḥ sakapaṭaḥ savīthīkaḥ । dvādaśanāḍīvihitaḥ prathamaḥ kāryaḥ kriyopetaḥ ।।
kāryastathā dvitīyaḥ samāśrito nāḍikāścatasrastu । vastusamāpanavihito dvināḍikaḥ syāttṛtīyastu ।। nāḍīsaṃjñā jñeyā mānaṃ kālasya yanmuhūrtārdham । tannāḍikāpramāṇaṃ yathoktamaṅkeṣu saṃyojyam ।।
yā nāḍiketi saṃjñā kālavibhāge kriyābhisaṃpannā । kāryā ca sā prayatnādyathā krameṇaiva śāstroktā ।। aṅko aṅkastvanyārthaḥ kartavyaḥ kāvyabandhamāsādya । arthaṃ hi samavakāre hyapratisambandhamicchanti ।।
yuddhajalasambhavo vā vāyvagnigajendrasaṃbhramakṛto vā । nagaroparodhajo vā vijñeyo vidravastrividhaḥ ।। vastugatakramavihito devavaśādvā paraprayukto vā । sukhaduḥkhotpattikṛtastrividhaḥ kapaṭo atra vijñeyaḥ ।।
trividhaścātra vidhijñaiḥ pṛthakpṛthakkāryavihitārthaḥ । śṛṅgāraḥ kartavyo dharme cārthe ca kāme ca ।। yasmin dharmaprāpakamātmahitaṃ bhavati sādhanaṃ bahudhā । vrataniyamatapoyukto jñeyo asau dharmaśṛṅgāraḥ ।।
arthasyecchāyogādbahudhā caivārthato arthaśṛṅgāraḥ । strīsaṃprayogaviṣayeṣvarthārthā vā ratiryatra ।। kanyāvilobhanakṛtaṃ prāptau strīpuṃsayostu ramyaṃ vā । nibhṛtaṃ sāvegaṃ vā yasya bhavetkāmaśṛṅgāraḥ ।।
uṣṇiggāyatryādīnyanyāni ca yāni bandhakuṭilāni । vṛttāni samavakāre kavibhistāni prayojyāni ।। evaṃ kāryastajjñairnānārasasaṃśrayaḥ samavakāraḥ । vakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇamīhāmṛgasyāpi ।।
divyāpuruṣāśrayakṛto divyastrīkāraṇopagatayuddhaḥ । suvihitavastunibaddho vipratyayakārakaścaiva ।। uddhatapuruṣaprāyaḥ strīroṣagrathitakāvyabandhaśca । saṃkṣobhavidravakṛtaḥ saṃpheṭakṛtastathā caiva ।।
strībhedanāpaharaṇāvamardanaprāptavastuśṛṅgāraḥ । īhāmṛgastu kāryaḥ susamāhitakāvyabandhaśca ।। yadvyāyoge kāryaṃ ye puruṣā vṛttayo rasāścaiva । īhāmṛge api te syuḥ kevalamamarastriyā yogaḥ ।।
yatra tu vadhepsitānāṃ vadho hyudagro bhaveddhi puruṣāṇām । kiñcidvyājaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ yuddhaṃ śamayitavyam ।। īhāmṛgasya lakṣaṇamuktaṃ viprāḥ samāsayogena । ḍimalakṣaṇaṃ tu bhūyo lakṣaṇayuktyā pravakṣyāmi ।।
prakhyātavastuviṣayaḥ prakhyātodāttanāyakaścaiva । ṣaḍrasalakṣaṇayuktaścaturaṅko vai ḍimaḥ kāryaḥ ।। śṛṅgārahāsyavarjaṃ śeṣaiḥ sarvai rasaiḥ samāyuktaḥ । dīptarasakāvyayonirnānābhāvopasampannaḥ ।।
nirghātolkāpātairuparāgeṇendusūryayoryuktaḥ । yuddhaniyuddhādharṣaṇasaṃpheṭakṛtaśca kartavyaḥ ।। māyendrajālabahulo bahupustotthānayogayuktaśca । devabhujagendrarākṣasayakṣapiśācāvakīrṇaśca ।।
ṣoḍaśanāyakabahulaḥ sātvattyārabhaṭīvṛttisampannaḥ । kāryo ḍimaḥ prayatnānnānāśrayabhāvasampannaḥ ।। ḍimalakṣaṇamityuktaṃ mayā samāsena lakṣaṇānugatam । vyāyogasya tu lakṣaṇamataḥ paraṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi ।।
vyāyogastu vidhijñaiḥ kāryaḥ prakhyātanāyakaśarīraḥ । alpastrījanayuktastvekāhakṛtastathā caiva ।। bahavaśca tatra puruṣā vyāyacchante yathā samavakāre । na ca divyanāyakayuktaḥ kāryastvekāṅka evāyam ।।
na ca divyanāyakakṛtaḥ kāryo rājarṣināyakanibaddhaḥ । yuddhaniyuddhāgharṣaṇasaṃgharṣakṛtaśca kartavyaḥ ।। evaṃvidhastu kāryo vyāyogo dīptakāvyarasayoniḥ । vakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ lakṣaṇamutsṛṣṭāṅkasya ।।
prakhyātavastuviṣayastvaprakhyātaḥ kadācideva syāt । divyapuruṣairviyuktaḥ śeṣairyukto bhavetpuṃbhiḥ ।। karuṇarasaprāyakṛto nivṛttayuddhodyataprahāraśca । strīparidevitabahulo nirveditabhāṣitaścaiva ।।
nānāvyākulaceṣṭaḥ sātvattyārabhaṭikaiśikīhīnaḥ । kāryaḥ kāvyavidhijñaiḥ satataṃ hyutsṛṣṭikāṅkastu ।। yaddivyanāyakakṛtaṃ kāvyaṃ saṃgrāmabandhavadhayuktam । tadbhārate tu varṣe kartavyaṃ kāvyabandheṣu ।।
kasmādbhāratamiṣṭaṃ varṣeṣvanyeṣu devavihiteṣu । hṛdyā sarvā bhūmiḥ śubhagandhā kāñcanī yasmāt ।। upavanagamanakrīḍā vihāranārīratipramodāḥ syuḥ । teṣu hi varṣeṣu sadā na tatra duḥkhaṃ na vā śokaḥ ।।
ye teṣāmadhivāsāḥ purāṇavādeṣu parvatāḥ proktāḥ । sambhogasteṣu bhavetkarmārambho bhavedasmin ।। prahasanamapi vijñeyaṃ dvividhaṃ śuddhaṃ tathā saṅkīrṇam । aṅkasya lakṣaṇamidaṃ vyākhyātamaśeṣayogamātragatam ।।
prahasanamataḥ paraṃ salakṣaṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi । vakṣyāmi tayoryuktyā pṛthagpṛthaglakṣaṇaviśeṣam ।। bhagavattāpasaviprairanyairapi hāsyavādasambaddham । kāpuruṣasaṃprayuktaṃ parihāsābhāṣaṇaprāyam ।।
avikṛtabhāṣācāraṃ viśeṣabhāvopapannacaritapadam । niyatagativastuviṣayaṃ śuddhaṃ jñeyaṃ prahasanaṃ tu ।। veśyāceṭanapuṃsakaviṭadhūrtā bandhakī ca yatra syuḥ । anibhṛtaveṣaparicchadaceṣṭitakaraṇaistu saṃkīrṇam ।।
lokopacārayuktā yā vārtā yaśca dambhasaṃyogaḥ । sa prahasane prayojyo dhūrtapravivādasampannaḥ ।। vīthyaṅgaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ kartavyaṃ prahasanaṃ yathāyogyam । bhāṇasyāpi tu lakṣaṇamataḥ paraṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi ।।
ātmānubhūtaśaṃsī parasaṃśrayavarṇanāviśeṣastu । vividhāśrayo hi bhāṇo vijñeyastvekahāryaśca ।। paravacanamātmasaṃsthaṃ prativacanairuttamottamagrathitaiḥ । ākāśapuruṣakathitairaṅgavikārairabhinayaiścaiva ।।
dhūrtaviṭasaṃprayojyo nānāvasthāntarātmakaścaiva । ekāṅko bahuceṣṭaḥ satataṃ kāryo budhairbhāṇaḥ ।। bhāṇasyāpi hi nikhilaṃ lakṣaṇamuktaṃ tathāgamānugatam । vīthyāḥ saṃprati nikhilaṃ kathayāmi yathākramaṃ viprāḥ ।।
sarvarasalakṣaṇāḍhyā yuktā hyaṅgaistrayodaśabhiḥ । vīthī syādekāṅkā tathaikahāryā dvihāryā vā ।। adhamottamamadhyābhiryuktā syātprakṛtibhistisṛbhiḥ । uddhātyakāvalagitāvaspanditanālyasatpralāpāśca ।।
vākkelyatha prapañco mṛdavādhibale chalaṃ trigatam । vyāhāro gaṇḍaśca trayodaśāṅgānyudāhṛtānyasyāḥ ।। atha vīthī saṃproktā lakṣaṇameṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi । padāni tvagatārthāni ye narāḥ punarādarāt ।।
yojayanti padairanyaistaduddhātyakamucyate । yatrānyasmin samāveśya kāryamanyatprasādhyate ।। taccāvalagitaṃ nāma vijñeyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ । ākṣipte arthe tu kasmiṇścicchubhāśubhasamutthite ।।
kauśalāducyate anyo arthastadavaspanditaṃ bhavet । hāsyenopagatārthaprahelikā nāliketi vijñeyā ।। mūrkhajanasannikarṣe hitamapi yatra prabhāṣate vidvān । na ca gṛhyate asya vacanaṃ vijñeyo asatpralāpo asau ।।
ekadviprativacanā vākkelī syātprayoge asmin । yadasadbhūtaṃ vacanaṃ saṃstavayuktaṃ dvayoḥ parasparaṃ yattu ।। ekasya cārthahetoḥ sa hāsyajananaḥ prapañcaḥ syāt । yatkāraṇād guṇānāṃ doṣīkaraṇaṃ bhavedvivādakṛtam ।।
doṣaguṇīkaraṇaṃ vā tanmṛdavaṃ nāma vijñeyam । paravacanamātmanaścottarottarasamudbhavaṃ dvayoryatra ।। anyonyārthaviśeṣakamadhibalamiti tad budhairjñeyam । anyārthameva vākyaṃ chalamabhisandhānahāsyaroṣakaram ।।
śrutisārūpyādyasmin bahavo arthā yuktibhirniyujyante । yaddhāsyamahāsyaṃ vā tattrigataṃ nāma vijñeyam ।। pratyakṣavṛttirukto vyāhāro hāsyaleśārthaḥ । saṃrambhasaṃbhramayutaṃ vivādayuktaṃ tathāpavādakṛtam ।।
bahuvacanākṣepakṛtaṃ gaṇḍaṃ pravadanti tattvajñāḥ । iti daśarūpavidhānaṃ sarvaṃ proktaṃ mayā hi lakṣaṇataḥ । punarasya śarīragataṃ sandhividhau lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye ।। itivṛttaṃ tu nāṭyasya śarīraṃ parikīrtitam ।
pañcabhiḥ sandhibhistasya vibhāgaḥ samprakalpitaḥ ।। itivṛttaṃ dvidhā caiva budhastu parikalpayet । ādhikarikamekaṃ syāt prāsaṅgikamathāparam ।। yatkāryaṃ hi phalaprāptyā sāmarthyātparikalpyate ।
tadādhikārikaṃ jñeyamanyatprāsaṅgikaṃ viduḥ ।। kāraṇātphalayogyasya vṛttaṃ syādādhikārikam । tasyopakaraṇārthaṃ tu kīrtyate hyānuṣaṅgikam ।। kaveḥ prayatnānnetṝṇāṃ yuktānāṃ viddhyupāśrayāt ।
kalpyate hi phalaprāptiḥ samutkarṣātphalasya ca ।। (laukikī sukhaduḥkhākhyā yathāvasthā rasodbhavā । daśadhā manmathāvasthā vyavasthāstrividhā matā) ।। saṃsāre phalayāge tu vyāpāraḥ kāraṇasya yaḥ ।
tasyānupūrvyā vijñeyā pañcāvasthā prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। prārambhaśca prayatnaśca tathā prāpteśca saṃbhavaḥ । niyatā ca phalaprāptiḥ phalayogaśca pañcamaḥ ।। autsukyamātrabandhastu yadbījasya nibadhyate ।
mahataḥ phalayogasya sa phalārambha iṣyate ।। apaśyataḥ phalaprāptiṃ vyāpāro yaḥ phalaṃ prati । paraṃ cautsukyagamanaṃ sa prayatnaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। īṣatprāptiryadā kācitphalasya parikalpate ।
bhāvamātreṇa tu prāhurvidhijñāḥ prāptisambhavam ।। niyatāṃ tu phalaprāptiṃ yadā bhāvena paśyati । niyatāṃ tāṃ phalaprāptiṃ saguṇāṃ paricakṣate ।। abhipretaṃ samagraṃ ca pratirūpaṃ kriyāphalam ।
itivṛtte bhavedyasmin phalayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। sarvasyaiva hi kāryasya prārabdhasya phalārthibhiḥ । etāstvanukrameṇaiva pañcāvasthā bhavanti hi ।। āsāṃ svabhāvabhinnānāṃ parasparasamāgamāt ।
vinyāsa ekabhāvena phalahetuḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। itivṛttaṃ samākhyātaṃ pratyagevādhikārikam । tadārambhādi kartavyaṃ phalāntaṃ ca yathā bhavet ।। pūrṇasandhi ca kartavyaṃ hīnasandhyapi vā punaḥ ।
niyamāt pūrṇasandhi syāddhīnasandhyatha kāraṇāt ।। ekalope caturthasya dvilope tricaturthayoḥ । dvitīyatricaturthānāṃ trilope lopa iṣyate ।। prāsaṅgike parārthatvānna hyeṣa niyamo bhavet ।
yadvṛttaṃ sambhavettatra tadyojyamavirodhataḥ ।। itivṛtte yathāvasthāḥ pañcārambhādikāḥ smṛtāḥ । arthaprakṛtayaḥ pañca tathā bījādikā api ।। bījaṃ binduḥ patākā ca prakarī kāryameva ca ।
arthaprakṛtayaḥ pañca jñātvā yojyā yathāvidhi ।। svalpamātraṃ samutsṛṣṭaṃ bahudhā yadvisarpati । phalāvasānaṃ yaccaiva bījaṃ tatparikīrtitam ।। prayojanānāṃ vicchede yadavicchedakāraṇam ।
yāvatsamāptirbandhasya sa binduḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। yadvṛttaṃ tu parārthaṃ syāt pradhānasyopakārakam pradhānavacca kalpyeta sā patāketi kīrtitā ।। phalaṃ prakalpyate yasyāḥ parārthāyaiva kevalam । anubandhavihīnatvāt prakarīti vinirdiśet ।।
yadādhikārikaṃ vastu samyak prājñaiḥ prayujyate । tadartho yaḥ samārambhastatkāryaṃ parikīrtitam ।। eteṣāṃ yasya yenārtho yataśca guṇa iṣyate । tat pradhānaṃ tu kartavyaṃ guṇabhūtānyataḥ param ।।
eko aneko api vā sandhiḥ patākāyāṃ tu yo bhavet । pradhānārthānuyāyitvādanusandhiḥ prakīrtyate ।। āgarbhādāvimarśādvā patākā vinivartate । kasmādyasmānnibandho asyāḥ parārthaḥ parikīrtyate ।।
yatrārthe cintite anyasminstallinṅgo anyaḥ prayujyate । āgantukena bhāvena patākāsthānakaṃ tu tat ।। sahasaivārthasampattirguṇavatyupakārataḥ । patākāsthānakamidaṃ prathamaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
vacaḥ sātiśayaṃ kliṣṭaṃ kāvyabandhasamāśrayam । patākāsthānakamidaṃ dvitīayaṃ parikīrtitam ।। arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yatra līnaṃ savinayaṃ bhavet । śliṣṭapratyuttaropetaṃ tṛtīyamidamiṣyate ।।
dvyartho vacanavinyāsaḥ suśliṣṭaḥ kāvyayojitaḥ । upanyāsasuyuktaśca taccaturthamudāhṛtam ।। [yatra sātiśayaṃ vākyamarthopakṣepaṇaṃ bhavet । vināśidṛṣṭamante ca patākārdhaṃ tu tadbhavet ] ।।
catuṣpatākāparamaṃ nāṭake kāryayiṣyate । pañcabhiḥ sandhibhiryuktaṃ tāṃśca vakṣyāmyataḥ param ।। mukhaṃ pratimukhaṃ caiva garbho vimarśa eva ca । tathā nirvahaṇaṃ ceti nāṭake pañca sandhayaḥ ।।
[pañcabhiḥ sandhibhiryuktaṃ pradhānamanu kīrtyate । śeṣāḥ pradhānasandhīnāmanugrāhyanusandhayaḥ] ।। yatra bījasamutpattirnānārtharasasambhavā । kāvye śarīrānugatā tanmukhaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
bījasyodghāṭanaṃ yatra dṛṣṭanaṣṭamiva kvacit । mukhanyastasya sarvatra tadvai pratimukhaṃ smṛtam ।। udbhedastasya bījasya prāptiraprāptireva vā । punaścānveṣaṇaṃ yatra sa garbha iti saṃjñitaḥ ।।
garbhanirbhinnabījārtho vilobhanakṛto athavā । krodhavyasanajo vāpi sa vimarśa iti smṛtaḥ ।। samānayanamarthānāṃ mukhādyānāṃ sabījinām । nānābhāvottarāṇāṃ yadbhavennirvahaṇaṃ tu tat ।।
ete tu sandhayo jñeyā nāṭakasya prayoktṛbhiḥ । tathā prakaraṇāsyāpi śeṣāṇāṃ ca nibodhata ।। ḍimaḥ samavakāraśca catuḥsandhī prakīrtitau । na tayoravamarśastu kartavyaḥ kavibhiḥ sadā ।।
vyāyogehāmṛgau cāpi sadā kāryau trisandhikau । garbhāvamarśau na syātāṃ tayorvṛttiśca kaiśikī ।। dvisandhi tu prahasanaṃ vīthyaṅko bhāṇa eva ca । mukhanirvahane tatra kartavye kavibhiḥ sadā ।।
[vīthī caiva hi bhāṇaśca tathā prahasanaṃ punaḥ । kaiśikīvṛttihīnāni kāryāṇi kavibhiḥ sadā ] ।। evaṃ hi sandhayaḥ kāryā daśarūpe prayoktṛbhiḥ । punareṣāṃ tu sandhīnāmaṅgakalpaṃ nibodhadata ।।
sandhināṃ yāni vṛttāni pradeśeṣvanupūrvaśaḥ । svasampadguṇayuktāni tānyaṅgānyupadhārayet ।। iṣṭasyārthasya racanā vṛttāntasyānupakṣayaḥ । rāgaprāptiḥ prayogasya guhyānāṃ caiva gūhanam ।।
āścaryavadabhikhyānaṃ prakāśyānāṃ prakāśanam । aṅgānāṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ hyetad dṝṣṭaṃ śāstre prayojanam ।। aṅgahīno naro yadvannaivārambhakṣamo bhavet । aṅgahīnaṃ tathā kāvyaṃ na prayogakṣamaṃ bhavet ।।
udāttamapi tatkāvyaṃ syādaṅgaiḥ parivarjitam । hīnatvāddhi prayogasya na satāṃ rañjayenmanaḥ ।। kāvyaṃ yadapi hīnārthaṃ samyadaṅgaiḥ samanvitam । dīptatvāttu prayogasya śobhāmeti na saṃśayaḥ ।।
[tasmāt sandhipradeśeṣu yathāyogaṃ yathārasam । kavināṅgāni kāryāṇi samyaktāni nibodhata] ।। upakṣepaḥ parikaraḥ parinyāso vilobhanam । yuktiḥ prāptiḥ samādhānaṃ vidhānaṃ paribhāvanā ।।
udbhedaḥ karaṇaṃ bheda etānyaṅgāni vai mukhe । tathā pratimukhe caiva śṛṇutāṅgāni nāmataḥ ।। vilāsaḥ parisarpaśca vidhūtaṃ tāpanaṃ tathā । narma narmadyutiścaiva tathā pragayaṇaṃ punaḥ ।।
nirodhaścaiva vijñeyaḥ paryupāsanameva ca । puṣpaṃ vajramupanyāso varṇasaṃhāra eva ca ।। etāni vai pratimukhe garbhe aṅgāni nibodhata । abhūtāharaṇaṃ mārgo rūpodāharaṇe kramaḥ ।।
saṃgrahaścānumānaṃ ca prārthanākṣiptameva ca । toṭakādhibale caiva hyudvego vidravastathā ।। etānyaṅgāni vai garbhe hyavamarśe nibodhata । apavādaśca saṃpheṭo vidravaḥ śaktireva ca ।।
vyavasāyaḥ prasaṅgaśca dyutiḥ khedo niṣedhanam । virodhanamathādānaṃ chādanaṃ ca prarocanā ।। vyavahāraśca yuktiśca vimarśāṅgānyamūni ca । sandhirnirodho grathanaṃ nirṇayaḥ paribhāṣaṇam ।।
dyutiḥ prasāda ānandaḥ samayo hyupagūhanam । bhāṣaṇaṃ pūrvavākyaṃ ca kāvyasaṃhāra eva ca ।। praśastiriti saṃhāre jñeyānyaṅgāni nāmataḥ । catuṣṣaṣṭhi budhairjñeyānyetānyaṅgāni sandhiṣu ।।
[sampādanārthaṃ bījasya samyaksiddhikarāṇi ca । kāryāṇyetāni kavibhirvibhajyārthāni nāṭake ] ।। punareṣāṃ pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇāni yathākramam । kāvyārthasya samutpattirupakṣepa iti smṛtaḥ ।।
yadutpannārthabāhulyaṃ jñeyaḥ parikarastu saḥ । tanniṣpattiḥ parinyāso vijñeyaḥ kavibhiḥ sadā ।। guṇanirvarṇanaṃ caiva vilobhanamiti smṛtam । sampradhāraṇamarthānāṃ yuktirityabhidhīyate ।।
sukhārthasyābhigamanaṃ prāptirityabhisaṃjñitā । bījārthasyopagamanaṃ samādhānamiti smṛtam ।। sukhaduḥkhakṛto yo arthastadvidhānamiti smṛtam । kutūhalottarāvego vijñeyā paribhāvanā ।।
bījārthasya praroho yaḥ sa udbheda iti smṛtaḥ । prakṛtārthasamārambhaḥ karaṇaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।। saṃghātabhedanārtho yaḥ sa bheda iti kīrtitaḥ । [etāni tu mukhāṅgāni vakṣye pratimukhe punaḥ] ।।
samīhā ratibhogārthā vilāsa iti saṃjñitaḥ । dṛṣṭanaṣṭānusaraṇaṃ parisarpa iti smṛtaḥ ।। kṛtasyānunayasyādau vidhūtaṃ hyaparigrahaḥ । apāyadarśanaṃ yattu tāpanaṃ nāma tadbhaveet ।।
krīḍārthaṃ vihitaṃ yattu hāsyaṃ narmeti tatsmṛtam doṣapracchādanārthaṃ tu hāsyaṃ narmadyutiḥ smṛtā ।। uttarottaravākyaṃ tu bhavetpragayaṇaṃ punaḥ । yā tu vyasanasaṃprāptiḥ sa nirodhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। kruddhasyanunayo yastu bhavettatparyupāsanam ।
viśeṣavacanaṃ yattu tatpuṣpamiti saṃjñitam ।। pratyakṣarūkṣaṃ yadvākyaṃ vajraṃ tadabhidhīyate । upapattikṛto yo artha upanyāsaśca sa smṛtaḥ ।। cāturvarṇyopagamanaṃ varṇasaṃhāra iṣyate ।
kapaṭāpāśrayaṃ vākyamabhūtāharaṇaṃ viduḥ ।। tattvārthavacanaṃ caiva mārga ityabhidhīyate । citrārthasamavāye tu vitarko rūpamiṣyate । yatsātiśayavadvākyaṃ tadudāharaṇaṃ smṛtam ।।
bhāvatattvopalabdhistu krama ityabhidhīyate । sāmadānādisaṃpannaḥ saṃgrahaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। ratiharṣotsavānāṃ tu prārthanā prārthanā bhavet । garbhasyodbhedanaṃ yatsākṣiptirityabhidhīyate ।।
saṃrambhavacanaṃ caiva toṭakaṃ tviti saṃjñitam । kapaṭenātisaṃdhānaṃ bruvate adhibalaṃ budhāḥ ।। bhayaṃ nṛpāridasyūtthamudvegaḥ parikīrtitaḥ । śaṅkā bhayatrāsakṛto vidrayaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।।
doṣaprakhyāpanaṃ yattu so apavāda iti smṛtaḥ । roṣagrathitavākyaṃ tu saṃpheṭaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। guruvyatikramo yastu sa dravaḥ parikīrtitaḥ । virodhipraśamo yaśca sa śaktiḥ parikīrtitā ।।
vyavasāyaśca vijñeyaḥ pratijñāhetusaṃbhavaḥ । prasaṅgaścaiva vijñeyo gurūṇā parikīrtanam ।। vākyamādharṣasaṃyuktaṃ dyutistajjñairudāhṛtā । manaśceṣṭāviniṣpannaḥ śramaḥ kheda udāhṛtaḥ ।।
īpsitārthapratīghātaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । kāryātyayopagamanaṃ virodhanamiti smṛtam ।। bījakāryopagamanamātānamiti saṃjñitam । apamānakṛtaṃ vākyaṃ kāryārthaṃ cchādanaṃ bhavet ।।
prarocanā sa vijñeyā saṃhārārthapradarśinī । [pratyakṣavacanaṃ yattu sa vyāhāra iti smṛtaḥ ।। savicchedaṃ vaco yatra sā yuktiriti saṃjñitā । jñeyā vicalanā tajjñairavamānārthasaṃyuta] ।।
[etānyavamṛśe aṅgāni saṃhāre tu nibodhata] । mukhabījopagamanaṃ sandhirityabhidhīyate ।। kāryasyānveṣaṇaṃ yuktyā nirodha iti kīrtitaḥ । upakṣepastu kāryāṇāṃ grathanaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
anubhūtārthakathanaṃ nirṇayaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ । parivādakṛtaṃ yasyāttadāhuḥ paribhāṣaṇam ।। labdhasyārthasya śamanaṃ dyutimācakṣate punaḥ । samāgamastathārthānāmānandaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
duḥkhasyāpagamo yastu samayaḥ sa nigadyate । śuśrūṣādyupasaṃpannaḥ prasādaḥ prītirucyate ।। adbhutasya tu saṃprāptirūpagūhanamiṣyate । sāmadānādi saṃpannaṃ bhāṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam ।।
pūrvavākyaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ yathoktārthapradarśanam । varapradānasaṃprāptiḥ kāvyasaṃhāra iṣyate ।। nṛpadeśapraśāntiśca praśastirabhidhīyate । yathāsandhi tu kartavyānyetānyaṅgāni nāṭake ।।
kavibhiḥ kāvyakuśalai rasabhāvamapekṣya tu । saṃmiśrāṇi kadācittu dvitriyogena vā punaḥ ।। jñātvā kāryamavasthāṃ ca kāryāṇyaṅgāni sandhiṣu । eteṣāmeva cāṅgānāṃ saṃbaddhānyarthayuktitaḥ ।।
sandhyantarāṇi sandhīnāṃ viśeṣāstvekaviṃśatiḥ । sāmabhedastathā daṇḍaḥ pradānaṃ vadha eva ca ।। pratyutpannamatitvaṃ ca gotraskhalitameva ca । sāhasaṃ ca bhayaṃ caiva hrīrmāyā krodha eva ca ।।
ojaḥ saṃvaraṇaṃ bhrāntistathā hetvapadhāraṇam । dūto lekhastathā svapnaścitraṃ mada iti smṛtam ।। [viṣkambhacūlikā caiva tatha caiva praveśakaḥ । aṅkāvatāro aṅkamukhamarthopakṣepapañcakam ।।
madhyamapuruṣaniyojyo nāṭakamukhasandhimātrasaṃcāraḥ । viṣkambhakastu kāryaḥ purohitāmātyakañcukibhiḥ ।। śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo vā dvividho viṣkaṃbhakastu vijñeyaḥ । madhyamapātraiḥ śuddhaḥ saṃkīrṇo nīcamadhyakṛtaḥ ।।
antaryavanikāsaṃsthaiḥ sūtādibhiranekadhā । arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yattu kriyate sā hi cūlikā ।। aṅkāntarānusārī saṃkṣepārthamadhikṛtya bindūnām । prakaraṇanāṭakaviṣaye praveśako nāma vijñeyaḥ ।।
aṅkānta eva cāṅko nipatati yasmin prayogamāsādya । bījārthayuktiyukto jñeyo hyaṅkāvatāro asau ।। viṣliṣṭamukhamaṅkasya striyā vā puruṣeṇa vā । yadupakṣipyate pūrvaṃ tadaṅkamukhamucyate] ।।
anyānyapi lāsyavidhāvaṅgāni tu nāṭakopayogīni । asmādviniḥsṛtāni tu bhāṇa ivaiakaprayojyāni ।। [bhāṇākṛtivallāsyaṃ vijñeyaṃ tvekapātrahāryaṃ vā । prakaraṇavadūhya kāryāsaṃstavayuktaṃ vividhabhāvam] ।।
geyapadaṃ sthitapāṭhyamāsīnaṃ puṣpagaṇḍikā । pracchedakaṃ trimūḍhaṃ ca saindhavākhyaṃ dvimūḍhakam ।। uttamottamakaṃ caivamuktapratyuktameva ca । lāsye daśavidhaṃ hyetadaṅganirdeśalakṣaṇam ।।
āsaneṣūpaviṣṭairyattantrībhāṇḍopabṛṃhitam । gāyaneairgīyate śuṣkaṃ tadgeyapadamucyate ।। [yā nṛtyatyāsanā nārī geyaṃ priyaguṇānvitam । sāṅgopāṅgavidhānena tadgeyapadamucyate] ।।
prākṛtaṃ yadviyuktā tu paṭhedāttarasaṃ sthitā । madanānalataptāṅgī sthitapāṭhyaṃ taducyate ।। [bahucārīsamāyuktaṃ pañcapāṇikalānugam । cañcatpuṭena vā yuktaṃ sthitapāṭhyaṃ vidhīyate] ।।
āsīnamāsyate yatra sarvātodyavivarjitam । aprasāritagātraṃ ca cintāśokasamanvitam ।। nṛttāni vividhāni syurgeyaṃ gāne ca saṃśritan । ceṣṭābhiścāśrayaḥ puṃsā yatra sā puṣpagaṇḍikā ।।
[yatra strī naraveṣeṇa lalitaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ paṭhet । sakhīnāṃ tu vinodāya sā jñeyā puṣpagaṇḍikā ।। nṛttaṃ tu vividhaṃ yatra gītaṃ cātodyasaṃyutam । striyaḥ puṃvacca ceṣṭante sā jñeyā puṣpagaṇḍikā] ।।
pracchedakaḥ sa vijñeyo yatra candrātapāhatāḥ । striyaḥ priyeṣu sajjante hyapi vipriyakāriṣu ।। aniṣṭhuraślakṣṇapadaṃ samavṛttairalaṅkṛtam । nāṭyaṃ puruṣabhāvāḍhyaṃ trimūḍhakamiti smṛtam ।।
pātraṃ vibhraṣṭasaṃketaṃ suvyaktakaraṇānvitam । prākṛtairvacanairyuktaṃ viduḥ saindhavakaṃ budhāḥ ।। [rūpavādyādisaṃyuktaṃ pāṭhyena ca vivarjitam । nāṭyaṃ hi tattu vijñeyaṃ saindhavaṃ nāṭyakovidaiḥ] ।।
mukhapratimukhopetaṃ caturaśrapadakramam । śliṣṭabhāvarasopetaṃ vaicitryārthaṃ dvimūḍhake ।। uttamottamakaṃ vidyādanekarasasaṃśrayam । vicitraiḥ lokabandhaiśca helāhāvavicitritam ।।
kopaprasādajanitaṃ sādhikṣepapadāśrayam । uktapratyuktamevaṃ syāccitragītārthayojitam ।। yatra priyākṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā vinodayati mānasam । madanānalataptāṅgī taccitrapadamucyate ।।
dṛṣṭvā svapne priyaṃ yatra madanānalatāpitā । karotivividhān bhāvāṃstadvai bhāvikamucyate ।। eteṣāṃ lāsyavidhau vijñeyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ prayogajñaiḥ । tadihaiva tu yannauktaṃ prasaṅgavinivṛttahetostu ।।
pañcasandhi caturvṛtti catuḥṣaṣṭyaṅgasaṃyutam । ṣaṭtriṃśallakṣaṇopetaṃ guṇālaṅkārabhūṣitam ।। mahārasaṃ mahābhogamudāttavacanānvitam । mahāpuruṣasaṃcāraṃ sādhvācārajanapriyam ।।
suśliṣṭasandhisaṃyogaṃ suprayogaṃ sukhāśrayam । mṛduśabdābhidhānaṃ ca kaviḥ kuryāttu nāṭakam ।। avasthā yā tu lokasya sukhaduḥkhasamudbhavā । nānāpuruṣasaṃcārā nāṭake asau vidhīyate ।।
na tajjñānaṃ na tacchilpaṃ na sā vidyā na sā kalā । na tat karma na vā yogo nāṭye asimnyanna dṛśyate ।। yo ayaṃ svabhāvo lokasya nānāvasthāntarātmakaḥ । so aṅgādyabhinayairyukto nāṭyamityabhidhīyate ।।
devatānāmṛṣīnāṃ ca rājñāṃ cotkṛṣṭamedhasām । pūrvavṛttānucaritaṃ nāṭakaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।। yasmātsvabhāvaṃ saṃtyajya sāṅgopāṅgagatikramaiḥ । prayujyate jñāyate ca tasmādvai nāṭakaṃ smṛtam ।।
sarvabhāvaiḥ sarvarasaiḥ sarvakarmapravṛttibhiḥ । nānāvasthāntaropetaṃ nāṭakaṃ saṃvidhīyate ।। [anekaśilpajātāni naikakarmakriayāṇi ca । tānyaśeṣāṇi rūpāṇi kartavyāni prayoktṛbhiḥ ] ।।
lokasvabhāvaṃ saṃprekṣya narāṇāṃ ca balābalam । saṃbhogaṃ caiva yuktiṃ ca tataḥ kāryaṃ tu nāṭakam ।। bhaviṣyati yuge prāyo bhaviṣyantyabudhā narāḥ । ye cāpi hi bhaviṣyanti te yatnaśrutabuddhayaḥ ।।
karmaśilpāni śāstrāṇi vicakṣaṇabalāni ca । sarvāṇyetāni naśyanti yadā lokaḥ praṇaśyati ।। tadevaṃ lokabhāṣāṇāṃ prasamīkṣya balābalam । mṛduśabdaṃ sukhārthaṃ ca kaviḥ kuryāttu nāṭakam ।।
caikrīḍitādyaiḥ śabdaistu kāvyabandhā bhavanti ye । veśyā iva na te bhānti kamaṇḍaludharairdvijaiḥ ।। daśarūpavidhānaṃ ca mayā proktaṃ dvijottamāḥ । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vṛttīnāmiha lakṣaṇam ।।
samutthānaṃ tu vṛttīnāṃ vyākhyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ । yathā vastūdbhavaṃ caiva kāvyānāṃ ca vikalpanam ।। ekārṇavaṃ jagat kṛtvā bhagavānacyuto yadā । śete sma nāgaparyaṅke lokān saṃkṣipya māyayā ।।
atha vīryabalonmatāvasurau madhukaiaṭabhau । tarjayāmāsaturdevaṃ tarasā yuddhakāṅkṣayā ।। nijabāhū vimṛdanantau bhūtabhāvanamakṣayam । jānubhirmuṣṭibhiścaiva yodhayāmāsatuḥ prabhum ।।
bahubhiḥ paruṣairvākyairanyonyasamabhidravam । nānādhikṣepavacanaiḥ kampayantāvivodadhim ।। tayornānāprakārāṇi vacāṃsi vadatostadā । śrutvā tvabhihatamanā druhiṇo vākyamabravīt ।।
kimidaṃ bharatīvṛttirvāgbhireva pravartate । uttarottarasaṃbaddhā nanvimau nidhanaṃ nayaḥ ।। pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā provāca madhusūdanaḥ । kāryahetormayā brahman bhāratīyaṃ vinirmitā ।।
vadatāṃ vākyabhūyiṣṭhā bhāratīyaṃ bhaviṣyati । tasmādetau nihanmyadyetyuvāca vacanaṃ hariḥ ।। śuddhairavikṛtairaṅgaiḥ sāṅgahāraistathā bhṛśam । yodhayāmāsaturdaityau yuddhamārgaviśāradau ।।
bhūmisaṃyogasaṃsthānaiḥ padanyāsairharestadā । atibhāro abhavad bhūmerbhāratī tatra nirmitā ।। valgitaiḥ śārṅgadhanuṣastīvrairdīptatathairatha । satvādhikairasaṃbhrāntaiḥ sāttvatī tatra nirmitā ।।
vicitrairaṅgahāraistu devo līlāsamanvitaiḥ । babandha yacchikhāpāśaṃ kaiśikī tatra nirmitā ।। saṃrambhāvegabahulairnānācārī samutthitaiḥ । niyuddhakaraṇaiścitrairutpannārabhaṭī tataḥ ।।
yāṃ yāṃ devaḥ samācaṣṭe kriyāṃ vṛttiṣu saṃsthitām । tāṃ tadarthānugairjapyeairdruhiṇaḥ pratyapūjayat ।। yadā hatau tāvasurau hariṇā madhukaiṭabhau । tato abravīt padmayonirnārāyaṇamarindamam ।।
aho vicitrairviṣamaiḥ sphuṭaiḥ salalitairapi । aṅgahāraiḥ kṛtaṃ deva tvayā dānavanāśanam ।। tasmādayaṃ hi lokasya niyuddhasamayakramaḥ । sarvaśastravimokṣeṣu nyāyasaṃjño bhaviṣyati ।।
nyāyāśritairaṅgahārairnyāyāccaiva samutthitaiḥ । yasmādyuddhāni vartante tasmānyāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। [cārīṣu ca samutpanno nānācārīsamāśrayaḥ । nyāyasaṃjñaḥ kṛto hyeṣa druhiṇena mahātmanā ।।
tato vedeṣu nikṣiptā druhiṇena mahātmanā । punariṣvastrajāte ca nānācārīsamākule ।। punarnāṭyaprayogeṣu nānābhāvasamnvitāḥ । vṛttisaṃjñāḥ kṛtā hyetāḥ kāvyabandhasamāśrayāḥ] ।।
caritairyasya devasya japyaṃ yadyādṛśaṃ kṛtam । ṛṣibhistādṛśī vṛttiaḥ kṛtā pāṭhyādisaṃyutā ।। nāṭyavedasamutpanā vāgaṅgābhinayātmikā । mayā kāvyakriayāhetoḥ prakṣiptā druhiṇājñayā ।।
ṛgvedādbhāratī kṣiptā yajurvedācca sāttvatī । kaiśikī sāmavedācca śeṣā cātharvaṇādapi ।। yā vākpradhānā puruṣaprayojyā strīvarjitā saṃkṛtapāṭhyayuktā । svanāmadheyairbharataiḥ prayuktā sā bhāratī nāma bhavettu vṛttiḥ ।।
bhedāstasyāstu vijñeyāścatvāro aṅgatvamāgatāḥ । prarocanāmukhaṃ caiva vīthī prahasanaṃ tathā ।। jayābhyudayinī caiva maṅgalyā vijayāvahā । sarvapāpapraśamanī pūrvaraṅge prarocanā ।।
[upakṣepeṇa kāvyasya hetuyuktisamāśrayā । siddhenāmantraṇā yā tu vijñeyā sā prarocanā] ।। naṭī vidūṣako vāpi pāripārśvika eva vā । sūtradhāreṇa sahitāḥ saṃlāpaṃ yattu kurvate ।।
citrairvākyaiḥ svakāryārotthairvītthyaṅgeranyathāpi vā । āmukhaṃ tattu vijñeyaṃ budhaiḥ prastāvanāpi vā ।। [lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvamuktaṃ tu vītthyāḥ prahasanasya ca । āmukhāṅgānyato vakṣye yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ] ।।
uddhātyakaḥ kathoddhātaḥ prayogātiśayastathā । pravṛttakāvalagite pañcāṅgānyāmukhasya tu ।। uddhātyakāvalagitalakṣaṇaṃ kathitaṃ mayā । śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ viprā vyākhyāsyāmyānupūrvaśaḥ ।।
sutradhārasya vākyaṃ vā yatra vākyārthameva vā । gṛhītāṃ praviśetpātraṃ kathoddhātaḥ sa kīrtitaḥ ।। prayoge tu prayogaṃ tu sūtradhāraḥ prayojayet । tataśca praviśetpātraṃ prayogātiśayo hi saḥ ।।
kālapravṛttimāśritya varṇanā yā prayujyate । tadāśrayācca pātrasya praveśastatpravṛttakam ।। eṣāmanyatamaṃ śliṣṭaṃ yojayitvārthayuktibhiḥ । [tasmādaṅgadvayasyāpi sambhavo na nivāryate ।।
pātragranthairasaṃbādha prakuryādāmukhaṃ tataḥ । evametadbudhairjñeyamāmukhaṃ vividhāśrayam ।। lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvamuktaṃ tu vīthyāḥ prahasanasya ca । [ityaṣṭārdhavikalpā vṛttiriyaṃ bhāratī mayābhihitā ।
sāttvatyāstu vidhānaṃ lakṣaṇayuktyā pravakṣyāmi] ।। yā sāttvateneha guṇena yuktā nyāyena vṛttena samanvitā ca । harṣotkaṭā saṃhṛtaśokabhāvā sā sāttvatī nāma bhavettu vṛttiḥ ।। vāgaṅgābhinayavatī sattvotthānavacanaprakaraṇeṣu ।
sattvādhikārayuktā vijñeyā sāttvatī vṛttiḥ ।। vīrādbhutaraudrarasā nirastaśṛṅgārakaruṇanirvedā । uddhatapuruṣaprāyā parasparādharṣaṇakṛtā ca ।। utthāpakaśca parivartakaśca sallāpakaśca saṃghātyaḥ ।
catvāro asyā bhedā vijñeyā nāṭyakovidaiaḥ ।। ahamapyutthāsyāmi tvaṃ tāvaddarśayātmanaḥ śaktim । iti saṃgharṣasamutthastajjñairutthāpako jñeyaḥ ।। utthānasamārabdhānarthānutsṛjya yo arthayogavaśāt ।
anyānarthān bhajate sa cāpi parivartako jñeyaḥ ।। [nirdiṣṭavastuviṣayaḥ prapañcabaddhastrihāsyasaṃyuktaḥ । saṃgharṣaviśeṣakṛtastrividhaḥ parivartako jñeyaḥ] ।। sādharṣajo nirādharṣajo api vā rāgavacasaṃyuktaḥ ।
sādhikṣepālāpo jñeyaḥ sallāpakaḥ so api ।। [dharmādharmasamutthaṃ yatra bhavedrāgadoṣasaṃyuktam । sādhikṣepaṃ ca vaco jñeyaḥ saṃlāpako nāma] ।। mantrarthavākyaśaktyā daivavaśādātmadoṣayogādvā ।
saṃghātabhedajananastajjñaiḥ saṃghātyako jñeyaḥ ।। [bahukapaṭasaṃśrayāṇāṃ paropaghātāśayaprayuktānām । kūṭānāṃ saṃghāto vijñeyaḥ kūṭasaṃghātyaḥ ] ।। ityaṣṭārdhavikalpā vṛttiriyaṃ sāttvatī mayābhihitā ।
kaiśikyāstvatha lakṣaṇamataḥparaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi ।। yā ślakṣṇanaipathyaviśeṣacitrā strīsaṃyutā yā bahunṛttagītā । kāmopabhogaprabhavopacārā tāṃ kaiśikīṃ vṛttimudāharanti ।। [bahuvadyanṛttagītā śṛṅgārābhinayacitranaipathyā ।
mālyālaṅkārayuktā praśastaveṣā ca kāntā ca ।। citrapadavākyabandhairalaṅkṛtā hasitaruditaroṣādaiḥ । strīpuruṣakāmayuktā vijñeyā kaiśikīvṛttiḥ] ।। narma ca narmasphuñjo narmasphoṭo atha narmagarbhaśca ।
kaiśikyāścatvāro bhedā hyete samākhyātāḥ ।। āsthāpitaśṛṅgāraṃ viśuddhakaraṇaṃ nivṛttavīrarasam । hāsyapravacanabahulaṃ narma trividhaṃ vijānīyāt ।। īrṣyākrodhaprāyaṃ sopālambhakaraṇānuviddhaṃ ca ।
ātmopakṣepakṛtaṃ savipralambhaṃ smṛtaṃ narma ।। navasaṅgamasambhogo ratisamudayaveṣavākyasaṃyuktaḥ । jñeyo narmasphuñjo hyavasānabhayātmakaścaiva ।। vividhānāṃ bhavānāṃ lavairlavairbhūṣito bahuviśeṣaiḥ ।
asamagrākṣiptaraso narmasphoṭastu vijñeyaḥ ।। vijñānarūpaśobhā dhanādibhirnāyako gaṇairyatra । pracchanāṃ vyavaharte karyavaṣānnarmagarbho asau ।। [pūrvasthitau vipadyeta nāyako yatra cāparastiṣṭhet ।
tamapīha narmagarbhaṃ vidyānnāṭyaprayogeṣu ] ।। ityaṣṭārśavikalpā vṛttiriyaṃ kaiśikī mayābhihitā । ata ūrdhvamuddhatarasāmarabhaṭiṃ sampravakṣyyami ।। ārabhaṭaprāyaguṇā tathaiva bahukapaṭavañcanopetā ।
dambhānṛtavacanavatī tvārabhaṭī nāma vijñeyā ।। [āvapātāplulaṅgitāni cchedyāni māyākṛtamindrajālam । citrāṇī yuddhāni ca yatra nityaṃ tāṃ tādṛśīmārabhaṭīṃ vadanti ।। śāḍguṇyasamārbdhā haṭhātisandhānavidravopetā ।
lābhālābhārthakṛtā vijñeyā vṛttirārabhaṭī ।। saṃkṣiptakāvapatau vastūtthāpanamathāpi saṃpheṭaḥ । ete hyasyā bhedā lakṣaṇameṣaṃ pravakṣyāmi ।। anvarthaśilpayukto bahupustotthānacitranepathyaḥ ।
saṃkṣiptavastu viṣayo jñeyaḥ saṃkṣiptakao nāma ।। bhayaharṣasamutthānaṃ vidravavinipātasambhramācaraṇam । kṣiprapraveśanirgamamavapātamimaṃ vijānīyāt ।। sarvarasasamāsakṛtaṃ savidravvvidravāśrayaṃ vvapi ।
nāṭyaṃ vibhāvyate yattadvastūtthāpanaṃ jñeyam ।। saṃrambhasaṃprayukto bahuyuddhakapaṭanirbhedaḥ । śastrapraharabahulaḥ sampheṭo nāma vijñeyaḥ ।। evametā budhairjñeyā vṛttayo nāṭyasaṃśrayā ।
rasaprayogamāsāṃ ca kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। hāsyaśṛṅgarabahulā kaiśikī paricakṣitā । sattvatī cāpi vijñeyā vīrādbhutaśamāśrayāḥ ।। raudre bhayānake caiva vijñeyārabhaṭī budhaiḥ ।
bībhatse karuṇe caiva bhāratī saṃprakīrtitā ।। [ na hyekarasajaṃ kavyaṃ kiñcidasti prayogataḥ । bhāvo vāpi raso vāpi pravṛttirvṛttireva vā ।। sarveṣāṃ samavetānāṃ yasya rūpaṃ bhavedbahu ।
sa mantavyo rasa sthāyi śeṣāḥ sañcāriṇaḥ smṛtāḥ] ।। vṛtyanta eśo abhinayo mayokto vāgaṅgasattvaprabhavo yathāvad । āhāryamevābhinayaṃ prayoge vakṣyāmi nepathyakṛtaṃ tu bhūyaḥ ।। āhāryābhinayaṃ viprā vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।
ysmāt prayogaḥ sarvo ayamāhāryābhinaye sthitaḥ ।। nānāvasthā prakṛtaya pūrvaṃ naipathyasādhitāḥ । aṅgādibhirabhivyaktimupagacchantyayatnataḥ ।। āhāryābhinayo nāma jñeyo nepathyajo vidhiḥ ।
tatra kāryaḥ prayatnastu nāṭyasya śubhamicchatā ।। [tasminyatnastu kartavyo naipathye siddhimicchatā । nāṭyasyeha tvalaṅkāro naipathyaṃ yatprakīrtitam] ।। caturvidhaṃ tu nepathyaṃ pusto alaṅkāra eva ca ।
tathāṅkaracanā caiva jñeyaṃ sajjīvameva ca ।। pustastu trividho jñeyo nānārūpapramāṇataḥ । sandhimo vyājimaścaiva veṣṭimaśca prakīrtitaḥ ।। kiliñjacarmavastrādyairyadrūpaṃ kriyate budhaiḥ ।
sandhimo nāma vijñeyaḥ pusto nāṭakasaṃsśrayaḥ ।। vyājimo nāma vijñeayo yantreṇa kriyate tu yaḥ । veṣṭyate caiva yadrupaṃ veṣṭimaḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ ।। śailayānavimānāni carmavarmadhvajā nagāḥ ।
ye kriyante hi nāṭye tu sa pusta iti saṃjñitaḥ ।। alaṅkārastu vijñeyo mālyābharaṇavāsasām । nānāvidhaḥ samāyogo apyaṅgopāṅgavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। veṣṭimaṃ vitataṃ caiva saṃghātyaṃ granthimaṃ tathā ।
prālambitaṃ tathā caiva mālyaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam ।। caturvidhaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ nāṭye hyābharaṇaṃ budhaiḥ । āvedhyaṃ bandhanīyaṃ ca kṣepyamāropyameva ca ।। āvedhyaṃ kuṇḍalādīha yatsyācchravaṇabhūṣaṇam ।
āropyaṃ hemasūtrādi hārāśca vividhāśrayāḥ ।। śroṇīsūtrāṅgade muktābandhanīyāni sarvadā । prakṣepya nūpuraṃ vidyādvastrābharaṇameva ca ।। bhūṣaṇānāṃ vikalpaṃ hi puruṣastrīsamāśrayam ।
nāvidhaṃ pravakṣyāmi deśajātisamudbhavam ।। cūḍāmaṇiḥ samukuṭaḥ śiraso bhūṣaṇaṃ smṛtam । kuṇḍalaṃ mocakaṃ kīlā karṇābharaṇamiṣyate ।। muktāvalī harṣakaṃ ca sūtrakaṃ kaṇṭhabhūṣaṇam ।
vetikāṅgulimudrā ca syādaṅgulivibhūṣaṇam ।। hastalī valayaṃ caiva bāhunālīvibhūṣaṇam । rucakaścūlikā kāryā maṇibandhavibhūṣaṇam ।। keyūre aṅgade caiva kūrparoparibhūṣaṇe ।
trisaraścaiva hāraśca tathā vakṣovibhūṣaṇam ।। vyālambamauktiko hāro mālā caivāṅgabhūṣaṇam । talakaṃ sūtrakaṃ caiva bhavetkaṭivibhūṣaṇam ।। ayaṃ puruṣaniryogaḥ kāryastvābharaṇāśrayaḥ ।
devānāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca punarvakṣyāmi yoṣitām ।। śikhāpāśaṃ śikhāvyālaṃ piṇḍīpatraṃ tathaiva ca । cūḍāmaṇirmakarikā muktājālagavākṣikam ।। śiraso bhūṣaṇaṃ caiva vicitraṃ śīrṣajolakam ।
kaṇḍakaṃ śikhipatraṃ ca veṇīpucchaḥ sadorakaḥ ।। lalāṭatilakaṃ caiva nānāśilpaprayojitam । bhrūgucchoparigucchaśca kusumānukṛtistathā ।। karṇikā karṇavalayaṃ tathā syātpatrakarṇikā ।
kuṇḍalaṃ karṇamudrā ca karṇotkīlakameva ca ।। nānāratnavicitrāṇi dantapatrāṇi caiva hi । karṇayorbhūṣaṇaṃ hyetatkarṇapūrastathaiva ca ।। tilakāḥ patralekhāśca bhavedgaṇḍavibhūṣaṇam ।
trivaṇī caiva vijñeyaṃ bhavedvakṣovibhūṣaṇam ।। netrayorañjanaṃ jñeyamadharasya ca rañjanam । dantānāṃ vividho rāgaścaturṇāṃ śuklatāpi vā ।। rāgāntaravikalpo atha śobhanenādhikojvalaḥ ।
mugdhānāṃ sundarīṇāṃ ca muktābhāsitaśobhanāḥ ।। suraktā vāpi dantā syuḥḥ padmapallavarañjanāḥ । aśmarāgoddyotitaḥ syādadharaḥ pallavaprabhaḥ ।। vilāsaśca bhavettāsāṃ savibhrāntanirīkṣitam ।
muktāvalī vyālapaṅktirmañjarī ratnamālikā ।। ratnāvalī sūtrakaṃ ca jñeyaṃ kaṇṭhavibhūṣaṇam । dvisarastrisaraścaiva catussarakameva ca ।। tathā śṛṅkhalikā caiva bhavetkaṇṭhavibhūṣaṇam ।
aṅgadaṃ valayaṃ caiva bāhumūlavibhūṣaṇam ।। nānāśilpakṛtāścaiva hārā vakṣovibhūṣaṇam । maṇijālāvanaddhaṃ ca bhavet stanavibhūṣaṇam ।। kharjūrakaṃ socchitikaṃ bāhunālīvibhūṣaṇam ।
kalāpī kaṭakaṃ śaṅkho hastapatraṃ sapūrakam ।। mudrāṅgulīyakaṃ caiva hyaṅgulīnāṃ vibhūṣaṇam । muktājālāḍhyatalakaṃ mekhalā kāñcikāpi vā ।। raśanā ca kalāpaśca bhavecchroṇīvibhūṣaṇam ।
ekayaṣṭirbhavetkāñcī mekhalā tvaṣṭayaṣṭikā ।। dviraṣṭayaṣṭi raśanā kalāpaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ । dvātriṃśacca catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tathā ।। muktāhārā bhavantyete devapārthivayoṣitām ।
nūpuraḥ kiṅkiṇīkāśca ghaṇṭikā ratnajālakam ।। saghoṣe kaṭake caiva gulphoparivibhūṣāṇam । jaṅghayoḥ pādapatraṃ syādaṅgulīṣvaṅgulīyakam ।। aṅguṣṭhatilakāścaiva pādayośca vibhūṣaṇam ।
tathālaktakarāgaśca nānābhaktiniveśitaḥ ।। aśokapalāvacchāyaḥ syāt svābhāvika eva ca । etadvibhūṣaṇaṃ nāryā ākeśādānakhādapi ।। yathābhavarasāvasthaṃ vijñeyaṃ dvijasattamāḥ ।
āgamaśca pramāṇaṃ ca rūpanirvarṇanaṃ tathā ।। viśvakarmamatātkāryaṃ subuddhyāpi prayoktṛbhiḥ । na hi śakyaṃ suvarṇena muktābhirmaṇibhistathā ।। svādhīnamiti rucyaiva kartumaṅgasya bhūṣaṇam ।
vibhāgato abhiprayuktamaṅgaśobhākaraṃ bhavet ।। yathā sthānāntaragataṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ ratnasaṃyutam । na tu nāṭyaprayogeṣu kartavyaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ guru ।। khedaṃ janayate taddhi savyāyataviceṣṭanāt ।
gurubhāvāvasannasya svedo mūrchā ca jāyate ।। gurvābharaṇasanno hi ceṣṭāṃ na kurute punaḥ । tasmāttanutvacakṛtaṃ sauvarṇaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ bhavet ।। ratnavajjatubaddhaṃ vā na khedajananaṃ bhavet ।
svecchayā bhūṣaṇavidhirdivyānāmupadiśyate ।। yatnabhāvaviniṣpannaṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam । [veṣṭitaṃ vitataṃ caiva saṃghātyaṃ grathimaṃ tatha ।। lambaśobhi tathā caiva mālyaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam ।
ācchādanaṃ bahuvidhaṃ nānāpattanasaṃbhavam ।। tajjñeyaṃ triprakāraṃ tu śuddhaṃ raktaṃ vicitritam] । divyānāṃ bhūṣaṇavidhirya eṣa parikīrtitaḥ ।। mānuṣāṇāṃ tu kartavyo nānādeśasamāśrayaḥ ।
bhūṣaṇaiścāpi veṣaiśca nānāvasthāsamāśrayaiḥ ।। divyāṅganānāṃ kartavyā vibhaktiḥ svasvabhūmijā । vidyādharīṇāṃ yakṣīṇāmapsaronāgayoṣitām ।। ṛṣidaivatakanyānāṃ veṣairnānātvamiṣyate ।
tathā ca siddhagandharvarākṣasāsurayoṣitām ।। divyānāṃ naranārīṇāṃ tathaiva ca śikhaṇḍakam । śikhāpuṭaśikhaṇḍaṃ tu muktābhūyiṣṭhabhūṣaṇam ।। vidyādharīṇāṃ kartavyaḥ śuddho veṣaparicchadaḥ ।
yakṣiṇyo apsaraścaiva karyā ratnavibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। samastānāṃ bhavedveṣo yakṣīṇā kevalaṃ śikhā । divyanāmiva kartavyaṃ nāgastrīṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam ।। muktāmaṇilatāprāyāḥ phaṇāstāsāṃ tu kevalāḥ ।
kāryaṃ tu munikanyānāmekaveṇīdharaṃ śiraḥ ।। na cāpi vibhūṣaṇavidhistāsāṃ veṣo vanocitaḥ । muktāmarakataprāyaṃ maṇḍanaṃ siddhayoṣitām ।। tāsāṃ tu caiva kartavyaṃ pītavastraparicchadam ।
padmarāgamaṇiprāyaṃ gandharvīṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam ।। vīṇāhastaśca kartavyaḥ kausumbhavasanastathā । indranīlaistu kartavyaṃ rākṣasīṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇam ।। sitadaṃṣṭrā ca kartavyā kṛṣṇavastraparicchadam ।
vaiḍūryamuktābharaṇāḥ kartavyā surayoṣitām ।। śukapiñchanibhaiarvastraiḥ kāryastāsāṃ paricchadaḥ । puṣyarāgaistu maṇibhiḥ kvacidvaiḍūryabhūṣitaiḥ ।। divyavānaranārīṇāṃ kāryo nīlaparicchadaḥ ।
evaṃ śṛṅgāriṇaḥ kāryā veṣā divyāṅganāśrayāḥ ।। avasthāntamāsādya śuddhāḥ kāryāḥ punastathā । mānuṣīṇāṃ tu kartavyā nānādeśasamudbhavāḥ ।। veṣābharaṇasaṃyogān gadatastānnibodhata ।
āvantyayuvatīnāṃ tu śirassālakakuntalam ।। gauḍīyānāmalakaprāyaṃ saśikhāpāśaveṇikam । ābhīrayuvatīnāṃ tu dviveṇīdhara eva tu ।। śiraḥ parigamaḥ kāryo nīlaprāyamathāmbaram ।
tathā pūrvotarastrīṇāṃ samunnaddhaśikhaṇḍakam ।। ākeśācchādanaṃ tāsāṃ deśakarmaṇi kīrtitam । tathaiva dakṣiṇastrīṇāṃ kāryamullekhyasaṃśrayam ।। kumbhībandhakasaṃyuktaṃ tathāvartalalāṭikam ।
[gaṇikānāṃ tu kartavyamicchāvicchitti maṇḍanam] ।। deśajātividhānena śeṣāṇāmapi kārayet । veṣaṃ tathā cābharaṇaṃ kṣurakarma paricchadam ।। [āgamaṃ cāpi naipathye nāṭyasyaivaṃ prayojayet] ।
adeśayukto veṣo hi na śobhāṃ janayiṣyati ।। mekhalorasi baddhā tu hāsyaṃ samupapādayet । tathā proṣitakāntāsu vyasanābhihatāsu ca ।। veṣo vai malinaḥ kārya ekaveṇīdharaṃ śiraḥ ।
vipralambhe tu nāryāstu śuddho veṣo bhavediha ।। nātyābharaṇasaṃyukto na cāpi mṛjayānvitaḥ । evaṃ strīṇāṃ bhavedveṣo deśāvasthāsamudbhavaḥ ।। puruṣāṇāṃ punaścaiva veṣānvakṣyāmi tattvataḥ ।
tatrāṅkaracanā pūrvaṃ kartavyā nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ।। tataḥ paraṃ prayoktavyā veṣā deśasamudbhavāḥ । sito nīlaśca pītaśca caturtho rakta eva ca ।। ete svabhāvajā varṇā yaiḥ kāryaṃ tvaṅgavartanam ।
saṃyogajāḥ punaścānye upavarṇā bhavanti hi ।। tānahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi yathākāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । sitanīlasamāyoge kāraṇḍava iti smṛtaḥ ।। sitapītasāmāyogātpāṇḍuvarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।
sitiaraktasamāyoge padmavarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। pītanīlasamāyogāddharito nāma jāyate । nīlaraktasamāyogātkaṣāyo nāma jāyate ।। raktapītasamāyogādgauravarṇa iti smṛtaḥ ।
ete saṃyogajā varṇā hyupavarṇāstathāpare ।। tricaturvarṇasaṃyuktā bahavaḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ । balastho yo bhavedvarṇastasya bhāgo bhavettataḥ ।। durbalasya ca bhāgau dvau nīlaṃ muktvā pradāpayet ।
nīlasyaiko bhavedbhāgaścatvāro anye tu varṇake ।। balavānsarvavarṇānāṃ nīla eva prakīrtitaḥ । evaṃ varṇavidhiṃ jñātvā nānāsaṃyogasaṃśrayam ।। tataḥ kuryādyathāyogamaṅgānāṃ vartanaṃ budhaḥ ।
vartanacchādanaṃ rūpaṃ svaveṣaparivarjitam ।। nāṭyadharmapravṛttaṃ tu jñeyaṃ tatprakṛtisthitam । svavarṇamātmanaśchādyaṃ varṇakairveṣasaṃśrayaiḥ ।। ākṛtistasya kartavyā yasya prakṛtirāsthitā ।
yathā jantuḥ svabhāvaṃ svaṃ parityajyānyadaihikam ।। tatsvabhāvaṃ hi bhajate dehāntaramupāśritaḥ । veṣeṇa varṇakaiścaiva cchāditaḥ puruṣastathā ।। parabhāvaṃ prakurute yasya veṣaṃ samāśritaḥ ।
devadānavagandharvayakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ ।। prāṇisaṃjñāḥ smṛtā hyete jīvabandhāśca ye apare । [strībhāvāḥ parvatāḥ nadyaḥ samudrā vāhanāni ca ।। nānāśastrāṇyapi tathā vijñeyāḥ prāṇisaṃjñayā] ।
śailaprāsādayantrāṇi carmavarmadhvajāstathā ।। nānāpraharaṇādyāśca te aprāṇina iti smṛtāḥ । athavā kāraṇopetā bhavantyete śarīriṇaḥ ।। veṣabhāṣāśrayopetā nāṭyadharmamavekṣya tu ।
varṇānāṃ tu vidhiṃ jñātvā vayaḥ prakṛtimeva ca ।। kuryādaṅgasya racanāṃ deśajātivayaḥśritatām । devā gaurāstu vijñeyā yakṣāścāpsarastathā ।। rudrārkadruhiṇaskandāstapanīyaprabhāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
somo bṛhaspatiḥ śukro varuṇastārakāgaṇāḥ ।। samudrahimavadgaṅgāḥ śvetā hi syurbalastathā । raktamaṅgārakaṃ vidyāt pītau budhahutāśanau ।। nārāyaṇo naraścaiva śyāmo nāgaśca vāsukiḥ ।
daityāśca dānavāścaiva rākṣasā guhyakā nagāḥ ।। piśācā jalamākāśamasitāni tu varṇataḥ । bhavanti ṣaṭsu dvīpeṣu puruṣaścaiva varṇataḥ ।। kartavyā nāṭyayogena niṣṭaptakanakaprabhāḥ ।
jāmbūdvīpasya varṣe tu nānāvarṇāśrayā narāḥ ।। uttarāṃstu kurustyaktvā te cāpi kanakaprabhāḥ । bhadrāśvapuruṣāḥ śvetāḥ kartavyā varṇatastathā ।। ketumāle narā nīlā gaurāḥ śeṣeṣu kīrtitāḥ ।
nānāvarṇāḥ smṛtā bhūtā gandharvā yakṣapannagāḥ ।। vidyādharāstathā caiva pitarastu samā narāḥ । punaśca bhārate varṣe tāṃstānvarṇānnibodhata ।। rājānaḥ padmavarṇāstu gaurāḥ śyāmāstathaiva ca ।
ye cāpi sukhino martyā gaurā kāryāstu vaiḥ budhaiḥ ।। kukarmiṇo grahagrastāḥ vyādhitāstapasi sthitāḥ । āyastakarmiṇaścaiva hyasitāśca kujātayaḥ ।। ṛṣyayaścaiva kartavyā nityaṃ tu badaraprabhāḥ ।
tapaḥsthitāśca ṛṣayo nityāmevāsitā budhaiḥ ।। kāraṇavyapadeśena tathā cātmecchayā punaḥ । varṇastatra prakartavyo deśajativaśānugaḥ ।। deśaṃ karma ca jātiṃ ca pṛthivyuddeśasaṃśrayam ।
vijñāya vartanā kāryā puruṣāṇāṃ prayogataḥ ।। kirātabarbarāndhrāśca draviḍāḥ kāśikosalāḥ । pulindā dākṣiṇātyāśca prāyeṇa tvasitāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। śakāśca yavanāścaiva pahlavā vāhlikāśca ye ।
prāyeṇa gaurāḥ kartavyā uttarā ye śritā diśam ।। pāñcālāḥ śaurasenāśca māhiṣāścauḍramāgadhāḥ । aṅgā vaṅgāḥ kaliṅgāśca śyāmāḥ kāryāstu varṇataḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścaiva gaurāḥ kāryāstathaiva hi ।
vaiśyāḥ śūdrāstathā caiva śyāmāḥ kāryāstu varṇataḥ ।। evaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ mukhāṅgopāṅgavartanām । śmaśrukarma prayuñjīta deśakālavayo anugam ।। śuddhaṃ vicitraṃ śyāmaṃ ca tathā romaśameva ca ।
bhaveccaturvidhaṃ śmaśru nānāvasthāntarātmakam ।। śuddhaṃ tu liṅgināṃ kāryaṃ tathāmātyapurodhasām । madhyasthā ye ca puruṣā ye ca dīkṣāṃ samāśritāḥ ।। divyā ye puruṣāḥ kecitsiddhavidyādharādayaḥ ।
pārthivāśca kumārāśca ye ca rājopajīvinaḥ ।। śṛṅgāriṇaśca ye martyā yauvanonmādinaśca ye । teṣāṃ vicitraṃ kartavyaṃ śmaśru nāṭyaprayoktṛbhiḥ ।। anistīrṇapratijñānāṃ duḥkhitānāṃ tapasvinām ।
vyasanābhihatānāṃ ca śyāmaṃ śmaśru prayojayet ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ tāpasānāṃ ca ye ca dīrghavratā narāḥ । tathā ca cīrabaddhānāṃ romaśaṃ śmaśru kīrtitam ।। evaṃ nānāprakāraṃ tu śmaśru kāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।
