ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi veṣānnānāprayogajān ।। śuddho vicitro malinastrividho veṣa ucyate । teṣāṃ niyogaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। devābhigamane caiva maṅgale niyamasthite ।
tithinakṣatrayoge ca vivāhakaraṇe tathā ।। dharmapravṛttaṃ yatkarma striyo vā puruṣasya vā । veṣasteṣāṃ bhavecchuddho ye ca prāyatnikā narāḥ ।। devadānavayakṣāṇāṃ gandharvoragarakṣasām ।
nṛpāṇāṃ karkaśānāṃ ca citro veṣa udāhṛtaḥ ।। vṛddhānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca śreṣṭhyamātyapurodhasām । vaṇijāṃ kāñcukīyānāṃ tathā caiva tapasvinām ।। viprakṣetriyavaiśyānāṃ sthānīyā ye ca mānavāḥ ।
śuddho vastravidhisteṣāṃ kartavyo nāṭakāśrayaḥ ।। unmattānāṃ pramattānāmadhvagānāṃ tathaiva ca । vyasanopahatānāṃ ca malino veṣa ucyate ।। śuddharaktavicitrāṇi vāsāṃsyūrdhvāmbarāṇi ca ।
yojayennāṭyatattvajño veṣayoḥ śuddhacitrayoḥ ।। kuryādveṣe tu maline malinaṃ tu vicakṣaṇaḥ । muninirgranthaśākyeṣu yatipāśupateṣu ca ।। vratānugastu kartavyo veṣo lokasvabhāvataḥ ।
cīravalkalacarmāṇi tāpasānāṃ tu yojayet ।। parivāṇmuniṣkyānāṃ vāsaḥ kāṣāyamiṣyate । nānācitrāṇi vāsāṃsi kuryātpāśupateṣvatha ।। kujātayaśca ye proktāsteṣāṃ caiva yathārhataḥ ।
antaḥpurapraveśe ca viniyuktā hi ye narāḥ ।। kāṣāyakañcukapaṭāḥ kāryāste api yathāvidhi । avasthānatarataścaiva nṛṇāṃ veṣo bhavedatha ।। veṣaḥ sāṃgrāmikaścaiva śūrāṇāṃ saṃprakīrtitaḥ ।
vicitraśastrakavaco baddhatūṇo dhanurdharaḥ ।। citro veṣastu kartavyo nṛpāṇāṃ nityameva ca । kevalastu bhavecchuddho nakṣatrotpātamaṅgale ।। evameṣa bhavedveṣo deśajātivayo anugaḥ ।
uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ strīṇāṃ nṛṇāmathāpi ca ।। evaṃ vastravidhiḥ kāryaḥ prayoge nāṭakāśraye । nānāvasthāṃ samāsādya śubhāśubhakṛtastathā ।। tathā pratiśiraścāpi kartavyaṃ nāṭakāśrayam ।
divyānāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca deśajātivayaḥśritam ।। pārśvāgatā mastakinastathā caiva kirīṭinaḥ । trividho mukuṭo jñeyo divyapārthivasaṃśritaḥ ।। devagandharvayakṣāṇāṃ pannagānāṃ sarakṣasām ।
kartavyā naikavihiata mukuṭāḥ pārśvamaulayaḥ ।। uttamā ye ca divyānāṃ te ca kāryāḥ kirīṭinaḥ । madhyamā maulinaścaiva kaniṣṭhāḥ ṣirṣamaulinaḥ ।। narādhipānāṃ kartavyā mastake mukuṭā budhaiḥ ।
vidyādharāṇāṃ ca siddhānāṃ cāraṇānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। granthimatkeśamukuṭāḥ kartavyāstu prayoktṛbhiḥ । rākṣodānavadaityānāṃ piṅgakeśekṣaṇāni hi ।। haricchśmaśrūṇi ca tathā mukuṭāsyāni kārayet ।
uttamaścāpi ye tatra te kāryāḥ pārśvamaulinaḥ ।। kasmāttu mukuṭāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ prayoge divypārthive । keśānāṃ chedanaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ vedavāde yathāśruti ।। bhadrīkṛtasya vā yajñe śirasaśchādanecchayā ।
keśānāmapyadīrghatvātsmṛtaṃ mukuṭadhāraṇam ।। senāpateḥ punaścāpi yuvarājasya caiva hi । yojayedardhamukuṭaṃ mahāmātrāśca ye narāḥ ।। amātyānāṃ kañcukināṃ tathā śreṣṭhipurodhasām ।
veṣṭanābaddhapaṭṭāni pratiśīrṣāṇi kārayet ।। piśāconmattabhūtānāṃ sādhakānāṃ tapasvinām । anistīrṇapratijñānāṃ lambakeśaṃ bhavecchiraḥ ।। śākyaśrotriyanirgranthaparivrāḍdīkṣiteṣu ca ।
śiromuṇḍaṃ tu kartavyaṃ yajñadīkṣānviteṣu ca ।। tathā vratānugaṃ caiva śeṣānāṃ liṅgināṃ śiraḥ । muṇḍaṃ vā kuñcitaṃ vāpi lambakeśamathāpi vā ।। dhūrtānāṃ caiva kartavyaṃ ye ca rātryupajīvinaḥ ।
śṛṅgāracittāḥ puruṣāsteṣāṃ kuñcitamūrdhajāḥ ।। bālānāmapi kartavyaṃ triśikhaṇḍavibhūṣitam । jaṭāmakuṭabaddhaṃ ca munīnāṃ tu bhavecchiraḥ ।। ceṭānāmapi kartavyaṃ triśikhaṃ muṇḍameva vā ।
vidūṣakasya khalatiḥ syātkākapadameva vā ।। śeeṣāṇāmarthayogena deśajātisamāśrayam । śiraḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ kāryaṃ nānāvasthāntarāśrayam ।। bhūṣaṇairvarṇakairvastrairmālyaiścaiva yathāvidhi ।
evaṃ nānāprakāraistu buddhyā veṣānprakalpayet ।। pūrvaṃ tu prakṛtiṃ sthāpya prayogaguṇasaṃbhavām । strīṇāṃ vā puruṣāṇāṃ vāpyavasthāṃ prāpya tādṛśīm ।। sarve bhāvāśca divyānāṃ kāryā mānuṣasaṃśrayāḥ ।
teṣāṃ cānimiṣatvādi naiva kāryaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। iha bhāvarasāścaiva dṛṣṭibhiḥ saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ । dṛṣṭyaiva sthāpito hyarthaḥ paścādaṅgairvibhāvyate ।। evaṃ jñeeyāṅgaracanā nānāprakṛtisaṃbhavā ।
sajīva iti yaḥ proktastasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। yaḥ prāṇināṃ praveśo vai sajīva iti saṃjñitaḥ । catuṣpado atha dvipadastathā caivāpadaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। uragānapadān vidyād dvipadānkhagamānuṣān ।
grāmyā āraṇyāḥ paśavo vijñeyāḥ syuścatuṣpadāḥ ।। ye te tu yaddhasaṃpheṭairuparodhaistathaiva ca । nānāpraharaṇopetāḥ prayojyā nāṭake budhaiḥ ।। āyudhāni ca kāryāṇi puruṣāṇāṃ pramāṇataḥ ।
tānyahaṃ vartayiṣyāmi yathāpustapramāṇataḥ ।। bhiṇḍirdvādaśatālaḥ syāddaśa kunto bhavedatha । aṣṭau śataghnī śūlaṃ ca tomaraḥ śaktireva vā ।। aṣṭau tālā dhanurjñeyamāyāmo asya dvihastakaḥ ।
śaro gadā ca vajrā ca catustālaṃ vidhīyate ।। aṅgulāni tvasiḥ kāryaścatvāriṃśatpramāṇataḥ । dvādaśāṅgulakaṃ cakraṃ tato ardhaṃ prāsa iṣyate ।। prāsavatpaṭṭasaṃ vidyāddaṇḍaścaiva tu viṃśatiḥ ।
viṃśatiḥ kaṇayaścaiva hyaṅgulāni pramāṇataḥ ।। śoḍaṣāṅgulavistīrṇaṃ sabalaṃ saṃpraghaṇṭikam । triṃśadaṅgulimānena kartavyaṃ kheṭakaṃ budhaiḥ ।। jarjaro daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ ca tathaiva pratiśīrṣakam ।
chatraṃ cāmaraṃ caiva dhvajo śṛṅgāra eva ca ।। yatkiñcinmānuṣe loke dravyaṃ puṃsāṃ prayojakam । yaccopakaraṇaṃ sarve nāṭye tatsaṃprakīrtitam ।। yadyasya viṣayaprāptaṃ tenohyaṃ tasya lakṣaṇam ।
jarjare daṇḍakāṣṭhe ca saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। māhendrā vai dhvajāj proktā lakṣaṇairviśvakarmaṇā । eṣānyatamaṃ kuryājjarjaraṃ dārukarmataḥ ।। athavā vṛkṣayoniḥ syātpraroho vāpi jarjaraḥ ।
veṇureva bhavecchreṣṭhastasya vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। śvetabhūmyāāṃ tu yo jātaḥ puṣyanakṣatrajastathā । saṃgrāhyo vai bhavedveṇurjarjarārthe prayatnataḥ ।। pramāṇamaṅgulānāṃ tu śatamaṣṭottaraṃ bhavet ।
pañcaparvā caturgranthistālamātrastathaiva ca ।। sthūlagranthirna kartavyo na śākhī na ca kīṭavān । na kṛmikṣataparvā ca na hīnaścānyaveṇubhiḥ ।। madhusarpissarṣapāktaṃ mālyadhūpapuraskṛtam ।
upāsya vidhivadveṇuṃ gṛhṇiyājjarjaraṃ prati ।। yo vidhiryaḥ kramaścaiva māhebdre tu dhvaje smṛtaḥ । sa jarjarasya kartavyaḥ puṣyaveṇusamāśrayaḥ ।। bhavedyo dīrghaparvā tu tanupatrastathaiva ca ।
parvāgrataṇḍulaścaiva puṣyaveṇuḥ sa kīrtitaḥ ।। vidhireṣa mayā prokto jarjarasya pramāṇatajḥ । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi daṇḍakāṣṭhasya lakṣaṇam ।। kapitthabilvavaṃśebhyo daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ bhavedatha ।
vakraṃ caiva hi kartavyaṃ tribhāge lakṣaṇānvitam ।। kīṭairnopahataṃ yacca vyādhinā na ca pīḍitam । mandaśākhaṃ bhavedyacca daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ tu tadbhavet ।। yastvebhirlakṣaṇairhīnaṃ daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ sajarjaram ।
kārayetsa tvapacayaṃ mahāntaṃ prāpnuyāddhruvam ।। atha śīrṣavibhāgārthaṃ ghaṭī kāryā prayatnataḥ । svapramāṇavinirdiṣṭā dvātriṃśatyaṅgulāni vai ।। bilvamadhyena kartavyā ghaṭī sirasamāśrayā ।
svinnena bilvakalkena draveṇa ca samanvitā ।। bhasmanā vā tuṣairvāpi kārayetpratiśīrṣakam । saṃchādya tu tato vastrairbilvadugdhairghaṭāśrayaiḥ ।। bilvakalkena cīraṃ tu digdhvā saṃyojayedghaṭīm ।
na sthūlāṃ nānatāṃ tanvīṃ dīrghāṃ naiva ca kārayet ।। tasyāmātapaśuṣkāyāṃ suśuṣkāyāmathāpi vā । chedyaṃ budhāḥ prakurvanti vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā ।। sutīkṣṇena tu śastreṇa ardhārdhaṃ pravibhajya ca ।
svapramāṇavinirdiṣṭaṃ lalāṭakṛtakoṇakam ।। ardhāṅgulaṃ lalāṭaṃ tu kāryaṃ chedyaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulam । ardhārdhamaṅgulaṃ chedyaṃ kaṭayordvyaṅgulaṃ bhavet ।। kaṭānte karṇanālasya chedyaṃ dvyadhikamaṅgulam ।
tryaṅgulaṃ karṇavivaraṃ tathā syācchedyameva hi ।। tataścaivāvaṭuḥ kāryā susamā dvādaśāṅgulā । ghaṭyāṃ hyetatsadā cchedye vidhānaṃ vihitaṃ mayā ।। tasyoparigatā kāryā mukuṭā bahuśilpajāḥ ।
nānāratnapraticchannā bahurūpopaśobhitāḥ ।। tathopakaraṇānīha nāṭyayogakṛtāni vai । bahuprakārayuktāni kurvīta prakṛtiṃ prati ।। yatkiñcidasmin loke tu carācarasamanvite ।
vihitaṃ karma śilpaṃ vā tattūpakaraṇaṃ smṛtam ।। yadyasya viṣayaṃ prāptaṃ tattadevābhigacchati । nāstantaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ hi nāṭyopakaraṇāśraye ।। yadyenotpāditaṃ karma śilpayogakriyāpi vā ।
tasya tena kṛtā sṛṣṭiḥ pramāṇaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tathā ।। yā kāṣṭhayantrabhūyiṣṭhā kṛtā sṛṣṭirmahātmanā । na sāsmākaṃ nāṭyayoge kasmātkhedāvahā hi sā ।। yaddravyaṃ jīvaloke tu nānālakṣaṇalakṣitam ।
tasyānukṛtisaṃsthānaṃ nāṭyoopakaraṇaṃ bhavet ।। prāsādagṛhayānāni nānāpraharaṇāni ca । na śakyaṃ tāni vai kartuṃ yathoktānīha lakṣaṇaiḥ ।। lokadharmī bhavettvanyā nāṭyadharmī tathāparā ।
svabhāvo lokadharmī tu vibhāvo nāṭyameva hi ।। āyasaṃ na tu kartavyaṃ na ca sāramayaṃ tathā । nāṭyopakaraṇaṃ tajjñairgurukhedakara bhavet ।। kāṣṭhacarmasu vastrṣu jatuveṇudaleṣu ca ।
nāṭyopakaraṇānīha laghukarmāṇi kārayet ।। carmavarmadhvajāḥ śailāḥ prāsādā devatāgṛhāḥ । hayavāraṇayānāni vimānāni gṛhāṇi ca ।। pūrvaṃ veṇudalaiḥ kṛtvā kṛtīrbhāvasamāśrayāḥ ।
tataḥ suraṅgairacchādya vastraiḥ sārūpyamānayet ।। athavā yadi vastrāṇāmasānnidhyaṃ bhavediha । tālīyairvā kiliñjairvā ślakṣṇairvastrakriyā bhavet ।। tathā praharaṇāni syustṛṇaveṇudalādibhiḥ ।
jantubhāṇḍakriyābhiśca nānārūpāṇi nāṭake ।। pratipādaṃ pratiśiraḥ pratihastaṃ pratitvacam । tṛṇaiḥ kiliñjairbhāṇḍairvā sārūpyāṇi tu kārayet ।। yadyasya sadṛśaṃ rūpaṃ sārūpyaguṇasaṃbhavam ।
mṛṇmayaṃ tattu kṛtsnaṃ tu nānārūpaṃ tu kārayet ।। bhāṇḍavastramadhūcchiṣṭairlākṣayābhradalena ca । nāgāste vividhāḥ kāryā hyatasīśaṇabilvajaiḥ ।। nānākusumajātīśca phalāni vividhāni ca ।
bhāṇḍavastramadhūcchiṣṭairlākṣayā vāpi kārayet ।। bhāṇḍavastramadhūcchiṣṭaistāmrapatraistathaiva ca । samyakca nīlīrāgeṇāpyabhrapatreṇa caiva hi ।। rañjitenābhrapatreṇa maṇīścaiva prakārayet ।
upāśrayamathāpyeṣaṃ śulbavaṅgena kārayet ।। vividhā mukuṭā divā pūrvaṃ ye gaditā mayā । te abhrapatrojvalāḥ kāryā maṇīvyālopaśobhitāḥ ।। na śāstraprabhavaṃ karma teṣāṃ hi samudāhṛtam ।
ācāryabuddhyā kartavyamūhāpohaprayojitam ।। eṣa martyakriyāyogo bhaviṣyatkalpito mayā । kasmādalpabalatvaṃ hi manuṣyeṣu bhaviṣyati ।। martyānāmapi no śakyā vibhāvāḥ sarvakāñcanāḥ ।
neṣṭāḥ suvarṇaratnaistu mukuṭā bhūṣaṇāni vā ।। yuddhe niyuddhe nṛtte vā vṛṣṭivyāpārakarmaṇi । gurubhāvāvasannasya svedo mūrchā ca jāyate ।। svedamūrchāklamārtasya prayogastu vinaśyati ।
prāṇātyayaḥ kadācicca bhavedvyāyataceṣṭayā ।। tasmāttāmramayaiḥ patrairabhrakai rañjitairapi । bheṇḍairapi madhūcchiṣṭaiḥ kāryāṇyābharaṇāni tu ।। evaṃ lokopacāreṇa svabuddhivibhavena ca ।
nāṭyopakaraṇānīha budhaḥ samyak prayojayet ।। na bhedyaṃ naiva ca cchedyaṃ na prahartavyameva ca । raṅge praharaṇaiḥ kāryaṃ saṃjñāmātraṃ tu kārayet ।। athavā yogaśikṣābhirvidyāmāyākṛtena vā ।
śastramokṣaḥ prakartavyo raṅgamadhye prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। evaṃ nānāprakāraistu āyudhābharaṇāni ca । noktāni yāni ca mayā lokād grāhyāṇi tānyapi ।। āhāryābhinayo hyeṣa mayā proktaḥ samāsataḥ ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sāmānyābhinayaṃ prati ।। sāmānyābhinayo nāma jñeyo vāgaṅgasattvajaḥ । tatra kāryaḥ prayatnastu nāṭyaṃ sattve pratiṣṭhitam ।। sattvātirikto abhinayo jyeṣṭha ityabhidhīyate ।
samasattvo bhavenmadhyaḥ satvahīno adhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। avyaktarūpaṃ sattvaṃ hi vijñeyaṃ bhāvasaṃśrayam । yathāsthānarasopetaṃ romāñcāsrādibhirguṇaiḥ ।। alaṅkārāstu nāṭyajñairjñeyā bhāvarasāśrayāḥ ।
yauvane abhyadhikāḥ strīṇā vikārā vaktragātrajāḥ ।। ādau trayo aṅgajasteṣāṃ daśa svābhāvikāḥ pare । ayatnajāḥ punaḥ sapta rasabhāvopabṛṃhitāḥ ।। dehātmakaṃ bhavetsattvaṃ sattvādbhāvaḥ samutthitaḥ ।
bhāvātsamutthito hāvo hāvāddhelā samutthitā ।। helā hāvaśca bhāvaśca parasparasamutthitāḥ । sattvabhede bhavantyete śarīre prakṛtisthitāḥ ।। vāgaṅgamukharāgaiśca sattvenābhinayena ca ।
kaverantargataṃ bhāvaṃ bhāvayanbhāva ucyate ।। [bhāvasyātikṛtaṃ sattvaṃ vyatiriktaṃ svayoniṣu । naikāvasthāntarakṛtaṃ bhāvaṃ tamiha nirdiśet] ।। tatrākṣibhrūvikārāḍhyaḥ śṛṅgārākārasūcakaḥ ।
sagrīvārecako jñeyo hāvaḥ sthitasamutthitaḥ ।। yo vai hāvaḥ sa evaiṣā śṛṅgārarasasaṃbhavā । samākhyātā budhairhelā lalitābhinayātmikā ।। līlā vilāso vicchittirvibhramaḥ kilikiñcitam ।
moṭṭāyitaṃ kuṭṭimitaṃ bibboko lalitaṃ tathā ।। vihṛtaṃ ceti vijñeyā daśa strīṇāṃ svabhāvajāḥ । punareṣāṃ svarūpāṇi pravakṣyāmi pṛthakpṛthak ।। vāgaṅgālaṅkāraiḥ śiṣṭaiḥ prītiprayojitairmadhuraiḥ ।
iṣṭajanasyānukṛtirlīlā jñeyā prayogajñaiḥ ।। sthānāsanagamanānāṃ hastabhrūnetrakarmaṇāṃ caiva । utpadyate viśeṣo yaḥ śliṣṭaḥ sa tu vilāsaḥ syāt ।। mālyācchādanabhūṣaṇa vilepanānāmanādaranyāsaḥ ।
svalpo api parāṃ śobhāṃ janayati yasmāttu vicchitiḥ ।। vividhānāmarthānāṃ vāgaṅgāhāryasattvānām । madarāgaharṣajanito vyatyāso vibhramo jñeyaḥ ।। smitaruditahasitabhayaharṣagarvaduḥkhaśramābhilāṣāṇām ।
saṅkarakaraṇaṃ harṣādasakṛt kilikiñcitaṃ jñeyam ।। iṣṭajanasya kathāyāṃ līlāhelādidarśane vāpi । tadbhāvabhāvanākṛtamuktaṃ moṭṭāyitaṃ nāma ।। keśastanadharādigrahaṇādatiharṣasaṃbhramotpannam ।
kuṭṭamitaṃ vijñeayaṃ sukhamapi duḥkhopacāreṇa ।। iṣṭānāṃ bhāvānāṃ prāptāvabhimānagarvasaṃbhūtaḥ । strīṇāmanādarakṛto bibboko nāma vijñeyaḥ ।। hastapādāṅgavinyāso bhrūnetroṣṭhaprayojitaḥ ।
saukumāryādbhavedyastu lalitaṃ tatprakīrtitam ।। [karacaraṇāṅganyāsaḥ sabhrūnetroṣṭhasaṃprayuktastu । sukumāravidhānena strībhiuritīdaṃ smṛtaṃ lalitam] ।। vākyānāṃ prītiyuktānāṃ prāptānāṃ yadabhāṣaṇam ।
vyājātsvabhāvato vāpi vihṛtaṃ nāma tadbhavet ।। [prāptānāmapi vacasāṃ kriyate yadabhāṣaṇaṃ hriyā strībhiḥ । vyājātsvabhāvato vāpyetatsamudāhṛtaṃ vihṛtam] ।। śobhā kāntiśca dīptiśca tathā mādhuryameva ca ।
dhairyaṃ prāgalbhyamaudāryamityete syurayatnajāḥ ।। rūpayauvanalāvaṇyairupabhogopabṛṃhitaiḥ । alaṅkaraṇamaṅgānāṃ śobheti parikīrtitā ।। vijñeyā ca tathā kāntiḥ śobhaivāpūrṇamanmathā ।
kāntirevātivistīrṇā dīptirityabhidhīyate ।। sarvāvasthāviśeṣeṣu dīpteṣu laliteṣu ca । anulbaṇatvaṃ ceṣṭāyā mādhuryamiti saṃjñitam ।। cāpalenānupahatā sarvārtheṣvavikatthanā ।
svābhāvikī cittavṛttirdhairyamityabhidhīyate ।। prayoganissādhvasatā prāgalbhyaṃ samudāhṛtam । audāryaṃ praśrayaḥ proktaḥ sarvāvasthānugo budhaiḥ ।। sukumāre bhavantyete prayoge lalitātmike ।
vilāsalalite hitvā dīpte apyete bhavanti hi ।। śobhā vilāso mādhuryaṃ sthairyaṃ gāmbhīryameva ca । lalitaudāryatejāṃsi sattvabhedāstu pauruṣāḥ ।। dākṣyaṃ śauryamathotsāho nīcārtheṣu jugupsanam ।
uttamaiśca guṇaiḥ spardhā yataḥ śobheti sā smṛtā ।। dhīrasaṃcāriṇī dṛṣṭirgatirgovṛṣabhāñcitā । smitapūrvamathālāpo vilāsa iti kīrtitaḥ ।। abhyāsatkaraṇānāṃ tu śliṣṭatvaṃ yatra jāyate ।
mahatsvapi vikāreṣu tanmādhuryamiti smṛtam ।। dharrmārthakāmasaṃyuktācchubhāśubhasamutthitāt । vyavasāyādacalanaṃ sthairyamityabhisaṃjñitam ।। yasya prabhāvādākārā harṣakrodhabhayādiṣu ।
bhāveṣu nopalakṣyante tadgāmbhīryamiti smṛtam ।। abuddhipūrvakaṃ yattu nirvikārasvabhājam । śṛṅgārākāraceṣṭatvaṃ lalitaṃ tadudāhṛtam ।। dānamabhyupapattiśca tathā ca priyabhāṣaṇam ।
svajane ca pare vāpi tadaudāryaṃ prakīrtitam ।। adhikṣepāvamānādeḥ prayuktasya pareṇa yat । prāṇatyaye apyasahanaṃ tattejaḥ samudāhṛtam ।। sattvajo abhinayoḥ pūrvaṃ mayā proktao dvijottamāḥ ।
śārīraṃ cāpyābhinayaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। ṣaḍātmakastu śārīro vākyaṃ sūcāṅkurastathā । śākhā nāṭyāyitaṃ caiva nivṛttyaṅkura eva ca ।। nānārasārthayuktairvṛttanibandhaiḥ kṛtaḥ sacūrṇapadaiḥ ।
prākṛtasaṃskṛtapāṭho vākyābhinayo budhairjñeyaḥ ।। vākyartho vākyaṃ vā sattvāṅgaiḥ sūcyate yadā pūrvam । paścādvākyābhinayaḥ sūcetyabhisaṃjñitā sā tu ।। hṛdayastho nirvacanairaṅgābhinayaḥ kṛto nipuṇasādhyaḥ ।
sūcaivotpattikṛto vijñeyastvaṅkurābhinayaḥ ।। yattu śiromukhajaṅghorupāṇipādairyathākramaṃ kriyate । śākhādarśanamārgaḥ śākhābhinayaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ ।। nāṭyāyitamupacārairyaḥ kriyate abhinayasūcayā nāṭye ।
kālaprakarṣahetoḥ praveśakaiḥ saṃgamo yāvat ।। sthāne dhruvāsvabhinayo yaḥ kriyate harṣaśokaroṣādyaiḥ । bhāvarasasaṃprayuktairjñeyaṃ nāṭyāyitaṃ tadapi ।। yatrānyoktaṃ vākyaṃ sūcābhinayena yojayedanyaḥ ।
tatsaṃbandhārthakathaṃ bhavennivṛttyaṅkuraḥ so atha ।। eteṣāṃ tu bhavenmārgo yathābhāvarasānvitaḥ । kāvyavastuṣu nirdiṣṭo dvādaśābhinayātmakaḥ ।। ālāpaśca pralāpaśca vilāpaḥ syāttathaiva ca ।
anulāpo atha saṃlāpastvapalāpastathaiva ca ।। sandeśāścātideśaśca nirdeśaḥ syāttathāparaḥ । upadeśo apadeśaśca vyapadeśaśca kīrtitaḥ ।। ābhāṣaṇaṃ tu yadvākyamālāpo nāma sa smṛtaḥ ।
anarthakaṃ vaco yattu pralāpaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ ।। karuṇaprabhavo yastu vilāpaḥ sa tu kīrtitaḥ । bahuśo abhihitaṃ vākyamanulāpa iti smṛtaḥ ।। uktipratyuktisaṃyuktaḥ saṃlāpa iti kīrtitaḥ ।
pūrvoktasyānyathāvādo hyapalāpa iti smṛtaḥ ।। tadidaṃ vacanaṃ brūhītyeṣa sandeśa ucyate । yattvayoktaṃ mayoktaṃ tatso atideśa iti smṛtaḥ ।। sa eṣo ahaṃ bravīmīti nirdeśa iti kīrtitaḥ ।
vyājāntareṇa kathanaṃ vyapadeśa ihocyate ।। idaṃ kuru gṛhāṇeti hyupadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । anyārthakathanaṃ yat syāt so apadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। ete mārgāstu vijñeyāḥ sarvābhinayayojakāḥ ।
saptaprakārameteṣāṃ punarvakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। pratyakṣaśca parokṣaśca tathā kālakṛtāstrayaḥ । ātmasthaśca parasthaśca prakārāḥ sapta eva tu ।। eṣā bravīmi nāhaṃ bho vadāmīti ca yadvacaḥ ।
pratyakṣaśca parokṣaśca vartamānaśca tadbhavet ।। ahaṃ karomi gacchāmi vadāmi vacanaṃ tava । ātmastho vartamānaśca pratyakṣaścaiva sa smṛtaḥ ।। kariṣyāmi gamiṣyāmi vadiṣyāmīti yadvacaḥ ।
ātmasthaśca parokṣaśca bhaviṣyatkāla eva ca ।। hatā jitā ca bhagnāśca mayā sarve dviṣadgaṇāḥ । ātmasthaśca parokṣaśca vṛttakālaśca sa smṛtaḥ ।। [tvayā hata jitāśceti yo vadennāṭyakarmaṇi ।
parokṣaśca parasthaśca vṛttakālastathaiva ca ।। eṣa bravīmi kurute gacchatītyādi yadvacaḥ । parastho vartamānaśca bhavettathā ।। sa gacchati karotīti vacanaṃ yadutāhṛtam ।
parasthaṃ vartamānaṃ ca parokṣaṃ caiva tadbhavet ।। kariṣyanti gamiṣyanti vadiṣyantīti yadvacaḥ । parasthameṣyatkālaṃ ca parokṣaṃ caiva tadbhavet] ।। hastamantarataḥ kṛtvā yadvadennāṭyakarmaṇi ।
ātmasthaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ ca parokṣaṃ caiva tanmatam ।। pareṣāmātmanaścaiva kālasya ca viśeṣaṇāt । saptaprakārasyāsyaiva bhedā jñeyā anekadhā ।। ete prayogā vijñeyā mārgābhinayayojitāḥ ।
eteṣviha viniṣpanno vividho abhinayo bhavet ।। śiro hastakaṭīvakṣojaṅghorukaraṇeṣu tu । samaḥ karmavibhāgo yaḥ sāmānyābhinayastu saḥ ।। lalitairhastasaṃcārastathā mṛdvaṅgaceṣṭitaiḥ ।
abhineyastu nāṭyajñai rasabhāvasamanvitaiḥ ।। anuddhatamasaṃbhrāntamanāviddhāṅgaceṣṭitam । layatālakalāpātapramāṇaniyatātmakam ।। suvibhaktapadālāpamaniṣṭhuramakāhalam ।
yadīdṛśaṃ bhavennāṭyaṃ jñeyamābhyantaraṃ tu tat ।। etadeva viparyastaṃ svacchandagaticeṣṭitam । anibaddhagītavādyaṃ nāṭyaṃ bāhyamiti smṛtam ।। lakṣaṇābhyantaratvāddhi tadābhyantaramiṣyate ।
śāstrabāhyaṃ bhavedyattu tadbāhyamiti bhaṇyate ।। anena lakṣyate yasmāt prayogaḥ karma caiva hi । tasmāllakṣaṇametaddhi nāṭye asmin saṃprayojitam ।। anācāryoṣitā ye ca ye ca śāstrabahiṣkṛtāḥ ।
bāhyaṃ prayuñjate te tu ajñātvācāryakīṃ kriyām ।। śabdaṃ sparśaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca rasaṃ gandhaṃ tathaiva ca । indriyānīndriyārthāṃśca bhāvairabhinayedbudhaḥ ।। kṛtvā sācīkṛtāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ śiraḥ pārśvanataṃ tathā ।
tarjanī karṇadeśe ca budhaḥ śabdaṃ vinirdiśet ।। kiñcidākuñcite netre kṛtvā bhrūkṣepameva ca । tathāṃ'sagaṇḍayoḥ sparśāt sparśamevaṃ vinirdiśet ।। kṛtvā patākau mūrdhasthau kiṃcitpracalitānanaḥ ।
nirvarṇayantyā dṛṣṭyā ca rūpaṃ tvabhinayed budhaḥ ।। kiñcidākuñcite netre kṛtvotphullāṃ ca nāsikām । ekocchvāsena ceṣṭau tu rasagandhau vinirdiśet ।। pañcānāmindriyārthānāṃ bhāvā hyete anubhāvinaḥ ।
śrotratvaṅnetrajihvānāṃ ghrāṇasya ca tathaiva hi ।। indriyārthāḥ samanaso bhavanti hyanubhāvinaḥ । na vetti hyamanāḥ kiṃcidviṣayaṃ pañcadhāgatam ।। manasastrividho bhāvo vijñeyo abhinaye budhaiḥ ।
iṣṭastathā hyaniṣṭaśca madhyasthaśca tathaiva hi ।। prahlādanena gātrasya tathā pulakitena ca । vadanasya vikāsena kuryādiṣṭanidarśanam ।। iṣṭe śabde tathā rūpe sparśe gandhe tathā rase ।
indriyairmanasā prāptaiḥ saumukhyaṃ saṃpradarśayet ।। parāvṛttena śirasā netranāsāvikarṣaṇaiḥ । cakṣuṣaścāpradānena hyaniṣṭamabhinirdiśet ।। nātihṛṣṭena manasā na cātyarthajugupsayā ।
madhyasthanaiva bhāvena madhyasthamabhinirdiśet ।। tenedaṃ tasya vāpīdaṃ sa evaṃ prakaroti vā । parokṣābhinayo yastu madhyastha iti sa smṛtaḥ ।। ātmānubhāvī yo arthaḥ syādātmastha iti sa smṛtaḥ ।
parārthavarṇanā yatra parasthaḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ ।। prāyeṇa sarvabhāvānāṃ kāmānniṣpattiriṣyate । sa cecchāguṇasampanno bahudhā parikalpitaḥ ।। dharmakāmo arthakāmaśca mokṣakāmastathaiva ca ।
strīpuṃsayostu yogo yaḥ sa tu kāma iti smṛtaḥ ।। sarvasyaiva hi lokasya sukhaduḥkhanibarhaṇaḥ । bhūyiṣṭhaṃ dṛṣyate kāmaḥ sa sukhaṃ vyasaneṣvapi ।। yaḥ strīpuruṣasaṃyogo ratisaṃbhogakārakaḥ ।
sa śṛṅgāra iti jñeya upacārakṛtaḥ śubhaḥ ।। bhūyiṣṭhameva loko ayaṃ sukhamicchati sarvadā । sukhasya hi striyo mūlaṃ nānā śīlāścā tāḥ punaḥ ।। devadānavagandharvarakṣonāgapatatriṇām ।
piśācayakṣavyālānāṃ naravānarahastinām ।। mṛgamīnoṣṭramakarakharasūkaravājinām । mahīṣājagavādīnāṃ tulyaśīlāḥ striyaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। snigdhairaṅgairupāṅgaiśca sthirā mandanimeṣiṇi ।
arogā dīptyupetā ca dānasattvārjavānvitā ।। alpasvedā samaratā svalpabhuk suratapriyā । gandhapuṣparatā hṛdyā devaśīlāṅganā smṛtā ।। adharmaśāṭhyābhiratā sthirakrodhātiniṣṭhurā ।
madyamāṃsapriayā nityaṃ kopanā cātimāninī ।। capalā cātilubdhā ca paruṣā kalahapriyā । īrṣyāśīlā calasnehā cāsuraṃ śīlamāśritā ।। krīḍāparā cārunetrā nakhadantaiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ ।
svaṅgī ca sthirabhāṣī ca mandāpatyā ratipriyā ।। gīte vādye ca nṛtte ca ratā hṛṣṭā mṛjāvatī । gandharvasattvā vijñeyā snigdhatvakkeśalocanā ।। bṛhadvyāyatasarvāṅgī raktavistīrṇalocanā ।
khararomā divāsvapnaniratātyuccabhāṣiṇī ।। nakhadantakṣatakarī krodherṣyākalahapriyā । niśāvihāraśīlā ca rākṣasaṃ śīlamāśritā ।। tīkṣṇanāsāgradaśanā sutanustāmralocanā ।
nīlotpalasavarṇā ca svapnaśīlā'tikopanā ।। tiryaggatiścalārambhā bahuśvāsātimāninī । gandhamālyāsavaratānāgasattvā'ṅganā smṛtā ।। atyantavyāvṛtāsyā ca tīkṣṇaśīlā saritpriyā ।
surāsavakṣīraratā bahvapatyā phalapriyā ।। nityaṃ śvasanaśīlāca tathodyānavanapriyā । capalā bahuvākchīghrā śākunaṃ sattvamāśritā ।। ūnādhikāṅgulikarā rātrau niṣkuṭacāriṇi ।
bālodvejanaśīlā ca piśunā kliṣṭabhāṣiṇi ।। surate kutsitācārā romaśāṅgī mahāsvanā । piśācasattvā vijñeyā madyamāṃsabalipriyā ।। svapnaprasvedanāṅgī ca sthiraśayyāsanapriyā ।
medhāvinī buddhimatī madyagandhāmiṣapriyā ।। ciradṛṣṭeṣu harṣaṃ ca kṛtajñatvādupaiti sā । adīrghaśāyinī caiva yakṣaśīlā'ṅganā smṛtā ।। tulyamānāvamānā yā paruṣatvak kharasvarā ।
śaṭhānṛtoddhatakathā vyālasattvā ca piṅgadṛk ।। vibhaktāṅgī kṛtajñā ca gurudevadvijapriyā । dharmakāmārthaniratā hyahaṅkāāravivarjitā । suhṛtpriyā suśīlā ca mānuṣaṃ sattvamāśritā ।।
saṃhatālpatanurhṛṣṭā piṅgaromā chalapriyā । pragalbhā capalā tīkṣṇā vṛkṣārāmavanapriyā ।। svalpamapyupakāraṃ tu nityaṃ yā bahumanyate । prasahyaratiśīlā ca vānaraṃ sattvamāśritā ।।
mahāhanulalāṭā ca śarīropacayānvitā । piṅgākṣī romaśāṅgī ca gandhamālyāsavapriyā ।। kopanā sthiracittā ca jalodyānavanapriyā । madhurābhiratā caiva hastisattvā prakīrtitā ।।
svalpodarī bhagnanāsā tanujaṅghā vanapriyā । calavīstīrṇanayanā capalā śīghragāminī ।। divātrāsaparā nityaṃ gītavādyaratipriyā । nivāsasthiracittā ca mṛgasattvā prakīrtitā ।।
dīrghapīnonnatoraskā calā nātinimeṣiṇī । bahubhṛtyā bahusutā matsyasattvā jalapriyā ।। lamboṣṭhī svedabahulā kiñcidvikaṭagāminī । kṛśodarī puṣpaphalalavaṇāmlakaṭupriyā ।।
udbandhakaṭipārśvā ca kharaniṣṭhurabhāṣiṇī । atyunnatakaṭīgrīvā uṣṭrasattvā'ṭavīpriyā ।। sthūlaśīrṣāñcitagrīvā dāritāsyā mahasvanā । jñeyā makarasattvā ca krūrā matsyaguṇairyutā ।।
sthūlajihvoṣṭhadaśanā rūkṣatvakkaṭubhāṣiṇī । ratiyuddhakarī dhṛṣṭā nakhadantakṣatapriyā ।। sapatnīdveṣiṇī dakṣā capalā śīghragāminī । sarogā bahvapatyā ca kharasattvā prakīrtitā ।।
dīrghapṛṣṭhodaramukhī romaśālī balānvitā । susaṃkṣiptalalāṭā ca kandamūlaphalapriyā ।। kṛṣṇā daṃṣṭotkaṭamukhī hrasvodaraśiroruhā । hīnācārā bahvapatyā saukaraṃ sattvamāśritā ।।
sthirā vibhaktapārśvorukaṭīpṛṣṭhaśirodharā । subhagā dānaśīlā ca ṛjusthūlaśiroruhā ।। kṛśā cañcalacittā ca snigdhavākchīghragāminī । kāmakrodhaparā caiva hayasattvāṅganā smṛtā ।।
sthūlapṛṣṭhākṣidaśanā tanupārśvodarā sthirā । hariromāñcitā raudrī lokadviṣṭā ratipriyā ।। kiñcidunnatavaktrā ca jalakrīḍāvanapriyā । bṛhallalāṭā suśroṇī māhiṣaṃ sattvamāśritā ।।
kṛśā tanubhujoraskā niṣṭabdhasthiralocanā । saṃkṣiptapāṇipādā ca sūkṣmaromasamācitā ।। bhayaśīlā jalodvignā bahvapatyā vanapriyā । cañcalā śīghragamanā hyajasattvā~ṅganā smṛtā ।।
udbandhagātranayanā vijṛmbhaṇaparāyaṇā । dīrghālpavadanā svalpapāṇipādavibhūṣitā ।। uccaḥsvanā svalpanidrā krodhanā sukṛtapriyā । hīnācārā kṛtajñā ca śvaśīlā parikīrtitā ।।
pṛthupīnoonnataśroṇī tanujaṅghā suhṛtpriyā । saṃkṣiptapāṇipādā ca dṛḍhārambhā prajāhitā ।। pitṛdevārcanaratā satyaśaucagurupriyā । sthirā parikleśasahā gavāṃ sattvaṃ samāśritā ।।
nānāśīlāḥ striyo jñeyāḥ svaṃ svaṃ sattvaṃ samāśritāḥ । vijñāya ca yathāsattvamupaseveta tāḥ punaḥ ।। upacāro yathāsattvaṃ strīṇāmalpo api harṣadaḥ । mahānapyanyathāyukto naiva tuṣṭikaro bhavet ।।
yathā saṃprarthitāvāptyā ratiḥ samupajāyate । strīpuṃsayośca ratyarthamupacāro vidhīyate ।। dharmārthaṃ hi tapaścaryā sukhārthaṃ dharma iṣyate । sukhasya mūlaṃ pramadāstāsu sambhoga iṣyate ।।
kāmopabhāgo dvividho nāṭyadharme abhidhīyate । bāhyābhyantarataścaiva nārīpuruṣasaṃśrayaḥ ।। ābhyantaraḥ pārthivānāṃ sa ca kāryastu nāṭake । bāhyo veśyāgataścaiva sa ca prakaraṇe bhavet ।।
tatra rājopabhogaṃ tu vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ । upacāravidhiṃ samyak kāmatantrasamutthitam ।। trividhā prakṛtiḥ strīṇāṃ nānāsattvasamudbhavā । bāhyā cābhyantarā caiva syādbāhyābhyantarāparā ।।
kulīnābhyantarā jñeyā bāhyā veśyāṅganā smṛtā । kṛtaśaucā tu yā nārī sā bāhyābhyantarā smṛtā ।। antaḥpuropacāre tu kulajā kanyakāpi vā । na hi rājopacāre tu bāhyastrībhoga iṣyate ।।
ābhyantaro bhavedrājño bāhyo bāhyajanasya ca । divyaveśāṅganānāṃ hi rājñāṃ bhavati saṅgamaḥ ।। kulajākāmitaṃ yacca tajjñeyaṃ kanyakāsvapi । yā cāpi veśyā sāpyatra yathaiva kulajā tathā ।।
iha kāmasamutpatīrnānābhāvasamudbhavā । strīṇāṃ vā puruṣāṇāṃ vā uttamādhamamadhyamā ।। śravaṇāddarśanādrūpādaṅgalīlāviceṣṭitaiḥ । madhuraiśca samālāpaiḥ kāmaḥ samupajāyate ।।
rūpaguṇādisametaṃ kalādivijñānayauvanopetam । dṛṣṭvā puruṣaviśeṣaṃ nārī madanāturā bhavati ।। tataḥ kāmayamānānāṃ nṛṇāṃ strīṇāmathāpi ca । kāmābhāveṅgitānīha tajjñaḥ samupalakṣayet ।।
lalitā calapakṣmā ca tathā ca mukulekṣaṇā । srastottarapuṭā caiva kāmyā dṛṣṭirbhavediha ।। [valitāntā salālityasaṃmitairvyañjitairastathā । dṛṣṭiḥ sā lalitā nāma strīṇāmardhāvalokane] ।।
īṣtsaṃraktagaṇḍastu sasvedalavacitritaḥ । praspandamānaromāñco mukharāgo bhavediha ।। kāmyenāṅgavikāreṇa sakaṭākṣanirīkṣitaiḥ । tathābharaṇasaṃsparśaiḥ karṇakaṇḍuyanairapi ।।
aṅguṣṭhāgravilikhanaiḥ stananābhipradarśanaiḥ । nakhanistodanāccaiva keśasaṃyamanādapi ।। veśyāmevaṃvidhairbhāvairlakṣayenmadanāturām । kulajāyāstathā caiva pravakṣyāmīṅgitāni tu ।।
prahasantīva netrābhyāṃ pratataṃ ca nirīkṣate । smayate sā nigūḍhaṃ ca vācaṃ cādhomukhī vadet ।। smitottarā mandavākyā svedākāranigūhanī । praspanditādharā caiva cakitā ca kulāṅganā ।।
evaṃvidhaiḥ kāmaliṅgairaprāptasuratotsavā । daśasthānagataṃ kāmaṃ nānābhāvaiḥ pradarśayet ।। prathame tvabhilāṣaḥ syād dvitīye cintanaṃ bhavet । anusmṛtistṛtīye tu caturthe guṇakīrtanam ।।
udvegaḥ pañcame prokto vilāpaḥ ṣaṣṭha ucyate । unmādaḥ saptame jñeyo bhavedvyādhistathāṣṭame ।। navame jaḍatā caiva daśame maraṇaṃ bhavet । strīpuṃsayoreṣa vidhirlakṣaṇaṃ ca nibodhata ।।
vyavasāyātsamārabdhaḥ saṃkalpecchāsamudbhavaḥ । samāgamopāyakṛtaḥ so abhilāṣaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। niryāti viśati ca muhuḥ karoti cākārameva madanasya । tiṣṭhati ca darśanapathe prathamasthāne sthitā kāme ।।
kenopāyena saṃprāptiḥ kathaṃ vāsau bhavenmama । dūtīniveditairbhāvairiti cintāṃ nidarśayet ।। ākekarārdhaviprekṣitāni valayaraśanāparāmarśaḥ । nīvīnābhyāḥ saṃsparśanaṃ ca kāryaṃ dvitīye tu ।।
sumuhurmuhurniḥśvasitairmanorathavicintanaiḥ । pradveṣāccānyakāryāṇāmanusmṛtirudāhṛtā ।। naivāsane na śayane dhṛtimupalabhate svakarmaṇi vihastā । taccintopagatatvāt tṛtīyameva prayuñjīta ।।
aṅgapratyaṅgalīlābhirvākceṣṭāhasitekṣitaiḥ । nāstyanyaḥ sadṛśastenetyetat syād guṇakīrtanam ।। guṇakīrtanollukasanairaśrusvedāpamārjanaiścāpi । dūtyavirahavisrambhairabhinayayogaścaturthe tu ।।
āsane śayane cāpi na tuṣyati na tiṣṭhati । nityamevotsukā ca syādudvegasthānamāśritā ।। cintāniḥśvāsakhedena hṛddāhābhinayena ca । kuryāttadevamatyantamudvegābhinayena ca ।।
iha sthita ihāsīna iha copagato mayā । iti taistairvilapitairvilāpaṃ saṃprayojayet ।। udvignātyarthamautsukyādadhṛtyā ca vilāpinī । tatastataśca bhramati vilāpasthānamāśritā ।।
tatsaṃśritāṃ kathāṃ yuṅkte sarvāvasthāgatāpi hi । puṃsaḥ pradveṣṭi cāpyanyānunmādaḥ saṃprakīrtitaḥ ।। tiṣṭhatyanimiṣadṛṣṭirdīrghaṃ niḥśvasiti gacchati dhyānam । roditi vihārakāle nāṭyamidaṃ syāttathonmāde ।।
sāmadānārthasaṃbhogaiḥ kāmyaiḥ saṃpreṣaṇairapi । sarvairnirākṛtaiḥ paścād vyādhiḥ samupajāyate ।। muhyati hṛdayaṃ kvāpi prayāti śirasaśca vedanā tīvrā । na dhṛtiṃ cāpyupalabhate hyaṣṭamamevaṃ prayuñjīta ।।
pṛṣṭā na kiñcit prabrate na śṛṇoti na paśyati । hākaṣṭavākyā tūṣṇīkā jaḍatāyāṃ gatasmṛtiḥ ।। akāṇḍe dattahuṃkārā tathā praśithilāṅgikā । śvāsagrastānanā caiva jaḍatābhinaye bhavet ।।
sarvaiḥ kṛtaiḥ pratīkārairyadī nāsti samāgamaḥ । kāmāgninā pradīptāyā jāyate maraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। evaṃ sthānāni kāryāṇi kāmatantraṃ samīkṣya tu । aprāptau yāni kāmasya varjayitvā tu naidhanam ।।
vividhaiḥ puruṣo apyevaṃ vipralambhasamudbhavaiḥ । bhāvairetāni kāmasya nānārūpāṇi yojayet ।। evaṃ kāmayamānānāṃ strīṇā nṛṇāmathāpi vā । sāmānyaguṇayogena yuñjītābhinayaṃ budhaḥ ।।
cintāniḥśvāsakhedena hṛddāhābhinayena ca । tathānugamannāccāpi tathaivādhvanirīkṣaṇāt ।। ākāśavīkṣaṇāccāpi tathā dīnaprabhāṣaṇāt । sparśanānmoṭanāccāpi tathā sāpāśrayāśrayāt ।।
ebhirnānāśrayotpannairvipralambhasamudbhavaiḥ । kāmasthānāni sarvāṇi bhūyiṣṭhaṃ samprayojayet ।। srajo bhūṣaṇagandhāṃśca gṛhāṇyupavanāni ca । kāmāgninā dahyamānaḥ śītalāni niṣevate ।।
pradahyamānaḥ kāmārto bahusthānasamarditaḥ । preṣayetkāmato dūtīmātmāvasthāpradarśinīm ।। sandeśaṃ caiva dūtyāstu pradadyānmadanāśrayam । tasyeyaṃ samavastheti kathayedvinayena sā ।।
athāveditabhāvārtho ratyupāyaṃ vicintayet । ayaṃ vidhirvidhānajñaiḥ kāryaḥ pracchannakāmite ।। vidhiṃ rājopacārasya punarvakṣyāmi tattvataḥ । abhyantaragataṃ samyak kāmatantrasamutthitam ।।
sukhaduḥkhakṛtān bhāvān nānāśīlasamutthitān । yānyān prakurute rājā tānstān lokānuvartate ।। na durlabhāḥ pārthivānāṃ stryarthamājñākṛtāḥ guṇāḥ । dākṣiṇyāttu samudbhūtaḥ kāmo ratikaro bhavet ।।
bahumānena devīnāṃ vallabhānāṃ bhayena ca । pracchannakāmitaṃ rājñā kāryaṃ parijanaṃ prati ।। yadyapyasti narendrāṇāṃ kāmatantramanekadhā । pracchannākāmitaṃ yattu tadvai ratikaraṃ bhavet ।।
yadvāmābhiniveśitvaṃ yataśca vinivāryate । durlabhatvaṃ ca yannāryāḥ sā kāmasya parā ratiḥ ।। rājñāmantaḥpurajane divāsambhoga iṣyate । vāsoapacāro yaścaiaṣāṃ sa rātrau parikīrtitaḥ ।।
paripāṭyāṃ phalārthe vā nave prasava eva vā । duḥkhe caiva pramode ca ṣaḍete vāsakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ucite vāsake strīnāmṛtukāle api vā nṛpaiḥ । preṣyāṇāmathaveṣṭānāṃ kāryaṃ caivopasarpaṇam ।।
tatra vāsakasajjā ca virahotkaṇṭhitāpi vā । svādhīnabhartṛkā cāpi kalahāntaritāpi vā ।। khaṇḍitā vipralabdhā vā tathā proṣitabhartṛkā । tathābhisārikā caiva jñeyāstvaṣṭau tu nayikāḥ ।।
ucite vāsakae yā tu ratisaṃbhogalālasā । maṇḍanaṃ kurute hṛṣṭā sā vai vāsakasajjikā ।। anekakāryavyāsaṅgādyasyā nāgacchati priyaḥ । tadanāgataduḥkhārtā virahotkaṇṭhitā tu sā ।।
suratātirasairbaddho yasyāḥ pārśve tu nāyakaḥ । sāndrāmodaguṇaprāptā bhavet svādhīnabhartṛkā ।। īrṣyākalahaniṣkrānto yasyā nāgacchati priyaḥ । sāmarṣavaśasaṃprāptā kalahāntaritā bhavet ।।
vyāsaṅgāducite yasyā vāsake nāgataḥ priyaḥ । tadanāgamaduḥkhārtā khaṇḍitā sā prakīrtitā ।। yasyā dūtīṃ priyaḥ preṣya dattvā saṃketameva vā । nāgataḥ kāraṇeneha vipralabdhā tu sā bhavet ।।
nānākāryāṇi sandhāya yasyā vai proṣitaḥ priyaḥ । sārūḍhālakakeśāntā bhavet proṣitabhartṛkā ।। hitvā lajjāṃ tu yā śliṣṭā madena madanena ca । abhisārayate kāntaṃ sā bhavedabhisārikā ।।
āsvavasthāsu vijñeyā nāyikā nāṭakāśrayā । etāsāṃ caiva vakṣyāmi kāmatantramanekadhā ।। cintāniḥśvāsakhedena hṛddāhābhinayena ca । sakhībhiḥ saha saṃlāpairātmāvasthāvalokanaiḥ ।।
glānidainyāśrupātaiśca roṣasyāgamanena ca । nirbhūṣaṇamṛjātvena duḥkhena ruditena ca ।। khaṇḍitā vipralabdhā vā kalahāntaritāpi vā । tathā proṣitakāntā ca bhāvānetān prayojayet ।।
vicitrojjvalaveṣā tu pramododyotitānanā । udīrṇaśobhā ca tathā kāryā svādhīnabhartṛkā ।। veśyāyāḥ kulajāyāyāśca preṣyāyāśca prayoktṛbhiḥ । ebhirbhāvaviśeṣaistu kartavyamabhisāraṇam ।।
samadā mṛduceṣṭā ca tathā parijanāvṛtā । nānābharaṇacitrāṅgī gacchedveśyāṅganā śanaiḥ ।। saṃlīnā sveṣu gātreṣu trastā vinamitānanā । avakuṇṭhanasaṃvitā hacchettu kulajāṅganā ।।
madaskhalitasaṃlāpā vibhramotphullalocanā । āviddhagatisaṃcārā gacchetpreṣyā samuddhatam ।। gatvā sā cedyadā tatra paśyetsuptaṃ priyaṃ tadā । anena tūpacāreṇa tasya kuryātprabodhanam ।।
alaṅkāreṇa kulajā veśyā gandhaistu śītalaiḥ । preṣyā tu vastravyajanaiḥ kurvīta pratibodhanam ।। kulāṅganānāmevāyaṃ noktaḥ kāmāśrayo vidhiḥ । sarvāvasthānubhāvyaṃ hi yasmādbhavati nāṭakam ।।
navakāmapravṛttāyā kruddhāyā vā samāgame । sāpadeśairupāyaistu vāsakaṃ saṃprayojayet ।। nānālaṅkaravastrāṇi gandhamālyāni caiva hi । priyayojitabhuktāni niṣeveta mudānvitaḥ ।।
na tathā bhavati manuṣyo madanavaśaḥ kāminīmalabhamānaḥ । dviguṇopajātaharṣo bhavati yatha saṅgataḥ priyayā ।। vilāsabhāveṅgitavākyalīlāmādhuryavistāraguṇopapannaḥ । parasparapremanirīkṣitena samāgamaḥ kāmakṛtastu kāryaḥ ।।
tataḥ pravṛtte madane upacārasamudbhave । vāsopacāraḥ kartavyo nāyakāgamanaṃ prati ।। gandhamālye gṛhītvā tu cūrṇavāsastathaiva ca । ādarśo līlayā gṛhyaśchandato vā punaḥ punaḥ ।।
vāsopacāre nātyarthaṃ bhūṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ bhavet । raśanānūpuraprāyaṃ svanavacca praśasyate ।। nāmbaragrahaṇaṃ raṅge na snānaṃ na vilepanam । nāñjanaṃ nāṅgarāgaśca keśasaṃyamanaṃ tathā ।।
nāprāvṛttā naikavastrā na rāgamadharasya tu । uttamā madhyamā vāpi kurvīta pramadā kvacit ।। adhamānāṃ bhavedeṣa sarva eva vidhiḥ sadā । kāraṇāntaramāsādya tasmādapi na kārayet ।।
preṣyādīnāṃ ca nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ vāpi nāṭake । bhūṣaṇagrahaṇaṃ kāryaṃ puṣpagrahaṇameva ca ।। gṛhītamaṇḍanā cāpi pratīkṣeta priyāgamam । līlayā maṇḍitaṃ veṣaṃ kuryādyanna virudhyate ।।
vidhivadvāsakaṃ kuryānnāyikā nāyakāgame । pratīkṣamāṇā ca tato nālikāśabdamādiśet ।। śrutvā tu nālikāśabdaṃ nāyakāgamaviklavā । viṣaṇṇā vepamānā ca gacchettoraṇameva ca ।।
toraṇaṃ vāmahastena kavāṭaṃ dakṣiṇena ca । gṛhītvā toraṇāśliṣṭā saṃpratīkṣeta nāyakam ।। śaṅkāṃ cintāṃ bhayaṃ caiva prakuryāttoraṇāśritā । adṛṣṭvā ramaṇaṃ nārī viṣaṇṇā ca kṣaṇaṃ bhavet ।।
dīrghaṃ caiva viniḥśvasya nayanāmbu nipātayet । sannaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ kṛtvā visṛjetadaṅgamāsane ।। vyākṣepādvimṛśeccāpi nāyakāgamanaṃ prati । taistairvicāraṇopāyaiḥ śubhāśubhasamutthitaiḥ ।।
gurukāryeṇa mitrairvā mantriṇā rājyacintayā । anubaddhaḥ priyaṃ kiṃ nu vṛto vallabhayāpi vā ।। utpātānnirdiśeccāpi śubhāśubhasamutthitān । nimitairātmasaṃsthaistu sphuritaiḥ spandiataistathā ।।
śobhaneṣu tu kāryeṣu nimittaṃ vāmataḥ striyāḥ । aniṣṭeṣvatha sarveṣu nimittaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ bhavet ।। savyaṃ netraṃ lalāṭaṃ ca bhrūnāsoṣṭhaṃ tathaiva ca । urubāhustanaṃ caiva sphuredyadi samāgamaḥ ।।
eteṣamanyathābhāve durnimittaṃ vinirdiśet । darśane durnimittasya mohaṃ gacchetkṣaṇaṃ tataḥ ।। anāgame nāyakasya kāryo gaṇḍāśrayaḥ karaḥ । bhūṣaṇe cāpyavajñānaṃ rodanaṃ ca samācaret ।।
atha cecchobhanaṃ tatsyānnimittaṃ nāyakāgame । sūcyo nāyikayāsanno gandhāghrāṇena nāyakaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā cotthāya saṃhṛṣṭā pratyudgacchedyathāvidhi । tataḥ kāntaṃ nirīkṣeta praharṣotphullalocanā ।।
sakhīskandhārpitakarā kṛtvā sthānakamāyatam । darśayeta tataḥ kāntaṃ sacihnaṃ sarasavraṇam ।। yadi syādaparāddhastu kṛtaistaistairupakramaiḥ । upālambhakṛatairvākyairupālabhyastu nāyakaḥ ।।
mānāpamānasaṃmohairavahitthabhayakramaiḥ । vacanasya samutpattiḥ strīṇāmīrṣyākṛtā bhavet ।। visraṃbhasneharāgeṣu sandehe praṇaye tathā । paritoṣe ca gharṣe ca dākṣiṇyākṣepavibhrame ।।
dharmārthakāmayogeṣu pracchannavacaneṣu ca । hāsye kutūhale caiva saṃbhrame vyasane tathā ।। strīpuṃsayoḥ krodhakṛte pṛthaṅmiśre tathāpi vā । anābhāṣyo api saṃbhāṣyaḥ priya ebhistu kāraṇaiḥ ।।
yatra sneho bhavettatra hīrṣyā madanasaṃbhavā । catasro yonayastasyāḥ kīrtyamānā nibodhata ।। vaimanasyaṃ vyalīkaṃ ca vipriyaṃ manyureva ca । eteṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇāni yathākramam ।।
nidrākhedālasagatiṃ sacihnaṃ sarasavraṇam । evavidhaṃ priyaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaimanasyaṃ bhavet striyāḥ ।। nidrābhyasūyitāvekṣaṇena roṣaprakampamānāṅgyā । sādhviti suṣṭhviti vacanaiḥ śobhata ityevamabhineyam ।।
bahudhā vāryamāṇo api yastasminneva dṛśyate । saṃgharṣamatsarāttatra vyalīkaṃ jāyate striyāḥ ।। kṛtvorasi vāmakaraṃ dakṣiṇahastaṃ tathā vidhunvantyā । caraṇaviniṣṭhambhena ca kāryo abhinayo vyalīke tu ।।
jīvantyā tvayi jīvāmi dāso ahaṃ tvaṃ ca me priyā । uktvaivaṃ yo anyathā kuryādvipriyaṃ tatra jāyate ।। dūtīlekhaprativacanabhedanaiḥ krodhahasitaruditaiśca । vipriyakaraṇe abhinayaḥ saśiraḥkampaiśca kartavyaḥ ।।
pratipakṣasakāśāttu yaḥ saubhāgyavikatthanaḥ । upasarpet sacinhnastu manyustatropajāyate ।। valayaparivartanairatha suśithalamutkṣepeṇena raśanāyāḥ । manyustvabhinetavyaḥ saśaṅkitaṃ bāṣpapūrṇākṣyā ।।
dṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ priyatamaṃ saśaṅkitaṃ sāparādhamatilajjam । īrṣyāvacanasamutthaiḥ khedayitavyo hyupālambhaiḥ ।। na ca niṣṭhuramabhibhāṣyo na cāpyatikrodhanastu parihāsaḥ । bāṣponmiśrairvacanairātmopanyāsasaṃyuktaiḥ ।।
madhyāṅgulyaṅguṣṭhāgravicyavātpāṇinorasi kṛtena । udvartitanetratayā pratatairabhivīkṣaṇaiścāpi ।। kaṭihastavivartanayā vicchinnatayā tathāñjaleḥ karaṇāt । mūrdhabhramaṇanihañcitanipātasaṃśleaṣṇāccāpi ।।
avahitthavīkṣaṇādvā aṅgulibhaṅgena tarjanailalitaiḥ । ebhirbhāvaviśeṣairanunayaneṣvabhinayaḥ kāryaḥ ।। śobhase sādhu dṛṣṭo asi gaccha tvaṃ kiṃṃ vilambase । mā māṃ sprākṣīḥ priyā yatra tatra yā te hṛdi sthitā ।।
gacchetyuktvā parāvṛtya vinivṛttāntareṇa tu । kenacidvacanārthena praharṣaṃ yojayetpunaḥ ।। rabhasagrahaṇāccāpi haste vastre ca mūrdhani । kāryaṃ prasādanaṃ nāryā hyaparādhaṃ samīkṣya tu ।।
haste vastre atha keśānte nāryāpyatha gṛhītayā । kāntamevopasarpantyā kartavyaṃ mokṣaṇaṃ śanaiḥ ।। gṛhītāyātha keśānte haste vastre athavā punaḥ । huṃ muñcetyupasarpantyā vācyaḥ sparśālasaṃ priyaḥ ।।
pādāgrasthitayā nāryā kiṃcitkuṭṭamitotkaṭam । aśvakrāntena kartavyaṃ keśānāṃ mokṣaṇaṃ śanaiḥ ।। amucyamāne keśānte saṃjātasvedaleśayā । haṃ hu muñcāpasarpeti vācyaḥ sparśālasāṅgayā ।।
gaccheti roṣavākyena gatvā pratinivṛtya ca । kenacidvacanārthena vācyaṃ yāsyasi neti ca ।। vidhūnanena hastena huṃkāraṃ saṃprayojayet । sa cāvadhūnane kāryaḥ śapathairvyāja eva ca ।।
akṣṇoḥ saṃvaraṇe kāryaṃ pṛṣṭhataścopagūhanam । nāryāstvapahṛte vastre dīpacchādanameva ca ।। tāvat khedayitavyastu yāvatpādagato bhavet । tataścaraṇayoryāte kuryāddūtīnirīkṣaṇam ।।
utthāpyāliṅgayeccaiva nāyikā nāyakaṃ tataḥ । ratibhogagatā hṛṣṭā śayanābhimukhī vrajet ।। etadgītavidhānena sukumāreṇa yojayet । yadā śṛṅgārasaṃyuktaṃ ratisambhogakāraṇam ।।
yadā cākāśapuruṣaparasthavacanāśrayam । bhavetkāvyaṃ tadā hyeṣa kartavyo abhinayaḥ striyā ।। yadantapurasambandhaṃ kāryaṃ bhavati nāṭake । śṛṅgārarasasaṃyuktaṃ tatrāpyeṣa vidhirbhavet ।।
na kāryaṃ śayanaṃ raṅge nāṭyadharmaṃ vijānatā । kenacidvacanārthena aṅkacchedo vidhīyate ।। yadvā śayītārthavaśādekākī sahito api vā । cumbanāliṅganaṃ caiva tatha guhyaṃ ca yadbhavet ।।
dantacchedyaṃ nakhacchedyaṃ nīvīsraṃsanameva ca । stanāntaravimardaṃ ca raṅgamadhye na kārayet ।। bhojanaṃ salilakrīḍā tathā lajjākaraṃ ca yat । evaṃvidhaṃ bhavedyadyattattadraṅge na kārayet ।।
pitāputrasnuṣāśvaśrūdṛśyaṃ yasmāttu nāṭakam । tasmādetāni sarvāṇi varjanīyāni yatnataḥ ।। vākyaiḥ sātiśayaiḥ śravyairmadhurairnātiniṣṭhuraiḥ । hitopadeśasaṃyuktaistajjñaḥ kuryāttu nāṭakam ।।
evamantaḥpurakṛtaḥ kāryastvabhinayo budhaḥ । samāgame atha nārīṇāṃ vācyāni madanāśraye ।। priyeṣu vacanānīha yāni tāni nibodhata । priayaḥ kānto vinītaśca nāthaḥ svāmyatha jīvitam ।।
nandanaścetyabhiprīte vacanāni bhavanti hi । duḥśīlo atha durācāraḥ śaṭho vāmo vikatthanaḥ ।। nirlajjo niṣṭhuraścaiava priyaḥ krodhe abhidhīyate । yo vipriyaṃ na kurute na cāyuktaṃ prabhāṣate ।।
tathārjavasamācāraḥ sa priyastvabhidhīyate । anyanārīsamudbhūtaṃ cihnaṃ yasya na dṛṣyate ।। adhare vā śarīre vā sa kānta iti bhāṣyate । saṃkruddhe api hi yo nāryā nottaraṃ pratipadyate ।।
paruṣaṃ vā na vadati vinītaḥ sā'bhidhīyate । hitaiṣī rakṣaṇe śakto na mānī na ca matsarī ।। sarvakāryeṣvasaṃmūḍhaḥ sa nātha iti saṃjñitaḥ । sāmadānārthasaṃbhogaistathā lālanapālanaiḥ ।।
nārīṃ niṣevate yastu sa svāmītyabhidhīyate । nārīpsitairabhiprāyairnipuṇaṃ śayanakriyām ।। karoti yastu saṃbhoge sa jīvitamiti smṛtaḥ । kulīno dhṛtimāndakṣo dakṣiṇo vāgviśāradaḥ ।।
ślāghanīyaḥ sakhīmadhye nandanaḥ so abhidhīyate । ete vacanavinyāsā ratiprītikarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tathā cāprītivākyāni gadato me nibodhata । niṣṭhuraścāhiṣṇuśca māni dhṛṣṭo vikatthanaḥ ।।
anavasthitacittaśca duḥśīla iti sa smṛtaḥ । tāḍanaṃ bandhanaṃ cāpi yo vimṛśya samācaret ।। tathā paruṣavākyaśca durācāraḥ sa tanyate । vācaiava madhuro yastu karmaṇa nopapādakaḥ ।।
yoṣitaḥ kiñcidapyarthaṃ sa śaṭhaḥ paribhāṣyate । vāryate yatra yatrārthe tattadeva karoti yaḥ ।। viparītaniveśī ca sa vāma iti saṃjñitaḥ । sarasavraṇacihno yaḥ strīsaubhāgyavikatthanaḥ ।।
atimānī tathā stabdho vikatthana iti smṛtaḥ । vāryamāṇo dṛḍhataraṃ yo nārīmupasarpati ।। sacihnāḥ sāparādhaśca sa nirlajja iti smṛtaḥ । yo aparāddhastu sahasā nārīṃ sevitumicchati ।।
aprasādanabuddhiśca niṣṭhuraḥ so abhidhīyate । ete vacanavinyāsāḥ priyāpriyavibhāṣitāḥ ।। nartakīsaṃśritāḥ kāryā bahavo anye api nāṭake । eṣa gītavidhāne tu sukumāre vidhirbhavet ।।
śṛṅgārarasasaṃbhūto ratisaṃbhogakhedanaḥ । yaccaivākāśapuruṣaṃ parasthavacanāśrayam ।। śṛṅgāra evaṃ vācyaṃ syāttatrāpyeṣa kramo bhavet । yadvā purusaṃbandhaṃ kāryaṃ bhavati nāṭake ।।
śṛṅgārarasasaṃyuktaṃ tatrāpyeṣa kramo bhavet । evamantaḥpuragataḥ prayojyo abhinayo bhavet ।। divyāṅganānāṃ tu vidhiṃ vyākhyāsyamyanupūrvaśaḥ । nityamevojvalo veṣo nityaṃ pramuditaṃ manaḥ ।।
nityameva sukhaḥ kālo devānāṃ lalitāśrayaḥ । na cairṣyā naiva ca krodho nāsūyā na prasādanam ।। divyānāṃ dṛṣyate puṃsāṃ śṛṅgāre yoṣitāṃ tathā । ye bhāvā mānuṣāṇāṃ syuryadaṅgaṃ yacca ceṣṭitam ।।
sarvaṃ tadeva kartavyaṃ divyairmānuṣasaṅgame । yadā mānuṣasaṃbhogo divyānāṃ yoṣitāṃ bhavat ।। tadā sarvāḥ prakartavyā ye bhāvā mānuṣāśrayāḥ । śāpabhraṃśāttu divyānāṃ tathā cāpatyalipsayā ।।
kāryo mānuṣasaṃyogaḥ śṛṅgārarasasaṃśrayaḥ । puṣpairbhūṣaṇajaiḥ śabdairadṛśyāpi pralobhayet ।। punaḥ saṃdarśanaṃ dattvā kṣaṇādantaritā bhavet । vastrābharaṇamālyādyairlekhasaṃpreṣaṇairapi ।।
īdṛśairupacāraistu samunmādyastu nāyakaḥ । unmādanātsamudbhūtaḥ kāmo ratikaro bhavet ।। svabhāvopagato yastu nāsāvatyarthabhāvikaḥ । evaṃ rājopacāro hi kartavyo abhyantarāśrayaḥ ।।
bāhyamapyupacāraṃ tu pravakṣyāmyatha vaiśike । viśeṣayetkalāḥ sarvā yasmāttasmāttu vaiśikaḥ । veśopacāre sādhurvā vaiśikaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। yo hi sarvakalopetaḥ sarvaśilpavicakṣaṇaḥ ।
strīcittagrahaṇābhijño vaiśikaḥ sa bhavetpumān ।। guṇastasya tu vijñeyāḥ svaśarīrasamutthitāḥ । āhāryāḥ sahajāścaiva trayastriṃśatsamāsataḥ ।। śāstravicchilpasaṃpanno rūpavān priyadarśanaḥ vikrānto dhṛtimāṃścaiva vayoveṣakulānvitaḥ ।।
surabhirmadhurastyāgi sahiṣṇuravikatthanaḥ aśaṅkitaḥ priyābhāṣī caturaḥ śubhadaḥ śuciḥ ।। kāmopacārakuśalo dakṣiṇo deśakālavit । adīnavākyaḥ smitavān vāgmī dakṣaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ ।। strīlubdhāḥ saṃvibhāgī ca śraddhadhāno dṛḍhasmṛtiḥ ।
gamyāsu cāpyavisrambhī mānī ceti hi vaiśikaḥ ।। anuyuktaḥ śucirdakṣo dakṣiṇaḥ pratipattimān । bhaveccitrābhidhāyī ca vayasyastasya tadguṇaḥ ।। vijñānaguṇasaṃpanā kathinī liṅginī tathā ।
prātiveśyā sakhī dāsī kumārī kāruśilpinī ।। dhātrī pāṣaṇḍinī caiva tathā raṅgopajīvinī । protsāhane athakuśalā madhurakathā dakṣiṇāthakālajñā ।। laḍahā saṃvṛtamantrā dūtī tvebhirguṇaiḥ kāryā ।
tayāpyutsāhanaṃ kāryaṃ nānādarśitakāraṇam ।। yathoktakathanaṃ caiva tathā bhāvapradarśanam । na jaḍaṃ rūpasampannaṃ nārthavantaṃ na cāturam ।। dūtaṃ vā'pyathavā dūtīṃ budhaḥ kuryātkadācana ।
kulabhogadhanādhikyaiḥ kṛtvādhikavikatthanam ।। dūtī nivedayetkāmamarthāṃścaivānuvarṇayet । na cākāmapravṛttāyāḥ kṛddhāyā vāpi saṅgamaḥ ।। nānupāyaḥ prakartavyo dūtyā hi puruṣāśrayaḥ ।
utsave ratrisañcāra uddyāne mitraveśmani ।। dhātrigṛheṣu sakhyā vā tathā caiva nimantraṇe । vyādhitavyapadeśena śunyāgāraniveśane ।। kāryaḥ samāgamo nṝṇāṃ strībhiḥ prathamasaṅgame ।
evaṃ samāgamaṃ kṛtvā sopāyaṃ vidhipūrvakam ।। anuraktā viraktā vā liṅgākāraistu lakṣayet । svabhāvabhāvātiśayairnārī yā madanāśrayā ।। karoti nibhṛtāṃ līlāṃ nityaṃ sā madanāturā ।
sakhīmadhye guṇān brūte svadhanaṃ ca prayacchati ।। pūjayatyasya mitrāṇi dveṣṭi śatrujanaṃ sadā । gamāgame sakhīnāṃ yā hṛṣṭā bhavati cādhikam ।। tuṣyatyasya kathābhistu sasnehaṃ ca nirīkṣate ।
supte tu paścāt svapiti cumbitā praticumbati ।। uttiṣṭhatyapi pūrvaṃ ca tathā kleśasahāpi ca । utsave muditā yā ca vyasane yā ca duḥkhitā ।। evaṃvidhairguṇairyuktā tvanuraktā tu sā smṛtā ।
viraktāyāstu cinhāni cumbitā nābhicumbati ।। samāsatastu prakṛtistrividhā parikīrtitā । puruṣāṇāmatha strīṇāmuttamādhamamadhyamā ।। jitendriya jñānavatī nānāśilpavicakṣaṇā ।
dakṣiṇādhamahālakṣyā bhītānāṃ parisāntvanī ।। nānāśāstrārthasaṃpannā gāmbhīryaudāryaśālinī । sthairyatyāgaguṇopetā jñeyā prakṛtiruttamā ।। lokopacāracaturā śilpaśāstraviśāradā ।
vijñānamādhuryayutā madhyamā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā ।। rūkṣavāco atha duḥśīlāḥ kusattvāḥ sthūlabuddhayaḥ । krodhanāghātakāścaiva mitraghnāśchidramāninaḥ ।। piśunāstūddhatairvākyairakṛtajñāstathālasāḥ ।
mānyāmānyā viśeṣajñā strīlolāḥ kalahapriyāḥ ।। sūcakāḥ pāpakarmāṇaḥ paradravyāpahāriṇaḥ । ebhirdoṣaistusaṃpannā bhavantīhādhamā narāḥ ।। evaṃ tu śīlato nṝṇāṃ prakṛtistrividhā smṛtā ।
strīṇāṃ punaśca prakṛtiṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।। mṛdubhābā cācapalā smitabhāṣiṇyaniṣṭhurā । gurūṇāṃ vacane dakṣā salajjā vinayānvitā ।। rūpābhijanamādhuryairguṇaiḥ svābhāvikeryutā ।
gāmbhīryadhairyasampannā vijñeyā pramadottamā ।। nātyutkṛṣṭairanikhilairebhirevānvitā guṇaiḥ । alpadoṣānuviddhā ca madhyamā prakṛtiḥ smṛtā ।। adhamā prakṛtiryā tu puruṣāṇāṃ prakīrtitā ।
vijñeyā saiva nārīṇāmadhamānāṃ samāsataḥ ।। napuṃsakastu vijñeyaḥ saṃkīrṇo adhama eva ca । preṣyādirapi vijñeyā saṃkīrṇā prakṛtidvijāḥ ।। śakāraśca viṭaścaiva ye cānyepyevamādayaḥ ।
saṃkīrṇāste api vijñeyā hyadhamā nāṭake budhaiḥ ।। etā jñeyāḥ prakṛtayaḥ puruṣastrīnapuṃsakaiḥ । āsāṃ tu saṃpravakṣyāmi vidhānaṃ śīlasaṃśrayam ।। atra catvāra eva syurnāyakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
madhyamottamaprakṛtau nānālakṣaṇalakṣitāḥ ।। dhīroddhatā dhīralalitā dhīrodāttāstathaiva ca । dhīrapraśāntakāścaiva nāyakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। devā dhīroddhatā jñeyāḥ syurdhīralalitā nṛpāḥ ।
senāpatiramātyaśca dhīrodāttau prakīrtitau ।। dhīrapraśāntā vijñeyā brāhmaṇā vāṇijastathā । eteṣāṃ tu punarjñeyāścatvārastu vidūṣakaḥ ।। liṃgī dvijo rājajīvī śiṣyaśceti yathākramam ।
devakṣitibhṛtāmātyabrāhmaṇānāṃ prayojayet ।। vipralaṃbhasuhṛdomī saṃkathālāpapeśalāḥ । vyasanī prāpya duḥkhaṃ vā yujyate abhyudayena yaḥ ।। tathā puruṣamāhustaṃ pradhānaṃ nāyakaṃ budhāḥ ।
yatrānekasya bhavato vyasanābhyudayau punaḥ ।। sapuṣṭau yatra tau syātāṃ na bhavettatra nāyakaḥ । divyā ca nṛpapatnī ca kulastrī gaṇikā tathā ।। etāstu nāyikā jñeya nānāprakṛtilakṣaṇāḥ ।
dhīrā ca lalitā ca syādudāttā nibhṛtā tathā ।। divyā rājāṅganāścaiva guṇairyuktā bhavanti hi । udāttā nibhṛtā caiva bhavettu kulajāṅganā ।। lalite cābhyudātte ca gaṇikāśilpakārike ।
prakṛtīnāṃ tu sarvāsāmupacārād dvidhā smṛtāḥ ।। bāhyaścābhyantaraścaiva tayorvakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam । tatra rājopacāro yo bhavedābhyantaro hi saḥ ।। tato vākyopacārastu yasya bāhyaḥ sa ucyate ।
atha rājopacāre ca rājñāmantaḥpurāśritam ।। strīvibhāgaṃ pravakṣyāmi vibhaktamupacārataḥ । rājopacāraṃ vakṣyāmi hyantaḥpurasamāśrayam ।। mahādevī tathā devyaḥ svāminyaḥ sthāpitā api ।
bhoginyaḥ śilpakāriṇyo nāṭakīyāḥ sanartakāḥ ।। anucārikāśca vijñeyāstathā ca paricārikāḥ । tathā saṃcārikāścaiva tathā preṣaṇakārikāḥ ।। mahattaryaḥ pratīhāryaḥ kumāryaḥ sthavirā api ।
āyuktikāśca nṛpaterayamantaḥpuro janaḥ ।। atra mūrdhābhiṣiktā yā kulaśīlasamanvitā । guṇairyuktā vayassthā ca madhyasthā krodhanā tathā ।। mukterṣyā nṛpaśīlajñā sukhaduḥkhasahā samā ।
śāntisvastyayanairbhartussatataṃ maṅgalaiṣiṇī ।। śāntā pativratā dhīrā antaḥpurahite ratā । ebhirguṇaistu saṃyuktā mahadevītyudāhṛtā ।। ebhireva guṇairyuktāstatsaṃskāravivarjitāḥ ।
garvitāścātisaubhāgyāḥ patisaṃbhogatatparāḥ ।। śucinityojvalākārāḥ patipakṣābhyasūyakāḥ । vayorūpaguṇāḍhyā yāstā devya iti bhāṣitāḥ ।। senāpateramātyānāṃ bhṛtyānāmathavā punaḥ ।
bhaveyustanayā yāstu pratisammānavarjitāḥ ।। śīlarūpaguṇairyāstu saṃpannā nṛpaterhitāḥ । svaguṇairlabdhasammānā svāminya iti tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। rūpayauvanaśālinyaḥ karkaśā vibhramānvitāḥ ।
ratisaṃbhogakuśalāḥ pratipakṣābhyasūyakāḥ ।। dakṣā bhartuśca cittajñā gandhamālyojvalāssadā । nṛpateśchandavartinyo na hīrṣyāmānagarvitāḥ ।। utthitāśca pramattāśca tyaktālasyā na niṣṭhurāḥ ।
mānyāmānyaviśeṣajñāḥ sthāpitā iti tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। kulaśīlalabdhapūjāmṛdavo nāticodbhaṭāḥ । madhyasthā nibhṛtāḥ kṣāntā bhoginya iti tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। nānākalāviśeṣajñā nānāśilpavicakṣaṇāḥ ।
gandhapuṣpavibhāgajñā lekhyālekhyavikalpikāḥ ।। śayanāsanabhāgajñāścaturā madhurāstathā । dakṣāḥ saumyāḥ sphuṭāḥ śliṣṭhā nibhṛtāḥ śilpakārikāḥ ।। grahamokṣalayajñā yā rasabhāvavikalpikāḥ ।
caturānāṭyakuśalāścohāpohavicakṣaṇāḥ ।। rūpayauvanasaṃpannā nāṭakīyāstu tāḥ smṛtāḥ । helābhāvaviśeṣāḍhyā satvenābhinayena ca ।। mādhuryena ca saṃpannā hyātodyakuśalā tathā ।
aṅgapratyaṅgasaṃpannā catuṣṣaṣṭhikalānvitā ।। caturāḥ praśnayopetāḥ strīdoṣaiśca vivarjitāḥ । sadā pragalbhā ca tathā tyaktālasyā jitaśramā ।। nānāśilpaprayogajñā nṛttagītavicakṣaṇā ।
atha rūpaguṇaudāryadhairyasaubhāgyaśīlasaṃpannā ।। peśalamadhurasnigdhānunādikalacitrakaṇṭhā ca । samāgatāsu nārīṣu rūpayauvanakantibhiḥ ।। na dṛśyate guṇairstulyā yasyāḥ sā nartakī smṛtā ।
sarvāvasthopacāreṣu yā na muñcati parthivam ।। vijñeyā dakṣiṇā dakṣā nāṭyajñairanucārikā । śayyāpālī chatradhārī tathā vyajanadhāriṇī ।। saṃvāhikā gandhayoktrī tathā caiva prasādhikā ।
tathābharaṇayoktrī ca mālyasaṃyojikā tathā ।। evaṃ vidhā bhaveyuryāḥ tā jñeyāḥ paricārikāḥ । nānākakṣyā vicāriṇyaḥ tathoapavanasaṃcarāḥ ।। devatāyatanakrīḍā prāsādaparicārikāḥ ।
yāmakinyastathā caiva yāścaivaṃ lakṣaṇāḥ striyaḥ ।। saṃcārikāstu vijñeyā nāṭyajñaiḥ samudāhṛtāḥ । preṣaṇe akāmasaṃyukte guhyāguhyasamutthite ।। nṛpairyāstu niyujyante tāḥ jñeyāḥ paricārikāḥ ।
sarvāntaḥpurarakṣāsu stutisvastyayanena ca ।। yā vṛddhimabhinandanti tā vijñeyā mahattarāḥ । sandhivigrahasaṃbaddhanānācārasamutthitam ।। nivedayanti yāḥ kāryaṃ pratihāryastu tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
aprāptarasasaṃbhogā na saṃbhrāntā na codbhaṭāḥ ।। nibhṛtāśca salajjāśca kumāryo bālikāḥ smṛtāḥ । purvarājanayajñā yāḥ purvarājābhipūjitāḥ ।। purvarājānucaritāstā vṛddhā iti sujñitāḥ ।
bhāṇḍāgāreṣvadhikṛtāścāyudhādhikṛtāstathā ।। phalamūlauṣadhīnāṃ ca tathā caivānvavekṣakī । gandhābharaṇavastrāṇāṃ mālyānāṃ caiva cintikā ।। bahvāśraye tathā yuktā jñeyā hyāyuktikāstu tāḥ ।
ityantaḥpuracāriṇyaḥ striyaḥ proktā samāsataḥ ।। viśeṣaṇaviśeṣeṇa tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vai dvijāḥ । anuraktāśca bhaktāśca nānāpārśvasamutthitāḥ ।। yā niyuktā niyogeṣu kāryeṣu vividheṣu ca ।
na codbhaṭā asaṃbhrāntā na lubdhā nāpi niṣṭhurāḥ ।। dāntāḥ kṣāntāḥ prasannāśca jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ । akāmā lobhaḍīnāśca strīdoṣaiśca vivarjitāḥ ।। sā tvantaḥpurasaṃcāre yojyā pārthivaveśmani ।
kārukāḥ kañcukīyāśca tathā varṣavarāḥ punaḥ ।। aupasthāyikanirmuṇḍā strīṇā preṣaṇakarmaṇi । rakṣaṇaṃ ca kumārīṇāṃ bālikānāṃ prayojayet ।। antaḥpurādhikāreṣu rājacaryānuvarttinām ।
sarvavṛttāntasaṃvāhāḥ patyāgāre niyojayet ।। vinītāḥ svalpasattvā ye klībā vai strīsvabhāvikāḥ । jātyā na doṣiṇaścaiva te vai varṣavarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। brahmāṇāḥ kuśalā vṛddhāḥ kāmadoṣavivarjitāḥ ।
prayojaneṣu devīnāṃ prayoktavyā nṛpaiḥ sadā ।। etadaṣṭādaśavidhaṃ proktamantaḥpuraṃ mayā । ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bāhyaṃ puruṣasaṃbhavam ।। rājā senāpatiścaiva purodhā mantriṇastathā ।
sacivāḥ prāḍvivākāśca kumārādhikṛtāstathā ।। eke cānye ca bahavo mānyā jñeyā nṛpasya tu । veśeṣameṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇena nibodhata ।। balavān buddhisaṃpannaḥ satyavādī jitendriyaḥ ।
dakṣaḥ pragalbho dhṛtimān vikrānto matimāñchuciḥ ।। dīrghadarśī mahotsāhaḥ kṛtajñaḥ priyavāṅmṛduḥ । lokapālavratadharaḥ karmamārgaviśāradaḥ ।। utthitaścāpramattaśca vṛddhasevyarthaśāstravit ।
parabhāveṅgitābhijñaḥ śūro rakṣāsamanvitaḥ ।। ūhāpohavicārī ca nānāśilpaprayojakaḥ । nītiśāstrārthakuśalastathā caivānurāgavān ।। dharmajño avyasanī caiva guṇaireterbhavennṛpaḥ ।
kulīnā buddhisaṃpannā nānāśāstravipaścitāḥ ।। snigdhā parerahāryaśca na pramattāśca deśajāḥ । alubdhāśca vinītāśca śucayo dhārmikāstathā ।। purodho mantriṇastvebhirguṇairyuktā bhavanti hi ।
buddhimānnītisaṃpannastyaktālasyaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ ।। pararandhravidhijñaśca yātrākālaviśeṣavit । arthaśāstrārthakuśalo hyanuraktaḥ kulodbhavaḥ ।। deśavitkālaviccaiva kartavyaḥ kṣitipaiḥ sadā ।
vyavahārārthatattvajñā buddhimanto bahuśrutāḥ ।। madhyasthā dhārmikā dhīrāḥ kāryākāryavivekinaḥ । kṣāntā dāntā jitakrodhā sarvatra samadarśinaḥ ।। īdṛśaḥ prāḍvivākāstu sthāpyā dharmāsane dvijāḥ ।
utthitāśca pramattāśca tyaktālasyā jitaśramāḥ ।। snigdhā śāntā vinītāśca madhyasthā nipuṇāstathā । nayajñā vinayajñāśca ūhāpohavicakṣaṇāḥ ।। sarvaśātrārthasaṃpannāḥ kumārādhikṛtāstathā ।
bṛhaspatimatādeṣāṃ guṇāṃścābhikāṃkṣayet ।। vijñeyaṃ copahāryaṃ ca sabhyānāṃ ca vikalpanam । ityeṣa vo mayā proktaḥ prāḍvivākanirṇayaḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi citrābhinayanaṃ punaḥ ।
aṅgābhinayasyaiva yo viśeṣaḥ kvacit kvacit । anukta ucyate citraḥ citrābhinayassmṛtaḥ ।। uttānau tu karau kṛtvā svastikau pārśvasaṃsthitau । udvāhitena śirasā tathā cordhvanirīkṣaṇāt ।।
prabhātaṃ gaganaṃ rātriḥ pradoṣaṃ divasaṃ tathā । ṛtūn ghanān vanāntāṃśca vistīrṇāṃśca jalāśayān ।। diśo grahān sanakṣatrān kiñcit svasthaṃ ca yadbhavet । tasya tvabhinayaḥ kāryo nānādṛṣṭisamanvitaḥ ।।
ebhireva karairbhūyastenaiva śirasā punaḥ । adho nirīkṣaṇenātha bhūmisthān saṃpradarśayet ।। sparśasya grahaṇenaiva tathollukasanena ca । candrajyostnāṃ sukhaṃ vāyuṃ rasaṃ gandhaṃ ca nirdiśet ।।
vastrāvakuṇṭhanātsūryaṃ rajodhūmānilāṃstathā । bhūmitāpamathoṣṇaṃ ca kuryācchāyābhilāṣataḥ ।। ūrdhvākekaradṛṣṭistu madhyāhne sūryamādiśet । udayāstagataṃ caiva vismayārthaiḥ pradarśayet ।।
yāni saumyārthayuktāni susvabhāvakṛtāni ca । gātrasparśaissaromāñcaisteṣāmabhinayo bhavet ।। yāni syustīkṣṇarūpāṇi tāni cābhinayetsudhīḥ । asaṃsparśaistathodvegaistathā mukhavikuṇṭhanaiḥ ।।
gambhīrodātasaṃyuktānarthānabhinayedbudhaḥ । sāṭopaiśca sagarvaiśca gātraiḥ sauṣṭhavasaṃyutaiḥ ।। yajñopavītadeśasthamarālaṃ hāsamādiśet । svastikau vicyutau hārasragdāmārthān nidarśayet ।।
bhramaṇena pradarśinyā dṛṣṭeḥ parigamena ca । alapadmakapīḍāyāḥ sarvārthagrahaṇaṃ bhavet ।। śravyaṃ śravaṇayogena dṛśyaṃ dṛṣṭivilokanaiḥ । ātmasthaṃ parasaṃsthaṃ vā madhyasthaṃ vā vinirdiśet ।।
vidyudulkāghanaravāviṣphuliṃgārciṣastathā । trastāṃgākṣinimeṣaiśca te abhineyāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। udveṣṭitakarāvṛttau karau kṛtvā nataṃ śiraḥ । asaṃsparśe tathāniṣṭe jihmadṛṣṭena kārayet ।।
vāyumuṣṇaṃ tamastejo mukhapracchādanena ca । reṇutoyapataṃgāṃśca bhramarāṃśca nivārayet ।। kṛtvā svastikasaṃsthānau padmakośāvadhomukhau । siaṃharkṣavānaravyāghraśvāpadāṃśca nirūpayet ।।
svastikau tripatākau tu gurūṇāṃ pādavandane । khaṭakasvasthikau cāpi pratodagrahaṇe smṛtau ।। ekaṃ dvi trīṇi catvāri pañca ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭadhā । nava vā daśa vāpi syurgaṇanāṃgulibhirbhavet ।।
daśākhyāśca śatākhyāśca sahasrākhyāstathaiva ca । patākābhyāṃ tu hastābhyāṃ prayojyāstāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। daśākhyagaṇanāyāstu parato yā bhavediha । vākyārthenaiva sādhyāsau parokṣābhinayena ca ।।
chatradhvajapatākāśca nirdeśyā daṇḍadhāraṇāt । nānāpraharaṇaṃ cātha nirdeśyaṃ dhāraṇāśrayam ।। ekacitto hyadhodṛṣṭiḥ kiñcinnataśirāstathā । savyahastaśca saṃdaṃśaḥ smṛte dhyāne vitarkite ।।
udvāhitaṃ śiraḥ kṛtvā haṃsapakṣau pradakṣiṇau । apatyarūpaṇe kāryāvuchrayau ca prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। udvāhitaṃ śiraḥ kṛtvā haṃsavaktraṃ tathordhvagam । prasādayacca yaṃ mānaṃ dīrghasatvaṃ ca nirdiśet ।।
arālaṃ ca śirasthāne samudvāhya tu vāmakam । gate nirvṛtte dhvaste ca śrāntavākye ca yojayet ।। sarvendriyasvasthatayā prasannavadanastathā । vicitrabhūtalālokaiḥ śaradantu vinirdiśet ।।
gātrasaṃkocanāccāpi sūryāgnipaṭusevanāt । hemantastvabhinetavyaḥ puruṣairmadhyamādhamaiḥ ।। śirodantoṣṭhakampena gātrasaṃkocanena ca । kūjitaiśca saśītkārairadhamaśśītamādiśet ।।
avasthāntaramāsādya kadācittūttamarairapi । śītābhinayanaṃ kūryāddevādvyasanasaṃbhavam ।। ṛtujānāṃ tu puṣpāṇāṃ gandhaghrāṇaistathaiva ca । rūkṣasya vāyoḥ sparśācca śiśiraṃ rūpayedbudhaḥ ।।
pramodajananāraṃbhairupabhogaiḥ pṛthagvidhiḥ । vasantastvabhinetavyo nānāpuṣpapradarśanāt ।। sveda pramārjanaiścaiva bhūmitāpaiḥ savījanaiḥ । uṣṇasya vāyoḥ sparśena grīṣmaṃ tvabhinayedbudhaḥ ।।
kadambanīpakuṭapaiḥ śādvalaiḥ sendragopakaiḥ । meghavātaiḥ sukhasparśaiḥ prāvṛṭkālaṃ pradarśayet ।। meghaughanādairgambhīrairdhārāprapatanaistadā । vidyunnirghātaghoṣaiśca varṣārātraṃ samādiśet ।।
yadyasya cihnaṃ veṣo vā karma vā rūpameva vā । nirdeśyaḥ sa ṛtustena iṣṭāniṣṭārthadarśanāt ।। etānṛtūnarthavaśāddarśayeddhi rasānugān । sukhinastu sukhopetān suḥkhārthān duḥkhasaṃyutān ।।
yo yena bhāvenāviṣṭaḥ sukhadenetareana vā । sa tadāhitasaṃkāraḥ sarvaṃ paśyati tanmayam ।। bhāvābhinayanaṃ kuryādvibhāvānāṃ nidarśanaiḥ । tathaiva cānubhāvānāṃ bhāvasiddhiḥ pravartitā ।।
vibhāvenāhṛtaṃ kāryamanubhāvena nīyate । ātmānubhavanaṃ bhāvo vibhāvaḥ paradarśanam ।। gururmitraṃ sakhā snigdhaḥ saṃbandhī bandhureva vā । āvedyate hi yaḥ prāptaḥ sa vibhāva iti smṛtaḥ ।।
yattvasya saṃbhramotthānairarghyapādyāsanādibhiḥ । pūjanaṃ kriyate bhaktyā so anubhāvaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। evamanyeṣvapi jñeyo nānākāryapradarśanāt । vibhāvo vāpi bhāvo vā vijñeyo arthavaśādbudhaiḥ ।।
yastvapi pratisaṃdeśo dūtasyeha pradīyate । so anubhāva iti jñeyaḥ pratisandeśadarśitaḥ ।। evaṃ bhāvo vibhāvo vāpyanubhāvaśca kīrtitaḥ । puruṣairabhineyaḥ syātpramadābhirathāpi vā ।।
svabhāvābhinaye sthānaṃ puṃsāṃ kāryaṃ tu vaiṣṇavam । āyataṃ vāvahitthaṃ vā strīṇāṃ kāryaṃ svabhāvataḥ ।। prayojanavaśāccaiva śeṣāṇyapi bhavanti hi । nānābhavābhinayanaiḥ prayogaiśca pṛthagvidhaiḥ ।।
dhairyalīlāṅgasaṃpannaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ viceṣṭitam । mṛdulīlāṅgahāraiśca strīṇāṃ kāryaṃ tu ceṣṭitam ।। karapādāṅgasañcārāsstrīṇāṃ tu lalitāḥ smṛtāḥ । sudhīraścoddhataścaiva puruṣāṇāṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
yathā rasaṃ yathā bhāvaṃ strīṇāṃ bhāvapradarśanam । narāṇāṃ pramadānāṃ ca bhāvābhinayanaṃ pṛthak ।। bhāvānubhāvanaṃ yuktaṃ vyākhyāsyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ । āliṅganena gātrāṇāṃ sasmitena ca cakṣuṣā ।।
tathollukasānaccāpi harṣaṃ saṃdarśayennaraḥ । kṣiprasa!njātaromāñcāt bāṣpeṇāvṛtalocanā ।। kurvīta nartakī harṣaṃ prītyā vākyaiśca sasmitaiḥ । udvṛttaraktanetraśca sandaṣṭādhara eva ca ।।
niśvāsakaṃpitāṃgaśca krodhaṃ cābhinayennaraḥ । netrābhyāṃ bāṣpapūrṇābhyāṃ cibukauṣṭhaprakaṃpanāt ।। śirasaḥ kaṃpanāccaiva bhrukuṭīkaraṇena ca । maunenāṅgulibhaṅgena mālyābharaṇavarjanāt ।।
āyatakasthānakakṣāyā īrṣyā krodhe bhavetstriyāḥ । niśvāsocchvāsabahulairadhomukhavicintanaiḥ ।। ākāśavacanāccāpi duḥkhaṃ puṃsāṃ tu yojayet । ruditaiḥ śvasitaiścaiva śirobhihananena ca ।।
bhūmipātābhighātaiśca duḥkhaṃ strīṣu prayojayet । ānandajaṃ cārtijaṃ vā īrṣyāsaṃbhūtameva vā ।। yatpūrvamuktaṃ ruditaṃ tatstrīnīceṣu yojayet । saṃbhramāvegaceṣṭābhiśśastrasaṃpātanena ca ।।
puruṣāṇāṃ bhayaṃ kāryaṃ dhairyāvegabalādibhiḥ । calatārakanetratvādgātraiḥ sphuritakampitaiḥ ।। santrastahṛdayatvācca pārśvābhyāmavalokanaiḥ । bhartṛranveṣaṇāccaivamuccairākrandanādapi ।।
priyasyāliṃganāccaiva bhayaṃ kāryaṃ bhavetstriyāḥ । madā ye abhihitāḥ pūrvaṃ te strīnīceṣu yojayet ।। mṛdubhiḥ skhalitairnityamākāśasyāvalaṃbanāt । netrāvaghūrṇanaiścaiva sālasyaiḥ kathitaistathā ।।
gātrāṇāṃ kaṃpanaiścaiva madaḥ kāryo bhavetstriyāḥ । anena vidhinā kāryaḥ prayogāḥ kāraṇotthitāḥ ।। pauruṣaḥ strīkṛto vāpi bhāvā hyabhinayaṃ prati । sarve salalitā bhāvāsstrībhiḥ kāryāḥ prayatnataḥ ।।
dhairyamādhuryasaṃpannā bhāvāḥ kāryāstu pauruṣāḥ । tripatākāṅgulībhyāṃ tu valitābhyāṃ prayojayet ।। śukāśca sārikāścaiva sūkṣmā ye cāpi pakṣiṇaḥ । śikhisārasahaṃsādyāḥ sthūlā ye api svabhāvataḥ ।।
recakairaṅgahāraiśca teṣāmabhinayo bhavet । kharoṣṭrāśvatarāsiṃhavyāghragomahiṣādaya ।। gatipracarairaṅgaiśca te abhineyāḥ prayoktṛbhiḥ । bhūtāḥ piśācā yakṣāśca dānavāḥ saharākṣasaiḥ ।।
aṅgahārairavinirdeśyā nāmasaṃkīrtanādapi । aṅgahārairvinirdeśyā apratyakṣā bhavanti ye ।। pratyakṣāstvabhinetavyā bhayodvegaiḥ savismayaiḥ । devāśca cihnaiśca praṇāmakaraṇairbhāvaiśca viceṣṭitaiḥ ।।
abhineyo hyarthavaśādapratyakṣāḥ prayogajñaiḥ । savyotthitena hastena hyarālena śiraḥ spṛśet ।। nare ahyabhivādanaṃ hyetadapratyakṣe vidhīyate । khaṭakāvardhamānena kapotākhyena vā punaḥ ।।
daivatāni gurūṃścaiva pramadāścābhivādayet । divaukasaśca ye pūjyāḥ pratyakṣāśca bhavanti ye ।। tān pramāṇaiḥ prabhāvaiśca gaṃbhīrārthaiśca yojayet । mahājanaṃ sakhīvargaṃ viṭadhūrtajanaṃ tathā ।।
parimaṇḍalasaṃsthena hastenābhinayenannaraḥ । parvatān prāṃśuyogena vṛkṣāṃścaiva samucchritān ।। prasāritābhyāṃ bāhubhyāmutkṣiptābhyāṃ prayojayet । samūhasāgaraṃ senā bahuvistīrṇameva ca ।।
patākābhyāṃ tu hastābhyāmutkṣiptābhyāṃ pradarśayet । śauryaṃ dhairyaṃ ca garvaṃ ca darpamaudāryamucchrayam ।। lalāṭadeśasthānena tvarālenābhidarśayet । vakṣodeśādapāviddhau karau tu mṛgaśīrṣakau ।।
vistīrṇapradrutotkṣepau yojyau yasyādapāvṛtam । adhomukhottānatalau hastau kiñcitprasāritau ।। kṛtvā tvabhinayedvelāṃ biladvāraṃ gṛhaṃ guhān । kāmaṃ śāpagrahagrastān jvaropahatacetasaḥ ।।
eteṣāṃ ceṣṭitaṃ kuryādaṅgādyaiḥ sadṛśairbudhaiḥ । dolābhinayanaṃ kuryāddolāyāstu vilokanaiḥ ।। saṃbhokṣeṇa ca gātrāṇāṃ rajvaśvāgrahaṇena ca । yadā cāṅgavatī ḍolā pratyakṣā pustajā bhavet ।।
āsaneṣu praviṣṭānāṃ kartavyaṃ tatra ḍolanam । ākāśavacanānīha vakṣyāmyātmagatāni ca ।। apavāritakaṃ caiva janāntikamathāpi ca । dūrasthābhāṣaṇaṃ yatsyādaśarīranivedanam ।।
parokṣāntaritaṃ vākyamākāśavacanaṃ tu tat । tatrottarakṛtairvākyaiḥ saṃlāpaṃ saṃprayojayet ।। nānākāraṇasaṃyuktaiḥ kāvyabhāvasamutthitaiḥ । hṛdayasya vaco yattū tadātmagatamīṣyate ।।
savitarkaṃ ca tadyojyaṃ prāyaśo nāṭakādiṣu । nigūḍhabhāvasaṃyuktamapavāritakaṃ smṛtam ।। kāryavaśādaśravaṇaṃ pārśvagatairyajjanāntikaṃ tatsyāt । hṛdayasthaṃ savikalpaṃ bhāvasthaṃ cātmagatameva ।।
iti gūḍhārthayuktāni vacanānīha nāṭake । janāntikāni karṇe tu tāni yojyāni yoktṛbhiḥ ।। pūrvavṛttaṃ tu yatkāryaṃ bhūyaḥ kathyaṃ tu kāraṇāt । karṇapradeśe tadvācyaṃ māgāttatpunaruktatām ।।
avyabhicāreṇa paṭhedākāśajanāntikātmagatapāṭhyam । pratyakṣaparokṣakṛtānāmātmasamutthān parakṛtāṃśca ।। hastamantaritaṃ kṛtvā tripatākaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ । janāntikaṃ prayoktavyamapavāritakaṃ tathā ।।
svapnāyitavākyārthaistvabhineyo na khalu hastasaṃcāraiḥ । suptābhihitaireva tu vākyārthaiḥ so abhineyaḥ syāt ।। mandasvarasañcārairvyaktāvyaktaṃ punaruktavacanārtham । pūrvānusmaraṇakṛtaṃ kāryaṃ svapnāñcite pāṭhyam ।।
praśithilagurukaruṇākṣaraghaṇṭānusvaritavākyagadgadajaiḥ । hikkāśvasopetāṃ kākuṃ kuryānmaraṇakāle ।। hikkāśvāsopetāṃ mūrcchopagame maraṇavatkathayet । atimatteṣvapi kāryaṃ tadvatsvapnāyite yathā pāṭhyam ।।
vṛddhānāṃ yojayetpāṭhyaṃ gadgadaskhalitākṣaram । asamāptākṣaraṃ caiva bālānāṃ tu kalasvanam ।। nānābhāvopagataṃ maraṇābhinaye bahukīrtitaṃ tu । vikṣiptahastapādairnibhṛtaiḥ sannaistathā kāryam ।।
vyādhiplute ca maraṇaṃ niṣaṇṇagātraistu saṃprayoktavyam । hikkāśvāsopetaṃ tathā parādhīnagātrasaṃcāram ।। viṣapīte api ca maraṇaṃ kāryaṃ vikṣiptagātrakaracaraṇam । viṣavegasaṃprayuktaṃ visphuritāṃgakriyopetam ।।
pratheme vege kārśyaṃ tvabhineye vepathurdvitīye tu । dāhastathā tṛtīye vilallikā syāccaturthe tu ।। phenastu pañcamasthe tu grīvā ṣaṣṭhe tu bhajyate । jaḍatā saptame tu syānmaraṇaṃ tvaṣṭame bhavet ।।
tatra prathamavege tu kṣāmavakrakapolatā । kṛśatve abhinayaḥ kāryo vākyānāmalpabhāṣaṇam ।। sarvāṅgavepathuṃ ca kaṇḍūyanaṃ tathāṅgānām । vikṣiptahastagātraṃ dāhaṃ caivāpyabhinayettu ।।
udvṛttanimeṣatvādudgāracchardanaistathākṣepaiḥ । avyaktākṣarakathanaiḥ vilallikāmabhinayedevam ।। udgāravamanayogaiḥ śirasaśca vilolanairanekavidhaiḥ । phenastvabhinetavyo niḥsaṃjñatayā nimeṣaiśca ।।
aṃsakapolasparśaḥ śiraso atha vināmanaṃ śiro apāṅgaḥ । sarvendriayasaṃmohājjaḍatāmevaṃ tvabhinayettu ।। saṃmīlitanetratvāt vyādhivivṛddhau bhujaṅgadaśanādvā । evaṃ hi nāṭyadharme maraṇāni budhaiḥ prayojyāni ।।
saṃbhrameṣvatha roṣeṣu śokāveśakṛteṣu ca । yāni vākyāni yujyante punaruktaṃ na teṣviha ।। sādhvaho māṃ ca heheti kiṃ tvaṃ māmāvadeti ca । evaṃvidhāni kāryāṇi dvitrisaṃkhyāni kārayet ।।
pratyaṅgahīnaṃ yatkāvyaṃ vikṛtaṃ ca prayujyate । na lakṣaṇakṛtastatra kāryastvabhinayo budhaiḥ ।। bhāvo yatrottamānāṃ tu na taṃ madhyeṣu yojayet । yo bhāvaścaiva madhyānāṃ na te nīceṣu yojayet ।।
pṛthak pṛthagbhāvarasairātmaceṣṭāsamutthitaiḥ । jyeṣṭhamadhyamanīceṣu nāṭyaṃ rāgaṃ hi gacchati ।। ete abhinayaviśeṣāḥ kartavyāḥ sattvabhāvasaṃyuktāḥ । anye tu laukikā ye tu te sarve lokavatkāryāḥ ।।
nānāvidhairyathā puṣpairmālāṃ grathnāti mālyakṛt । aṃgopāṃgai rasairbhāvaistathā nāṭyaṃ prayojayet ।। yā yasya līlā niyatā gatiśca raṅgapraviṣṭasya nidhānayuktaḥ । tāmeva kuryādavimuktasattvo yāvannaraṅgātpratinirvṛtaḥ syāt ।।
evamete mayā proktā nāṭye cābhinayāḥ kramāt । anye tu laukikā ye te lokādgrāhyāḥ sadā budhaiḥ ।। loko vedastathādhyātmaṃ pramāṇaṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam । vedādhyātmapadārtheṣu prāyo nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।
vedādhyātmopapannaṃ tu śabdacchandassamanvitam । lokasiddhaṃ bhavetsiddhaṃ nāṭyaṃ lokātmakaṃ tathā ।। na ca śakyaṃ hi lokasya sthāvarasya carasya ca । śāstreṇa nirṇayaṃ kartuṃ bhāvaceṣṭāvidhiṃ prati ।।
nānāśīlāḥ prakṛtayaḥ śīle nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhiatam । tasmāllokapramāṇaṃ hi vijñeyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ।। etān vidhīṃścābhinayasya samyagvijñāya raṅge manujaḥ prayuṅkte । sa nāṭyatattvābhinayaprayoktā saṃmānamagryaṃ labhate hi loke ।।
evamete hyabhinayā vāṅnepathyāṅgasaṃbhavāḥ । prayogajñena kartavyā nāṭake siddhimicchatā ।। anurūpā virūpā ca tathā rūpānurūpiṇī । triprakāreha pātrāṇāṃ prakṛtiśca vibhāvitā ।।
nānāvasthākriyopetā bhūmikā prakṛtistathā । bhṛśamudyotayennāṭyaṃ svabhāvakaraṇāśrayam ।। bahubāhūbahumukhāstathā ca vikṛtānanāḥ । paśuśvāpadavaktrāśca kharoṣṭrāśca gajānanāḥ ।।
ete cānye ca bahavo nānārūpā bhavanti ye । ācāryeṇa tu te kāryā mṛtkāṣṭhajatucarmabhiḥ ।। svābhāvikena rūpena praviśedraṅgamaṇḍalam । ātmarūpamavacchādya varṇakairbhūṣaṇairapi ।।
yādṛśaṃ yasya yadrūpaṃ prakṛtyā tatra tādṛśam । vayoveṣānurūpeṇa prayojyaṃ nāṭyakarmaṇi ।। yathā jīvatsvabhāvaṃ hi parityajyānyadehikam । parabhāvaṃ prakurute parabhāvaṃ samāśritaḥ ।।
evaṃ budhaḥ paraṃbhāvaṃ so asmīti manasā smaran । yeṣāṃ vāgaṅgalīlābhiśceṣṭābhistu samācaret ।। sukumāraprayogo yo rājñāmāmodasaṃbhavaḥ । śṛṅgārarasamāsādya tannārīṣu prayojayet ।।
yuddhoddhatāviddhakṛtā saṃraṃbhārabhaṭāśca ye । na te strībhiḥ prayoktavyāḥ yoktavyāḥ puruṣeṣu te ।। anudbhaṭamasaṃbhrāntamanāviddhāṅgaceṣṭitam । layatālakalāpātapramāṇaniyatākṣaram ।।
suvibhaktapadālāpamaniṣṭhuramakāhalam । īdṛśaṃ yadbhavennāṭyaṃ nārībhiśca prayojayet ।। evaṃ kāryaṃ prayogajñairbhūmikāviniveśanam । striyo hi strīgato bhāvaḥ pauruṣaḥ puruṣasyaca ।।
yathā vayo yathāvasthamanurūpeti sā smṛtā । puruṣaḥ strīkṛtaṃ bhāvaṃ rūpātprakurute tu yaḥ ।। rūpānurūpā sā jñeyā prayoge prakṛtirbudhaḥ । chandataḥ pauruṣīṃ bhūmiṃ strī kuryādanurūpataḥ ।।
na parasparaceṣṭāsu kāryau sthavirabāliśau । pāṭhyaprayoge puruṣāḥ prayoktavyā hi saṃskṛte ।। strīṇāṃ svabhāvamadhurāḥ kaṇṭhāḥ puṃsāṃ tu balavantaḥ । yadyapi puruṣo vidyāt gītavidhānaṃ ca lakṣaṇopetam ।।
mādhuryaguṇavihīnaṃ śobhāṃ janayenna tadgītam । yatra strīṇāṃ pāṭhyādguṇairnarāṇāṃ ca kaṇṭhamādhuryam ।। prakṛtiviparyayajanitau vijñeyau tāvalaṅkārau । prāyeṇa devapārthivasenāpatimukhyapuruṣabhavaneṣu ।।
strījanakṛtāḥ prayogā bhavanti puruṣasvabhāvena । rambhorvaśīprabhṛtiṣu svarge nāṭyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। tathaiva mānuṣe loke rājñāmantaḥpureṣviha । upadeṣṭavyamācāryaiḥ prayatnenāṅganājane ।।
na svayaṃ bhūmikābhyāso budhaiḥ kāryastu nāṭake । strīṣu yojyaḥ prayatnena prayogaḥ puruṣāśrayaḥ ।। yasmātsvabhāvopagato vilāsaḥ strīṣu vidyate । tasmātsvabhāvamadhuramaṅgaṃ sulabhasauṣṭhavam ।।
lalitaṃ sauṣṭhavaṃ yacca so alaṅkāraḥ paro mataḥ । prayogo dvividhaścaiva vijñeyo nāṭakāśrayaḥ ।। sukumārastathāviddho nānābhāvarasāśrayaḥ । nāṭakaṃ saprakaraṇaṃ bhāṇo vīthyaṅka eva ca ।।
jñeyāni sukumārāṇi mānuṣairāśritāni tu । sukumāraprayogo ayaṃ rājñāmāmodakārakaḥ ।। śṛṅgārasamāsādya strīṇāṃ tattu prayojayet । yuddhoddhatāviddhakṛtāsaṃraṃbhārabhaṭāśca ye ।।
na te strīṇāṃ prakartavyāḥ kartavyāḥ puruṣairhi te । yathāviddhāṅgahāraṃ tu bhedyabhedyāhavātmakam ।। māyendrajālabahulaṃ pustanaipathyadīpitam । puruṣaprāyasaṃcāramalpastrīkamathoddhatam ।।
sātvatyārabhaṭīyuktaṃ nāṭyamāviddhasaṃjñitam । ḍimaḥ samavakāraśca vyāyogehāmṛgau tathā ।। etānyāviddhasaṃjñāni vijñeyāni prayoktṛbhiḥ । eṣāṃ prayogaḥ kartavyo devadānavarākṣasaiḥ ।।
uddhatā ye ca puruṣāḥ śauryavīryasamanvitāḥ । yogyaḥ sa ca prayatnaḥ kartavyaḥ satatapramādena ।। na hi yogyayā vinā bhavati ca bhāvarasasauṣṭhavaṃ kiṃcit । saṃgītaparikleśo nityaṃ pramadājanasya guṇa eva ।।
yanmadhurakarkaśatvaṃ labhate nāṭyaprayogeṇa । pramadāḥ nāṭyavilāsairlabhate yat kusumairvicitralāvaṇyam । kāmopacārakuśalā bhavanti ca kāmyā viśeṣeṇa ।। gītaṃ vṛttaṃ tathā vādyaṃ prastāragamanakriyā ।
śiṣyaniṣpādanaṃ caiva ṣaḍācāryaguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। etāni pañca yo vetti sa ācāryaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । ūhāpohau matiścaiva smṛtirmedhā tathaiva ca ।। medhāsmṛtirguṇaślāghārāgaḥ saṃgharṣa eva ca ।
utsāhaśca ṣaḍevaitān śiṣyasyāpi guṇān viduḥ ।। evaṃ kāryaṃ prayogajñairnānābhūmivikalpanam । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhīnāmapi lakṣaṇam ।। siddhīnāṃ tu pravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ nāṭakāśrayam ।
yasmātprayogaḥ sarvo ayaṃ siddhyarthaṃṃ saṃpradarśitaḥ ।। siddhistu dvividhā jñeyā vāṅmanoṅgasamudbhavā । daivī ca mānuṣī caiva nānābhāvasamutthitā ।। daśāṅgā mānuṣī siddhīrdaivī tu dvividhā smṛtā ।
nānāsattvāśrayakṛtā vāṅnaipathyaśarīrajā ।। smitāpahāsinī hāsā sādhvaho kaṣṭameva ca । prabaddhanādā ca tathā siddhirjñeyātha vāṅmayī ।। pulakaiśca saromāñcairabhyutthānaistathaiva ca ।
celadānāṅgulikṣepaiḥ śārīrī siddhiriṣyate ।। kiñcicchiṣṭo raso hāsyo nṛtyadbhiryatra yujyate । smitena sa pratigrāhyaḥ prekṣakairnityameva ca ।। kiñcidaspaṣṭahāsyaṃ yattathā vacanameva ca ।
arthahāsyena tadgrāhyaṃ prekṣakairnityameva hi ।। vidūṣakocchedakṛtaṃ bhavecchilpakṛtaṃ ca yat । atihāsyena tadgrāhyaṃ prekṣakairnityameva tu ।। ahokārastathā kāryo nṛṇāṃ prakṛtisaṃbhavaḥ ।
yaddharmapadasaṃyuktaṃ yathātiśayasaṃbhavam ।। tatra sādhviti yadvākyaṃ prayoktavyaṃ hi sādhakaiḥ । vismayāviṣṭabhāveṣu praharṣārtheṣu caiva hi ।। karuṇe api prayoktavyaṃ kaṣṭaṃ śāstrakṛtena tu ।
prabaddhanādā ca tathā vismayārtheṣu nityaśaḥ ।। sādhikṣepeṣu vākyeṣu praspanditatanūruhaiḥ । kutūhalottarāvedhairbahumānena sādhayet ।। dīptapradeśaṃ yatkāryaṃ chedyabhedyāhavātmakam ।
savidravamathotphullaṃ tathā yuddhaniyuddhajam ।। prakampitāṃsaśīrṣañca sāśraṃ sotthānameva ca । tatprekṣakaistu kuśalaissādhyamevaṃ vidhānataḥ ।। evaṃ sādhayitavyaiṣā tajjñaiḥ siddhistu mānuṣī ।
daivikīñca punaḥ siddhiṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tattvataḥ ।। yā bhāvātiśayopetā sattvayuktā tathaiva ca । sā prekṣakaistu kartavyā daivī siddhiḥ prayogataḥ ।। na śabdo na yatra na kṣobho na cotpātanidarśanam ।
saṃpūrṇatā ca raṃgasya daivī siddhistu sā smṛtā ।। daivī ca mānuṣī caiva siddhireṣā mayoditā । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ghātāndaivasamutthitan ।। daivātmaparasamutthā trividhā ghātā budhaistu vijñeyā ।
autpātikaścaturthaḥ kadācidatha saṃbhavatyeṣu ।। vātāgnivarṣakuñjarabhujaṅgamaṇḍapanipātāḥ । kīṭavyālapipīlikapaśupraveśanāśca daivakakṛtā ।। ghātanataḥ paramahaṃ parayuktān saṃpravakṣyāmi ।
[vaivarṇyaṃ cāceṣṭaṃ vibhramitatvaṃ smṛtipramohaśca ।। anyavacanaṃ ca kāvyaṃ tathāṃgadoṣo vihastatvam । ete tvātmasamutthā ghātā jñeyā prayogajñaiḥ] ।। mātsaryāddveṣādvā tatpakṣatvāttathārthabhedatvāt ।
ete tu parasamutthā jñeyā ghātā budhairnityam ।। atihasitaruditavisphoṭitānyathotkṛṣṭanālikāpātāḥ । gomayaloṣṭapipīlikāvikṣepāścārisaṃbhūtāḥ ।। autpatikāśca ghātā mattonmattapraveśaliṅgakṛtaḥ ।
punarātmasamutthā ye ghātāṃstāṃstān pravakṣyāmi ।। vailakṣaṇyamaceṣṭitavibhūmikatvaṃ smṛtipramoṣaśca । anyavacanaṃ ca kāvyaṃ tathārtanādo vihastatvam ।। atihasitaruditavisvarapipīlikākīṭapaśuvirāvāśca ।
mukuṭābharaṇanipātā puṣkarajāḥ kāvyadoṣāśca ।। atihasitaruditahasitāni siddhairbhāvasya dūṣakāṇi syuḥ । kīṭapipīlikapātā siddhiṃ sarvātmanā ghnānta ।। vivasvaramajātatālaṃ varṇasvarasaṃpadā ca parihīṇam ।
ajñātasthānalayaṃ svaragatamevaṃvidhaṃ hanyāt ।। mukuṭābharaṇanipātaḥ prabaddhanādaśca nāśano bhavati । paśuviśasanaṃ tatha a syādbahuvacanaghnaṃ prayogeṣu ।। viṣamaṃ mānavihīnaṃ vimārjanaṃ cākulaprahāraṃ ca ।
avibhaktagrahamokṣaṃ puṣkaragatamīdṛśaṃ hanti ।। punarukto hyasamāso vibhaktibhedo visandhayo apārthaḥ । trailiṅgajaśca doṣaḥ pratyakṣaparokṣasaṃmohāḥ ।। chandovṛttatyāgo gurulāghavasaṅkaro yaterbhedaḥ ।
etāni yathā sthūlaṃ ghātasthānāni kāvyasya ।। jñeyau tu kāvyajātau dvau ghātāvapratikriyau nityam । prakṛtivyasanasamutthaḥ śeṣodakanālikatvam ।। apratibhāgaṃ skhalanaṃ visvaramuccāraṇaṃ ca kāvyasya ।
asthānabhūṣaṇatvaṃ patanaṃ mukuṭasya vibhraṃśaḥ ।। vājisyandanakuñjarakharoṣṭraśibikāvimānayānānām । ārohaṇāvataraṇeṣvanabhijñatvaṃ vihastvam ।। praharaṇakavacānāmapyayathāgrahaṇaṃ vidhāraṇaṃ cāpi ।
amukuṭabhūṣaṇayogaścirapraveśo athavā raṅge ।। ebhiḥ sthānaviśeṣairghātā lakṣyāstu sūribhiḥ kuśalaiḥ । yūpāgnicayanadarbhastragbhāṇḍaparigrahānmuktvā ।। siddhyā miśro ghātassarvagataścaikadeśajo vāpi ।
nāṭyakuśalaiḥ salekhyā siddhirvā syādvighāto vā ।। nālekhyo bahudinajaḥ sarvagato avyaktalakṣaṇaviśeṣaḥ । yastvaikadivasajātassa pratyavaro api lekhyassyāt ।। jarjaramokṣyasyānte siddhermokṣastu nālikāyāstu ।
kartavyastviha satataṃ nāṭyajñaiḥ prāśnikairvidhinā ।। dainye dīnatvamāyānti te nāṭye prekṣakāḥ smṛtāḥ । ye tuṣṭau tuṣṭimāyānti śoke śokaṃ vrajanti ca ।। yo anyasya mahe mūrdho nāṃdīślokaṃ paṭheddhi devasya ।
svavaśena pūrvaraṅge siddherghātaḥ prayogasya ।। yo deśabhāvarahitaṃ bhāṣākāvyaṃ prayojayedbuddhyā । tasyāpyabhilekhyaḥ syādghāto deśaḥ prayogajñaiḥ ।। kaḥ śakto nāṭyavidhau yathāvadupapādanaṃ prayogasya ।
kartuṃ vyagramanā vā yathāvaduktaṃ parijñātam ।। tasmādgambhīrārthāḥ śabdā ye lokavedasaṃsiddhāḥ । sarvajanena grāhyā yojyā nāṭake vidhivat ।। na ca kiñcidguṇahīnaṃ doṣaiḥ parivarjitaṃ na cākiñcit ।
tasmānnāṭyaprakṛtau doṣā nāṭyārthato grāhyā ।। na ca nādarastu kāryo naṭena vāgaṅgasattvanepathye । rasabhāvayośca gīteṣvātodye lokayuktyāṃ ca ।। evametattu vijñeyaṃ siddhīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ budhaiḥ ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi prāśnikānāṃ tu lakṣaṇam ।। cāritrābhijanopetāḥ śāntavṛttāḥ kṛtaśramāḥ । yaśodharmaparāścaiva madhyasthavayasānvitāḥ ।। ṣaḍaṅganāṭyakuśalāḥ prabuddhāḥ śucayaḥ samāḥ ।
caturātodyakuśalāḥ vṛttajñāstattvadarśinaḥ ।। deśabhāṣāvidhānajñāḥ kalāśilpaprayojakāḥ । caturthābhinayopetā rasabhāvavikalpakāḥ ।। śabdacchandovidhānajñā nānāśāstravicakṣaṇāḥ ।
evaṃ vidhāstu kartavyāḥ prāśnikā daśarūpake ।। avyagrairindriyaiḥ śuddha ūhāpohaviśāradaḥ । tyaktadoṣonuarāgī ca sa nāṭye prekṣakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। na caivete guṇāḥ samyak sarvasmin prekṣake smṛtāḥ ।
vijñeyasyāprameyatvātsaṃkīrṇānāṃ ca pārṣadi ।। yadyasya śilpaṃ nepathyaṃ karmaceṣṭitameva vā । tattathā tena kāryaṃ tu svakarmaviṣayaṃ prati ।। nānāśīlāḥ prakṛtayaḥ śīle nāṭyaṃ vinirmitam ।
uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ vṛddhabāliśayoṣitām ।। tuṣyanti taruṇāḥ kāme vidagdhāḥ samayātvite । artheṣvarthaparāścaiva mokṣe cātha virāgiṇaḥ ।। śūrāstu vīraraudreṣu niyuddheṣvāhaveṣu ca ।
dharmākhyāne purāṇeṣu vṛddhāstuṣyanti nityaśaḥ ।। na śakyamadhamairjñātumuttamānāṃ viceṣṭitam । tattvabhāveṣu sarveṣu tuṣyanti satataṃ budhāḥ ।। bālā mūrkhāḥ striyaścaiva hāsyanaipathyayoḥ sadā ।
yastuṣṭo tuṣṭimāyāti śoke śokamupaiti ca ।। kruddhaḥ krodhe bhaye bhītaḥ sa śreṣṭhaḥ prekṣakaḥ smṛtaḥ । evaṃ bhāvānukaraṇe yo yasmin praviśennaraḥ ।। sa tatra prekṣako jñeyo guṇairebhiralaṅkṛtaḥ ।
evaṃ hi prekṣakā jñeyāḥ prayoge daśarūpataḥ ।। saṃgharṣe tu samutpanne prāśnikān saṃnibodhata । yajñavinnartakaścaiva chandovicchabdavittathā ।। astraviccitrakṛdveśyā gandharvo rajasevakaḥ ।
yajñavidyajñayoge tu nartako abhinaye smṛtaḥ ।। chandovidvṛttabandheṣu śabdavitpāṭhyavistare । iṣvastravitsauṣṭhave tu nepathye caiva citrakṛt ।। kāmopacāre veśyā ca gāndharvaḥ svarakarmaṇi ।
sevakastūpacāre syādete vai prāśnikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ebhirdṛṣṭāntasaṃyuktairdoṣā vācyāstathā guṇāḥ । aśāstrajñā vivādeṣu yathā prakṛtikarmataḥ ।। athaite praśnikā jñeyāḥ kathitā ye mayānaghāḥ ।
śāstrajñānādyadā tu syātsaṃgharṣaḥ śāstrasaṃśrayaḥ ।। śāstraprāmāṇanirmāṇairvyavahāro bhavettadā । bhartṛniyogādanyo anyavigrātspardhayāpi bharatānām ।। arthapatākā hetossaṃgharṣo nāma saṃbhavati ।
teṣāṃ kāryaṃ vyavahāradarśanaṃ pakṣapātaviraheṇa ।। kṛtvā paṇaṃ patākāṃ vyavahāraḥ sa bhavitavyastu । sarvairananyamatibhiḥ sukhopaviṣṭaiśca śuddhabhāvaiśca ।। yairlekhakagamakasahāyāssaha siddhibhirghātāḥ ।
nātyāsanairnadūrasaṃsthitaiḥ prekṣakaistu bhavitavyam ।। teṣāmāsanayogo dvādaśahastasthitaḥ kāryaḥ । yāni vihitāni pūrvaṃ siddhisthānāni tāni lakṣyāṇi ।। ghātāśca lakṣaṇīyāḥ prayogato nāṭyayoge tu ।
daivādghātasamutthāḥ parotthitā vā budhairnavairlekhyāḥ ।। ghātā nāṭyasamutthā hyātmasamutthāstu lekhyāḥ syuḥ । ghātā yasya tvalpāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ siddhayaśca bahulāḥ syuḥ ।। viditaṃ kṛtvā rājñastasmai deyā patākā hi ।
sidhyatiśayātpatākā samasiddhau pārthivājñayā deyā ।। atha narapatiḥ samaḥ syādubhayorapi sā tadā deyā । evaṃ vidhijñairyaṣṭavyo vyavahāraḥ samañjasām ।। svasthacittasukhāsinaiḥ suviśiṣṭairguṇārthibhiḥ ।
vimṛśya prekṣakairgrāhyaṃ sarvarāgaparāṅgamukhaiḥ ।। sādhana dūṣaṇābhāsaḥ prayogasamayāśritaiḥ । samatvamaṅgamādhuryaṃ pāṭhyaṃ prakṛtayo rasāḥ ।। vādyaṃ gānaṃ sanepathyametajjñeyaṃ prayatnataḥ ।
gītavāditratālena kalāntarakalāsu ca ।। uadaṅgaṃ kriyate nāṭyaṃ samantāt samamucyate । aṅgopāṅgasamāyuktaṃ gītatālalayānvitam ।। gānavādyasamatvaṃ ca tadbudhaiḥ samamucyate ।
sanirbhugnamuraḥ kṛtvā caturaśrakrutau karau ।। grīvāñcitā tathā karyā tvaṅgamādhuryameva ca । pūrvroktānīha śeṣāṇi yāni dravyāṇi sādhakaiḥ ।। vadyādīnāṃ punarvuprā lakṣaṇaṃ sannibodhata ।
vādyaprabhṛtayo gānaṃ vādyamāṇāni nirdiśet ।। yāni sthānāni siddhīnāṃ taiḥ siddhiṃ tu prakāśayet । harṣādaṅgasamudbhūtāṃ nānārasasamutthitām ।। vārakālāstu vijñeyā nāṭyajñairvividhāśrayāḥ ।
divasaiścaiva rātriśca tayorvārān nibodhata ।। pūrvāhṇastvatha madhyāhnastvaparāhṇastathaiva ca । divā samutthā vijñeyā nāṭyavārāḥ prayogataḥ ।। prādoṣikārdharātriśca tathā prābhātiko aparaḥ ।
nāṭyavārā bhavantyete rātrāvityanupūrvaśaḥ ।। eteṣāṃ atra yadyojyaṃ nāṭyakāryaṃ rasāśrayam । tadahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi vārakālasamāśrayam ।। yacchrotraramaṇīyaṃ syāddharmotthanakṛtaṃ ca yat ।
pūrvāhṇe tatprayoktavyaṃ śuddhaṃ vā vikṛtaṃ tathā ।। sattvotthānaguṇairyuktaṃ vādyabhūyiṣṭhameva ca । puṣkalaṃ sattvayuktaṃ ca aparāhṇe prayojayet ।। kaiśikīvṛttisaṃyuktaṃ śṛṅgārasasaṃśrayam ।
nṛtyavāditragītāḍhyaṃ pradoṣe nāṭyamiṣyate ।। yannarmahāsyabahulaṃ karuṇaprāyameva ca । prabhātakāle tatkāryaṃ nāṭyaṃ nidrāvināśanam ।। ardharātre niyuñjīta samadhyāhne tathaiva ca ।
sandhyābhojanakāle ca nāṭyaṃ naiva prayojayet ।। evaṃ kālaṃ ca deśaṃ ca samīkṣya ca balābalam । nityaṃ nāṭyaṃ prayuñjīta yathābhāvaṃ yathārasam ।। athava deśakālau ca na parīkṣyau prayoktṛbhiḥ yathaivājñāpayedbhartā tadā yojyamasaṃśayam ।।
tathā samudiātāścaiva vijñeyā nāṭakāśritāḥ । pātraṃ prayogamṛddhiśca vijñeyāstu trayo guṇāḥ ।। buddhimatvaṃ surūpatvaṃ layatālajñatā tathā । rasabhāvajñatā caiva vayassthatvaṃ kutūhalam ।।
grahaṇaṃ dhāraṇaṃ caiva gātrāvaikalyameva ca । nijasādhvasatotsāha iti pātragato vidhiḥ ।। suvādyatā sugānatvaṃ supāṭhyatvaṃ tathaiva ca । śāstrakarmasamāyogaḥ prayoga iti saṃjñitaḥ ।।
śucibhūṣaṇatāyāṃ tu mālyābharaṇavāsasām । vicitraracanā caiva samṛddhiriti saṃjñitā ।। yadā samuditāḥ sarve ekībhūtā bhavanti hi । alaṅkārāḥ sakutapā mantavyo nāṭakāśrayāḥ ।।
etaduktaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ siddhīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ mayā । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmyātodyānāṃ vikalpanam ।। tataṃ caivāvanaddhaṃ ca ghanaṃ suṣirameva ca । caturvidhaṃ tu vijñeyamātodyaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam ।।
tataṃ tantrīkṛtaṃ jñeyamavanaddhaṃ tu pauṣkaram । ghanaṃ tālastu vijñeyaḥ suṣiro vaṃśa ucyate ।। prayogastrividho hyeṣāṃ vijñeyo nāṭakāśrayaḥ । tataṃ caivāvanaddhaṃ ca tathā nāṭyakṛto aparaḥ ।।
tataḥ kutapavinyāso gāyanaḥ saparigrahaḥ । vaipañciko vaiṇikaśca vaṃśavādastathaiva ca ।। mārdaṅgikaḥ pāṇavikastathā dārduriko budhaiḥ । avanaddhavidhāveṣa kutapaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।।
uttamādhamamadhyābhistathā prakṛtibhiryutaḥ । kutapo nāṭyayoge tu nānādeśasamāśrayaḥ ।। evaṃ gānaṃ ca vādyaṃ ca nāṭyaṃ ca vividhāśrayam । alātacakrapratimaṃ kartavyaṃ nāṭyayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
yattu tantrīkṛtaṃ proktaṃ nānātodyasamāśrayam । gāndharvamiti tajjñeyaṃ svaratālapadātmakam ।। atyarthamiṣṭaṃ devānāṃ tathā prītikaraṃ punaḥ । gandharvāṇāṃ ca yasmāddhi tasmādgandharvamucyate ।।
asya yonirbhavedgānaṃ vīṇā vaṃśastathaiva ca । eteṣāṃ caiva vakṣyāmi vidhiṃ svarasamutthitam ।। gāndharvaṃ trividhaṃ vidyātsvaratālapadātmakam । trividhasyāpi vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ karma caiva hi ।।
dvyadhiṣṭhānāḥ svarā vaiṇāḥ śārīrāśca prakīrtitāḥ । eteṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi vidhānaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam ।। svarā grāmau mūrcchanāśca tānāḥ sthānāni vṛttayaḥ । śuṣkaṃ sādhāraṇe varṇā hyalaṅkārāśca dhātavaḥ ।।
śrutayo yatayaścaiva nityaṃ svaragatātmakāḥ । dāravyāṃ samavāyastu vīṇāyāṃ samudāhṛtaḥ ।। svarā grāmāvalaṅkārā varṇāḥ sthānāni jātayaḥ । sādhāraṇe ca śarīryāṃ vīṇāyāmeṣa saṃgrahaḥ ।।
vyañjanāni svarā varṇāḥ sandhayo atha vibhaktayaḥ । nāmākhyātopasargāśca nipātāstaddhitāḥ kṛtaḥ ।। chandovidhiralaṅkārā jñeyaḥ padagato vidhiḥ । nibaddhaṃ cānibaddhaṃ ca dvividhaṃ tatpadaṃ smṛtam ।।
dhruvastvāvāpaniṣkāmau vikṣepo atha praveśanam । śamyā tālaḥ sannipātaḥ parivartaḥ savastukaḥ ।। mātrā prakaraṇāṅgāni vivārī yatayo layāḥ । gītayo avayavā mārgāḥ pādamārgāḥ sapāṇayaḥ ।।
ityekaviṃśatividhaṃ jñeyaṃ tālagataṃ budhaiḥ । gāndharvasaṃgraho hyeṣa vistaraṃ tu nibodhata ।। ṣaḍjaśca ṛṣabhaścaiva gāndhāro madhyamastathā । pañcamo dhaivataścaiva saptamo atha niṣādavān ।।
caturvidhatvameteṣāṃ vijñeyaṃ gānayoktṛbhiḥ । vādī caivātha saṃvādī vivādī cānuvādyapi ।। saṃvādo madhyamagrāme pañcamasyarṣabhasya ca । ṣaḍjagrāme tu ṣaḍjasya saṃvādaḥ pañcamasya ca ।।
tisro dve ca catasraśca catasrastisra eva ca । dve caivādya catasraśca ṣaḍjagrāme bhavedvidhiḥ ।। catuḥśrutirbhavet ṣaḍja ṛṣabhastriśrutiḥ smṛtaḥ । dviśrutiścaiva gāndhāro madhyamaśca catuḥśrutiḥ ।।
