pañcamastadvadeva syāt triśrutirdhaivato mataḥ । dviśrutiśca niṣādaḥ syāt ṣaḍjagrāme vidhirbhavet ।। ādāvuttaramandrā syādrajanī cottarāyatā । caturthī śuddhaṣaḍjā tu pañcamī matsarīkṛtā ।।
aśvakrāntā tathā ṣaṣṭhī saptamī cābhirudgatā । ṣaḍjagrāmāśritā hyetā vijñeyāḥ saptamūrcchanāḥ ।। ṣaḍje cottaramandrā syādṛṣabhe cābhirudgatā । aśvakrāntā tu gāndhāre madhyame matsarīkṛtā ।।
pañcame śuddhaṣaḍjā syāddhaivate cottarāyatā । niṣāde rajanī ca syādityetāḥ ṣaḍjamūrcchanāḥ ।। sauvīrī hariṇāśvā ca syātkalopanatā tathā । śuddhamadhyā tathā mārgī pauravī hṛṣyakā tathā ।
madhyamagrāmajā hyetā vijñeyāḥ saptamūrcchanāḥ ।। kramayuktāḥ svarāḥ sapta mūrcchanetyabhisaṃjñitāḥ । ṣaṭpañcasvarakāstānāḥ ṣāḍavauḍuvitāśrayāḥ ।। sādhāraṇakṛtāścaiva kākalīsamalaṅkṛtāḥ ।
antarasvarasaṃyuktā mūrcchanā grāmayordvayoḥ ।। chāyāsu bhavati śītaṃ prasvedo bhavati cātapasthasya । na ca nāgato vasanto na ca niḥśeṣaḥ śiśirakālaḥ ।। antarasvarasaṃyogo nityamārohisaṃśrayaḥ ।
kāryo hyalpo viśeṣeṇa nāvarohī kadācana ।। kriyamāṇo avarohī syādalpo vā yadi vā bahuḥ । jātirāgaṃ śrutiṃ caiva nayante tvantarasvarāḥ ।। svarasādhāraṇagatāstisro jñeyāstu jātayaḥ ।
madhyamā pañcamī caiva ṣaḍjamadhyā tathaiva ca ।। āsāmaṃśāstu vijñeyāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ । yathā svaṃ durbalatarā vyaktā sā pañcamī tathā ।। jātayo aṣṭādaśetyevaṃ brahmaṇābhihitaṃ purā ।
tāstvahaṃ vartayiṣyāmi grahāṃśādivibhāgataḥ ।। ṣāḍjī caivārṣabhī caiva dhaivatyatha niṣādinī । ṣaḍjodīcyavatī caiva tathā vai ṣaḍjakaiśikī ।। ṣaḍjamadhyā tathā caiva ṣaḍjagrāmasamāśrayāḥ ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi madhyamagrāmasaṃśritāḥ ।। gāndhārī madhyamā caiva gāndhārodīcyavā tathā । pañcamī raktagāndhārī tathā gāndhārapañcamī ।। madhyamodīcyavā caiva nandayanti tathaiva ca ।
karmāravī ca vijñeyā tathāndhrī kaiśikī matā ।। svarasādhāraṇagatāstisro jñeyāstu jātayaḥ । madhyamā ṣaḍjamadhyā ca pañcamī caiva sūribhiḥ ।। āsāmaṃśāstu vijñeyāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ ।
yathāsvaṃ durbalataraṃ vyatyāsāttvatra pañcamī ।। śuddhā vikṛtāścaiva hi samavāyājjātayastu jāyante । punarevāśuddhakṛtā bhavantyathaikādaśānyāstu ।। tāsāṃ yannirvṛttāḥ svareṣvathāṃśeṣu jātiṣu ca jātiḥ ।
tadvakṣyāmi yathāvatsaṃkṣepeṇa krameṇeha ।। parasparaviniṣpannā jñeyā hyevaṃ tu jātayaḥ । pṛthaglakṣaṇasaṃyuktā dvaigrāmikāḥ svarāśrayāḥ ।। catasro jātayo nityaṃ jñeyāḥ saptasvarā budhaiḥ ।
catasraḥ ṣaṭsvarā jñeyāḥ smṛtāḥ pañcasvarā daśa ।। madhyamodīcyavā caiva tathā vai ṣaḍjakaiśikī । kārmāravī ca saṃpūrṇā tathā gāndhārapañcamī ।। ṣāḍjyāndhrī nandayantī ca gāndhārodīcyavā tathā ।
catasraḥ ṣaṭsvarā hyetāḥ jñeyāḥ pañca svarā daśa ।। naiṣādī cārṣabhī caiva dhaivatī ṣaḍjamadhyamā । ṣaḍjodīcyavatī caiva pañca ṣaḍjāśritāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। gāndhārī raktagāndhārī madhyamā pañcamī tathā ।
kaiśikī caiva pañcaitā madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ ।। yāstāḥ saptasvarā jñeyā yāścaitāḥ ṣaṭsvarāḥ smṛtāḥ । kadācit ṣāḍavībhūtāḥ kadāciccauḍuve matāḥ ।। ṣaḍjagrāme tu sampūrṇā vijñeyā ṣaḍjakaiśikī ।
ṣaṭsvarā caiva vijñeyā ṣāḍjī gāndhārayogataḥ ।। gāndhārapañcamī caiva madhyamodīcyavā tathā । punaśca ṣaṭsvarā jñeyā gāndhārodīcyavā budhaiḥ ।। āndhrī ca nandayantī ca madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ ।
evametā budhairjñeyā dvaigrāmikyo api jātayaḥ ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi tāsāmaṃśavikalpanam । ṣaṭsvarāḥ saptame hyaṃśe neṣyante ṣaḍjamadhyamāḥ ।। saṃvādyalopādgāndhāre tadvadeva hi neṣyate ।
gāndhārīraktagāndhārīkaiśikīnāṃ tu pañcamaḥ ।। ṣaḍjāyāṃ caiva gāndhāramaṃśakaṃ viddhi ṣāḍavam । ṣāḍavaṃ dhaivate nāsti ṣaḍjodīcyāmathāṃśake ।। saṃvādyalopātsaptaitāḥ ṣāṭsvaryeṇa vivarjitāḥ ।
gāndhārīraktagāndhāryoḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ ।। saptamaścaiva vijñeyo yeṣu nauḍuvitaṃ bhavet । dvau ṣaḍjamadhyamāṃśo tu gāndhāro atha niṣādavān ।। ṛṣabhaścaiva pañcamyāṃ kaiśikyāṃ caiva dhaivataḥ ।
evaṃ tu dvādaśaiveha varjyāḥ pañca svarāḥ sadā ।। tāstvanauḍuvitā nityaṃ kartavyā hi svarāśrayāḥ । sarvasvarāṇāṃ nāśastu vihitastvatha jātiṣu ।। na madhyamasya nāśastu kartavyo hi kadācana ।
sarvasvarāṇāṃ pravaro hyanāśī madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ । gāndharvakalpe vihitaḥ sāmasvapi ca madhyamaḥ ।। grahāṃśau tāramandrau ca nyāso apanyāsa eva ca । alpatvaṃ ca bahutvaṃ ca ṣāḍavauḍuvite tathā ।।
grahāstu sarvajātīnāmaṃśavatparikīrtitāḥ । yatpravṛttaṃ bhavedgeyamaṃśo grahavikalpitaḥ ।। yasmin bhavati rāgaśca yasmāccaiva pravartate । mandraśca tāramandraśca yo atyarthaṃ copalabhyate ।।
grahāpanyāsavinyāsasaṃnyāsanyāsagocaraḥ । anuvṛttaśca yasyeha soṃ'śaḥ syāddaśalakṣaṇaḥ ।। aṃśāttāragatiṃ vidyādācaturthasvarādiha । ā pañcamātpañcamādvā nātaḥparamiheṣyate ।।
tridhā mandragatiḥ । aṃśaparā nyāsaparā aparanyāsaparā ceti । mandrastvaṃśaparo nāsti nyāsau tu dvau vyavasthitau । gāndhāranyāsaliṅge tu dṛṣṭamārṣabhasevanam ।। atha nyāsa ekaviṃśatisaṅkhyaḥ । aṅgasamāptau nyāsaḥ । tadvadapanyāso hyaṅgamadhye ṣaṭpañcāśatsaṅkhyaḥ ।
nyāso aṅgasamāptau sa caikaviṃśatisaṅkhyastathā । akṣarāṇi ṣaṭpañcāśatsaṃkhyo apanyāso aṅgamadhye bhavet ।। tatra prathamaṃ vidārīmadhye nyāsasvaraprayuktastu । vivadanaśīlaṃ muktvā saṃnyāsaḥ so abhidhātavyaḥ ।
kṛtvā padāvasāne vinyāsātkvāpi vinyāsaḥ ।। alpatve atha bahutve balavadabalatā viniścayādeva । jātisvaraistu nityaṃ jātyalpatvaṃ dvividhametat ।। sañcārāṃśe balasthānāmalpatve durbalāsu ca ।
nyāsaścāntaramārgastu jātīnāṃ vyaktikārakaḥ ।। pañcasvaramauḍuvitaṃ vijñeyaṃ daśavidhaṃ prayogajñaiḥ । triṃśatprakāravihitaṃ pūrvoktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ cāsya ।। ṣaṭsvarasya prayogo asti tathā pañcasvarasya ca ।
catuḥsvaraprayogo api hyavakṛṣṭadhruvāsviha ।। dvaigrāmikīṇāṃ jātīnāṃ sarvāsāmapi nityaśaḥ । aṃśāstriṣaṣṭirvijñeyāsteṣāṃ caivāṃśavad grahāḥ ।। aṃśagrahamidānīṃ vakṣyāmaḥ ।
madhyamodīcyavāyāstu nandayantyāstathaiva ca । tathā gāndhārapañcamyāḥ pañcamoṃ'śo grahastathā ।। dhaivatyāśca tathā hyaṃśau vijñeyau dhaivatarṣabhau । pañcamyāśca tathā jñeyau grahāṃśau pañcamarṣabhau ।।
gāndhārodīcyavāyāstu grahāṃśau ṣaḍjamadhyamau । ārṣabhyāśca grahā aṃśā dhaivatarṣabhasaptamāḥ ।। gāndhāraśca niṣādaśca hyārṣabhaśca tathāparaḥ । niṣādinyāstrayo hyete grahā aṃśāśca kīrtitāḥ ।।
ṣaḍjapañcamagāndhāraistribhireva prakīrtitāḥ । aṃśairgrahaistathā caiva vijñeyā ṣaḍjakaiśikī ।। ṣaḍjaśca madhyamaścaiva niṣādo dhaivatastathā । ṣaḍjodīcyavatījātergrahā aṃśāśca kīrtitāḥ ।।
pañcamaścārṣabhaścaiva niṣādo dhaivatastathā । kārmāravyā budhairaṃśā grahāśca parikīrtitāḥ ।। gāndhāraścārṣabhaścaiva pañcamo atha niṣādavān । catvaroṃśā bhavantyāndhryā grahāścaiva tathaiva hi ।।
ṣaḍjaścātharṣabhaścaiva madhyamaḥ pañcamastathā । madhyamāyā grahā jñeyā aṃśāścaiva sadhaivatāḥ ।। niṣādaṣaḍjagāndhāramadhyamāḥ pañcamastathā । gāndhārīraktagāndhāryorgrahā aṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
ṣaḍjī dhaivatagāndhāraṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamaiḥ । grahairaṃśaiśca vijñeyā vikṛtā svarayogataḥ ।। kaiśikyāścārṣabhaṃ hitvā grahāṃśāḥ ṣaṭ svarāḥ smṛtāḥ । saptasvaragrahāṃśā tu vijñeyā ṣaḍjamadhyamā ।।
ete triṣaṣṭirvijñeyāḥ sarvāsvaṃśāstu jātiṣu । aṃśavacca grahāstāsāṃ sarvāsāmeva nityaśaḥ ।। sarvāsāmeva jātīnāṃ trijātistu gaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ । te ca sapta gaṇā jñeyā vardhamānasvarā budhaiḥ ।।
ekasvaro dvisvaraśca trisvaro atha catuḥsvaraḥ । pañcasvaraścaturthā syādekadhā saptaṣaṭsvarau ।। etaduktaṃ mayā tvāsāṃ grahāṃśaparikalpanam । punaścaiva pravakṣyāmi nyāsāpanyāsayogataḥ ।।
pañcāṃśā tu bhavet ṣāḍjī niṣādarṣabhavarjitā । apanyāso bhavedatra gāndhāraḥ pañcamastathā ।। nyāsaścātra bhavet ṣaḍjo lopyaḥ saptama eva ca । ṣaḍjagāndhārasañcāraḥ ṣaḍjadhaivatayostathā ।।
ṣāḍavaṃ saptamopetamalpau vai saptamarṣabhau । gāndhārasya ca bāhulyaṃ tvatra kāryaṃ prayoktubhiḥ ।। ārṣabhyāmṛṣabhastvaṃśo niṣādo dhaivatastathā । eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsaścāpyṛṣabhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
ṣaṭpañcasvaratā cātra ṣaḍjapañcamayorvinā ।। dhaivatyāṃ dhaivato nyāsastvaṃśāvṛṣabhadhaivato । apanyāsā bhavantyatra dhaivatārṣabhamadhyamāḥ ।। ṣaḍjapañcamahīnaṃ tu pāñcsvaryaṃ vidhīyate ।
pañcamena vinā caiva ṣāḍavaṃ parikīrtitam ।। ārohiṇau ca tau kāryau laṅghanīyau tathaiva ca । niṣādaścarṣabhaścaiva gāndhāro balavāṃstathā ।। niṣādinyāṃ niṣādoṃ'śo sagāndhārarṣabhastathā ।
eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsaścaivātra saptamaḥ ।। dhaivatyā iva kartavye ṣāḍavauḍuvite tathā । tadvacca laṅghanīyau tu balavantau tathaiva ca ।। aṃśāstu ṣaḍjakaiśikyāḥ ṣaḍjagāndhārapañcamāḥ ।
apanyāsā bhavantyatra ṣaḍjapañcamasaptamāḥ ।। gāndhāraśca bhavennyāso hainasvaryaṃ na cātra tu । daurbalyaṃ cātra kartavyaṃ dhaivatasyārṣabhasya ca ।। ṣaḍjaśca madhyamaścaiva niṣādo dhaivatastathā ।
syuḥ ṣaḍjodīcyavāṃśāstu nyāsaścaiva tu madhyamaḥ ।। apanyāso bhavatyasya dhaivataḥ ṣaḍja eva ca । parasparāṃśagamanamiṣṭataśca vidhīyate ।। ṣāṭsvaryamṛṣabhāpetaṃ kāryaṃ gāndharvavedibhiḥ ।
pañcamārṣabhahīnaṃ tu pāñcasvaryaṃ tu tatra vai ।। ṣaḍjaścāpyṛṣabhaścaiva gāndhāraśca balī bhavet । gāndhārasya ca bāhulyaṃ mandrasthāne vidhīyate ।। sarveṃśāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyāyāmapanyāsāstathaiva ca ।
ṣaḍjaśca madhyamaścāpi nyāsau nāryau prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। gāndhārasaptamāpetaṃ pāñcasvaryaṃ vidhīyate । ṣāḍavaṃ saptamāpetaṃ kāryaṃ cātra prayogataḥ ।। sarvasvarāṇāṃ sañcāra iṣṭatastu vidhīyate ।
ṣaḍjagrāmāśritā hyetā vijñeyāḥ sapta jātayaḥ ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ । gāndhāryāḥ pañca evāṃśā dhaivatarṣabhavarjitāḥ ।। ṣaḍjaśca pañcamaścaiva hyapanyāsau prakīrtitau ।
gāndhāraśca bhavennyāsaḥ ṣāḍavaṃ carṣabhaṃ vinā ।। dhaivatarṣabhayorhīnaṃ tathā cauḍuvitaṃ bhavet । laṅghanīyau ca tau nityamārṣabhāddhaivataṃ vrajet । vihitastviti gāndhāryāḥ svaranyāsāṃśagocaraḥ ।।
lakṣaṇaṃ raktagāndhāryā gāndhāryā eva yatsmṛtam । dhaivato balavānatra daurbalyaṃ tasya lopataḥ ।। gāndhāraṣaḍjayoścātra sañcāraścārṣabhādvinā । apanyāsastathā caiva madhyamastu vidhīyate ।।
gāndhārodīcyavāṃśau tu vijñeyau ṣaḍjamadhyamau । pāñcasvaryaṃ na caivātra ṣāṭsvaryamṛṣabhaṃ vinā ।। kāryaścāntaramārgaśca nyāsopanyāsa eva ca । ṣaḍjodīcyavatīvattu pāñcasvaryeṇa jātucit ।।
madhyamāyā bhavantyaṃśā vinā gāndhārasaptamau । eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsaścaiva tu madhyamaḥ ।। gāndhārasaptamāpetaṃ pāñcasvaryaṃ vidhīyate । ṣāḍavaṃ cāpyagāndhāraṃ kartavyaṃ tu prayogataḥ ।।
ṣaḍjamadhyamayoścātra kāryaṃ bāhulyameva hi । gāndhāralaṅghanaṃ cātra kāryaṃ nityaṃ prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। madhyamodīcyavā pūrṇā hyaṃśa ekastu pañcamaḥ । śeṣo vidhistu kartavyo gāndhārodīcyavāṃ gataḥ ।।
dvāvaṃśāvatha pañcamyāmṛṣabhaḥ pañcamastathā । sa niṣādāvapanyāsau nyāsaścaiva tu pañcamaḥ ।। madhyamāvattu kartavye ṣāḍavauḍuvite tathā । daurbalyaṃ cātra kartavyaṃ ṣaḍjagāndhāramadhyamaiḥ ।।
kuryādapyatra sañcāraṃ pañcamasyārṣabhasya ca । gāndhāragamanaṃ caiva kāryaṃ tvalpaśca saptamaḥ ।। atha gāndhārapañcamyāḥ pañcamoṃ'śaḥ prakīrtitaḥ । tāragatyā tu ṣaḍjo api kadācinnātivartate ।।
ṛṣabhaḥ pañcamaścaiva hyapanyāsau prakīrtitau । nyāsaścaiva tu gāndhāro sā ca pūrṇasvarā sadā । pañcamyā yaśca gāndhāryāḥ sañcāraḥ sa vidhīyate ।। pañcamaścārṣabhaścaiva gāndhāro atha niṣādavān ।
catvāroṃ'śā bhavantyāndhryāmapanyāsāsta eva hi ।। gāndhāraśca bhavennyāsaḥ ṣaḍjāpetaṃ tu ṣāḍavam । gāndhārārṣabhayoścāpi sañcārastu parasparam ।। saptamasya ca ṣaṣṭhasya nyāso gatyanupūrvaśaḥ ।
ṣaḍjasya laṅghanaṃ cātra nāsti cauḍuvitaṃ sadā ।। nandayantyāḥ kramān nyāsāpanyāsāṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ । gāndhāro madhyamaścaiva pañcamaścaiva nityaśaḥ ।। ṣaḍjo lopyaśca laṅghyaśca nāndhrīsañcaraṇaṃ bhavet ।
laṅghanaṃ hyṛṣabhasyāpi tacca mandragataṃ smṛtam ।। tāragatyā tu ṣaḍjastu kadācinnātivartate । gāndhāro vā grahaḥ kāryastathā nyāsaśca nityaśaḥ ।। kārmāravyāḥ smṛtā hyaṃśā ārṣabhaḥ pañcamastathā ।
dhaivataśca niṣādaścāpyapanyāsāsta eva tu । pañcamaśca bhavennyāso hainasvaryaṃ na cātra tu ।। gāndhārasya viśeṣeṇa sarvato gamanaṃ bhavet ।। kaiśikyāstu tathā hyaṃśāḥ sarve caivārṣabhaṃ vinā ।
eta eva hyapanyāsā nyāsau gāndhārasaptamau ।। dhaivateṃśe niṣāde ca nyāsaḥ pañcama iṣyate । apanyāsaḥ kadācittu ṛṣabho api vidhīyate ।। ārṣabhe ṣāḍavaṃ cātra dhaivatarṣabhavarjitam ।
tathā cauḍuvitaṃ kuryād balinau cāntyapañcamau ।। daurbalyamṛṣabhasyātra laṅghanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ । aṃśavat kalpitaścānyaiḥ ṣāḍave tu vidhīyate । ṣaḍjamadhyāvadatrāpi sañcārastu bhavediha ।।
evametā budhairjñeyā jātayo daśalakṣaṇāḥ । yathā yasmin rase yāśca gadato me nibodhata ।। ṣaḍjodīcyavatī caiva ṣaḍjamadhyā tathaiva ca । madhyapañcamabāhulyāt kāryā śṛṅgārahāsyayoḥ ।।
ṣāḍjī tvathārṣabhī caiva svasvarāṃśaparigrahāt । vīraraudrādbhuteṣvete prayojye gānayoktṛbhiḥ ।। niṣāde aṃśe tu naiṣādī gāndhāre ṣaḍjakaiśikī । karuṇe tu rase kāryā jātigānaviśāradaiḥ ।।
dhaivatī dhaivatāṃśe tu bībhatse sabhayānake । dhruvāvidhāne kartavyā jātirgāne prayatnataḥ । rasaṃ kāryamavasthāṃ ca jñātvā yojyā prayoktṛbhiḥ । ṣaḍjagrāmāśritā hyetāḥ prayojyā jātayo budhaiḥ ।।
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi madhyamagrāmasaṃśrayāḥ । gāndhārīraktagāndhāryau gāndhārāṃśopapattitaḥ । karuṇe tu rase kārye niṣāde aṃśe tathaiva ca ।। madhyamā pañcamī caiva nandayantī tathaiva ca ।
gāndhārapañcamī caiva madhyamodīcyavā tathā । madhyamapañcamabāhulyāt kāryāḥ śṛṅgārahāsyayoḥ ।। kārmāravī tathā cāndhrī gāndhārodīcyavā tathā । vīre raudre adbhute kāryāḥ ṣaḍjarṣabhāṃśayojitāḥ ।
kaiśikī dhaivatāṃśe tu bībhatse sabhayānake ।। ekaiva ṣaḍjamadhyā jñeyā sarvarasasaṃśrayā jātiḥ । tasyāstvaṃśāḥ sarve svarāstu vihitāḥ prayogavidhau ।। yo yadā balavān yasmin svaro jātisamāśrayāt ।
tatpravṛttaṃ rase kāryaṃ gānaṃ geye prayoktṛbhiḥ ।। madhyapañcamabhūyiṣṭhaṃ gānaṃ śṛṅgārahāsyayoḥ । ṣaḍjarṣabhaprāyakṛtaṃ vīraraudrādbhuteṣu ca ।। gāndhāraḥ saptamaścāyaṃ karuṇe gānamiṣyate ।
tathā dhaivatabhūyiṣṭhaṃ bībhatse sabhayānake ।। ekaiva ṣaḍjamadhyā vijñeyākhilarasāśrayā jātiḥ । tasyāstvaṃśāḥ sarve svarāśca vihitāḥ prayogavidhau ।। sarveṣvaṃśeṣu rasā niyamavidhānena saṃprayoktavyāḥ ।
kākalyantaravihitā viśeṣayuktāstu balavantaḥ । evametā budhairjñeyā jātayo nāṭyasaṃśrayāḥ ।। pāṭhyaprayogavihitān svarāṃścāpi nibodhata । hāsyaśṛṅgārayoḥ kāryau svarau madhyamapañcamau ।।
ṣaḍjarṣabhau ca kartavyau vīraraudrādbhuteṣvatha । gāndhāraśca niṣādaśca kartavyau karuṇe rase ।। dhaivataśca prayogajñairbībhatse sabhayānake । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi varṇālaṅkāralakṣaṇam ।।
ārohī cāvarohī ca sthāyisañcāriṇau tathā । varṇāścatvāra evaite hyalaṅkārāstadāśrayāḥ ।। ārohanti svarā yatrārohīti sa tu saṃjñitaḥ । yatra caivāvarohanti so avarohī prakīrtitaḥ ।।
sthirāḥ svarāḥ samā yatra sthāyī varṇaḥ sa ucyate । sañcaranti svarā yatra sa sañcārīti kīrtitaḥ ।। śārīrasvarasambhūtāstristhānaguṇagocarāḥ । catvāro lakṣaṇopetā varṇāstatra prakīrtitāḥ ।।
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ yadā varṇo anukarṣati । tadā varṇasya niṣpattirjñeyā svarasamudbhavā ।। ete varṇāstu vijñeyāścatvāro gītayojakāḥ । etān samāśritān samyagalaṅkārān nibodhata ।।
prasannādiḥ prasannāntaḥ prasannādyanta eva ca । prasannamadhyaśca tathā kramarecita eva ca । prastāraśca prasādaśca saptaite sthāyivarṇagāḥ ।। atha sañcārijān bhūyaḥ kīrtyamānānnibodhata ।
mandrastathā prasannādiḥ preṅkhito bindureva ca । sannivṛttaḥ pravṛttaśca recitaḥ kampitaḥ samaḥ ।। kuharaścaiva veṇuśca rañcito hyavalokitaḥ । āvartakaḥ parāvṛttaḥ sañcāriṇyaścaturdaśa ।।
niṣkarṣobhyucayaścaiva hasito bindureva ca । preṅkholitastathākṣipto vistīrṇoddhaṭitastathā ।। hrādamānaḥ sampradānaḥ sandhiḥ pracchādanastathā । prasannādiḥ prasannānta ityārohe trayodaśa ।।
vidhūtaśca trivarṇaśca tathodvāhita eva ca । udgītaśca tathā veṇirvijñeyā hyavarohiṇaḥ ।। saptarūpagatā jñeyā alaṅkārā budhaistvime । naite sarve dhruvāsviṣṭāḥ śrutivarṇaprakarṣaṇāt ।।
na hi varṇaprakarṣastu dhruvāṇāṃ siddhiriṣyate । śyeno vāpyathavā bindurye cānyeti prakarṣiṇaḥ ।। te dhruvāṇāṃ prayogeṣu na kāryāḥ svapramāṇataḥ । taddhruvāṇāṃ prayoge tu kāryā hyārohiṇaḥ svarāḥ ।।
yasmādarthānurūpā hi dhruvā kāryārthadarśikā । varṇānāṃ tu punaḥ kāryaṃ kṛśatvaṃ padasaṃśrayam ।। ye atra prayoge gacchanti tāṃśca varṇān nibodhata । prasannādiḥ prasannāntaḥ prasannādyanta eva ca ।।
prasannamadhyamaścaiva binduḥ kampitarecitau । tāraścaiva hi mandraśca tathā tārataraḥ punaḥ । preṅkholitastāramandro mandratāraḥ samastathā ।। sannivṛttaḥ pravṛttaśca prasādo apāṅga eva ca ।
ūrmiḥ preṅkho avalokaśca ityete sarvavarṇagāḥ ।। sthāyivarṇādṛte caiṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam । kramaśo dīpito yaḥ syāt prasannādiḥ sa kathyate ।। vyastoccārita evaiṣa prasannānto vidhīyate ।
ādyantayoḥ prasannatvāt prasannādyanta iṣyate ।। prasannamadhyo madhye tu prasannatvādudāhṛtaḥ । sarvasāmyāt samo jñeyaḥ sthitastvekasvaro api yaḥ ।। ādimadhyalayo yatra sa cormiriti saṃjñitaḥ ।
śrutayo antyād dvitīyasya mṛdumadhyāyatāḥ svarāḥ ।। āyatatvaṃ bhavennīce mṛdutvaṃ tu viparyaye । sve svare madhyamatvaṃ ca mṛdumadhyamayostathā । dīptāyate karuṇānāṃ śrutīnāmeṣa niścayaḥ ।।
bindurekakalo jñeyaḥ kampitaśca kalādvayam । gatāgatapravṛtto yaḥ sa preṅkholita iṣyate ।। yastu kaṇṭhe svaro adhaḥ syāt sa tu tāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ । urogatastathā mandro mūrdhni tāratarastathā ।।
kramāgatastu yastāraḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ pañcama eva vā । tāramandraprasannastu jñeyo mandragataḥ sa ca ।। laṅghayitvā parān mandrāt parāṃ tāragatiṃ gataḥ । mandratāraprasannastu vijñeyo hyavarohaṇāt ।।
prasannāntaḥ svaro yatra prasādaḥ sa tu saṃjñitaḥ । apāṅgakistu vijñeyaḥ svarāṇāmatha sañcarāt ।। recitaḥ śirasi jñeyaḥ kampitaṃ tu kalātrayam । kaṇṭhe niruddhapavanaḥ kuharo nāma jāyate ।।
evamete tvalaṅkārā vijñeyā varṇasaṃśrayāḥ । atha gītīḥ pravakṣyāmi chando akṣarasamanvitāḥ ।। śaśinā rahiteva niśā vijaleva nadī latā vipuṣpeva । avibhūṣiteva ca strī gītiralaṅkārahīnā syāt ।।
prathamā māgadhī jñeyā dvitīyā cārdhamāgadhī । sambhāvitā tṛtīyā tu caturthī pṛthulā smṛtā ।। trinivṛttapragītā yā gītiḥ sā māgadhī smṛtā । ardhataḥ sannivṛttā ca vijñeyā hyardhamāgadhī ।।
sambhāvitā ca vijñeyā gurvakṣarasamanvitā । pṛthulākhyā ca vijñeyā nityaṃ laghvakṣarānvitā ।। etāstu gītayo jñeyā dhruvāyogaṃ vinaiva hi । gāndharva eva yojyāstu nityaṃ gānaprayoktṛbhiḥ ।।
gītayo gaditāḥ samyag dhātūṃścaiva nibodhata । vistāraḥ karaṇaśca syādāviddho vyañjanastathā । catvāro dhātavo jñeyā vāditrakaraṇāśrayāḥ ।। saṅghātajo atha samavāyajaśca vistārajo anubandhakṛtaḥ ।
jñetaścatuṣprakāro dhāturvistārasaṃjñaśca ।। vidhayastu smṛtāstasya pūrvaṃ vistāra eva ca । saṅghātasamavāyau tu vijñeyau tau dviatrikau ।। pūrvaścaturvidhastatra paścimo aṣṭavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
karaṇānāṃ viśeṣeṇa vijñeyau tau pṛthak pṛthak ।। adhaścordhvaṃ ca vijñeyāvadharottarajau svarau । saṅghātajo vidhistveṣa vijñeyo vādanaṃ prati ।। dviruttaro dviradharastvadharādiścottarāvasānaśca ।
jñeyastathottarādiḥ punarapyadharāvasānaśca ।। samavāyajastathā syāt triruttarastriradharaśca vijñeyaḥ । dviradharottarādharānto dviradharaścottaravirāmaśca ।। uttaramukho dviradharo dviruttarāvasānaśca ।
madhyottaro dviradharo dviruttaro apyadharamadhyaśca ।। anubandhastu jñeyo vyāsasamāsācca niyatameṣāṃ hi । evaṃ caturdaśavidho vistāro dhāturākhyātaḥ ।। ribhitoccayanīribhito hrādastu tathānubandhaḥ syāt ।
pañcavidho vijñeyo vīṇāvādye karaṇadhātuḥ ।। trikapañcasaptanavakairyathākramaṃ saṃyuto bhavedvādye । sarvairanubandhakṛtairgurvantaḥ syāt karaṇadhātuḥ ।। kṣepaḥ pluto atipāto atikīrṇamanubandhasaṃjñitaścaiva ।
āviddho viṣṭo yo dhāturvai pañcavidha eva ।। dvitricatuṣkanavakaiḥ prahāraiḥ kramaśaḥ kṛtaiḥ । āviddhadhāturvijñeyaḥ sānubandhavibhūṣitaḥ ।। vyañjanadhātoḥ puṣpaṃ kalatalaniṣkoṭitaṃ tathoddhṛṣṭam ।
repho anubandhasaṃjño anusvanitaṃ binduravamṛṣṭam ।। kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhasaṃyuktaṃ puṣpamityabhisaṃjñitam । aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ samaṃ tantryoḥ sparśanaṃ yat kalaṃ tu tat ।। vāmena pīḍanaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇenāhatistale ।
savyāṅguṣṭhaprahārastu niṣkoṭitamihocyate ।। prahāro vāmatarjanyā uddhṛṣṭamiti saṃjñitam । sarvāṅgulisamākṣepo repha ityabhisaṃjñitaḥ ।। talasthāne adhastantrīṇāmanusvanitamucyate ।
gurvakṣarakṛtā tantrī bindurityabhisaṃjñitaḥ ।। kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhakābhyāṃ tu dakṣiṇābhyāmadhomukham । tantrīṣu triprahāraṃ cāpyavamṛṣṭaṃ prakīrtitam ।। vyāsasamāsādeṣāmanubandhaḥ sārvadhātuko jñeyaḥ ।
iti daśavidhaḥ prayojyo vīṇāyāṃ vyañjano dhātuḥ ।। ityete dhātavaḥ proktāścatvāro lakṣaṇānvitāḥ । tisṛṇāmapi vṛttīnāṃ yeṣu vādyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। tisrastu vṛttayaścitrādakṣiṇāvṛttisaṃjñitāḥ ।
vādyagītobhayaguṇā nirdiṣṭāntā yathākramam ।। tisro gītivṛttayaḥ prādhānyena grāhyāḥ । citrā vṛttirdakṣiṇā ceti । tāsāṃ tālagītilayayatimārgaprādhānyāni yathāsvaṃ vyañjakāni bhavanti । tatra citrāyāṃ saṅkṣiptavādyatāladrutalayasamāyatynāgatagrahāṇāṃ prādhānyam । tathā vṛttau gītavāditradvikalātālamadhyalayasrotogatāyatisamagrahamārgāṇāṃ prādhānyam । dakṣiṇāyāṃ gīticatuṣkalatālavilambitalayagopucchāyatyatītagrahamārgāṇāṃ prādhānyam । sarvāsāmeva vṛttīnāṃ lalitādyāstu jātayaḥ । dhātubhiḥ saha saṃyuktā bhavanti guṇavattarāḥ ।।
eteṣāṃ dhātūnāṃ samavāyājjātayastu jāyante । syādudāttalalitaribhitaghanasaṃjñāścatasrastu ।। tatrodātā vistāradhātuviṣayā hyudāttatvāt । lalitā vyañjanadhātorlalitatvādeva saṃprayoktavyā ।।
āviddhadhātuviṣayā ribhitā laghusañcayād vinirdiṣṭā । karaṇaviṣayā ca ghanasaṃjñā gurulaghusañcayāttu syāt ।। trividhaṃ gīte kāryaṃ vādyaṃ vīṇāsamudbhavaṃ tajjñaiḥ । tattvaṃ hyanugatamoghaḥ sthānaikakaraṇasamāyuktāḥ ।।
layatālavarṇapadayatigītyakṣarabhāvakaṃ bhavet tattvam । gītaṃ tu yadanugacchatyanugatamiti tadbhavedvādyam ।। āviddhakaraṇabahulaṃ hyuparyuparipāṇikaṃ drutalayaṃ ca । anapekṣitagītārthaṃ vādyaṃ tvoghe vidhātavyam ।।
evaṃ jñeyā vaiṇe vādyavidhāne tu dhātavastajjñaiḥ । lakṣyāmyataḥ paramahaṃ nirgītavidhānasamavāyam ।। āśrāvaṇā tathā'rambho vaktrapāṇistathaiva ca । saṅkhoṭanā tathā kāryaṃ punaśca parighaṭṭanā ।।
mārgāsāritametat syāllīlākṛtamathāpi ca । āsāritāni ca tathā triprakārakṛtāni tu ।। etāni tu bahirgītānyāhurvādyavido janāḥ । satālāni hyatālāni cittavṛttau kṛtāni tu ।।
prayojanaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ pūrvaraṅgavidhiṃ prati । eteṣāṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ sanidarśanam ।। vistāradhātuvihitaiḥ karaṇaiḥ pravibhāgaśo dvirabhyastaiḥ । dviścāpi sannivṛttaiḥ karaṇopacayaiḥ krameṇa syāt ।।
guruṇī tvādāvekādaśakaṃ caturdaśaṃ sapañcadaśam । sacaturviṃśakamevaṃ dviguṇīkṛtametadeva syāt ।। laghunī guru caiva syādathāṣṭamaṃ guru bhavettathā ca punaḥ । ṣaṭ ca laghūni tato antye gurvādyāśrāvaṇāyāṃ tu ।।
triḥśamyoparipāṇau tālāvapyevameva caikikavān । samapāṇau dve śamye tālāvapyevamevātha ।। bhūyaḥ śamyātālāvavapāṇāvuttarasthā caiva । cañcatpuṭastathā syādevaṃ hyāśrāvaṇātālaḥ ।।
atrodāharaṇam । jhaṇṭuṃ jagati yavalitaka jambuka jhaṇṭuṃ titi ca laghu ca jhaṇṭum । diṅgale gaṇapatipaśupatijambuka diṅgale varabhuja diginagi cā । titi cādini nigicā paśupati nīticā ।।
athārambhaḥ । dīrghāṇyādāvaṣṭau dvādaśa ca laghūni naidhanaṃ caiva । catvāri gurūṇi tathā hrasvānyaṣṭau ca dīrghaṃ ca ।। laghusaṃjñāni caturdhā nidhanaṃ dviguṇīkṛtāni dīrghe dve ।
aṣṭau laghūni naidhanamityārambhe akṣaravidhānam ।। atrodāharaṇam । jhaṇṭuṃ jhaṇṭuṃ jhaṇṭuṃ jhaṇṭuṃ jagati yavalitaka diginigicā । diṅgle diṅgle titi jhajhalakucajhalajambuka titicā ।
gaṇapati surapati paśupati cā ।। asya tu vādyam । kāryaṃ triparvarahitairudvahanairapyatha samavarohaiḥ । talaribhitahrādayutaiḥ karaṇairvistārabhūyiṣṭhaiḥ ।।
apacayayuktairdvistristathā nivṛttairdvirabhyastaiḥ । ārambho apyavataraṇastriparvayuktaiśca kartavyaḥ ।। tālastrikalastvādau śamyaikakalā kalādvaye tālaḥ । dvikalā ca punaḥ śamyā tālo dvikalaśca kartavyaḥ ।।
trikalaśca sannipātaḥ punaḥ pitāputrakaśca ṣaṭpūrvaḥ । cañcatpuṭastathā syādārambhe tālayogastu ।। kāryaṃ triparvarahitairudvahanairapyatha samavarohaiḥ । talaribhitahrādayutaiḥ karaṇairvistābhūyiṣṭhaiḥ ।।
apacayayuktairdvistristathā nivṛttairdvirabhyastaiḥ । ārambho apyavataraṇastriparvayuktaiśca kartavyaḥ ।। gurūṇi pañca hrasvāni ṣaḍguruśca caturguṇaḥ । guruṇī dve laghu tvekaṃ catvāryatha gurūṇi hi ।।
catvāryatha laghūni syustrīṇi dīrghāṇi caiva hi । laghūnyaṣṭau ca dīrghaṃ ca vaktrapāṇau bhavedvidhiḥ ।। atrodāharaṇam । diṅgale jhaṇṭuṃ jambuka jagati ya jhaṇṭuṃ diṅgale ।
ghendṛṃ gheṭo ghāṭo bhaṭṭunakiṭi inaṃ duṅ ।। ghadugadukiṭamaṭanam । asya vādyam । āviddhakaraṇayukto dvyaṅgaḥ syādekapravṛttau vā ।
alpavyañjanadhāturvādyavidhirvaktrapāṇau tu ।। dvikale madrake yattu śamyātālādipātam । tatsarvaṃ vaktrapāṇau tu kāryamaṣṭakalānvitam ।। tasyādhastāt punaḥ kāryaṃ pañcapāṇicatuṣṭayam ।
vaktrapāṇerayaṃ tālo mukhapratimukhāśrayaḥ ।। guruṇī laghūnyathāṣṭau dīrghaṃ dviguṇaṃ tathā ca kartavyam । laghudīrghe laghu ca punaścaturguṇaṃ saṃprakartavyam ।। punaraṣṭau hrasvāni syuriha tathā naidhanaṃ ca kartavyam ।
saṅkhoṭanavastuvidhau hrasvaguruvidhiḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ ।। saṅkhoṭanāyā udāharaṇaṃ prakalpya kṛtam । diṅgale jagati ya valati katecāticātijha laghu cajhala paśupaticā । asyā vādyavidhiḥ ।
adhidaṇḍaṃ hastābhyāṃ vīṇāṃ vinigṛhya dakṣiṇāṅgulyā । aṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ ca tathā kāryaṃ saṅkhoṭanāvādyam ।। saṅkhoṭayet svaraṃ vādinā tu saṃvādinā tathādhibalam । samavāyibhiśca śeṣairanuvādibhiralpakaiścāṃśaiḥ ।।
vistāracitrakaraṇairdvistrirvinivartitairdvirabhyastaiḥ । upacayayuktaiḥ kramaśo vadanti saṅkhoṭanāvādyam । tālo asyā gaditastajjñaiḥ śīrṣavat pañcapāṇinā ।। dīrghāṇyādāvaṣṭau laghūni kuryāt punardviguṇitāni ।
hrasvānyapi catvāri dviguṇāni syuḥ sadīrghāṇi ।। ṣoḍaśa laghūni ca syuḥ saha nidhane caiva kāryāṇi । eṣa parighaṭṭanāyāṃ gurulaghuvastukramaḥ proktaḥ ।। etasyāmapyudāharaṇaṃ prakalpya kṛtam । diṅgale diṅgale diṅgale diṅgale jagati ya valati ka । titijhalakucajhaladiginigi gaṇapati cā । calati ka gaṇapati paśupatisurapati cā ।
vādyaṃ cāsyāstajjñaiḥ sodvahanaṃ hastalāghavāt kāryam । vyañjanadhātusamutthaṃ nānākaraṇāśrayopetam ।। sampiṣṭakavaccāsyāstālaḥ karaṇaistu dhātusaṃyuktaiḥ । gurulaghuyogādevaṃ vihitaḥ kāryo budhairnityam ।।
mārgāsāritavādyaṃ vistārāviddhakaraṇasaṃyuktam । sakalaiḥ satalaiḥ karaṇairatha gurulaghusañcayaścāyam ।। catvāri gurūṇi syurlaghūni catvāri ca dviguṇitāni । guruṇī laghūnyathāṣṭau guruṇī cetyetat tridhā yojyam ।।
catvāri tu gurūṇi syurhrasvānyaṣṭau bhavanti hi । guruṇī nava hrasvāni dīrghamantyamathāpi ca ।। atrodāharaṇam । diṅgale jhaṇṭuṃ jagati ya ।
thalitaka jhaṇṭuṃ titi । jhalakuca jhalatiticā । bālāsāritavaccaiva tālo asya parikīrtitaḥ ।। śravaṇamadhurāṇi līlākṛtānyabhisṛtaparisṛtāntarakṛtāni ।
tānyapyarthavaśādiha kartavyāni prayogavidhau ।। yathāsāritāni jyeṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni tālapramāṇanirdiṣṭāni tāni tālavidhāne vakṣyāmaḥ । evametat svaragataṃ jñeyaṃ vīṇāśarīrajam । vipañcīvādyayuktāni karaṇāni nibodhata ।।
rūpaṃ kṛtaṃ pratikṛtaṃ pratibhedo rūpaśeṣamoghaśca । ṣaṣṭhī vai pratiśuṣkā tvevaṃ jñeyaṃ karaṇajātam ।। vīṇāvādyadviguṇaṃ gurulāghavavādanaṃ bhavedrūpam । rūpaṃ pratibhedakṛtaṃ pratikṛtamityucyate vādyam ।।
yugapatkṛte anyakaraṇaṃ pratibhedo dīrghalāghavakṛtaḥ syāt । kṛtamekasyāṃ tantryāṃ pratiśuṣkā nāma vijñeyā ।। vīṇāvādyavirāme apyaviratakaraṇaṃ tu rūpaśeṣaḥ syāt । āviddhakaraṇayukto hyuparyuparipāṇikastvoghaḥ ।।
kāryaṃ dhruvāvidhāne prāyeṇa hi koṇavādanaṃ tajjñaiḥ । sthānaprāptyarthaṃ cedyattatra bhavedayaṃ niyamaḥ ।। taccaughatulyakaraṇaṃ vācyaṃ kāryaṃ vipañcyāstu । saptatantrī bhaveccitrā vipañcī tu bhavennava ।
koṇavādanā vipañcī syāccitrā cāṅgulivādanā ।। tatavādyavidhānamidaṃ sarvaṃ proktaṃ samāsayogena । vakṣyāmyataśca bhūyaḥ suṣirātodyaprayogaṃ tu ।। atodyaṃ suṣiraṃ nāma jñeyaṃ vaṃśagataṃ budhaiḥ ।
vaiṇa eva vidhistatra svaragrāmasamāśrayaḥ ।। dvikatrikacatuṣkāstu jñeyā vaṃśagatāḥ svarāḥ । kampyamānārthamuktāśca vyaktamuktāstathaiva ca ।। tatropari yathā hyekaḥ svaro vaiṇasvarāntare ।
prāpnotyanyatvameveha tathā vaṃśagato api hi ।। dvikastrikaścatuṣko vā śrutisaṅkhyo bhavet svaraḥ । anīraṇāttu śeṣāṇāṃ svarāṇāmapi sambhavaḥ । aṅgulīvādanakṛtaṃ tacca me sannibodhata ।।
vyaktamuk{tāṅgulistatra svaro jñeyaścatuḥśrutiḥ । kampyamānāṅguliścaiva triśrutiḥ parikīrtitaḥ । dviko ardhāṅgulimuktaḥ syāditi śrutyāśritāḥ svarāḥ ।। ete syurmadhyamagrāme bhūyaḥ ṣaḍjāśritāḥ punaḥ ।
vyaktamuk{tāṅgulikṛtāḥ ṣaḍjamadhyamapañcamāḥ ।। ṛṣabho dhaivataścāpi kampyamānāṅgulīkṛtau । ardhamuktāṅguliścaiva gāndhāro atha niṣādavān ।। svarasādhāraṇaścāpi kākalyantarasaṃjñayā ।
niṣādagāndhārakṛtau ṣaḍjamadhyamayorapi ।। viparyayā sannikarṣe śrutilakṣaṇasiddhitaḥ । vaiṇakaṇṭhapraveśena siddhā ekāśritāḥ svarāḥ ।। yaṃ yaṃ gātā svaraṃ gacchet taṃ taṃ vaṃśena vādayet ।
śārīravaiṇavaṃśyānāmekībhāvaḥ praśasyate ।। avicalitamavicchinnaṃ varṇālaṅkārasaṃyutaṃ vidhivat । lalitaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ veṇorevaṃ smṛtaṃ vādyam ।। evametat svaragataṃ vijñeyaṃgānayoktṛbhiḥ ।
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dhanātodyavikalpanam ।। guṇāt pravartate gānaṃ doṣaṃ caiva nirasyate । tasmādyatnena vijñeyau guṇadoṣau samāsataḥ ।। gātā pratyagravayāḥ snigdho madhurasvaropacitakaṇṭhaḥ ।
layatālakalāpātapramāṇayogeṣu tattvajñaḥ ।। rūpaguṇakāntiyuktā mādhuryopetasatvasampannāḥ । peśalamadhurasnigdhānunādisamarakta gurukaṇṭhāḥ ।। suvihitagamakavidhāyinyo akṣobhyās tālalayakuśalāḥ ।
ātodyārpitakaraṇā vijñeyā gāyikāḥ śyāmāḥ ।। prāyeṇa tu svabhāvāt strīṇāṃ gānaṃ nṛṇāṃ ca pāṭhyavidhiḥ । strīṇāṃ svabhāvamadhuraḥ kaṇṭho nṛṇāṃ balitvaṃ ca ।। yatra strīṇāṃ pāṭhyaṃ guṇairnarāṇāṃ ca gānamadhuratvam ।
jñeyo alaṅkāro asau na hi svabhāvo hyayaṃ teṣām ।। suniviṣṭapāṇilayayatiyogajñausumadhuralaghuhastau । gātṛguṇaiścopetāvavahitamanasau susaṅgītau ।। sphuṭaracitacitrakaraṇau gītaśravaṇācalaupravīṇau ca ।
citrādivādyakuśalauvīṇābhyāṃ vādakau bhavataḥ ।। balavānavahitabuddhirgītalayajñastathāsusaṅgītaḥ । śrāvakamadhurasnigdho dṛḍhapāṇirvaṃśavādako jñeyaḥ ।। avicalitamavicchannaṃ varṇālaṅkārabodhakaṃmadhuram ।
snigdhaṃ doṣavihīnaṃ veṇorevaṃ smṛtaṃ vādyam ।। jñānavijñānakaraṇavacanaprayogasiddhiniṣpādanāni ṣaḍācāryaguṇā iti । tatra jñānaṃ śāstrāvabodhaḥ । yathā ca kriyāsampādanaṃ vijñānam । kaṇṭhahastagauṇyaṃ karaṇam । jitagranthatā vacanam ।
deśādisampadārādhanaṃ prayogasiddhiḥ । śiṣyasvabhāvamaviśeṣyopāttaya upadeśācchiṣyaniṣpādanamiti ।। śrāvaṇo atha ghanaḥ snigdho madhurohyavadhānavān । tristhānaśobhītyevaṃ tu ṣaṭ kaṇṭhasya guṇā matāḥ ।।
udāttaṃ śrūyate yasmāttasmācchrāvaṇa ucyate । śrāvaṇaḥ susvaro yasmādacchinnaḥ sa ghano mataḥ ।। arūkṣadhvanisaṃyuktaḥ snigdhastajjñaiḥ prakīrtitaḥ । manaḥprahlādanakaraḥ sa vai madhura ucyate ।।
svare adhike ca hīne ca hyavirakto vidhānavān । śiraḥkaṇṭheṣvabhihitaṃtristhānamadhurasvaraḥ । tristhānaśobhītyevaṃ tu sa hi tajjñairudāhṛtaḥ ।। kapilo hyavasthitaścaiva tathā sandaṣṭa eva ca ।
kākī ca tumbakī caiva pañca doṣā bhavanti hi ।। vaisvaryaṃ ca bhavedyatra tathā syād ghargharāyitam । kapilaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ śleṣmakaṇṭhastathaiva ca ।। ūnatā'dhikatā cāpi svarāṇāṃ yatra dṛśyate ।
rūkṣadoṣahataścaiva jñeyaḥ sa tvavyavasthitaḥ ।। daṇḍaprayogāt sandaṣṭastvācāryaiḥ parikīrtitaḥ । yo na vistarati sthāne svaramuccāraṇāgatam ।। nāsāgragrastaśabdastutumbakī so abhidhīyate ।।
samapraharaṇe caiva javinau viśadau tathā । jitaśramau vikṛṣṭau ca madhurau svedavarjitau । tathā bṛyannakhau caiva jñeyau hastasya vai guṇāḥ ।। ete guṇāśca doṣāśca tattvataḥ kathito mayā ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi hyavanaddhavidhiṃ punaḥ ।। pūrvaṃ yaduktaṃ prapitāmahena kuryāt ya evaṃ tu naraḥ prayoge sammānamagrayaṃ labhate sa loke ।। vinyāsaṃ bhūmikānāṃ ca sampravakṣyāmi nāṭake । yādṛśo yasya kartavyo vinyāso bhūmikāsvatha ।।
gativāgaṅgaceṣṭābhiḥ sattvaśīlasvabhāvataḥ । parīkṣya pātraṃ tajjñastu yuñjyād bhūminiveśane ।। tasminnanviṣya hi guṇavān kāryā pātrasamāśrayā । na khedajananaṃ buddherācāryasya bhaviṣyati ।।
ācāryaḥ pātrajāṃścaiva guṇāñjñātvā svabhāvajān । tataḥ kuryād yathāyogaṃ nṛṇāṃ bhūminiveśanam ।। aṅgapratyaṅgasaṃyuktamahīnāṅgaṃ vayonvitam । na sthūlaṃ na kṛśaṃ caiva na dīrghaṃ na ca mantharam ।।
śliṣṭāṅgaṃ dyutimantaṃ ca susvaraṃ priyadarśanam । etairguṇaiśca saṃyuktaṃ devabhūmiṣu yojayet ।। sthūlaṃ prāṃśuṃ bṛhaddehaṃ meghagambhīranisvanam । raudrasvabhāvanetraṃ ca svabhāvabhrukuṭīmukham ।।
rakṣodānavadaityānāṃ bhūmikāsu prayojayet । puruṣāṇāṃ prayogastu tathāṅgakriyayānvitaḥ ।। sunetrasubhruvaḥ svaṅgāḥ sulalāṭāḥ sunāsikāḥ । svoṣṭhāḥ sugaṇḍāḥ sumukhāḥ sukaṇṭhāḥ suśirodharāḥ ।।
svaṅgapratyaṅgasaṃyuktā na dīrghā na ca mantharāḥ । na sthūlā na kṛśāścaiva svabhāvena vyavasthitāḥ ।। suśīlā jñānavantaśca tathā ca priyadarśanāḥ । kumārarājabhūmau tu saṃyojyāśca narottamāḥ ।।
aṅgairavikalairdhīraṃ sphuṭaṃ vasanakarmaṇi । na dīrghaṃ naiva ca sthūlamūhāpohavicakṣaṇam ।। adīnaṃ ca pragalbhaṃ ca pratyutpannaviniścayam । senāpateramātyānāṃ bhūmikāsu prayojayet ।।
piṅgākṣaṃ ghoṇanāsaṃ ca netramuccamathāpi vā । kañcukiśrotriyādīnāṃ bhūmikāsu niyojayet ।। evamanyeṣvapi tathā nāṭyadharmavibhāgataḥ । deśaveṣānurūpeṇa pātraṃ yojyaṃ svabhūmiṣu ।।
mantharaṃ vāmanaṃ kubjaṃ vikṛtaṃ vikṛtānanam । viṣṭabdhanetraṃ kāṇākṣaṃ sthūlaṃ cipiṭanāsikam ।। durjanaṃ dusvabhāvaṃ ca vikṛtācārameva ca । dāsabhūmau prayuñjīta budho dāsāṅgasambhavam ।।
prakṛtyā'tikṛśaṃ kṣāmaṃ tapaḥśrānteṣu yojayet । tathā ca puruṣaṃ sthūlamuparodheṣu yojayet ।। yadi vā nedṛśāḥ santi prakṛtyā puruṣā dvijāḥ । ācāryabuddhyā yojyāstu bhāvaceṣṭāsvabhāvataḥ ।।
yā yasya sadṛśī ceṣṭā hyuttamādhamamadhyamā । sa tathā''cāryayogena niyamyā bhāvabhāvinī ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi bharatānāṃ vikalpanam । bharatāśrayāśca bharato vidūṣakaḥ saurikastathā nāndī ।
nandī sasūtradhāro nāṭyaraso nāyakaścaiva ।। mukuṭābharaṇavikalpau vijñeyo mālyavastuvividhaiśca । kārakakuśīlavādyā vijñeyā nāmataścaiva ।। dhuryavadeko yasmāduddhāro anekabhūmikāyuktaḥ ।
bhāṇḍagrahopakaraṇaināṭyaṃ bharato bhavet tasmāt ।। lokāhṛdāśrayakṛtā sarvaprakṛtipracārasaṃyuktā । nānāśrayāṃ prakurute tathā ca nārī tu sarvatra ।। pratyutpannapratibho narmakṛto narmagarbhanirbhedaḥ ।
chedavidūṣitavacano vidūṣako nāma vijñeyaḥ ।। tūryatistu naraḥ sarvātodyapravādane kuśalaḥ । tūraparigrahayukto vijñeyastauriko nāma ।। naṭanṛti dhātvartho ayaṃ bhūtaṃ nāṭayati lokavṛttāntam ।
rasabhāvasatvayuktaṃ yasmāt tasmānnaṭo bhavati ।। stutyabhivādanakṛtairmadhurairvākyaiḥ sumaṅgalācāraiḥ । sarva stauti hi lokaṃ yasmāt tasmādbhavedvādī ।। bhāvebhyo bahudhā'smin rasā vadati nāṭyayogeṣu ।
prākṛtasaṃskṛtapāṭhyo nandī nāmeti sa jñeyaḥ ।। gītasya ca vādyasya ca pāṭhyasya ca naikabhāvavihitasya । śiṣṭopadeśayogāt sūtrajñaḥ sūtradhārastu ।। yasmāt yathopadiṣṭān rasāṃśca bhāvāṃśca satvasaṃyuktān ।
bhūmivikalpairnayati ca nāṭyakaraḥ kīrtitastasmāt ।। caturātodyavidhānaṃ sarvasya tu śāstrakhe davihitasya । nāṭyasyāntaṃ gacchati tasmādvai nāyako abhihitaḥ ।। nānāprakṛtisamutthaṃ karoti yaḥ śīrṣakaṃ mukuṭayoge ।
vividhairveṣaviśeṣaiḥ sa ca kuṭakārastu vijñeyaḥ ।। bhāṇḍakavādyajñā yā layatālajñā rasānuviddhā ca । sarvāṅgasundarī vai kartavyā nāṭakīyā tu ।। yastvābharaṇaṃ kuryād bahuvidhavihitaṃ sa cābharaṇaḥ ।
yaścopakaraṇayogāt sa tena nāmnā'bhidhātavyaḥ ।। yo vai mālyaṃ kurute paṅcavidhaṃ mālyākṛt sa vijñeyaḥ । yaścāpi veṣayogaṃ kurute sa ca veṣakārī tu ।। citrajñaścitrakaro vastrasya rañjānāttathā rajakaḥ ।
jatvaśmalohakāṣṭhairdravyakaraiḥ kārukaścaiva ।। nānātodyavidhāne prayogayuktaḥ pravādane kuśalaḥ । atodye apyatikuśalo yasmāt sa kuśalavo jñeyaḥ ।। yadyat samāśrayante śilpaṃ vā karma vā prayogaṃ vā ।
tanaivopagataguṇā vijñeyā nāmataḥ puruṣāḥ ।। evaṃ tu nāṭakavidhau jātirnaṭasaṃśrayā budhairjñeyā । nāṭyopakaraṇayuktā nānāśilpaprasaktā ca ।। ukto atra bhūmikānyāsaḥ prayoktāraśca yogataḥ ।
ādiṣṭaṃ nāṭyaśāstraṃ ca munayaḥ kimihocyatām ।। athātreyo vasiṣṭhaśca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ । aṅgirā gautamo agastyo manurāyustathātmavān ।। viśvāmitraḥ sthūlaśirāḥ saṃvartaḥ pramatirdanuḥ ।
uśanā bṛhaspatirvyāsaścyavanaḥ kāśyapo dhruvaḥ ।। durvāsā jāmadagnyaśca mārkaṇḍeyo atha gālavaḥ । bharadvājaśca raibhyaśca yavakrītastathaiva ca ।। sthūlākṣaḥ śakalākṣaśca kāṇvo meghātithiḥ kratuḥ ।
nāradaḥ parvataścaiva suvarmāthaikajo dvijaḥ ।। nitamburbhuvanaḥ saumyaḥ śatānandaḥ kṛtavraṇaḥ । jāmadagnyastathā rāmaḥ kacaścetyevamādayaḥ ।। evaṃ te munayaḥ śrutvā sarvajñaṃ bharataṃ tataḥ ।
punarūcuridaṃ vākyaṃ kutūhalapurogamam ।। yastvayā gadito hyeṣa nāṭyavedaḥ purātanaḥ । ekacittaiḥ sa cāsmābhiḥ samyak samupadhāritaḥ ।। ekaśca saṃśayo asmākaṃ taṃ no vyākhyātumarhasi ।
ko vānyo nāṭyavedasya niścayaṃ vaktumarhati ।। na vayaṃ parihāsena na virodhena na cerṣyayā । pṛcchāmo bhagavan nāṭyamupadeśārthameva tu ।। asmābhiśca tadā noktaṃ kathācchedo bhavediti ।
idānīṃ tūpaśikṣārthaṃ nāṭyaguhyaṃ nidarśaya ।। lokasya caritaṃ nāṭyamityavocastvamīdṛśam । teṣāṃ tu lokaṃ guhyānāṃ niścayaṃ vaktumarhasi ।। devasya kasya caritaṃ pūrvaraṅge dvijarṣabha ।
kimarthaṃ bhujyate hyeṣa prayuktaḥ kiṃ karoti vā ।। kasmāccaiva punaḥ śaucaṃ samyak carati sūtradṛk । kathamurvītale nāṭyaṃ svargānnipatitaṃ vibho ।। kathaṃ tavāyaṃ vaṃśaśca naṭasaṃjñaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।
sarvameva yathātattvaṃ kathayasva mahāmune ।। teṣaṃ tu vacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ bharato muniḥ । pratyuvāca punarvākyaṃ guhyārthābhinayaṃ prati ।। bravīmi vaḥ kathāṃ guhyāṃ yanmāṃ pṛcchan suvratāḥ ।
pūrvaraṅgavidhānasya tāṃ ca me sannibodhata ।। proktavānasmi yatpūrvaṃ śubhaṃ vighnanibarhaṇam । tasyānubandhena mayā pūrvaraṅgaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। śastrāṇāṃ pratikārārthaṃ śarīrāvaraṇaṃ yathā ।
kriyate hi tathā pāpaṃ hutenaiva praśāmyati ।। evaṃ japyaiśca homaiśca devatābhyarcanena ca । sarvātodyavidhānaiśca tathā gītasvanena ca ।। stutyāśīrvacanaiḥ śāntaiḥ karmabhāvānukīrtanaiḥ ।
mayā pāpāpaharaṇaiḥ kṛte vighnanibarhaṇe ।। stutigītādisaṃsṛṣṭairdevairabhihito asmyaham । nitarāṃ parituṣṭāḥ smaḥ prayogeṇāmunā ca te ।। devatāsuramānandya yasmāṃllokaśca nandati ।
tasmādayaṃ prayogastu nāndīnāmā bhaviṣyati ।। gītavādyānunādo hi yatra kākusvanaḥ śubhaḥ । tasmin deśe vipāpmāno māṅgalyaṃ ca bhaviṣyati ।। yāvattaṃ pūrayeddeśaṃ dhvanirnāṭyasamāśrayaḥ ।
na sthāsyanti hi rakṣāṃsi taṃ deśaṃ na vināyakāḥ ।। āvāhe ca vivāhe ca yajñe nṛpatimaṅgale । nāndīśabdamupaśrutya hiṃsrā naśyanti caiva hi ।। pāṭhyaṃ nāṭyaṃ tathā geyaṃ citravāditrameva ca ।
vedamantrārthavacanaiḥ samaṃ hyetad bhaviṣyati ।। śrutaṃ mayā devadevāt tattvataḥ śaṅkarāddhitam । snānajapyasahasrebhyaḥ pavitraṃ gītavāditam ।। yasminnātodyanāṭyasya gītapāṭhyadhvaniḥ śubhaḥ ।
bhaviṣyatyaśubhaṃ deśe naiva tasmin kadācana ।। evaṃ pūjādhikārārthaṃ pūrvaraṅgaḥ kṛto mayā । nānāstutikṛtairvākyairdevatābhyarcanena ca ।। yato abhivādanaṃ kliṣṭaṃ śiṣṭaṃ tadraṅgamaṇḍale ।
tatastasya hi tacchaucaṃ vihitaṃ tu dvijottamāḥ ।। śaucaṃ kṛtvā yato mantraṃ pūjanaṃ jarjarasya tu । ucyate pūrvaraṅge asmin tasmācchaucaṃ prakīrtitam ।। yathāvatāritaṃ caiva nāṭyametanmahītale ।
vaktavyaṃ sarvametaddhi na śakyaṃ hi nigūhitum ।। mamaite tanayāḥ sarve nāṭyavedasamanvitāḥ । sarvalokaṃ prahasanaiḥ bādhante nāṭyasaṃśrayaiḥ ।। kasyacittvatha kālasya śilpakaṃ grāmyadharmakam ।
ṛṣīṇāṃ vyaṅgyakaraṇaṃ kurvadbhirguṇasaṃśrayam ।। aśrāvyaṃ taddurācāraṃ grāmyadharmapravartitam । niṣṭhuraṃ cāprastutaṃ ca kāvyaṃ saṃsadi yojitam ।। tacchrutvā munayaḥ sarve bhīmaroṣaprakampitāḥ ।
ūcustān bharatān kruddhā nirdahanta ivāgnayaḥ ।। mā tāvadbho dvijā yuktamidamasmadviḍambanam । ko nāmāyaṃ paribhavaḥ kiñca nāsmāsu sammatam ।। yasmājjñānamadonmattā na vetthāvinayāśritāḥ ।
tasmādetaddhi bhavatāṃ kujñānaṃ nāśameṣyati ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca samavāyasamāgatāḥ । nirāhutā vinā homaiḥ śūdrācārā bhaviṣyatha ।। apāṅkteyāḥ kutsitāścāvamā eva bhaviṣyatha ।
yaśca vo bhavitā vaṃśaḥ sarvāśauco bhaviṣyati ।। ye ca vo vaṃśajāste api bhaviṣyantyatha nartakāḥ । paropasthānavantaśca śastrapaṇyopajīvinaḥ ।। śāpaṃ dattaṃ tathā jñātvā sutebhyo me tadā surāḥ ।
sarve vimanaso bhūtvā tānṛṣīn samupasthitāḥ ।। yācamānaistataḥ proktaṃ devaiḥ śakrapurogamaiḥ । idānīṃ duḥkhamutpannaṃ nāṭyametad vinaṅkṣati ।। ṛṣibhiśca tataḥ proktaṃ na caitaddhi vinakṣyati ।
śeṣamanyatra yad proktaṃ sarvametad bhaviṣyati ।। etacchrutvā tu vacanaṃ munīnāmugratejasām । viṣṇṇāste tataḥ sarve śrutvā māṃ samupasthitāḥ ।। proktavantaśca māṃ putrāstvayāho nāśitā vayam ।
anena nāṭyadoṣeṇa śūdrācārā hi yat kṛtāḥ ।। mayāpi sāntvayitvoktā mā krodhaṃ vrajatānaghāḥ । kṛtāntavihito asmākaṃ nūnameṣa vidhiḥ sutāḥ ।। munīnāṃ hi mṛṣā vākyaṃ bhaviṣyati kadācana ।
nidhane ca mano mā bhūd yuṣmākamiti sāntvitāḥ ।। jānīdhvaṃ tattathā nāṭyaṃ brahmaṇā saṃpravartitam । śiṣyebhyaśca tadanyebhyaḥ prayacchāmaḥ prayogataḥ ।। mā vai praṇaśyatāmetannāṭyaṃ duḥkhapravartitam ।
mahāśrayaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ vedāṅgopāṅgasambhavam ।। apsarobhya idaṃ caiva yathātattvaṃ yathāśrutam । nāṭyaṃ dattvā tataḥ sarve prāyaścittaṃ cariṣyatha ।। kasyacittvatha kālasya nahuṣo nāma pārthivaḥ ।
prāptavān devarājyaṃ hi nayabuddhiparākramaḥ ।। praśaśāsa tadā rājyaṃ devairvyuṣṭimavāpnuvan । gāndharvaṃ caia nāṭyaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā cintāmupāgamat ।। sa cintayitvā manasā kathameṣa gṛhe mama ।
nāṭyaprayogo hi bhavediti sādara eva san ।। kṛtāñjaliḥ prayogārthaṃ proktavāṃstu surān nṛpaḥ । apsarobhiridaṃ sārdhaṃ nāṭyaṃ bhavatu me gṛhe ।। pratyuktaśca tato devairbṛhaspatipurogamaiḥ ।
divyāṅganānāṃ naiveha mānuṣaiḥ saha saṅgatiḥ ।। hitaṃ pathyaṃ ca vaktavyo bhavān svargādhipo hi yat । ācāryāstatra gacchantu gatvā kurvantu te priyam ।। proktavāṃstu tato māṃ tu nṛpatiḥ sa kṛtāñjaliḥ ।
idamicchāmi bhagavan nāṭyamurvyāṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। pūrvamācāryakaṃ caiva bhavatā'bhihitaṃ śrutam । vyaktabhāvātvidaṃ labdhaṃ tvatsakāśād dvijottama ।। pitāmahagṛhe asmākaṃ tadantaḥpure jane ।
pitāmahakriyāyukta murvaśyāṃ sampravartitam ।। tasyāḥ praṇāśaśokena unmādoparate nṛpe । vipanne antaḥpurajane punarnāśamupāgatam ।। prakāśametadicchāmo bhūyastat saṃprayojitam ।
tithiyajñakriyāsvetad yathā syān maṅgalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। tasmin mama gṛhe baddhaṃ nānāprakṛtisaṃśrayam । strīṇāṃ lalitavinyāsairyato naḥ prathayiṣyati ।। tathā'stviti mayā prokto nahuṣaḥ pārthivastadā ।
sutāścāhūya samproktā sāmapūrvaṃ suraiḥ saha ।। ayaṃ hi nahuṣo rājā yācate naḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ । gamyatāṃ sahitairbhūmiṃ prayoktuṃ nāṭyameva ca ।। kariṣyamaśca śāpāntamasmin samyak prayojite ।
brāhmaṇānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca bhaviṣyatha na kutsitāḥ ।। tatra gatvā prayujyantāṃ prayogān vasudhātale । na śakyaṃ cānyathā kartuṃ vacanaṃ pārthivasya hi ।। asmākaṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ nahuṣasya mahātmanaḥ ।
ātmopadeśasiddhaṃ hi nāṭyaṃ proktaṃ svayaṃbhuvā ।। śeṣamuttaratantreṇa kohalastu kariṣyati । prayogaḥ kārikāścaiva niruktāni tathaiva ca ।। apsarobhiridaṃ sārdhaṃ krīḍanīyakahetukam ।
adhiṣṭhitaṃ mayā svarge svātinā nāradena ca ।। tataśca vasudhāṃ gatvā nahuṣasya gṛhe dvijāḥ । strīṇāṃ prayogaṃ bahudhā baddhavanto yathākramam ।। atropabhogataste tu mānuṣīṣu māmātmajāḥ ।
baddhavanto adhikasnehaṃ tāsu tad dvijasattamāḥ ।। putrānutpādya vadhvā ca prayogaṃ ca yathākramam । brahmaṇā samanujñātāḥ prāptāḥ svargaṃ punaḥ sutāḥ ।। evamurvītale nāṭyaṃ śiṣyaiḥ samavatāritam ।
bharatānāṃ ca vaṃśo ayaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca pravartitaḥ ।। kohalādibhirevaṃ tu vatsaśāṇḍilyadhūrtitaiḥ । matyadharmakriyāyuktaiḥ kaścitkālamavasthitaiḥ ।। etacchātraṃ praṇītaṃ hi nārāṇāṃ buddhivardhanam ।
trailokyasya kriyopetaṃ sarvaśāstranidarśanam । maṅgalyaṃ lalitaṃ caiva brahmaṇo vadanodbhavam ।। ya idaṃ śruṇuyān nityaṃ proktaṃ cedaṃ svayambhuvā । kuryāt prayogaṃ yaścaivamathavā'dhītavān naraḥ ।।
yā gatirvedaviduṣāṃ yā gatiryajñakāriṇām । yā gatirdānaśīlānāṃ tāṃ gatiṃ prāpnuyāddhi saḥ ।। dānadharmeṣu sarveṣu kīrtyate tu mahat phalam । prekṣaṇīyapradānaṃ hi sarvadāneṣu śasyate ।।
na tathā gandhamālyena devāstuṣyanti pūjitāḥ । yathā nāṭyaprayogasthairnityaṃ tuṣyanti maṅgalaiḥ ।। gāndharvaṃ ceha nāṭyaṃ ca yaḥ samyak paripālayet । sa īśvaragaṇeśānāṃ labhate sadgatiṃ parām ।।
evaṃ nāṭyaprayoge bahuvidhivihitaṃ karmaśāstraṃ praṇītam । noktaṃ yaccātra lokādanukṛtikaraṇāt । saṃvibhāvyaṃ tu tajjñaiḥ ।। kiṃ cānyat samprapūrṇā bhavatu vasumatī naṣṭadurbhikṣarogā ।
śāntirgobrāhmaṇānāṃ bhavatu narapatiḥ pātu pṛthvīṃ samagrām ।।
